## V17 PHOTObOOK REALISM — COMPLETE SYSTEM
### Source: references/LIL_TROUBLR_V17_SKILL.md
================================================================================

     1|# LIL_TROUBLR V17 — PHOTObOOK REALISM PHASE
     2|### Consolidated Master Skill
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — V17 Includes V14.6 + V17 Systems
     4|### Created: May 31, 2026
     5|
     6|---
     7|
     8|## WHAT IS V17
     9|
    10|**One-liner:** Generate images that feel like actual photographs taken in real moments — with believable reason to exist, spatial depth, realistic fabric physics, authentic film stock rendering, proof-of-life objects, and guided eye flow.
    11|
    12|**Core Philosophy:**
    13|```
    14|V14: Environment → Body → Camera → Memory Fragment
    15|V17: Environment → WHY Photo Exists → Body Physics → Spatial Depth → Film Science → Proof-of-Life → Eye Flow
    16|```
    17|
    18|**Architecture:** V14.6 Memory Realism + V17 Photobook Realism = Complete Generation System
    19|
    20|---
    21|
    22|## V17 PRIORITY HIERARCHY (HIGH → LOW)
    23|
    24|1. **PHOTO EXISTENCE** — WHY this photo exists (NEW V17)
    25|2. **GARMENT PHYSICS** — WHY clothing looks this way (NEW V17)
    26|3. **SPATIAL COMPOSITION** — Foreground/Subject/Background depth (NEW V17)
    27|4. **EYE FLOW** — Visual reading path (NEW V17)
    28|5. **LIVED-IN OBJECTS** — Proof-of-life evidence (NEW V17)
    29|6. **POSE MECHANICS** — HOW body arrives at pose (NEW V17)
    30|7. **FILM STOCK** — Specific rendering science (EXPANDED V17)
    31|8. **MOTION + INTERRUPTION** — from V14.6
    32|9. **ENVIRONMENTAL CAUSATION** — from V14.6
    33|10. **MEMORY IMPERFECTION** — from V14.6
    34|
    35|---
    36|
    37|## 10-LAYER PROMPT STRUCTURE
    38|
    39|### LAYER 1 — IDENTITY LOCK
    40|```
    41|"Create a photorealistic image of lil.troublr: stable facial geometry, 
    42|soft oval face, slight apple-cheek fullness, expressive almond-shaped eyes, 
    43|chestnut-dark layered hair, softly full lips, realistic warm East Asian skin texture, 
    44|tiny faint beauty mark beside left eye near outer corner, 170cm mature hourglass 
    45|silhouette expressed through fabric behavior and posture. No face drift, no generic influencer face."
    46|```
    47|**Trigger:** ALL generation sessions. Re-anchor every 20-30 generations.
    48|
    49|---
    50|
    51|### LAYER 2 — PHOTO EXISTENCE LOGIC ⭐ V17 NEW PRIORITY
    52|```
    53|"[EXISTENCE REASON]: [specific human behavior generating the photo]
    54|— [Context: where/why]
    55|— [Visible evidence supporting reason]"
    56|```
    57|**Existence Reasons by Space:**
    58|
    59|| Space | Reasons | Evidence |
    60||-------|---------|----------|
    61|| Hotel | Outfit check, just arrived, post-shower, waiting for friend | Key card, phone in hand, one shoe on |
    62|| Beach | Testing swimsuit, resting after swim, applying sunscreen | Phone, towel, half-drunk water |
    63|| MTR | Waiting for train, killing time, heading home | Octopus card, shopping bag, earphones |
    64|| Apartment | Post-shower, testing outfit, morning coffee | Towel, mirror, mug |
    65|| Café | Waiting for food, killing time, friend photo | Cup, phone, bag on chair |
    66|
    67|**Rule:** Every image MUST have a believable reason to exist.
    68|
    69|---
    70|
    71|### LAYER 3 — ENVIRONMENT CAUSATION FIRST
    72|```
    73|"[ENVIRONMENT TYPE]: [specific location from families A-E]
    74|— [weather type if present: rain/wind/humidity/heat]
    75|— [physical causation chain visible in scene]
    76|— [environment-specific HK texture]"
    77|```
    78|**Families:**
    79|- A (Transitional): MTR corridor, ferry boarding, airport, elevator, parking garage
    80|- B (Micro-destinations): Bowling shoe rental, photo booth, laundromat, karaoke waiting
    81|- C (Domestic): Apartment entrance, bathroom mirror after shower, kitchen late-night, couch after nap
    82|- D (Weather-dominated): Typhoon shelter, humid bus stop, post-rain reflections, windy harbor
    83|- E (Transportation): Late-night taxi, ferry window seat, MTR peak hour, bus upper deck corner
    84|
    85|---
    86|
    87|### LAYER 4 — SPATIAL COMPOSITION ⭐ V17 NEW SYSTEM
    88|```
    89|"[SPATIAL DEPTH]: [three-zone structure]
    90|— FOREGROUND: [object at frame edge, 5-15% frame]
    91|— SUBJECT: [clear focus, mid-ground]
    92|— BACKGROUND: [location context, [sharp/soft/bokeh]]"
    93|```
    94|**Spatial Templates:**
    95|```
    96|BEACH: foreground sand/towel edge → subject on towel → background ocean
    97|HOTEL: foreground blanket/pillow → subject on bed → background window
    98|MTR: foreground pole/rail → subject in car → background door/depth
    99|BEDROOM: foreground bedding fold → subject face → background window
   100|CAFÉ: foreground cup edge → subject at table → background interior
   101|```
   102|
   103|---
   104|
   105|### LAYER 5 — CAMERA AWARENESS
   106|```
   107|"[AWARENESS LEVEL]: [choose one]
   108|— Level 1 = influencer (knowingly documented)
   109|— Level 2 = friend-shot (acknowledged but casual)
   110|— Level 3 = forgotten PRIMARY ⭐ (in her moment, camera intercepted)
   111|— Level 4 = documentary (observer at distance, subject unaware)"
   112|```
   113|**Rule:** Level 3 or 4 for 80%+ of generations.
   114|
   115|---
   116|
   117|### LAYER 6 — POSE MECHANICS ⭐ V17 NEW SYSTEM
   118|```
   119|"[BODY MECHANICS]: [how body physically arrives]
   120|— [Weight: shifts/drops/sinks]
   121|— [Joints: bend/rotate/extend]
   122|— [Micro-movement: one element in-progress]
   123|— [Surface: contact/pressure/release]"
   124|```
   125|**Mechanics Examples:**
   126|- "Weight lowering onto bed edge, hand reaching back to feel mattress"
   127|- "Knees on towel, hip still slightly raised, about to lower"
   128|- "Shoulder lifting, arm reaching toward phone on table"
   129|- "Back foot pushing off, weight transferring, not yet balanced"
   130|
   131|**Rule:** Describe the BECOMING, not the BEEN.
   132|
   133|---
   134|
   135|### LAYER 7 — MEMORY CAPTURE + FILM STOCK
   136|```
   137|"[MEMORY CAPTURE]: [imperfect type, minimum 1, combine 2-3]
   138|— INCOMPLETE FRAMING: body partly leaving frame, accidental crop
   139|— MOTION CONTAMINATION: slight blur from walking, shutter lag
   140|— EMOTIONAL TIMING: before smile apex, interrupted laugh
   141|— ENVIRONMENTAL INTERRUPTION: umbrella edge, wind blur
   142|
   143|[FILM STOCK]: [specific from V17 system]
   144|— Fujifilm Pro 400H: peach skin, magenta shadow, fine grain, soft halation
   145|— Fujicolor C200: warm peachy, slight fade, muted green
   146|— Kodak Gold 200: golden amber, honey skin, orange halation
   147|— Kodak Portra 400: natural pink skin, cyan shadow, clean
   148|— CineStill 800T: tungsten orange + blue shadow war
   149|— Gravure Photobook: soft focus skin, sharp clear eyes, centered composition"
   150|```
   151|**Film + Environment Match:**
   152|```
   153|OVERCAST: Pro 400H (enhances peach skin)
   154|GOLDEN HOUR: Gold 200 (maximizes warmth)
   155|INDOOR WINDOW: Pro 400H (window light ideal)
   156|NIGHT STREET: CineStill 800T (orange/blue war)
   157|CASUAL: C200 (everyday aesthetic)
   158|GRAVURE: Pro 400H + soft focus (idol look)
   159|```
   160|
   161|---
   162|
   163|### LAYER 8 — GARMENT PHYSICS ⭐ V17 NEW SYSTEM
   164|```
   165|"[FABRIC PHYSICS]: [WHY clothing looks this way]
   166|— [Gravity: pulls/drapes/pools/compresses]
   167|— [Body interaction: contours/gaps/pressure]
   168|— [Layer behavior: stacks/exposes/shadows]
   169|— [Weight: heavy/light/fatigued]"
   170|```
   171|**Physics Examples:**
   172|- "Cardigan hanging open, front panels separated by gravity, inner shirt visible through gap"
   173|- "Skirt bunched at back from sitting, front fabric pulled taut"
   174|- "Thin camisole clinging to torso, body contour visible through fabric"
   175|- "Sleeve slipped from shoulder, seam resting on upper arm"
   176|- "Wet fabric heavier, clinging to body contour from rain"
   177|
   178|**Rule:** Explain WHY fabric looks this way, not just WHAT it is.
   179|
   180|---
   181|
   182|### LAYER 9 — LIVED-IN OBJECTS ⭐ V17 NEW SYSTEM
   183|```
   184|"[PROOF-OF-LIFE OBJECTS]: [3-5 visible, imperfect state]
   185|— [Object]: [imperfect state evidence]"
   186|```
   187|**Objects by Space:**
   188|```
   189|HOTEL: key card on desk, charger cable visible, slippers kicked off, water bottle half-empty
   190|BEACH: towel spread unevenly, sunscreen half-used sandy, flip flops to side, water bottle half-empty
   191|MTR: Octopus card on knee, earphones cable visible, shopping bag at feet, phone face-down on lap
   192|HOME: phone charging cable, mug with residue, remote on couch, blanket half-folded
   193|CAFÉ: cup half-finished, phone on table, bag on chair, napkin torn
   194|```
   195|
   196|**Rule:** Objects in USE state, not decorative placement.
   197|
   198|---
   199|
   200|### LAYER 10 — EYE FLOW ⭐ V17 NEW SYSTEM
   201|```
   202|"[EYE FLOW PATH]: [visual reading journey]
   203|— ANCHOR: [where eye starts — brightest element/foreground/corner]
   204|— PATH: [leading line to subject]
   205|— DESTINATION: [face/eyes as final resting point]"
   206|```
   207|**Eye Flow Templates:**
   208|```
   209|BOTTOM-UP: Floor object → body → face (ground level shots)
   210|DIAGONAL: Corner → leading line → subject (dynamic)
   211|FOREGROUND LEAD: Foreground object → subject → face (depth emphasis)
   212|LIGHT SOURCE: Window light → lit body → face (romantic/dreamy)
   213|OBJECT→EYE: Phone/product → hand → face → eyes (activity focus)
   214|ENVIRONMENTAL: Space → position → face (documentary)
   215|```
   216|
   217|---
   218|
   219|## COMPOUND INTEGRATION EXAMPLES
   220|
   221|### Example 1: BEACH HOTEL SESSION
   222|```
   223|Layer 1: lil.troublr identity
   224|Layer 2: OUTFIT CHECK — testing new swimsuit, sending photo to boyfriend
   225|Layer 3: Hotel room with beach view, late afternoon humid heat
   226|Layer 4: FG: suitcase edge + bikini top on bed → SUBJECT: at mirror → BG: beach visible
   227|Layer 5: Level 3 forgotten (checking herself, not camera)
   228|Layer 6: Weight shifting, arm reaching toward mirror, foot planted for balance
   229|Layer 7: MEM: motion blur from reaching + FILM: Pro 400H (gravure)
   230|Layer 8: Swimsuit clinging from humid air, fabric showing body contour
   231|Layer 9: Phone in hand, mirror fog from humidity, half-drunk water on desk
   232|Layer 10: ANCHOR: phone in hand → PATH: arm to shoulder → DEST: face in mirror
   233|```
   234|
   235|### Example 2: MTR LATE NIGHT
   236|```
   237|Layer 1: lil.troublr identity
   238|Layer 2: HEADING HOME — late night MTR after drinks with friends
   239|Layer 3: E-family, empty MTR car, late night, tired
   240|Layer 4: FG: handrail + someone's bag → SUBJECT: seated → BG: train door
   241|Layer 5: Level 4 documentary (candid, unaware)
   242|Layer 6: Body settling into seat, weight sinking, eyes half-closed
   243|Layer 7: MEM: imperfect focus + FILM: CineStill 800T (tungsten warmth)
   244|Layer 8: Dress fabric showing fatigue, slight wrinkles, not crisp
   245|Layer 9: Shopping bag on lap, earphones in, phone face-down, tired expression
   246|Layer 10: ANCHOR: shopping bag → PATH: up body → DEST: tired face looking down
   247|```
   248|
   249|### Example 3: HOTEL MORNING
   250|```
   251|Layer 1: lil.troublr identity
   252|Layer 2: JUST WOKE UP — morning phone check, hasn't left bed yet
   253|Layer 3: C-family domestic, hotel room, morning light through curtains
   254|Layer 4: FG: tangled blanket edge → SUBJECT: half on pillow → BG: window light
   255|Layer 5: Level 3 (phone in hand, not performing)
   256|Layer 6: Still half-lying, arm reaching for phone, morning stiffness
   257|Layer 7: MEM: incomplete framing + FILM: Pro 400H (soft morning glow)
   258|Layer 8: Robe loose, fabric pooling, skin showing where robe shifted
   259|Layer 9: Phone on chest, pillow dented, curtains letting in uneven light
   260|Layer 10: ANCHOR: phone on chest → PATH: hand → DEST: squinting face
   261|```
   262|
   263|---
   264|
   265|## MODERATION RULES (8 HARD RULES)
   266|
   267|1. **No glamour framing** — worm-eye = environmental immersion, NEVER = body elongation
   268|2. **Photo existence required** — every image needs WHY it exists
   269|3. **Fabric physics required** — explain WHY clothing looks this way
   270|4. **Proof-of-life objects required** — 3-5 imperfect objects visible
   271|5. **Spatial depth required** — always foreground + subject + background
   272|6. **Camera awareness Level 3/4 for intimate content** — no Level 1 with exposure
   273|7. **Gravure = soft focus skin, sharp eyes** — never clinical/harsh
   274|8. **Anti-fetish physics** — wet fabric = weather-caused, garment physics = realistic
   275|
   276|---
   277|
   278|## ANTI-AI COMPOUND REFERENCE
   279|
   280|| Scene | Compound Layers | Anti-AI Level |
   281||-------|----------------|--------------|
   282|| Beach outfit check | EXIST + SPATIAL + POSE + FILM + GARMENT + LIVE + EYE | EXTREME |
   283|| MTR late night | EXIST + SPATIAL + MEM + FILM + GARMENT + LIVE + EYE | EXTREME |
   284|| Hotel morning | EXIST + SPATIAL + POSE + FILM + GARMENT + LIVE + EYE | EXTREME |
   285|| Gravure portrait | FILM + EYE + GARMENT + SPATIAL | EXTREME |
   286|| Documentary street | SPATIAL + MEM + FILM + POSE + EXIST | HIGH |
