## CHARACTER IDENTITY & SYSTEM REFERENCE
### Source: references/SKILL.md
================================================================================

     1|# lil.troublr Prompting Skill — Latest Version
     2|
     3|## Purpose
     4|
     5|This skill is for the AContent / Prompt Ref project. It helps generate and refine prompts for a consistent Instagram virtual KOL character named **lil.troublr**.
     6|
     7|This is not a one-off beauty image workflow. This is a character-consistency, prompt-engineering, and image-generation pipeline for an adult-but-Instagram-safe soft-glam virtual KOL.
     8|
     9|## Source Context
    10|
    11|Current project workflow:
    12|
    13|Character → Prompt Pack → Batch Request Pack → Human Review → Image Generation → Approval → Draft → Schedule → Post
    14|
    15|Public account identity:
    16|
    17|- **lil.troublr**
    18|
    19|Internal legacy repo label:
    20|
    21|- **Celine**
    22|
    23|Rule:
    24|
    25|- If older repo files mention `Celine`, treat that as the same core character anchor.
    26|- For new outward-facing prompts, always use **lil.troublr**.
    27|
    28|## Core Character Identity
    29|
    30|lil.troublr is:
    31|
    32|- adult Hong Kong woman, age 24+
    33|- Instagram virtual KOL
    34|- Hong Kong girl energy
    35|- elegant, pure, soft, feminine, 氣質美
    36|- clean and gentle at first glance
    37|- cute, shy, softly playful
    38|- smiles often
    39|- sometimes has a cute 瞇眼 smile
    40|- sometimes slightly naughty
    41|- attractive in a subtle, believable, Instagram-safe way
    42|- natural, lived-in, observational, not over-staged
    43|
    44|Fixed identity anchors:
    45|
    46|- same woman across all images, not just same vibe
    47|- soft oval face
    48|- bright natural eyes
    49|- dark brown medium-long softly wavy hair
    50|- warm natural skin texture
    51|- natural softly full lips
    52|- refined brows
    53|- clean refined makeup
    54|- small dark beauty mark under the left eye, slightly toward the outer corner
    55|
    56|Avoid identity drift into:
    57|
    58|- generic influencer face
    59|- Korean-idol face unless specifically requested as a style influence
    60|- anime / doll-like face
    61|- younger-looking teen-coded face
    62|- plastic beauty-filter skin
    63|
    64|## Current Priority: Reference Lock First
    65|
    66|The immediate priority is to create a comprehensive **reference-lock set** for lil.troublr before generating profit / bold KOL images.
    67|
    68|Generate one image per prompt only.
    69|
    70|Do not create:
    71|
    72|- collage
    73|- grid
    74|- contact sheet
    75|- thumbnail set
    76|- magazine layout
    77|- multi-panel image
    78|
    79|Recommended first reference-lock set:
    80|
    81|### 1. Front Face Anchor
    82|
    83|- indoor natural window light
    84|- chest-up or upper-waist portrait
    85|- full front face
    86|- soft shy smile
    87|- hair down, medium-long dark brown waves
    88|- simple fitted sage / cream knit top
    89|- neutral Hong Kong apartment background
    90|
    91|### 2. Left 3/4 Soft Smile
    92|
    93|- same room / same wardrobe family
    94|- left 3/4 face angle
    95|- looking slightly past camera
    96|- cute shy smile
    97|- similar hair, maybe half-tied
    98|- window side light
    99|
   100|### 3. Right 3/4 Shy Phone Moment
   101|
   102|- right 3/4 angle
   103|- slight chin-down, eyes softly lifted
   104|- gentle 瞇眼 smile
   105|- phone or mug as small lifestyle prop
   106|- warm natural indoor realism
   107|
   108|### 4. Mirror Selfie Identity Test
   109|
   110|- bright window beside mirror
   111|- deep burgundy fitted top or cream fitted knit
   112|- high-waist shorts or simple skirt
   113|- side-profile mirror selfie
   114|- head turned back toward phone camera
   115|- phone partially covers one side of face
   116|- natural room clutter
   117|- upper-thigh crop
   118|
   119|Reason:
   120|
   121|Do not start with the boldest profit image. If the first reference images are too bold, the model may lock onto body pose, outfit tension, private mood, or specific clothing instead of the face. First lock the face, eyes, hair, skin, beauty mark, and cute shy soft-glam personality.
   122|
   123|## Prompt Hierarchy
   124|
   125|Use this order:
   126|
   127|place → atmosphere → activity → camera realism → styling / fabric → personality → attractiveness as emergent result
   128|
   129|Do not start with:
   130|
   131|body → exposure → attractiveness → scene
   132|
   133|The final image should feel like:
   134|
   135|> a naturally attractive Hong Kong KOL existing inside a believable moment
   136|
   137|not:
   138|
   139|> an image designed to maximize attraction
   140|
   141|## Prompt Writing Standard
   142|
   143|Every final image prompt should be:
   144|
   145|- long
   146|- detailed
   147|- scene-specific
   148|- camera-aware
   149|- texture-aware
   150|- explicit about what to keep
   151|- explicit about what to avoid
   152|
   153|Do not rely on short tags alone.
   154|
   155|A good final prompt should include:
   156|
   157|1. adult age anchor
   158|2. exact scene and Hong Kong context
   159|3. lil.troublr identity lock
   160|4. activity / reason for the pose
   161|5. pose geometry
   162|6. outfit and exposure level
   163|7. fabric / material behavior
   164|8. composition and camera feel
   165|9. lighting quality
   166|10. texture realism
   167|11. emotional tone
   168|12. safety / drift-prevention constraints
   169|
   170|## Hong Kong Realism Rules
   171|
   172|Hong Kong scenes should feel lived-in, not empty or generic.
   173|
   174|Use local texture:
   175|
   176|- passersby
   177|- residents
   178|- scooters
   179|- tiled walls
   180|- potted plants
   181|- laundry racks
   182|- wet pavement
   183|- storefront glow
   184|- local clutter
   185|- small community corners
   186|- older cafés
   187|- piers
   188|- ferries
   189|- rooftops
   190|- stair landings
   191|- public housing edges
   192|- small waterfronts
   193|- shop signs
   194|- household objects
   195|
   196|Avoid:
   197|
   198|- suspiciously empty public scenes
   199|- overusing famous postcard tourist spots
   200|- fake sterile backgrounds
   201|
   202|## Composition Rules
   203|
   204|Do not make every image front-facing.
   205|
   206|Use more:
   207|
   208|- half-side view
   209|- over-shoulder glance
   210|- looking away
   211|- looking at phone screen instead of lens
   212|- mid-action framing
   213|- observational framing
   214|- slightly imperfect selfies
   215|- mirror selfies
   216|- knee-up shots
   217|- full-body shots
   218|- environment-heavy shots
   219|- subject smaller in frame when the place matters
   220|
   221|Vary face angles:
   222|
   223|- full front but shy smile
   224|- left 3/4 soft smile
   225|- right 3/4 closed-eye laugh
   226|- full side profile
   227|- over-shoulder turning back
   228|- chin slightly down, eyes softly lifted
   229|- looking slightly past camera
   230|- looking down at an object
   231|- 瞇眼 smile
   232|
   233|Important personality direction:
   234|
   235|lil.troublr is cute, shy, softly playful. She smiles a lot, but expressions should stay human and not exaggerated.
   236|
   237|## Environmental Intimacy
   238|
   239|Build closeness through the environment, not through viewer-intimacy.
   240|
   241|Use:
   242|
   243|- lived-in room detail
   244|- window frames
   245|- sofa
   246|- coffee table
   247|- phone charger
   248|- mug
   249|- papers
   250|- open handbag
   251|- bedside lamp
   252|- wardrobe
   253|- kitchenette
   254|- mirror
   255|- scattered accessories
   256|- warm light
   257|- natural clutter
   258|- foreground / midground / background layering
   259|
   260|Avoid stacking:
   261|
   262|- boyfriend POV
   263|- private encounter
   264|- intimate-feeling
   265|- charged
   266|- seductive
   267|- teasing in a direct sexual way
   268|- viewer intimacy simulation
   269|- “shot by someone sitting nearby”
   270|- “private off-shot”
   271|- “gently parted lips” plus close indoor scene
   272|- “touching rim with tongue”
   273|
   274|Use:
   275|
   276|- believable domestic realism
   277|- casual candid moment
   278|- everyday pause
   279|- observed from a natural angle
   280|- organic IG lifestyle post
   281|- documentary-style realism
   282|
   283|## Top-to-Bottom Body-Clothing Causality Grammar
   284|
   285|Latest major skill upgrade:
   286|
   287|When describing a specific action or pose, build physical logic from top to bottom:
   288|
   289|head angle → neck / shoulder direction → upper-body weight shift → arm support point → waist / core support → seated leg base → outer clothing response → inner fabric edge / layer overlap → folds / shadows / fabric stacking → lifestyle mood anchor
   290|
   291|This is useful for:
   292|
   293|- sofa homewear
   294|- phone snapshot
   295|- leaning forward
   296|- kneeling on sofa
   297|- mirror selfie
   298|- holding a drink
   299|- checking phone
   300|- laughing naturally
   301|
   302|Keep the prompt safe by making **activity and environment** the reason for the pose.
   303|
   304|Good causality language:
   305|
   306|- natural weight distribution
   307|- relaxed fabric drape
   308|- visible fold behavior
   309|- layered fabric edge
   310|- seated-posture fabric stacking
   311|- soft shadow transitions
   312|- realistic clothing response
   313|- clothing falls naturally with posture
   314|- fabric texture stays believable
   315|- seam and hem shadows
   316|- layered edges
   317|- matte cotton texture
   318|- soft stretch fabric
   319|
   320|Avoid overusing:
   321|
   322|- body curve
   323|- chest tension
   324|- strong compression
   325|- inner underwear
   326|- strong pulling
   327|- huge neckline
   328|- curve of her form
   329|- fabric drawn forward
   330|- body-contouring
   331|- breast / chest physics
   332|
   333|## Successful Home Prompt Lesson
   334|
   335|A successful Cantonese prompt used this structure:
   336|
   337|體型 → 服裝 → ポーズ
   338|
   339|Core learning:
   340|
   341|pose causes weight distribution → weight distribution affects body support → body support affects clothing layers → clothing layers create folds, shadows, stacking → mood is pulled back to relaxed home realism
   342|
   343|Useful concepts:
   344|
   345|- 真實人體比例
   346|- 重量分佈
   347|- 自然重心
   348|- 生活化姿勢
   349|- 布料受力
   350|- 柔和陰影
   351|- 細微皺摺
   352|- 自然布料堆疊
   353|- 生活化與自然人體重量感
   354|- 隨意、真實、非刻意展示
   355|- 捕捉使用電話時甜笑的自然瞬間
   356|- 避免刻意擺 pose
   357|
   358|For lil.troublr:
   359|
   360|- age must be 24+
   361|- activity first
   362|- identity lock first
   363|- home realism
   364|- phone action
   365|- cute shy smile
   366|- no youth-coded framing
   367|
   368|Soften risky terms:
   369|
   370|- 20歲 → adult 24+
   371|- 巨型領口 → relaxed wide neckline
   372|- 內褲 → inner fabric edge / layered fabric edge
   373|- 嚴重受壓 → visible natural folds
   374|- 強烈拉扯 → fabric shifts naturally from posture
   375|
   376|## Mirror Selfie Prompt Structure
   377|
   378|A strong mirror selfie prompt structure:
   379|
   380|- realistic indoor smartphone mirror selfie
   381|- bright window near mirror
   382|- ordinary apartment living room or bedroom corner
   383|- phone near face, partially covering one side
   384|- subject sideways with head turned back toward phone camera
   385|- deep burgundy fitted long-sleeve top
   386|- black high-waisted fitted shorts
   387|- window backlight almost overexposed white
   388|- darker indoor space
   389|- low-contrast gray smartphone look
   390|- lived-in room details
   391|- phone-camera compression
   392|- mild grain / realistic smartphone noise
   393|
   394|What is strong:
   395|
   396|- capture format first
   397|- clear mirror logic
   398|- strong window lighting behavior
   399|- lived-in environment objects
   400|- phone-camera compression
   401|- mild grain
   402|- realistic smartphone noise
   403|- clothing described through color, cut, textile, and silhouette
   404|
   405|Improve for lil.troublr:
   406|
   407|- reduce “back arch,” “hip shift,” “fingers touching thigh”
   408|- avoid exposed-skin inventory
   409|- make expression cute / shy / softly playful
   410|- make pose more observational than model-directed
   411|
   412|## Y2K / CCD Indoor Snapshot Module
   413|
   414|Use this style family for nightlife / hotel / room shots:
   415|
   416|**Y2K CCD Indoor Snapshot / Environmental Intimacy Fashion**
   417|
   418|Core structure:
   419|
   420|identity lock → room clutter → fashion styling → direct flash → imperfect crop → cute shy / softly playful expression
   421|
   422|Camera vocabulary:
   423|
   424|- direct on-camera flash
   425|- compact digital camera feel
   426|- CCD snapshot character
   427|- Y2K party-camera realism
   428|- flash falloff into a dim room
   429|- slightly harsh flash highlights
   430|- mild digital noise
   431|- imperfect candid framing
   432|- background falls darker
   433|- off-center vertical composition
   434|- mid-thigh crop
   435|- low-light indoor realism
   436|
   437|Wardrobe / fashion vocabulary:
   438|
   439|- nightlife-inspired styling
   440|- cut-out fashion top
   441|- wraparound detail
   442|- low-rise trousers
   443|- matte stretch fabric
   444|- layered edges
   445|- seam shadows
   446|- flash sheen on fabric
   447|- fitted knit layer
   448|- soft stretch fabric
   449|- silver necklace
   450|- small hoop earrings
   451|- thin bracelet
   452|- subtle navel accessory
   453|- small tattoo detail
   454|
   455|Expression vocabulary:
   456|
   457|- cute
   458|- shy
   459|- softly playful
   460|- calm nighttime confidence
   461|- gentle 瞇眼 smile
   462|- self-aware but casual
   463|- relaxed natural expression
   464|
   465|Avoid stacking:
   466|
   467|- seductive
   468|- provocative
   469|- erotic
   470|- private encounter
   471|- intimate viewer framing
   472|- body-first wording
   473|
   474|## Swimsuit / Resort / Pool Handling
   475|
   476|Swimwear can be used, but context matters.
   477|
   478|Do not use advertisement / poster context because it may generate:
   479|
   480|- fake slogans
   481|- logos
   482|- product labels
   483|- campaign typography
   484|- poster layout
   485|
   486|Use IG post context instead:
   487|
   488|- IG photo dump
   489|- staycation diary
   490|- poolside check-in
   491|- travel vlog still
   492|- friend-shot vacation candid
   493|- hotel amenity visit
   494|- beach café day
   495|- resort routine
   496|- summer weekend diary
   497|- organic KOL lifestyle post
   498|
   499|Always add:
   500|
   501|

================================================================================
## V14 MEMORY CAPTURE SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V14/MEMORY_CAPTURE_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# MEMORY_CAPTURE_SYSTEM.md
     2|### AContent / lil.troublr V14.6 Core Module
     3|### Human Memory Realism — Camera Imperfectly Remembering a Lived Moment
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## WHY THIS SYSTEM EXISTS
     8|
     9|AI image generators produce **optimized images**:
    10|
    11|- Perfect centering
    12|- Full anatomy in frame
    13|- Sharp focus throughout
    14|- Ideal composition
    15|- Complete expressions
    16|- Static perfection
    17|
    18|Human memory captures **imperfect reconstructions**:
    19|
    20|- Emotional timing prioritised over technical perfection
    21|- Incomplete fragments
    22|- Imperfect focus
    23|- Distracted gaze
    24|- Environmental interruption
    25|- Timing-over-anatomy
    26|
    27|The V14.6 engine shifts from "beautiful social realism" to **"emotionally remembered human-world realism"**.
    28|
    29|The image should feel: recovered, interrupted, imperfectly captured, physically constrained, emotionally unfinished, socially believable, environmentally caused.
    30|
    31|NOT: designed, optimized, glamour-framed, viewer-serving, pose-first.
    32|
    33|---
    34|
    35|## THE MEMORY ENCODING PRINCIPLE
    36|
    37|Human memory prioritises:
    38|
    39|1. **Emotional peak moment** — the exact heartbeat when something felt real
    40|2. **Environmental texture** — what the room/light/air felt like, not the perfect angle
    41|3. **Sensory fragment** — a specific detail that triggered the memory (wet fabric, cold tile, someone's laugh)
    42|4. **Temporal position** — before/during/after a social moment, not perfectly on-moment
    43|5. **Constraint acknowledgment** — what limited the shot (darkness, distance, movement)
    44|
    45|When a camera genuinely captures a moment worth remembering:
    46|- The moment is usually already passing
    47|- Composition is secondary to preserving the feeling
    48|- Imperfection is the signature of authenticity
    49|- Incomplete framing means the photographer was inside the moment, not outside directing it
    50|
    51|**Core principle:**
    52|*"The photo exists because the photographer was moved. Not because the scene was set."*
    53|
    54|---
    55|
    56|## SYSTEM 1: INCOMPLETE FRAMING
    57|
    58|### What AI Does
    59|- Always keeps full anatomy in frame
    60|- Centers subject precisely
    61|- Maintains rule-of-thirds idealization
    62|- Renders complete environmental context
    63|
    64|### What Human Memory Does
    65|- Framing is accidental, not designed
    66|- Body parts leave frame naturally (turning, bending, leaning)
    67|- Horizon tilts without awareness
    68|- Objects obstruct because the photographer was chasing a feeling
    69|- Cropping happens mid-expression, mid-movement
    70|
    71|### Incomplete Framing Types
    72|
    73|**A. Accidental Crop**
    74|- Shoulder or arm cutting frame edge at angle, not straight cut
    75|- Head tilted slightly past frame boundary
    76|- Waist or hip消失在frame boundary，而非刻意midriff shot
    77|- Hair部分離開畫面邊緣（甩出咗嚟）
    78|- Leg消失在膝蓋以上，唔係標準full-leg framing
    79|
    80|**B. Timing-Over-Anatomy**
    81|- Subject's hand moves out of frame mid-gesture
    82|- Foot steps just beyond frame edge (caught mid-step)
    83|- Hair flips past frame boundary at apex of movement
    84|- Body turns away AND head tilts, chest nearly invisible
    85|- Phone held too high, chin部分cut off
    86|
    87|**C. Horizon Imbalance**
    88|- Slight tilt (8-15 degrees) — not dramatic aesthetic tilt, just unlevel
    89|- Horizon line intersects subject at awkward position (neck, waist)
    90|- Sea/ceiling/wall dominates unexpectedly
    91|- Subject positioned extremely off-center because photographer tracked movement
    92|
    93|**D. Obstructed Objects**
    94|- Foreground object partially obscures subject (bag strap, glass edge, furniture corner)
    95|- Subject behind/beside another person — face partially hidden
    96|- Umbrella or plant interrupts view
    97|- Someone's shoulder in frame edge
    98|- 燈柱/柱/欄杆/電線杆 positioned awkwardly, not artistically
    99|
   100|**E. Body Partially Leaving Frame**
   101|- Leaning forward/backward causes torso to leave frame top/bottom
   102|- Turning causes hip to leave frame side
   103|- Sitting causes leg to leave frame
   104|- Reaching causes arm to leave frame
   105|
   106|### Prompt Grammar
   107|
   108|```
   109|[MAIN SUBJECT] captured at [ANGLE] by [OPERATOR]
   110|— [frame disruption type] — [cause/reason in-world]
   111|— [body part] exiting frame at [side/angle]
   112|— [obstruction type] partially blocking [subject area]
   113|— [horizon description]
   114|```
   115|
   116|### Trigger Conditions
   117|- **Moonlit / nighttime scenes**: darkness naturally causes imperfect framing
   118|- **Movement sequences**: turning, laughing, walking naturally produce crop
   119|- **Environmental intimacy scenes**: foreground clutter creates natural obstruction
   120|- **Social group contexts**: human obstacles produce natural obstruction
   121|- **Beach/water scenes**: reflective/rippling surfaces cause partial visibility
   122|
   123|### Implementation Examples
   124|
   125|```
   126|// Moonlit shoreline, accidentally captured
   127|realistic moonlight shoreline, warm korean slim woman,
   128|casual white linen shirt unbuttoned at top 2 buttons,
   129|dark denim shorts, bare feet in shallow warm tidal water,
   130|[HALF-BODY FORM nearchest frame left edge, body weight shifted
   131|forward as if about to pick up shell from wet sand],
   132|waist-level angle from slightly behind girlfriend's right shoulder,
   133|evening blue-hour shoreline, cool moonlight on water surface,
   134|phone snapshot from girlfriend, casual walking-away moment,
   135|[PHONE HELD SLIGHTLY HIGH, chin部分cut off above lip],
   136|skin showing natural warm redness from evening sun,
   137|3-degree tilt, [WATER EDGE cuts through subject's bare ankles],
   138|slight motion blur on water behind, phone-camera compression,
   139|// EMOTIONAL MEMORY FRAGMENT: [frozen mid-laugh
   140|breath just expelled, mouth not yet closed back]
   141|
   142|// Seated on sofa, interrupted by phone
   143|realistic ordinary apartment living room, afternoon warm light,
   144|slim korean woman seated on gray linen sofa, oversized cream
   145|long-sleeve knit cardigan worn loose, [RIGHT ARM extended along
   146|sofa backrest, hand disappearing past frame right edge],
   147|white bralette visible at deep V-neckline of cardigan,
   148|[stray hair strand falling across cheek at mouth height],
   149|half-profile turned toward phone held low,
   150|[EXPRESSION frozen at moment before smile, lips just parting],
   151|soft natural light from left window, mild digital noise,
   152|casual girlfriend candid, body angled 30 degrees from camera,
   153|// EMOTIONAL MEMORY: [eye contact just broken, gaze drifting
   154|toward something outside frame — photographer was second choice]
   155|
   156|// Overhead poolside — water-splash moment
   157|overhead hotel poolside, late afternoon rim-light,
   158|slim korean woman [LOWER LEGS submerged in pool from mid-shin,
   159|knees appearing to cut frame BOTTOM edge at sharp diagonal],
   160|[ONE ARM holding phone above water, wrist invisible above frame],
   161|skin flushed warm from water temperature,
   162|black one-piece swimsuit with subtle V-open back,
   163|hair gathered to one side, wet dark hair clinging to neck,
   164|[CROPPED at chest height, subject filling only upper 60% of frame],
   165|reflective pool surface visible, [TILTED 10 DEGREES off horizontal],
   166|hotographer lying on pool deck, iphone held underwater-at-surface,
   167|// EMOTIONAL MEMORY: [caught in moment between looking at
   168|phone and surfacing, eyes half-closed from chlorine]
   169|```
   170|
   171|---
   172|
   173|## SYSTEM 2: MOTION CONTAMINATION
   174|
   175|### What AI Does
   176|- Perceptually frozen
   177|- Sharp edges on moving parts
   178|- No temporal ambiguity
   179|- Perfect stability
   180|
   181|### What Human Memory Does
   182|- Moving through space = soft focus on parts in transit
   183|- Shutter lag = image caught slightly after the moment
   184|- Camera shake = photographer physically part of the moment
   185|- Walking softness = real movement happening
   186|- Turning body blur = natural act, not performance
   187|
   188|### Motion Contamination Types
   189|
   190|**A. Slight Motion Blur**
   191|- Only on extremities (hand, foot, hair tip) — NOT entire body
   192|- Direction-and-speed consistent with described action
   193|- Blur radius: 1-3px equivalent, not dramatic
   194|- Strands of hair show movement trails, not all hair
   195|
   196|**B. Walking Softness**
   197|- Subtle unsharpness on lower legs/steps during walk
   198|- Upper body relatively sharper than feet/legs
   199|- Body weight temporarily centered between steps
   200|- Slight forward lean inconsistent with standing-still
   201|
   202|**C. Camera Shake**
   203|- Slight rotational smudge (not linear blur)
   204|- Environmental details soft at edges
   205|- Subject core relatively stable but periphery unstable
   206|- Caused by: cold hands, laughing while shooting, excitement
   207|
   208|**D. Shutter Lag Feeling**
   209|- Expression caught 0.3-0.5 seconds AFTER the peak emotion
   210|- Subject's gaze has moved but torso haven't caught up
   211|- Hand position suggests gesture mid-execution
   212|- Mouth in position between two sound expressions
   213|
   214|**E. Turning-Body Blur**
   215|- Torso rotates faster than legs
   216|- Head leads, body follows with delay
   217|- Shoulder line tilted from neutral
   218|- Blur gradient: sharpest at eyes, softest at hip
   219|
   220|### Prompt Grammar
   221|
   222|```
   223|[ACTION description] — [motion type]
   224|— [blur direction/speed consistency]
   225|— [what is sharper vs softer]
   226|— [camera shake description if present]
   227|```
   228|
   229|### Trigger Conditions
   230|- **Walking/running scenes**: always generate walking softness
   231|- **Laughing/expression scenes**: natural shutter lag
   232|- **Beach/pool scenes**: wind/air/water causes hair motion blur
   233|- **Night/low-light scenes**: slower shutter = more shake
   234|- **Excited/emotional moments**: photographer's camera shake
   235|
   236|### Implementation Examples
   237|
   238|```
   239|// Walking along wet pavement
   240|realistic urban hk alley, early evening, post-rain wet pavement,
   241|slim korean woman in [oversized white cotton shirt,
   242|lightly damp from light rain mist, two buttons undone at collar],
   243|black midi skirt, [bare feet stepping carefully on wet tiles
   244|visible foot COMING DOWN onto pavement with slight impact softness],
   245|black crossbody bag worn across chest,
   246|[stray hairs at temple starting to lift away from cheek with walk],
   247|mid-body camera-level shot, [slight forward lean consistent w walk],
   248|phone photo from walking friend, evening ambient warm light,
   249|// MOTION SIGNATURE: [feet/ankles show 1.5px directional blur;
   250|// upper body relatively stable; face sharpest element]
   251|
   252|// Laughing at food stall
   253|realistic hk dai pai dong food stall area, warm yellow tungsten
   254|lights, auntie stall behind, slim korean woman [LAUGHING with head
   255|tilted back, lips parting mid-exhale], oversized cream cable-knit
   256|sweater worn off one shoulder, high-waisted dark denim skirt,
   257|bare shoulders visible,
   258|[CAMERA SHAKE: subtle 1-degree rotational smudge on right edge],
   259|phone held at chest height from girlfriend beside her,
   260|warm yellow light on wet skin from food stall steam,
   261|// MOTION SIGNATURE: [expression caught SLOWER than body —
   262|// smile full but gaze already drifting somewhere else]
   263|// SHUTTER LAG: [moment AFTER peak laugh, breath just released]
   264|
   265|// Turning away from camera
   266|realistic small hong kong cafe interior, afternoon soft window light,
   267|slim korean woman [TURNING AWAY slowly from camera,
   268|[right shoulder already 3/4 from viewer, LEFT shoulder still
   269|facing camera producing asymmetric body angle)],
   270|oversized sage-green linen shirt, tucked-front tuck,
   271|black high-waisted straight trousers,
   272|// [skin visible at shirt neckline where shoulder turning exposed it],
   273|[HAIR moving: several strands lifting away from neck with turn],
   274|phone photo from friend standing behind-left,
   275|caffe latte on wooden table beside her,
   276|// MOTION SIGNATURE: [transition blur on torso; head sharpest;
   277|hip area softest; blur gradient from face to leg]
   278|```
   279|
   280|---
   281|
   282|## SYSTEM 3: EMOTIONAL TIMING
   283|
   284|### What AI Does
   285|- Perfect expression at decision point
   286|- Eyes at full contact
   287|- Smile at apex
   288|- Emotion locked at peak
   289|
   290|### What Human Memory Does
   291|- Memory preserves the MOMENT BEFORE peak emotion
   292|- Eyes fluctuate — contact, break, reconnect
   293|- Expression catches mid-formation
   294|- Laughter interrupted or abandoned
   295|- Conflicted emotional states: happy AND distracted, sad AND composing
   296|
   297|### Emotional Timing Types
   298|
   299|**A. Expression Before Smile Completes**
   300|- Lips just parting, not yet forming shape
   301|- Cheeks beginning to lift, not yet full roundness
   302|- Breathing audible — chest visible rising/falling
   303|- Sound-forming mouth shape before laugh sound or speech
   304|
   305|**B. Eye Contact Reconnecting**
   306|- Eyes looking away at moment before re-engagement
   307|- Gaze drift: subject looking at something in environment (not at viewer)
   308|- Eyes in process of finding camera (not already locked on)
   309|- Pupil slightly unfocused (processing, not presenting)
   310|- Blink mid-expression (not staged full-eye contact)
   311|
   312|**C. Distracted Gaze**
   313|- Eyes focused past camera/photographer on something else
   314|- Attention split between camera and environmental element
   315|- Thought interrupted by photo: expression registers camera-acknowledgment late
   316|- Eyes looking DOWN at something, then slowly lifting to meet camera
   317|- Gaze through/around obstruction: partial obstruction, partial eye contact
   318|
   319|**D. Interrupted Laughter**
   320|- Laugh started but interrupted by breath/switch/bewilderment
   321|- Smile settling back down from peak (not rising toward it)
   322|- Breath being controlled/measured mid-expression
   323|- Mouth transitioning from expression back to neutral
   324|- One side of mouth still lifted but other already relaxing
   325|
   326|**E. Sleepy Reaction Timing**
   327|- Eyes half-lidded, not fully open
   328|- Blink-stamp: eyes briefly closing, not camera-induced timed-blink
   329|- Face not fully awake despite attempt
   330|- Movement slower, more deliberate
   331|- Expression processing at lower cognitive priority
   332|
   333|### Prompt Grammar
   334|
   335|```
   336|[EMOTIONAL STATE description with timing]
   337|— [expression in process / mid-formation]
   338|— [eye contact status AND trajectory]
   339|— [breathing/posture movement in progress]
   340|— [what emotion is being interrupted by what]
   341|```
   342|
   343|### Trigger Conditions
   344|- **Early morning / just-waking scenes**: sleepy reaction timing
   345|- **Just-finished-laughing moments**: interrupted laughter
   346|- **Environmental distraction scenes**: distracted gaze (look at ocean, sky, rain, food, someone else)
   347|- **Warm indoor scenes (friends/food/drinks)**: expression-before-smile
   348|- **Post-activity scenes**: expression returning to neutral
   349|
   350|### Implementation Examples
   351|
   352|```
   353|// Post-laughing: settling back down
   354|realistic hk rooftop bar with skyline view, evening warm air,
   355|slim korean woman [LAUGHTER JUST SETTLING, right side of mouth
   356|still slightly lifted, left side already dropping back to neutral],
   357|oversized charcoal cashmere sweater, tucked-front tuck,
   358|[warm flush spreading from cheeks downward to neck],
   359|drink in right hand near face, [EYES DARTING from skyline
   360|back to camera, pupil adjusting focus],
   361|phone held high from girlfriend standing beside,
   362|city lights beginning to glow in background,
   363|// EMOTIONAL TIMING: [smile apex ALREADY PASSED;
   364|// breath being measured; expression in DECAY phase not RISE]
   365|// EYE PATTERN: [gaze found camera, held 0.5s, now looking away
   366|at skyline again before camera captured]
   367|
   368|// Mid-distracted: looking at ocean
   369|beach shoreline at golden hour, warm tidal water,
   370|slim korean woman [LOOKING OUT AT OCEAN, gaze unfocused
   371|on horizon, eyes at 20% focus, no attempt to meet camera],
   372|ocean-blue one-piece swimsuit with subtle ruched detail,
   373|[skin flushed warm from 30min in water — redness on shoulders],
   374|wind lifting hair away from face,
   375|sand-flecked bare feet, [PHONE hanging relaxed at right side
   376|not being held — photographer forgot to look at it mid-scene],
   377|wide shot: subject small in frame with ocean dominant,
   378|// EMOTIONAL TIMING: [ DISTANCED GAZE — caught in sensory
   379|moment, not performance; camera caught her in private moment]
   380|// POSTURE: [weight on back foot, side to camera,
   381|shoulders relaxed — not pose-stance]
   382|
   383|// Morning moment: not yet awake
   384|small simple apartment bedroom, early morning warm light,
   385|slim korean woman [LYING BACK on white linen pillow,
   386|eyes HALF-OPEN, consciousness visibly not fully present],
   387|bare shoulders above white cotton cami top,
   388|chestnut hair spread on pillow, [SLEEP-WRINKLE visible
   389|on one cheek pressed into pillow],
   390|morning light from right window catching skin at angle,
   391|// EMOTIONAL TIMING: [NOT performing — expression processing
   392|at low cognitive priority; face relaxed in private morning moment]
   393|// POSTURE: [weight entirely surrendered to gravity;
   394|// no muscle tone in shoulders — completely natural]
   395|```
   396|
   397|---
   398|
   399|## SYSTEM 4: ENVIRONMENTAL INTERRUPTION
   400|
   401|### What AI Does
   402|- Perfect environmental conditions
   403|- Stable lighting throughout
   404|- Objects in static idealization
   405|- Weather serves composition
   406|- Reflections as aesthetic
   407|
   408|### What Human Memory Does
   409|- Wind doesn't follow direction of light — it moves hair unplanned
   410|- Wet fabric clings and shifts unpredictably
   411|- Objects slip and change position mid-scene
   412|- Moving shadows cut across faces unpredicted
   413|- Reflections distort shape beyond recognition
   414|
   415|### Environmental Interruption Types
   416|
   417|**A. Wind Affecting Hair**
   418|- Hair lifts in unplanned direction (not styled wind)
   419|- Uneven wind: one side lifted, other side flat
   420|- Hair shifts during exposure: image shows movement trail on one section
   421|- Bangs blown across eye or cheek in messy unplanned way
   422|- Hair lifts off neck, neck skin now exposed at unexpected angle
   423|
   424|**B. Wet Fabric Shifting**
   425|- Swimwear/skin wet with water: fabric clings differently than dry
   426|- Water trails on skin: gravity-affected drip patterns, not even sheen
   427|- Sheer fabric becomes MORE revealing when wet (cotton, linen)
   428|- Fabric clings to body contours with water-weight drag
   429|- Wet hair on skin: cools and causes goosebump response
   430|
   431|**C. Object Slipping**
   432|- Phone nearly dropped — grip tension visible in hand/forearm
   433|- Drink sliding on table — hand chasing it
   434|- Hairclip slipping out — half-escaped from hair
   435|- Slipper sliding off foot — foot adjusting
   436|- Bag strap sliding off shoulder — shoulder hiking up
   437|
   438|**D. Moving Shadows**
   439|- Sun moving across scene during exposure
   440|- Cloud passing: shadow sweeps across face mid-shot
   441|- Person walking past: shadow sweeps background
   442|- Tree/shutter shadow oscillating with breeze
   443|- Light quality changing through frame (half in sun, half in shadow)
   444|
   445|**E. Reflections Changing Shape**
   446|- Water rippling: reflection unrecognizable as coherent shape
   447|- Phone screen / glass: face distorted and fragmented in reflection
   448|- Wet floor: reflection of figure partially broken by foot contact
   449|- Sunglasses: double-reflection from both lenses
   450|
   451|### Prompt Grammar
   452|
   453|```
   454|[PRIMARY ENVIRONMENT description]
   455|— [environmental interruption type]
   456|— [physical causation chain]
   457|— [what changed mid-scene from causal trigger]
   458|— [resulting element: shifted fabric, blown hair, shadow sweep]
   459|```
   460|
   461|### Trigger Conditions
   462|- **Beach/pool scenes**: water-related fabric and skin effects
   463|- ** Outdoor scenes with humidity**: wind + wet fabric combo
   464|- **Night scenes near water**: reflections + movement
   465|- **Moving vehicles**: light changes, reflections, sliding objects
   466|- **Food/drink scenes**: drink-related interactions
   467|
   468|### Implementation Examples
   469|
   470|```
   471|// Wind + wet hair at beach
   472|beach shoreline, late afternoon golden light, slim korean woman
   473|[sitting on warm sand near water edge, SUN-TAN LOTION still
   474|visible as slight white caste on upper back and shoulders],
   475|[WET one-piece swimsuit: black with subtle side ruched detail,
   476|CLINGING to body from ocean water, more revealing than dry],
   477|[WIND lifted hair off neck and blown it asymmetric to right side,
   478|several strands stuck to cheek wet with saltwater],
   479|[SKIN showing natural pink from 1hr ocean activity —
   480|redness concentrated on shoulders and collarbone],
   481|bare feet half-buried in warm sand, ocean lapping at ankles,
   482|// ENVIRONMENTAL INTERRUPTION: [ WATER caused swimsuit to
   483|cling revealingly; WIND shifted hair asymmetrically;
   484|// uneven wet causing irregular skin redness patterns]
   485|// CAUSATION: ocean swim → wet clinging fabric + wet hair
   486|
   487|// Rain-interrupted: sheltering with wet elements
   488|hk narrow covered walkway, light rain tapping overhead,
   489|slim korean woman [STANDING in shelter, OVERSIZED cream
   490|long-sleeve knit cardigan DAMP at shoulders where rain
   491|sprayed through shelter gap, fabric darkened and clinging],
   492|[shelter rain causing unexpected damp on upper arm skin],
   493|hair damp from humidity not rain direct, [WET HAIR CLINGING
   494|to NECK showing goosebump texture pattern],
   495|black wide-leg trousers, [LEFT SHOULDER slightly higher
   496|from carrying bag — one sleeve riding up unevenly],
   497|looking down at phone, wet pavement visible below walkway,
   498|// ENVIRONMENTAL INTERRUPTION: [INCOMPLETE SHELTER caused
   499|unexpected damp on specific body areas; rain indirect but
   500|physically present and affecting fabric and skin]
   501|

================================================================================
## V14 CAMERA AWARENESS SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V14/CAMERA_AWARENESS_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# CAMERA_AWARENESS_SYSTEM.md
     2|### AContent / lil.troublr V14.6 Core Module
     3|### Awareness States — Realism Architecture
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## WHAT CAMERA AWARENESS DOES
     8|
     9|Camera awareness level is the **single most influential variable** in image realism — more than outfit, more than environment, more than composition.
    10|
    11|Why:
    12|
    13|- Outfit styling just sets visual register
    14|- Environment sets scene quality
    15|- **CAMERA AWARENESS sets emotional register**
    16|
    17|Two subjects in identical settings, different camera awareness levels, produce completely different emotional textures:
    18|
    19|| Set | Aware | Forget |
    20||-----|-------|--------|
    21|| Beach | Influencer performs | Memory fragment |
    22|| Cafe | Model shoots | Friend documents moment |
    23|| Street | Posing | Existing |
    24|
    25|Camera awareness determines:
    26|- Expression type and timing
    27|- Eye contact pattern
    28|- Posture orientation  
    29|- Framing tendency
    30|- Realism density
    31|- Moderation interpretation
    32|- Attraction generation mechanic
    33|
    34|---
    35|
    36|## THE FOUR AWARENESS LEVELS
    37|
    38|```
    39|LEVEL 1 — FULLY AWARE
    40|Level 2 — SEMI-AWARE  
    41|Level 3 — CAMERA-FORGOTTEN ⭐ (strongest anti-AI)
    42|Level 4 — UNAWARE
    43|```
    44|
    45|---
    46|
    47|## LEVEL 1: FULLY AWARE
    48|
    49|### Definition
    50|Subject knows camera is present and performing for it. This is conscious photography — content creation mode.
    51|
    52|### Character Types
    53|- Influencer doing a shoot
    54|- Content creator choosing a spot
    55|- Model working an angle
    56|- Person who planned to wear-something-photogenic
    57|- Travel photographer stop
    58|
    59|### Expression Behavior
    60|- Full smile held at best position
    61|- Eyes at peak contact (not too close, not looking away)
    62|- Expression at maximum engagement
    63|- Multiple takes possible: same pose, similar expressions
    64|- Chin-lifted, eye-angle corrections
    65|- Posture adjustment toward camera
    66|
    67|### Eye Contact Pattern
    68|- Camera-locked: eyes directly meeting camera/photographer
    69|- No blink mid-contact
    70|- Gaze stable, controlled
    71|- Pupils focused and present
    72|- Duration: camera operator and subject both comfortable with duration
    73|
    74|### Posture Behavior
    75|- Full body orientation toward camera
    76|- Weight distributed for aesthetic balance
    77|- Arms positioned for visual interest, not function
    78|- Shoulder line angled for flattering presentation
    79|- Hand poses: intentional display gestures
    80|- Standing: weight evenly distributed aesthetically
    81|
    82|### Framing Tendency
    83|- Rule-of-thirds close: subject fills 60-80% of frame
    84|- Center or off-center by 1/3 only
    85|- Complete anatomy in frame
    86|- No accidental crop
    87|- Environmental context but secondary to subject
    88|- Background blurred or clean to not distract from subject
    89|
    90|### Realism Density
    91|LOWEST of all levels — subject is at maximum control
    92|- Expression: staged perfection
    93|- Body: performance stance
    94|- Environment: backdrop
    95|- Clothing: intentional outfit
    96|- Gaze: presentational
    97|
    98|### Moderation Interpretation
    99|- HIGHEST risk — subject is clearly performing in content-creator mode
   100|- Platform scoring: likely influencer/content creator code
   101|- Posture framing: presentational angles register as aesthetic-display
   102|- Close-up possibility increases flagging risk
   103|- Body language registered as self-display intent
   104|
   105|### Attraction Mechanic
   106|Viewer sees: someone performing beauty → admiration, desire-aspiration
   107|Effect: Subject receives praise for looking-good, not for being-real
   108|
   109|---
   110|
   111|## LEVEL 2: SEMI-AWARE
   112|
   113|### Definition
   114|Subject aware camera is present but not fully performing. Social photography — caught between casual and intentional.
   115|
   116|### Character Types
   117|- Friend group dinner, someone inlcuded
   118|- Rooftop gathering with friends
   119|- Beach trip, someone keeps being photographed
   120|- Post-workout, photo from someone passing by
   121|- Birthday/housewarming — documentarians in group
   122|
   123|### Expression Behavior
   124|- Natural expression but calibrated: awareness creates slight restraint
   125|- Genuine smile but held a beat longer than spontaneous
   126|- Eyes meet camera but not locked — breaks and reconnects
   127|- Slight composure layer: "don't look ridiculous" awareness in expression
   128|- Move from authentic to social-presentation mid-scene
   129|- "Just act natural!" — paradox of awareness making natural harder
   130|
   131|### Eye Contact Pattern
   132|- Contact→Break→Recontact sequence
   133|- Eyes find camera, hold 1-2 seconds, look away, return
   134|- Gaze not fully relaxed
   135|- Pupil partially present, partially processing
   136|- Blink-stamp: eyes briefly closing mid-contact (not natural blink, camera-aware)
   137|- "Wait, I'm in a photo" micro-expression may flash through
   138|
   139|### Posture Behavior
   140|- 60-70% natural posture — rest is "don't look weird" adjustment
   141|- Orientation mixed between environment (normal) and camera (aware)
   142|- Arms doing something functional but aware enough to make it interesting
   143|- Weight mostly natural but slight aesthetic adjustment
   144|- Shoulders: 60% relaxed, 40% "presenting"
   145|- Hand gestures: functional but slightly performance-adjacent
   146|
   147|### Framing Tendency
   148|- 40-60% subject in frame
   149|- More environmental context than Level 1
   150|- Some accidental crop happens (subject not controlling framing)
   151|- Subject participates slightly in framing decisions
   152|- Still completes anatomy (most of the time)
   153|- Some body parts may be obscured by friends/elements
   154|
   155|### Realism Density
   156|MEDIUM — mixed authentic and performance
   157|- Expression: 50% genuine, 50% social-presentation
   158|- Body: 70% natural, 30% aesthetic adjustment
   159|- Environment: medium weight, slightly more than backdrop
   160|- Clothing: intentional but not performance-outfit
   161|- Gaze: partially present, partially aware
   162|
   163|### Moderation Interpretation
   164|- MEDIUM risk — semi-aware expressions are less performative than Level 1
   165|- Natural smiles with social context read as "friend photos"
   166|- Slightly more platform tolerance than influencer-content
   167|- Posture mixed natural/presentational — less purely display
   168|- Casual environment context reduces body-display code
   169|
   170|### Attraction Mechanic
   171|Viewer sees: someone being photographed by friend → intimacy-feel, inclusion-feel
   172|Effect: Viewer wants to be there too, not just admiring subject
   173|
   174|---
   175|
   176|## LEVEL 3: CAMERA-FORGOTTEN ⭐ [STRONGEST ANTI-AI]
   177|
   178|### Definition
   179|Subject momentarily forgot camera was there. Natural photography. Peak emotional realism.
   180|
   181|### Character Types
   182|- Genuine moment with focus entirely on environment/experience
   183|- Just-finished-laughing-at-something — camera caught moment after-awareness
   184|- Responding to something in environment, not camera
   185|- Lost in thought — camera caught unguarded
   186|- Reading, eating, doing something — camera documenting not performing
   187|- Looking at something beautiful — forgot to pose
   188|
   189|### Expression Behavior
   190|- Expression not for camera: completely absorbed in what they're doing/feeling
   191|- Genuine emotions — joy/surprise/curiosity without presentation layer
   192|- Expression caught in-process: before-it-arrives, during-formation, or-already-past-peak
   193|- Micro-expressions: fear of being ugly/unflattering momentarily absent
   194|- "Camera who?" — no performer-monitoring during moment
   195|- Spontaneous laugh captured in original moment — not called for
   196|
   197|### Eye Contact Pattern
   198|- Eyes NOT on camera: looking at something in enviro/camera op is invisible
   199|- OR: eyes just found camera mid-drift, 0.3-0.5s into contact before awareness
   200|- OR: awareness just arrived — "oh there's a camera" micro-reaction visible
   201|- Gaze unfocused or softly focused on external element
   202|- Blink pattern: natural (not camera-aware timed blink)
   203|- Pupil naturally unfocused or processing without camera in mind
   204|
   205|### Posture Behavior
   206|- 95% natural: completely in the moment, no aesthetic adjustment
   207|- Weight distribution: functional, not presentational
   208|- Arms/legs doing whatever the moment requires
   209|- Shoulders entirely surrendered to gravity/effort/experience
   210|- Hand gestures: entirely functional, not placed for visual interest
   211|- NO hand-on-hip, finger-pointing, chin-lifting, hair-flipping
   212|- Body responding to environment, not to camera
   213|
   214|### Framing Tendency
   215|- 30-50% subject in frame
   216|- Maximum environmental weight
   217|- Incomplete frame common: body parts leaving frame, awkward crop
   218|- Subject doesn't control framing — camera op chose moment over composition
   219|- Horizon may be tilted or off-level
   220|- Subject smallish in frame — environment dominates
   221|
   222|### Realism Density
   223|HIGHEST of all levels — complete emotional authenticity
   224|- Expression: 98% genuine, 2% micro-awareness at most
   225|- Body: 99% natural, 1% unconscious posture accommodation
   226|- Environment: primary — this isn't a portrait, it's a memory from inside a moment
   227|- Clothing: as-worn (wrinkled, shifted, asymmetric from real use)
   228|- Gaze: completely disconnected from camera-presented-self
   229|
   230|### Moderation Interpretation
   231|- LOWEST risk of all levels — natural moment beats performance every time
   232|- Platform-scanner logic: "friend caught this" vs "content creator working"
   233|- Expression not presentational — mid-process/catching/spontaneous
   234|- Posture no display-intent — body is simply doing what it needs to do
   235|- Environment weight means it's a photo OF a moment, not a photo OF a body
   236|- Exposure often imperfect — not optimized for body presentation
   237|
   238|### Attraction Mechanic
   239|Viewer sees: someone completely real in a real moment → emotional resonance
   240|Effect: Viewer wants to be THAT person or be WITH that person (not just view them)
   241|
   242|**Why this generates the strongest attraction:**
   243|- Performance generates admiration
   244|- Authenticity generates wanting-to-be-near
   245|- Friend-zone memory: camera-forgotten moments feel like being let into someone's private moment
   246|- The model is the most subtly powerful attraction: someone so comfortable she forgot to monitor herself
   247|- Viewer experiences: "if I were there, I'd be the one holding that moment"
   248|
   249|**Why AI cannot replicate Level 3:**
   250|- AI generates moments for a viewer (always performer-aware)
   251|- AI cannot generate genuine forgetting — it doesn't forget, it doesn't not-know the camera exists
   252|- AI expression: camera-locked, presentational, performer-aware even at low levels
   253|- AI posture: aesthetic optimization even in "casual" shots
   254|- AI gaze: always finds camera or gives viewer-intended "away" gaze
   255|- Result: Level 3 image from AI = uncanny; Level 3 image from real camera = magnetic
   256|
   257|### Trigger Conditions for Level 3
   258|- **Just-finished-laughing**: highest yield Level 3 trigger
   259|- **Environment-absorbing gaze**: looking at ocean, sky, food, someone else, sunset
   260|- **Occupation with object**: reading, eating, applying sunscreen, playing with hair
   261|- **Just-waking / not-aware**: morning moments, post-shower towel-wrapped
   262|- **Movement sequence**: walking, climbing, turning — caught mid-transition
   263|- **Social priority conflict**: attention on friend/person, camera is side-effect
   264|
   265|### How to Write Level 3 Prompts
   266|Key: Describe a scenario where camera-awareness would realistically drop:
   267|
   268|```
   269|[Genuine moment trigger] — [camera-forgotten body behavior]
   270|— [expression in process, not on display]
   271|— [gaze on environmental element, not camera]
   272|— [body doing just-what-the-moment-needs]
   273|```
   274|
   275|Must avoid: any sign of photographer directing, subject posing, or environment being backdrop.
   276|
   277|---
   278|
   279|## LEVEL 4: UNAWARE
   280|
   281|### Definition
   282|Subject completely unaware camera exists. Documentary observation. Social distance maintained.
   283|
   284|### Character Types
   285|- Street photography subject: walked into photo range but camera isn't directed at her specifically
   286|- Background figure in someone else's photo
   287|- Group shot: friend takes photo of scenery, she's part of background
   288|- Person on phone, completely absent to surroundings
   289|- Transit: bus/mtr shot, subject in background
   290|
   291|### Expression Behavior
   292|- Expression not related to camera at all
   293|- Thinking about something completely unrelated
   294|- Reacting to environment/personal moment with no camera context
   295|- Expression may be negative/unflattering (bored, annoyed, frustrated)
   296|- Complete absence of awareness = complete absence of performance management
   297|- Some expressions that would never be deliberately displayed
   298|
   299|### Eye Contact Pattern
   300|- Never make contact with camera
   301|- Eyes either: looking at environment, looking at phone, looking down, blank
   302|- Completely absent camera from cognitive priority
   303|- Pupil unfocused on whatever subject-matter is occuring
   304|
   305|### Posture Behavior
   306|- 100% natural — possibly awkward
   307|- Walking trajectory (not stopped to pose)
   308|- Sitting in transit/mid-task
   309|- No awareness to adjust for camera angle
   310|- Body may be in unflattering functional position
   311|- Gestures entirely about environmental engagement, not presentation
   312|
   313|### Framing Tendency
   314|- Subject smallish: 10-30% of frame
   315|- Maximum environmental / documentary framing
   316|- Subject in background or edge
   317|- Horizon very present
   318|- Street/documentary noise included
   319|- Other strangers/procession visible
   320|- Unflattering angle possible (back of head, side-face, mid-stride)
   321|
   322|### Realism Density
   323|HIGH but with caveats — authentically documentary
   324|- Expression: no performance management at all (negative possible)
   325|- Body: fully functional, not presentational
   326|- Environment: FULL weight — this might not even be about her
   327|- Clothing: as-worn, caught mid-transition
   328|- Gaze: absent, unrelated, or functional
   329|
   330|### Moderation Interpretation
   331|- LOWEST risk from perspective of subject being photographed
   332|- BUT: street/documentary framing may include stranger detail — needs care
   333|- Expression may be unflattering or emotionally complex — platform may treat differently
   334|- Group shots: other people visible — consent/cropping considerations
   335|
   336|### Attraction Mechanic
   337|Viewer sees: random woman in documentary context → voyeuristic inclusion
   338|Effect: "I wonder what she was thinking / where she was going"
   339|Drawback: Lower legibility for character identity — she may be unrecognizable
   340|
   341|**Use Level 4 for:**
   342|- Environmental world-reality injection
   343|- Documentary texture
   344|- Street-level HK authenticity
   345|- Human density injection into scenes
   346|
   347|**Use Level 4 sparingly for main character:**
   348|- Level 4 unrecognizable subject = unidentifiable character
   349|- Use for establishing shots, background texture, environmental diversity
   350|- Use as one frame in a sequence for narrative progression
   351|
   352|---
   353|
   354|## AWARENESS → REALISM MATRIX
   355|
   356|| Dimension | Level 1 (Aware) | Level 2 (Semi) | Level 3 (Forgot) | Level 4 (Unaware) |
   357||-----------|-----------------|----------------|-------------------|-------------------|
   358|| **Expression** | Staged peak | Social+authentic | Genuine in-process | Unrelated/absent |
   359|| **Eyes** | Camera-locked | Contact-break-reconnect | On enviro/just-found | Never on camera |
   360|| **Posture** | Presentational | Mixed | Fully natural | 100% functional |
   361|| **Framing** | Subject fills 60-80% | Subject 40-60% | Subject 30-50% | Subject 10-30% |
   362|| **Environment** | Backdrop | Slight weight | Dominant | Primary |
   363|| **Realism** | Lowest | Medium | HIGHEST | High (documentary) |
   364|| **Anti-AI effect** | None | Weak | STRONGEST | Strong |
   365|| **Mod risk** | HIGHEST | Medium | LOWEST | Lowest |
   366|| **Attraction type** | Admiration | Inclusion | Proximity-desire | Curiosity |
   367|| **Prompt weight** | Body/presentation | Social moment | Moment-internal | Documentary witness |
   368|
   369|---
   370|
   371|## AWARENESS TRANSITIONS
   372|
   373|A single scene can describe an awareness **transition** — caught moving from one level to another:
   374|
   375|**Level 2 → Level 3: Just-noticed moment**
   376|```
   377|[TURNING toward camera with expression of slight surprise,
   378|"oh when did you —" mid-word — eyes just found camera,
   379|arms mid-gesture from whatever she was doing before]
   380|```
   381|Realism trigger: Awareness arrived AFTER moment started — she's being caught being caught
   382|
   383|**Level 3 → Level 2: Composition arrived**
   384|```
   385|[LOOKING OUT at ocean, then gaze drifting toward something
   386|someone said, then eyes finding camera at LEFT EDGE of her
   387|periphery, expression settling into acknowledgment, posture
   388|shifting slightly toward camera — 0.5s after photo was taken]
   389|```
   390|Realism trigger: The moment happened, now she's aware it was captured
   391|
   392|**Level 1 → Level 3: Accidentally perfect**
   393|```
   394|[POSING for camera, full awareness, then someone said something
   395|hilarious and laugh caught mid-start before photographer
   396|caught her guard-down — laugh completed but not for camera]
   397|```
   398|Realism trigger: Performance interrupted by genuine moment
   399|
   400|---
   401|
   402|## WRITING AWARENESS LEVEL INTO PROMPTS
   403|
   404|### Grammar Pattern
   405|```
   406|[SCENE] — [awareness level descriptor]
   407|— [expression/gaze/posture consistent with level]
   408|— [eye contact type]
   409|— [framing implication for level]
   410|```
   411|
   412|### Level 1 Prompt Example
   413|```
   414|realistic hk rooftop bar at golden hour, slim korean woman
   415|[FULLY AWARE AND POSING — standing at railing,
   416|weight balanced for aesthetic, both hands resting on railing
   417|in intentional display pose, fingers deliberately spread],
   418|oversized cream linen shirt tucked at front, black high-waisted
   419|straight trousers, [FULL SMILE held at apex, eyes directly meeting
   420|camera], chin slightly lifted, [SUBJECT FILLS 70% OF FRAME],
   421|rule-of-thirds positioning, bokeh city lights in background,
   422|phone photo from tripod timer,
   423|// AWARENESS: [fully performing — every element optimized for viewer]
   424|```
   425|
   426|### Level 2 Prompt Example
   427|```
   428|small hk izakaya at 11pm, slim korean woman dining with friends,
   429|[SEMI-AWARE — smiling at something friend said, then noticed
   430|phone in friend's hand, smile holds but shifts slightly toward
   431|"ok fine take your photo" adjustment],
   432|oversized black henley-tee, white lounge shorts underneath,
   433|[EYES making contact with camera briefly (1-2s), then glancing
   434|away at friend, then back to camera with slight relaxation],
   435|[stray hairs at temple from cooking steam, one sleeve slipped
   436|off shoulder slightly, seated posture 60% natural with 40%
   437|"don't look weird" adjustment],
   438|[SUBJECT FILLS 50% OF FRAME, small plate of gyoza in frame],
   439|casual warm yellow light from izakaya pendant lamp above,
   440|// AWARENESS: [social moment but aware she was being photographed]
   441|```
   442|
   443|### Level 3 Prompt Example (⭐ PRIMARY ENGINE LEVEL)
   444|```
   445|beach shoreline at golden hour, slim korean woman [CAMERA-FORGOTTEN
   446|— standing knee-deep in warm tidal water, completely absorbed in
   447|watching something farther out in ocean, [EYES unfocused on
   448|horizon, expression soft with genuine wonder — not for camera],
   449|[ARMS doing natural thing: RIGHT HAND steadying against water-current
   450|resistance, not placed for visual interest], skin flushed warm
   451|from 30min in ocean, [WET ocean-blue one-piece swimsuit clinging
   452|differently than dry — more revealing with water weight],
   453|[ONE FOOT shifting weight in sand, that leg becoming unstable
   454|as sand gripped by wave], [GENTLE WAVE pushed against hip,
   455|water splashing at waist level, phone forgotten at right side],
   456|phone hanging relaxed, photographer's girlfriend trying to capture
   457|moment before awareness returns,
   458|// [SUBJECT FILLS 40% OF FRAME, ocean dominant in composition],
   459|[SUN AT 20-DEGREE ANGLE low behind her, body half-illuminated
   460|warm, half in cool shadow from water],
   461|[EMOTIONAL MEMORY: face caught in moment of genuine awe at
   462|something in ocean, completely unaware she will be photographed]
   463|// AWARENESS: [peak memory-realism — moment captured because
   464|it felt significant, not because she looked good]
   465|```
   466|
   467|### Level 4 Prompt Example
   468|```
   469|humble hk wet market at 7am, narrow wet alley between fish
   470|and vegetable stalls, slim korean woman in background,
   471|[UNAWARE — walking past slowly, completely absorbed in
   472|looking at phone, expression of slight confusion/frustration
   473|at something on screen], oversized gray cotton hoodie,
   474|black leggings, [HAIR in messy bun with several loose strands],
   475|[BACK 3/4 toward camera — she didn't know camera was there],
   476|[SUBJECT FILLS 15% OF FRAME, stallholders and produce dominant],
   477|early morning market light — tungsten and natural mixed,
   478|// [wet market texture: blue plastic crates, fish on ice, red
   479|chili strings, condensation on plastic awning overhead],
   480|documentary street photography framing, mild grain from
   481|compact digital camera,
   482|// AWARENESS: [complete stranger — she was there, camera caught it, it's not about her]
   483|```
   484|
   485|---
   486|
   487|## V14.6 INTEGRATION NOTES
   488|
   489|### Primary Engine Level: Level 3
   490|V14.6 engine should default to Level 3 (Camera-Forgotten) as the PRIMARY realism driver.
   491|
   492|Level 2 (Semi-Aware) acceptable for social/group dynamic content.
   493|
   494|Level 1 (Fully Aware) and Level 4 (Unaware) should be used sparingly — Level 1 for specific curated content, Level 4 for environmental/texture diversity.
   495|
   496|### The Awareness Realism Rule
   497|**CAMERA AWARENESS LEVEL < STYLING CHOICES <<< EMOTIONAL PRESENCE**
   498|
   499|What this means:
   500|- A $500 outfit in Level 1 = still influencer-performative
   501|

================================================================================
## V14 ENVIRONMENT EXPANSION SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V14/ENVIRONMENT_EXPANSION_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENVIRONMENT_EXPANSION_SYSTEM.md
     2|### V14.6 Core Module — Human-World Behavioral Ecosystems
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — Promoted from V14_RESEARCH_v14_6/01
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## WHAT THIS SYSTEM IS
     8|
     9|V14.5 environments were becoming repetitive — rooftop, café, beach, pool, generic nightlife.
    10|
    11|V14.6 replaces "pretty background" with **human-world behavioral ecosystems**:
    12|environment is not backdrop, it's the causal system.
    13|
    14|80+ environment combinations achievable from 5 new families × specific behaviors.
    15|
    16|---
    17|
    18|## PHILOSOPHY
    19|
    20|**"The image should feel like a moment inside a real human world.**
    21|**Not scenery-with-person. Environment→Physical causation→Body response→Camera intercept.**
    22|
    23|---
    24|
    25|## FAMILY A: TRANSITIONAL SPACES
    26|
    27|*People emotionally "between moments" — spaces of movement, waiting, change.*
    28|
    29|A1. **Apartment elevator** — flush skin proximity, breath audible, eye-avoidance micro-movement, phone-check as escape, enclosed-warmth awkwardness
    30|
    31|A2. **MTR transfer corridor** — fastest pace, out-of-breath quality, checking watch, weight-shift mid-walk, announcement echo, crowd murmur, motion-blur on adjacent commuters
    32|
    33|A3. **Airport waiting corridor** — nervous anticipation energy, gate-checking, weight on one leg, arms in pockets, departures-board focus, fluorescent institutional light
    34|
    35|A4. **Indoor skybridge** — temperature shift felt on bare skin, breeze visible (hair movement), sound acoustics shift, between-buildings suspension, slight surreal midpoint, raised self-awareness
    36|
    37|A5. **Parking garage stairwell** — echo sound, concrete echo, exhaust/smoke-cellar smell, single fluorescent tubes compartment lighting, late-night isolation or early-morning start-of-day energy, car-key-in-hand weight
    38|
    39|A6. **Ferry boarding lane** — anticipatory energy, checking phone, sea breeze on skin, hip-level shot with passengers visible, ferry in background, engine rumble + seagull + announcement echo, harbor blue-white or golden-hour warm
    40|
    41|A7. **Hotel hallway** — key-card-in-hand, room-number-checking, hand on handle about-to-enter, hotel corridor warm-blue fluorescent, damp-from-shower possibility, hair-towel turban possibility
    42|
    43|A8. **Public changing corridor** — gym/pool/studio changing area, bag on floor, bag-locker click, mirror check, slightly communal-shower adjacency, gym-bag weight, casual-sportswear on body, functional not aesthetic
    44|
    45|A9. **Shopping-mall service hallway** — staff-only back-of-house, storage shelf visible, cleaning cart, quiet empty space off-duty feeling, functional fluorescent harsh single-strip, bored-waiting-checking-phone in empty public space
    46|
    47|A10. **Footbridge escalator** — vertical movement, hand-rail grip weight, peripheral glance at street below, wind acceleration mid-escalator, step rhythm, ascent-descent posture shift
    48|
    49|---
    50|
    51|## FAMILY B: MICRO-DESTINATIONS
    52|
    53|*Socially specific spaces where behavior is constrained by space function — not generic social.*
    54|
    55|B1. **Bowling shoe rental area** — sitting on rental bench, hand reaching for shoes, concentration-boredom, lace-tying moment, bag on floor, overhead score screen, automatic music loop, bowling-alley smell, non-focal ordinary behavior
    56|
    57|B2. **Photo booth entrance / area** — waiting outside booth, friend-adjusting-hair anticipation, strip-curtain feeling, confining space, squeaky chair, photo-strip output moment: joy-dismay reaction reviewing with friend, joy-formality social documentation
    58|
    59|B3. **Laundromat folding table** — folding motion, arms folded, skin warm from dryer heat, cotton fabric in hands, sitting on plastic chair, timer waiting, checking phone, watching other people's laundry, warm fabric-softener scent, domestic chore in semi-public space
    60|
    61|B4. **Vending machine corner** — pushing buttons, finger on selection, lean-in moment, coin-in-hand weight, product falling, crouch-reach into pickup slot, machine LED glow, vending machine hum, solitary micro-moment self-service
    62|
    63|B5. **Karaoke waiting bench** — friends on bench, nervous-excited energy, songbook in hand, numbered rooms visible, sound-sealed doors, muffled music from each room, anticipation before performance, group energy, social excitement, private-room red LED sign glow
    64|
    65|B6. **Badminton court rest bench** — between-game rest, energy after exertion, drink bottle in hand, face flushed, slouch thigh-spread from exertion heat, elbow on knee, court in background, net visible, shuttlecocks, exertion-flush skin, post-effort breathing, casual and athletic
    66|
    67|B7. **Arcade token machine** — inserting coin, token cascade sound, hand catching tokens, token weight in palm, backlit button, neon glow, gaming-arcade humidity in air, teenage energy / adult nostalgia overlap
    68|
    69|B8. **Indoor skating-rink railing** — holding railing for balance, beginner-wobble posture, rental skates visible, cold-rink air on skin, other skaters in peripheral, skating-rink echo sound, protective-knee-pad visible, vulnerable learner feeling
    70|
    71|B9. **Capsule toy machine wall** — leaning against machine, arm reaching to select, knee-protecting bag on floor, capsule-in-hand shaking, anticipation-twist-off moment, twist-off cap, LED glow machine, random impulse, childhood-adult excitement for small thing
    72|
    73|B10. **Ferry seat corner** — corner window seat, chin-on-window ledge, looking out at sea, contemplation absorbed, breath fog on glass, vibration from engine, low rumble, window reflection: face in glass + sea visible behind, silence-between-passengers
    74|
    75|---
    76|
    77|## FAMILY C: DOMESTIC TRANSITIONAL REALISM
    78|
    79|*Private behavior — off-guard domestic moments, believable socially.*
    80|
    81|C1. **Apartment entrance hallway** — key-in-door moment, hand on handle, bag slipping off shoulder, shoe-removal: one foot on other ankle, slight imbalance, time-since-arrival breathless, setting bag down, hallway light from above, shoe rack visible, umbrella dry/wet catch
    82|
    83|C2. **Bathroom mirror after shower** — mirror reappearing through steam, hair towel turban on head, steam on mirror slowly clearing, face close to mirror, skin routine moment, phone propped on sink, steam warmth, condensation on mirror edges, water droplet on floor, completely off-guard, damp skin, no makeup, hair in natural state
    84|
    85|C3. **Kitchen late-night snack** — fridge-open moment, light from fridge illuminating face, squint at options, standing at counter eating directly from container, chopsticks or spoon, late-night dark apartment, only kitchen light, quiet city sound, solitary functional drowsy, ramen steam, midnight oil, domestic solitude
    86|
    87|C4. **Couch after falling asleep** — slumped on sofa, position of sleep settling, arm under pillow or under body, TV still on (blue-white glow on skin), room otherwise dark, after-nap disorientation slow blinking, face sleep-creased from pillow, completely surrendered to gravity, not for camera at all
    88|
    89|C5. **Unpacking groceries** — kitchen counter, bag on floor, items being sorted, hand selecting from bag, packaging visible, kitchen still messy from cooking or still organized from before, plastic grocery bag crinkle rustle, domestic chore, not aesthetic, natural function, productivity moment
    90|
    91|C6. **Hair drying beside TV** — standing in front of TV with hair dryer, heat-feel visible, hair volume being worked, one hand in hair, dryer in other, watching TV casually, heat shimmer slight air distortion from dryer, multi-tasking domestic, specific heat-affected posture
    92|
    93|C7. **Sitting on floor near charger cables** — floor-sitting with phone charging, cables visible on floor, leaning against sofa base or wall, casual exhausted floor-sit, sock feet, charger brick on floor, looking at phone screen while charging, charger cable in hand, intimate-floorspace domestic
    94|
    95|C8. **Folding laundry** — on bed or floor, piles of laundry, folding motion, sorting into piles, fabric in hands towel-folding sock-pairing, laundry basket at foot, clean fabric scent, casual clothing, domestic chore alone or half-attentive, specific hands-in-fabric behavior, warmth and repetition
    96|
    97|C9. **Balcony AC compressor area** — narrow balcony, AC compressor hum, city heat, limited space, leaning on railing, weight on railing, casual stance, looking at city view, heat and noise from compressor, trapped between indoor cool and outdoor heat, city-boundary specific behavior
    98|
    99|C10. **Bedside table morning moment** — alarm clock visible, phone on charger, half-empty water glass, book open face-down on bed, morning light from side window, hair slept-on-side-messy, half-conscious reaching for phone, domestic morning ritual
   100|
   101|---
   102|
   103|## FAMILY D: WEATHER-DOMINATED ENVIRONMENTS
   104|
   105|*Environment physically affects behavior — weather is causal, not aesthetic.*
   106|
   107|D1. **Typhoon rain shelter** — rain hammering shelter roof, splash-back mist reaching shelter edge, water dripping from clothing edges, puddles at feet, shoulders hiked compact cold posture, cold-air shiver, rain roar + wind whistle muffled city, weather-caused behavior, posture from cold and damp NOT from aesthetic
   108|
   109|D2. **Humid summer bus stop** — heat accumulation, sweat on neck visible, clothing sticking to skin, metal seat hot to touch, shelter trapping heat, humidity frizz hair sticking to neck, skin flushed from heat, air-conditioned air inside the bus vs heat outside, diesel exhaust heat odor
   110|
   111|D3. **Post-rain reflective street** — wet pavement mirror-mirror reflections, street light elongation in puddle, ground still wet, puddles reflecting lights, air post-rain cool, splash-aware walking, stepping-carefully behavior, feet getting wet, car headlight smear in wet pavement, world visually doubled in reflection
   112|
   113|D4. **Windy harbor walkway** — wind pressure body leaning into wind, hair blown back forcefully, cold skin flushed from wind-chill, goosebump visible on bare legs, fabric billowing, one side of body more affected by wind, wind roar + wave slap louder, protective squint, wind as physical force on body and clothing
   114|
   115|D5. **Overcast ferry terminal** — gray sky no shadows, flat light blue-gray color cast, no sun-angle, muffled sound ferry terminal, contemplative subdued less energetic, cloud ceiling visible through terminal roof, overcast absorption quality, weather-depression mood, absence of shadow as sensation
   116|
   117|D6. **Drizzle-covered mall entrance** — umbrella dripping, floor wet, condensation on glass door, air-conditioned air vs humidity outside temp shift, water on surfaces shopping bags wet, subject damp from exposure, mall warm fluorescent vs gray exterior, weather boundary moment just-inside vs just-outside moisture on everything
   118|
   119|D7. **Fog-covered hillside path** — fog immersion, horizon disappearing, cool damp air, condensation on hair, path uncertain underfoot, muffled sound, isolated visibility, fog on skin, breath visible, visibility-limiting walking, eerie calm, fog as visual editor hiding everything beyond 5 meters
   120|
   121|D8. **Heat shimmer street corner** — summer afternoon extreme heat, visible heat shimmer rising from pavement, heat haze distortion of building lines above, sweat on skin, slow-motion quality from heat, air thick, heat shimmering off asphalt, visible heat distortion above hot surfaces
   122|
   123|---
   124|

   130|
   131|E2. **Ferry window seat** — chin on window ledge, breath-fog on glass, face in glass reflection, sea visible through and behind, ferry engine vibration felt, low rumble, announcement sound, solitude-in-public, looking at non-city landscape, introspective, sea horizon visible, ferry window condensation, salt air smell, sea spray on window
   132|
   133|E3. **Airport moving walkway** — standing relaxed on conveyor, bag at side, looking ahead, conveyor belt carrying body, slight weight shift, walkway hum, distant announcement, airport PA, between-terminal suspension, transition zone contemplative, luggage roller sound, travel-transition energy
   134|
   135|E4. **Train platform edge** — waiting weight on railing or standing with bag, watching approaching train, yellow safety line visible, platform length in background, fluorescent platform light, train heat-wind arriving, headlight approaching, anticipatory transition between-departures moment, departure-board visible, commuter crowd movement
   136|
   137|E5. **Bus upper deck corner** — empty rear corner, street below visible through window, upper deck vibration, engine hum, route announcements, open window wind, elevated position over street, city voyaging, contemplative city-watching, other passenger less visible, slight elevated-height vertigo feeling
   138|
   139|E6. **Rideshare pickup zone** — waiting with phone checking app, looking for car, recognition wave, walking toward car, door opening, seated seatbelt click, looking at phone screen, app-mediated arrival departure, digital-age transition moment, car interior visible, passenger space, between-destination placeholder
   140|
   141|E7. **MTR cabin interior — peak hour** — compressed body proximity, other bodies in frame peripheral, forehead sweat, elbow-bag cushion, floor stance wide for stability, looking up from phone, commuter exhaustion, body against body, stranger proximity, peak-hour anonymous intimacy, MTR humming, station announcement echo
   142|
   143|E8. **Ferry outdoor deck** — sea wind strong on face, hair blown, holding railing, looking at harbor, sea spray catch, leaning into wind for balance, Kowloon visible across harbor, city view from water, sea air salt smell, container ship in harbor, ship motion rock, outdoor deck limit, between-t码头 feeling
   144|

   146|
   147|## V14.6 UPGRADE MODULES
   148|
   149|### Module ENV-TRANS-01: TRANSITIONAL_SPACE_EMOTIONAL_SYSTEM
   150|**Trigger:** Environment is transitional space (A1-A10)
   151|**Implementation:**
   152|```
   153|[TRANSITIONAL SPACE type]
   154|— [time-since-arrival body language]
   155|— [environmental specific: temp/sound/light]
   156|— [emotional register: introspective/exhausted/anticipatory]
   157|— [gesture consistent with space-transition behavior]
   158|```
   159|
   160|### Module ENV-MICRO-01: MICRO_DESTINATION_BEHAVIOR_SYSTEM
   161|**Trigger:** Environment is micro-destination (B1-B10)
   162|**Implementation:**
   163|```
   164|[MICRO DESTINATION specific space]
   165|— [socially-specific gesture]
   166|— [space-constraining behavior]
   167|— [emotional register from micro-moment type]
   168|```
   169|
   170|### Module ENV-DOM-01: DOMESTIC_TRANSITIONAL_LAYER
   171|**Trigger:** Scene within private domestic space (C1-C10)
   172|**Implementation:**
   173|```
   174|[DOMESTIC LOCATION specific]
   175|— [DOMESTIC TRANSITIONAL behavior type]
   176|— [specific domestic gesture]
   177|— [off-guard emotional state]
   178|```
   179|
   180|### Module ENV-WEATHER-01: WEATHER_PHYSICAL_CAUSATION_SYSTEM ⭐
   181|**Trigger:** Weather element present (D1-D8)
   182|**Implementation:**
   183|```
   184|[PRIMARY ENVIRONMENT]
   185|— [WEATHER CAUSATION type]
   186|— [body responding physically to weather]
   187|— [fabric responding physically to weather]
   188|— [posture/shelter adjustment from weather]
   189|```
   190|
   191|### Module ENV-TRANSIT-01: TRANSPORTATION_MEMORY_SPACE_SYSTEM
   192|**Trigger:** Subject inside vehicle or at transit point (E1-E8)
   193|**Implementation:**
   194|```
   195|[TRANSPORTATION SPACE type]
   196|— [isolation intimacy vs contemplative introspection]
   197|— [enclosed-space proximity]
   198|— [transit-motion physical effect]
   199|— [light quality inside vehicle]
   200|```
   201|
   202|---
   203|
   204|## AVOID BOUNDARIES
   205|
   206|| # | AVOID | REASON |
   207||---|-------|--------|
   208|| AV01 | Empty tourist spots | Scenery-with-person, not human-in-world |
   209|| AV02 | Generic café/nightlife (V14.5 overused) | No added value — use micro-destinations instead |
   210|| AV03 | Empty pool/rooftop (V14.5 overused) | Clean aesthetic, not memory-realism |
   211|| AV04 | Studio-loopback backdrop | Opposite of environmental immersion |
   212|| AV05 | Weather as aesthetic filter (not causation) | Weather must physically affect body/fabric/posture |
   213|
