================================================================================
## V14 ENVIRONMENTAL COLOR MEMORY SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V14/ENVIRONMENTAL_COLOR_MEMORY_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENVIRONMENTAL_COLOR_MEMORY_SYSTEM.md
     2|### V14.6 Core Module — Film Stock as Emotional Memory Encoding
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — Promoted from V14_RESEARCH_v14_6/02
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## CORE PHILOSOPHY
     8|
     9|**"Humans remember environments emotionally, not color-accurately."**
    10|
    11|When you recall a place you loved, you remember the FEELING — golden warmth, dreamy softness, electric night magic. Not precise colorimeter readings.
    12|
    13|Film stocks work as memory systems because they impose an **emotional color signature** on the scene that matches how humans actually encode place-experience.
    14|
    15|V14.6 renders environments through 11 distinct emotional-memory systems. These are NOT "looks" to apply — they are the way a human being would emotionally encode this environment based on their memory of it.
    16|
    17|---
    18|
    19|## 11 COLOR MEMORY SYSTEMS
    20|
    21|### COL-01: Kodak Gold 200 — Warm Golden Nostalgic Memory
    22|
    23|**Emotional signature:** "Remember when we were kids" — summer afternoon, golden hour that felt eternal, skin with life.
    24|
    25|**Color behavior:**
    26|- Warm shift: slight yellow-orange push across entire frame
    27|- Skin: yellow-peach undertones, warmer than reality, healthy warmth
    28|- Saturation: elevated but not garish — rich
    29|- Grain: visible but fine — texture suggesting "this moment existed in time"
    30|- Shadow: warm amber shadow, NOT cool blue — memories are warm
    31|- Contrast: medium — softer roll-off, shadow detail present
    32|
    33|**When fires:** Late afternoon outdoor (4-7pm), indoor tungsten before sunset, skin catching warm window light, "this feels like a memory" quality
    34|
    35|**Moderation:** Warm nostalgic framing implies past-tense memory, not present-tense performance. No glamour energy.
    36|
    37|---
    38|
    39|### COL-02: Fuji Pro 400H — Soft Cool Dreamy Memory
    40|
    41|**Emotional signature:** "I was there but it felt like a dream" — not quite real, beautiful in an unknowable way.
    42|
    43|**Color behavior:**
    44|- Cool push: slight blue-green cast in shadows
    45|- Low contrast: everything flattened slightly, soft roll-off
    46|- Skin: soft, smooth, slightly ethereal — great skin but dreamy
    47|- Saturation: slightly muted — colors don't shout
    48|- Grain: very fine, almost invisible
    49|- Shadow: faint green — signature Pro 400H contamination
    50|
    51|**When fires:** Overcast light (no harsh shadows = perfect for this stock), shaded outdoor areas, indoor indirect light, "this felt unreal" quality
    52|
    53|**Moderation:** Dreamy = passive, not performative. Subject is being, not showing. Low risk.
    54|
    55|---
    56|
    57|### COL-03: CineStill 800T — Tungsten-Balanced Night Street Magic
    58|
    59|**Emotional signature:** "That night" — tungsten street lights fighting blue darkness, halation glow around highlights, electricity of night-out with friends.
    60|
    61|**Color behavior:**
    62|- Tungsten balance: designed for orange light, pushes blue in shadows
    63|- Halation: bright highlights bleed into surrounding area — signature glow
    64|- Warring colors: orange (tungsten) vs blue (darkness) in SAME frame
    65|- Night street: skin under streetlight goes orange-gold, shadow goes blue-black
    66|- Grain: visible, halation creates "glow on film" feeling
    67|
    68|**When fires:** Night street scenes, indoor tungsten at night, bar/club entrance (tungsten inside, blue outside), warm+cool light fighting
    69|
    70|**Anti-AI:** CineStill halation is physically caused by film emulsion — AI cannot replicate via prompt. The orange/blue warring requires active anti-correction.
    71|
    72|**Moderation:** Night street magic = city energy, not glamour. Low angle and atmospheric depth natural here, not sexualized.
    73|
    74|---
    75|
    76|### COL-04: Disposable Camera — Social Memory Documentary
    77|
    78|**Emotional signature:** "I was there with my friends" — social documentation energy, moment captured not posed.
    79|
    80|**Color behavior:**
    81|- Harsh close flash: nearest subject lit, background drops — signature
    82|- Oversaturated: colors too vivid, slightly out-of-control
    83|- Slightly washed: highlights blow out, blacks crush
    84|- Chaotic grain: not even, more in darker areas
    85|- Composition: slightly off, accidental, nobody cared about rule-of-thirds
    86|- Flash shadow: hard shadow one side, deep shadow other
    87|
    88|**When fires:** Social gatherings (party, concert, festival), casual friend documentation, "someone just took a photo" energy, indoor social spaces with mixed lighting
    89|
    90|**Anti-AI:** Disposable camera aesthetic is defined by FAILURES — flash too close, colors too saturated, grain chaotic. AI tends to "clean up." Explicitly maintain flaws.
    91|
    92|**Moderation:** Disposable = casual, social, NOT curated. No body-display. Natural anti-influencer energy.
    93|
    94|---
    95|
    96|### COL-05: CCD (Early 2000s Digicam) — Y2K Imperfect Realism
    97|
    98|**Emotional signature:** "2003" — first digital cameras, before phones, lo-fi digital aesthetic. Slightly broken, warm, friendly.
    99|
   100|**Color behavior:**
   101|- Warm shift: slight yellow/orange push like early sensor compensation
   102|- Soft: edges slightly soft, not sharp — lo-fi not hi-fi
   103|- Noise pattern: different from film grain — digital pixel noise, slightly blocky
   104|- Highlight bloom: bright areas bleed slightly
   105|- Color bleed: adjacent colors slightly contaminate each other
   106|- Skin: warm, slightly smoothed, imperfect
   107|
   108|**When fires:** Early 2000s aesthetic moments, friend photo documentation, casual selfie energy (pre-phone-camera-quality), "point and shoot" quality
   109|
   110|**Moderation:** Y2K lo-fi = friendly, casual, not aspirational. Low body-display. Anti-influencer by virtue of being imperfect.
   111|
   112|---
   113|
   114|### COL-06: Smartphone HDR — High Detail Slightly Artificial
   115|
   116|**Emotional signature:** "I took this with my phone" — vibrant, detailed, slightly uncanny. Real but processed.
   117|
   118|**Color behavior:**
   119|- High detail: sharp, clear, every pore visible
   120|- Vivid color: saturation pushed, not quite natural
   121|- Skin smoothing: computational photography softens automatically
   122|- Dynamic range: shadows lifted, highlights preserved — HDR visible
   123|- Slight artificial quality: "too good to be true"
   124|- Over-processing: noise reduction creates plastic texture in skin
   125|
   126|**When fires:** Casual phone documentation, social media documentation, phone camera type scenes
   127|
   128|**Anti-AI paradox:** Smartphone HDR is ironically "AI-enhanced" — it uses computational photography. Using it HELPS counter AI smoothness by introducing phone processing artifacts. Ironic but effective.
   129|
   130|**Moderation:** Phone photo = casual, self-documentation. Natural anti-glamour. Phone photos don't capture glamour-model energy.
   131|
   132|---
   133|
   134|### COL-07: Humid Hong Kong Summer Tungsten Contamination — HK SPECIFIC
   135|
   136|**Emotional signature:** "HK summer at night" — yellow haze, warm contamination, heat that won't leave even after sunset.
   137|
   138|**Color behavior:**
   139|- Yellow haze: entire frame shifted toward yellow-orange
   140|- Warm fog: atmospheric warmth throughout, not just in highlights
   141|- Skin: more orange than usual, humidity affects how light reads on skin
   142|- Shadows: still warm, not cool — even shadow areas have yellow contamination
   143|- Contrast: reduced by atmospheric haze
   144|- Street light bloom: more pronounced in humid air
   145|
   146|**When fires:** Summer night in Hong Kong (June-August), humid evening with street lights, post-rain heat without wind
   147|
   148|**Moderation:** Atmospheric = environmental. Yellow haze = emotional weight on environment, not body. Good for HK-specific night realism.
   149|
   150|---
   151|
   152|### COL-08: Mixed-Light Realism — Tungsten + Daylight Warring
   153|
   154|**Emotional signature:** "The light is doing something weird and it's real" — orange and blue fighting in same frame.
   155|
   156|**Color behavior:**
   157|- Orange from tungsten: warm sources push orange
   158|- Blue from daylight: shadow areas go cool blue
   159|- Warring quality: neither color wins — visible tension
   160|- Skin: orange one side (tungsten), blue other (daylight)
   161|- Color temperature split: visible across frame — not corrected
   162|- Technically "incorrect" but actually correct for real mixed light
   163|
   164|**When fires:** Indoor tungsten + window daylight, street at dusk (tungsten on, daylight fading), shopping mall entrance (fluorescent inside, daylight outside)
   165|
   166|**Anti-AI:** AI tends to "correct" mixed light to one temperature. Maintaining the tension requires explicit anti-correction: "DO NOT CORRECT — WARM + COOL WARS IN SAME FRAME."
   167|
   168|**Moderation:** Mixed light = realistic, not stylized. No glamour. Good for documentary-style environmental immersion.
   169|
   170|---
   171|
   172|### COL-09: Low-Cost Lens Softness — Soft-Center Imperfect Rendering
   173|
   174|**Emotional signature:** "Someone gave me their old camera and I used it" — not professional, personal, slightly broken but lovable.
   175|
   176|**Color behavior:**
   177|- Soft center: middle of frame slightly soft, not sharp
   178|- Sharper edges: corners sharper than center — unusual optical
   179|- Warm coating: slight warm cast from lens coating
   180|- Light falloff: corners darken more than modern lenses
   181|- Imperfect sharpness: not all focal planes equally sharp
   182|- Character: lens has "personality"
   183|
   184|**When fires:** Casual personal photography, vintage lens use, "this specific camera was here" feeling
   185|
   186|**Anti-AI:** Defined by imperfections. AI tends toward uniform sharpness. Imperfect optical behavior = anti-AI by definition.
   187|
   188|**Moderation:** Lens softness = personal, not professional. Natural anti-glamour. Low body-display.
   189|
   190|---
   191|
   192|### COL-10: Moonlight Retention — Cool Blue Preservation
   193|
   194|**Emotional signature:** "The night was so clear the moon was doing things" — cool blue preservation in deep shadows, moonlight as source.
   195|
   196|**Color behavior:**
   197|- Cool shadow: deep shadows go blue-black, not neutral or warm
   198|- Blue retention: blue tones preserved even in very dark areas
   199|- Light source: moonlight creates cool light, not warm
   200|- Contrast: high — deep shadows, lit areas separated
   201|- Skin: blue-white under moonlight, NOT orange
   202|
   203|**When fires:** Night scenes with visible moon, clear night, outdoor night with moonlight as primary source
   204|
   205|**Anti-AI:** AI tends to add warmth to night scenes. Moonlight retention requires explicit cool-blue preservation — stopping AI's warmth bias.
   206|
   207|**Moderation:** Moonlight = contemplative, cool, not performative. Good for introspective environmental shots.
   208|
   209|---
   210|
   211|### COL-11: Shadow Color Retention — Deep Blue Shadow Tones
   212|
   213|**Emotional signature:** "There's a sky and it's reflecting in the shadows" — color lives in dark areas, not just highlights.
   214|
   215|**Color behavior:**
   216|- Blue shadows: shadow areas go deep blue, not crushed black
   217|- Color in dark: blue, purple, teal retained in shadow areas
   218|- Sky reflection: shadows reflect sky color (blue by day, deep at night)
   219|- Shadow detail: visible but dark — not lifted, not crushed
   220|- Contrast: medium to high — clear lit/shadow separation
   221|- Rich, full, "alive" even in dark areas
   222|
   223|**When fires:** Overcast days, open shade situations, scenes where sky is large percentage of frame
   224|
   225|**Anti-AI:** AI tends to crush shadows to black. Shadow color retention = specifically anti-crush — maintaining blue/purple/teal in shadows even when dark.
   226|
   227|**Moderation:** Shadow color = environmental, atmospheric. Not body-display. Good for sky-dominant environmental shots.
   228|
   229|---
   230|
   231|## V14.6 UPGRADE MODULES
   232|
   233|### Module COL-SYSTEM-01: EMOTIONAL_COLOR_MEMORY_SYSTEM
   234|**What:** Replaces "color accurate" with "emotionally remembered" — 11 systems imposing emotional signatures
   235|**Trigger:** Environment has emotional memory quality OR specific light condition present
   236|**Prompt:**
   237|```
   238|[COLOR MEMORY: warm nostalgia / cool dream / electric night / social doc]
   239|— [specific stock or behavior: warmth/shadow/halation/grain/shadow-blue]
   240|— [grain quality: fine/medium/absent]
   241|— [contrast: soft/medium/high]
   242|```
   243|
   244|### Module COL-SYSTEM-02: FILM_STOCK_EMOTIONAL_FILTER
   245|**What:** Applies specific film stock characteristics as emotional memory filter
   246|**Trigger:** Explicit film stock reference in prompt OR social documentation moment
   247|**Prompt:**
   248|```
   249|[FILM STOCK type: Kodak Gold / Fuji Pro 400H / CineStill 800T / Disposable / CCD]
   250|— [specific color behavior signature]
   251|— [grain pattern: stock-specific]
   252|— [halation/imperfection: stock-specific artifact PRESERVED]
   253|```
   254|
   255|### Module COL-HK-01: HONG_KONG_ATMOSPHERE_COLOR_SYSTEM — HK PRIORITY
   256|**What:** Applies HK summer humidity tungsten contamination, mixed-light HK realism
   257|**Trigger:** Scene is Hong Kong, summer/hot/humid, indoor-outdoor light transition
   258|**Prompt:**
   259|```
   260|[HK ATMOSPHERE: humid yellow haze]
   261|— [tungsten + daylight warring]
   262|— [warm shadow preservation]
   263|— [street light bloom in humidity]
   264|```
   265|
   266|### Module COL-SHADOW-01: SHADOW_COLOR_PHYSICS_SYSTEM
   267|**What:** Maintains blue in shadows, prevents shadow crush, preserves sky reflection in dark
   268|**Trigger:** Overcast sky, large sky %, open shade, post-weather
   269|**Prompt:**
   270|```
   271|[SHADOW COLOR PHYSICS: blue shadow retention]
   272|— [sky reflection in shadows]
   273|— [shadow detail: visible not crushed]
   274|— [contrast separation: lit vs shadow]
   275|```
   276|
   277|### Module COL-MIXED-01: MIXED_LIGHT_CORRECTION_INHIBITOR
   278|**What:** Stops "correction" of mixed-light to single temperature — maintains orange/blue warring
   279|**Trigger:** Multiple light sources with different color temperatures
   280|**Prompt:**
   281|```
   282|[MIXED LIGHT — NO CORRECTION]
   283|— [orange tungsten areas PRESERVED]
   284|— [blue shadow/digital areas PRESERVED]
   285|— [temperature war MAINTAINED — DO NOT CORRECT]
   286|```
   287|
   288|---
   289|
   290|## ANTI-AI LOGIC
   291|
   292|1. **Imperfection preservation:** Film stocks (Gold, Pro 400H, CineStill) have specific imperfections that AI tends to "correct." Anti-AI logic: PRESERVE halation, grain, shadow warmth.
   293|2. **Wrong-but-right color:** CineStill tungsten-blue war, mixed-light orange-blue split — technically "incorrect" but emotionally correct.
   294|3. **Imperfect optical:** Low-cost lens softness defined by imperfections. AI tends toward uniform sharpness.
   295|4. **Shadow crush prevention:** Shadow color retention prevents AI crushing shadows to black.
   296|5. **Warmth bias prevention:** Moonlight retention requires anti-warmth — stopping orange addition to night.
   297|6. **Disposable failures:** Explicitly maintaining harsh flash, oversaturation, chaotic grain, blown highlights = strongest anti-AI.
   298|
   299|---
   300|
   301|## MODERATION PROFILE: HIGH SAFETY
   302|
   303|All 11 systems carry emotional/nostalgic/dreamy/documentary energy. None carry glamour or body-display energy.
   304|
   305|- Warm nostalgic (Col-01): Past-tense memory, not present performance
   306|- Cool dreamy (Col-02): Passive being, not showing
   307|- Night street (Col-03): City energy, not sexual
   308|- Disposable (Col-04): Casual social, not curated
   309|- Y2K lo-fi (Col-05): Friendly casual, not aspirational
   310|- Phone doc (Col-06): Casual self-documentation, not glamour
   311|- HK humidity (Col-07): Environmental atmospheric, not body-display
   312|- Mixed light (Col-08): Realistic documentary, not stylized
   313|- Lens softness (Col-09): Personal, not professional
   314|- Moonlight (Col-10): Contemplative cool, not performative
   315|- Shadow color (Col-11): Environmental, not body-display
   316|

================================================================================
## V14 WORM EYE ENVIRONMENT SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V14/WORM_EYE_ENVIRONMENT_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# WORM_EYE_ENVIRONMENT_SYSTEM.md
     2|### V14.6 Core Module — Environmentally Immersive Low-Angle Perspective
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — Promoted from V14_RESEARCH_v14_6/03
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## CRITICAL DISTINCTION
     8|
     9|### ❌ WRONG: Worm-eye AS glamour
    10|Camera below subject, looking up at body, emphasizing curves/bust/legs. Subject is hero. Environment is backdrop.
    11|
    12|### ✅ CORRECT: Worm-eye AS environmental immersion
    13|Camera at ankle-knee height, looking at world from below. Emphasizing scale of environment, smallness of human within it, dominance of atmospheric conditions. Subject is PART of the world. Environment is the hero.
    14|
    15|**Low-angle does NOT equal glamour in this system.**
    16|Any use that creates body-display framing (curves emphasis, bust, leg display) violates this system.
    17|
    18|Moderation check: *"Is the environment dominant? Is the human small? Is this about atmospheric presence, not body display?"*
    19|
    20|---
    21|
    22|## 7 ENVIRONMENTAL IMMERSION SYSTEMS
    23|
    24|### WRM-01: Foot-Level Realism — Ankle-Knee Camera Height
    25|
    26|**Camera height:** Ankle to knee level (15-50cm from ground)
    27|**What viewer sees:** World from ground-level where buildings tower, sky dominates, human scale is small
    28|
    29|**Visual behavior:**
    30|- Environment dominates frame: subject small, environment large
    31|- Scale contrast: buildings look massive, human looks tiny
    32|- Ground visible: floor, pavement, feet, shoes, ground texture prominent
    33|- Sky percentage: 50%+ of frame is sky
    34|- Perspective compression: vertical lines converge strongly, buildings appear to lean
    35|
    36|**Environmental authority mechanics:**
    37|- Subject small → environment large
    38|- Ground-level POV → viewer feels like standing in the scene
    39|- Ankle-height visibility → human world texture at floor level visible
    40|
    41|**Anti-AI logic:** Ground-level is uncommon in AI training data — not a "flattering" angle, it's an immersive angle. Ankle-knee height counters eye-level default.
    42|
    43|---
    44|
    45|### WRM-02: Environment Scale Amplification — Buildings Tower, Human Small
    46|
    47|**Environment so large human becomes minor** — not diminishing, but showing vastness of world and specific smallness of being inside it.
    48|
    49|**Visual behavior:**
    50|- Building scale: towers above, leaning against frame edges
    51|- Human placement: lower third or below, small in frame
    52|- Compression: wide-angle feel, environment crowded in
    53|- Dominance: 70-80% environmental frame, 20-30% human
    54|- Emotional weight: world bigger than person — vulnerability without weakness
    55|
    56|**Environmental authority mechanics:**
    57|- HK density creates specific compression feel — church-in-grid
    58|- Weather integration: rain dripping from above, wind affecting hair at human height
    59|- Environment as primary visual interest
    60|
    61|**Anti-AI logic:** AI frames human as hero, environment as backdrop. Environment scale amplification requires: environment PRIMARY, human SECONDARY.
    62|
    63|---
    64|
    65|### WRM-03: Sky Dominance — Large Sky %, Atmospheric Layer
    66|
    67|**Sky is NOT backdrop — it's the active frame element that imposes emotional register.**
    68|
    69|**Visual behavior:**
    70|- Sky percentage: 40-70% of frame is sky
    71|- Atmospheric layer: clouds, pollution, color temperature, weather visible in sky
    72|- Non-human elements primary: building outlines, crane silhouettes, cloud formations
    73|- Emotional register from sky: overcast = contemplative, clear = open, stormy = heavy, golden = nostalgic
    74|
    75|**Environmental authority mechanics:**
    76|- Sky as emotional anchor: mood of scene determined by sky, not subject
    77|- Atmospheric perspective: layers of atmosphere visible
    78|- Color temperature from sky: entire frame color-shifted by sky condition
    79|
    80|**Anti-AI logic:** AI tends to make sky "nice backdrop" rather than active frame element. Large sky + weather presence requires treating sky as PRIMARY.
    81|
    82|---
    83|
    84|### WRM-04: Silhouette Elongation — Subject Stretched Toward Sky
    85|
    86|**When camera below and subject above (standing, stairs, elevated), subject appears stretched vertically** — NOT sexual elongation, environmental response to scale.
    87|
    88|**Visual behavior:**
    89|- Vertical stretch: subject appears taller than reality
    90|- Upward emphasis: face/head toward sky, feet toward ground
    91|- Against sky: subject becomes dark silhouette against bright sky
    92|- Scale relationship: subject bridges ground and sky
    93|- Elongation direction: up toward sky, NOT laterally toward camera
    94|
    95|**Environmental authority mechanics:**
    96|- Subject connects earth and sky: standing figure is bridge between ground and atmosphere
    97|- Silhouette against sky: subject becomes atmospheric element, not framed subject
    98|- Scale demonstration: silhouetted against large sky, subject demonstrates sky scale
    99|
   100|**Anti-AI logic:** AI interprets vertical stretch as "unrealistic" and corrects. This system treats stretch as environmental response — subject stretching toward environment, not being distorted for glamour.
   101|
   102|**CRITICAL MODERATION:** Vertical stretch toward sky = environmental connectivity, NOT sexual elongation. Subject silhouetted, not framed for body.
   103|
   104|---
   105|
   106|### WRM-05: Walking Realism — Ground-Level Walking Shot
   107|
   108|**Camera captures walking from low angle — feet hitting ground, weight transfer, human in motion through space.**
   109|
   110|**Visual behavior:**
   111|- Ground visible: pavement, shoes, feet, ground texture
   112|- Walking motion: one foot possibly lifted, weight mid-transfer
   113|- Low angle: camera at ankle-knee height
   114|- Environment: ground plane visible, sense of walking through space
   115|- Realism: any person walking — not model-walking, just walking
   116|
   117|**Environmental authority mechanics:**
   118|- Ground-plane emphasis: where human walks, what surface
   119|- Motion captured: human in motion, not static — natural, unplanned
   120|- Scale reference: ground visibility establishes environment scale
   121|
   122|**Anti-AI logic:** AI tends to capture "standing and posing." Walking shots require motion blur, imperfect framing, ground visibility — elements AI doesn't default to.
   123|
   124|---
   125|
   126|### WRM-06: Accidental Tourist-Photo Energy — Unplanned Upward Angle
   127|
   128|**Camera angle feels unplanned — like someone held camera at waist level and accidentally pointed up, awkward but authentic.**
   129|
   130|**Visual behavior:**
   131|- Awkward framing: not composed, not rule-of-thirds, slightly off
   132|- Unplanned feel: like camera raised without thinking
   133|- Tourist energy: "I was there and the building was big so I pointed up"
   134|- Imperfect: not polished, not professional — authentic
   135|- Composition: environment dominates, human small, awkward angle
   136|
   137|**Environmental authority mechanics:**
   138|- No professionalism: tourist photos aren't trying to be good — they're documenting
   139|- "Look how big this was": exactly what V14.6 needs
   140|- Accidental composition = real documentation
   141|
   142|**Anti-AI logic:** AI tends to compose "correctly" — rule-of-thirds, balanced, professional. Tourist accidental energy requires explicit imperfectness.
   143|
   144|---
   145|
   146|### WRM-07: Atmospheric Weight — Environment Emotional Authority
   147|
   148|**When environment is larger than human in frame, environment GAINS emotional authority.**
   149|
   150|**Visual behavior:**
   151|- Environment frame dominance: 70%+ environment, <30% human
   152|- Emotional register: environment mood dominates scene mood
   153|- Scale consequence: human small → environment significant
   154|- Weather/light: environmental conditions are frame's primary visual interest
   155|
   156|**Environmental authority mechanics:**
   157|- Environment as emotional protagonist: NOT backdrop, but protagonist
   158|- Human as element: human is part of environment, not separate from it
   159|- Emotional weight from scale: by making environment large, scene gains weight
   160|- Contemplative quality: big environment = contemplative mood = introspective moment
   161|
   162|**Anti-AI logic:** AI makes human "pop" — bright, sharp, significant. Atmospheric weight requires human to be quiet, small, atmospheric, not competing with environment.
   163|
   164|---
   165|
   166|## V14.6 UPGRADE MODULES
   167|
   168|### WRM-SYSTEM-01: GROUND_LEVEL_IMMERSION
   169|**Trigger:** Environment dominant (building/sky/pavement scale) OR emotional weight requires world larger than human
   170|**Prompt grammar:**
   171|```
   172|[CAMERA HEIGHT: ground level ankle-knee]
   173|— [environment dominates frame]
   174|— [human small in frame]
   175|— [ground plane visible]
   176|— [sky percentage: 40-70%]
   177|```
   178|
   179|### WRM-SYSTEM-02: ENVIRONMENT_SCALE_REVERSAL
   180|**Trigger:** Emotional register contemplative/heavy/awe OR environment architecturally significant
   181|**Prompt grammar:**
   182|```
   183|[ENVIRONMENT PRIMARY]
   184|— [human secondary: small atmospheric not competing]
   185|— [scale contrast: environment large human small]
   186|— [70-80% environmental frame]
   187|— [compression: environment crowded in human tiny]
   188|```
   189|
   190|### WRM-SYSTEM-03: SKY_DOMINANCE
   191|**Trigger:** Overcast, clear, stormy, golden hour, or any moment where sky mood affects scene
   192|**Prompt grammar:**
   193|```
   194|[SKY PRIMARY: 40-70% of frame]
   195|— [weather active in sky: clouds/pollution/haze]
   196|— [color temperature from sky]
   197|— [non-human elements: buildings cranes clouds]
   198|```
   199|
   200|### WRM-SYSTEM-04: SILHOUETTE_VERTICAL
   201|**Trigger:** Subject above camera (standing, stairs, elevated) AND sky is large
   202|**Prompt grammar:**
   203|```
   204|[SILHOUETTE AGAINST SKY]
   205|— [vertical stretch: subject toward sky]
   206|— [face/head toward sky feet toward ground]
   207|— [scale: subject bridges ground and sky]
   208|— [NEVER lateral stretch toward camera for display]
   209|```
   210|
   211|### WRM-SYSTEM-05: WALKING_MOTION_CAPTURE
   212|**Trigger:** Scene is about transit, movement, going somewhere, environmental transit
   213|**Prompt grammar:**
   214|```
   215|[WALKING CAPTURE: ground visible]
   216|— [motion: weight transfer mid-step]
   217|— [low angle: ankle-knee height]
   218|— [realism: any walking not model-walking]
   219|```
   220|
   221|### WRM-SYSTEM-06: TOURIST_ACCIDENTAL_COMPOSITION
   222|**Trigger:** Moment is about being present in massive environment (building/mountain/harbor/landmark)
   223|**Prompt grammar:**
   224|```
   225|[TOURIST COMPOSITION: unplanned]
   226|— [no rule-of-thirds awkward framing]
   227|— [upward angle: accidental pointing up]
   228|— [environment proves scale: building/mountain/harbor large]
   229|— [authenticity: not professional just real]
   230|```
   231|
   232|### WRM-SYSTEM-07: ATMOSPHERIC_WEIGHT
   233|**Trigger:** Emotional register requires contemplation/heaviness/awe/nostalgia OR weather/time creates mood
   234|**Prompt grammar:**
   235|```
   236|[ATMOSPHERIC WEIGHT: environment protagonist]
   237|— [human quiet: small atmospheric not competing]
   238|— [emotional weight from scale: big environment = weighted scene]
   239|— [contemplative mood: big world small human time passing]
   240|```
   241|
   242|---
   243|
   244|## ANTI-AI LOGIC
   245|
   246|1. **Eye-level default prevention:** AI defaults to eye-level for "normal" shots. Ground-level requires explicit override.
   247|2. **Human-as-subject prevention:** AI defaults human-as-hero, environment-as-backdrop. Reversal required.
   248|3. **Composition correctness prevention:** AI composes "correctly." Tourist accidental energy requires explicit incorrectness.
   249|4. **Perfect framing prevention:** AI frames to make subject look good. Ground visibility + sky dominance counters optimization.
   250|5. **Vertical stretch rejection:** AI interprets vertical stretch as "error." Treat as environmental response, not distortion.
   251|6. **Body-emphasis prevention:** AI uses low angle for curves/bust/legs. Ground-level + environment-dominance prevents emphasis.
   252|
   253|---
   254|
   255|## MODERATION: CRITICAL SAFETY DISTINCTION
   256|
   257|**All 7 systems = HIGH SAFETY** when used correctly.
   258|
   259|The key is: worm-eye in V14.6 is about **ENVIRONMENTAL IMMERSION, not GLAMOUR PRESENTATION.**
   260|
   261|❌ VIOLATION: Low angle + body-display (curves, bust emphasis, leg display) = glamour = NOT permitted
   262|✅ PERMITTED: Low angle + environment-dominance + human-small = atmospheric immersion
   263|
   264|**Per-module moderation:**
   265|- WRM-01 Ground-Level: ✅ No body-display, subject small
   266|- WRM-02 Scale Reversal: ✅ Environment primary, human atmospheric
   267|- WRM-03 Sky Dominance: ✅ Sky is frame element, not body
   268|- WRM-04 Silhouette Vertical: ✅ Stretch toward sky, NOT toward camera for display
   269|- WRM-05 Walking: ✅ Functional, not performative
   270|- WRM-06 Tourist Accidental: ✅ Anti-professional, anti-glamour
   271|- WRM-07 Atmospheric Weight: ✅ Environment is protagonist
   272|
   273|---
   274|
   275|## CROSS-REFERENCE
   276|
   277|- **ENVIRONMENT_EXPANSION_SYSTEM.md** — Ground-level works best with D-series (Weather) and E-series (Transit): wet pavement reflections, typhoon rain shelter, post-rain street
   278|- **ENVIRONMENTAL_COLOR_MEMORY_SYSTEM.md** — CineStill + ground-level = electric HK night immersion; overcast + Fuji Pro 400H; clear night + moonlight retention
   279|- **CAMERA_AWARENESS_SYSTEM.md** — Level 3-4 natural for worm-eye (documentary/street)
   280|- **MEMORY_CAPTURE_SYSTEM.md** — Incomplete framing (System 1) natural pairing — worm-eye causes accidental crop
   281|

## V14 CAMERA DISTANCE PSYCHOLOGY
### Source: modules/V14/CAMERA_DISTANCE_PSYCHOLOGY.md
================================================================================

     1|# CAMERA_DISTANCE_PSYCHOLOGY.md
     2|### V14.6 Core Module — Camera Distance as Emotional Interpretation
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — Promoted from V14_RESEARCH_v14_6/04
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## CORE INSIGHT
     8|
     9|**Distance is not just technical — it's an emotional contract between viewer and subject.**
    10|
    11|The same scene at different distances produces fundamentally different psychological responses:
    12|
    13|| Distance | Viewer Contract | Emotional Feeling |
    14||----------|----------------|-------------------|
    15|| Close | "I am near this person" | Intimacy, warmth, belonging |
    16|| Mid | "I am with this group" | Social inclusion, friendship |
    17|| Observational | "I am watching from outside" | Observation, voyeur tension |
    18|| Telephoto | "I am studying from afar" | Clinical detachment |
    19|| Forgotten | "This is a memory fragment" | Documentary intimacy, authenticity |
    20|
    21|---
    22|
    23|## 10 DISTANCE SYSTEMS
    24|
    25|### DIS-01: Close Distance — Intimate Proximity
    26|
    27|**Emotional contract:** "I am in this person's physical space."
    28|
    29|**Physical behavior:**
    30|- Subject 70-90% of frame
    31|- Skin texture highly visible (pores, slight redness, fine hair)
    32|- Breath warmth perceivable
    33|- Depth of field: very shallow — background extremely soft
    34|- Shallow DOF: face ultra-sharp, environment soft-blur
    35|
    36|**Scene types:** Phone close (selfie, checking reflection), morning pillow scene, intimate indoor space, friend close (celebration moment)
    37|
    38|**Anti-AI:** AI smooths skin in close-ups. IMPERFECT skin texture (pores, slight redness, sleep-wrinkles) = anti-AI.
    39|
    40|**Moderation:** High intimacy but NOT inherently sexual. Skin texture visible creates realism. Use domestic context (bedroom, bathroom) for tenderness boundary.
    41|
    42|---
    43|
    44|### DIS-02: Mid Social Distance — Friend-Shot Belonging
    45|
    46|**Emotional contract:** "I could be in this photo."
    47|
    48|**Physical behavior:**
    49|- Subject 40-60% of frame
    50|- Group or environment present alongside subject
    51|- Background context clear (where this is matters)
    52|- Depth of field: medium — both subject and immediate context sharp
    53|- Body language visible in full social context
    54|
    55|**Scene types:** Friend group dining, rooftop gathering, café table shot, beach group, party group moment
    56|
    57|**Anti-AI:** AI isolates attractive individual, softening/removing social context. PRESERVE group context — other people, environment, activity.
    58|
    59|**Moderation:** Highest safety. Group context distributes attention. Camera operator likely group member. Natural anti-display.
    60|
    61|---
    62|
    63|### DIS-03: Observational Distance — Voyeur Tension Detachment
    64|
    65|**Emotional contract:** "I am watching without being seen."
    66|
    67|**Physical behavior:**
    68|- Subject 20-40% of frame
    69|- Photographer outside social moment, not participant
    70|- Viewer feels slightly unauthorized
    71|- Background present but secondary (candid feel)
    72|- Candid qualities: subject in natural activity, not aware of camera
    73|
    74|**Scene types:** Street photography at a distance, restaurant candid of stranger, public space candid, taxi window observation
    75|
    76|**Moderation:** Moderate attention. Authenticated public space required. Moment should be neutral (not highly vulnerable). No exploitation signal.
    77|
    78|**Anti-AI:** AI tends to soften voyeur quality into aesthetic documentary. Maintain unauthorized-feeling: subject truly unaware, moment not posed, no exploitation.
    79|
    80|---
    81|
    82|### DIS-04: Telephoto Distance — Compressed Environmental Weight
    83|
    84|**Emotional contract:** "I am studying this from afar like an artifact."
    85|
    86|**Physical behavior:**
    87|- Subject 10-20% of frame
    88|- Background compressed against subject
    89|- Background clearly visible, compressed
    90|- Lens compression: perspective flattened, no depth separation
    91|- HK environment compressed (street/building/harbor density visible)
    92|
    93|**Scene types:** Street scene across road, building facade observation, HK harbor compressed scene, mountain/landmark where human is scale reference
    94|
    95|**Anti-AI:** AI uses telephoto compression to enhance attractiveness. V14.6 uses compression specifically for ENVIRONMENTAL DENSITY — subject TRAPPED in compressed environment, not beauty-optimized.
    96|
    97|**Moderation:** Inherently observational, not sexual. Compression + distance reduces sexual presence. Good for environmental frame shots.
    98|
    99|---
   100|
   101|### DIS-05: Forgotten-Camera Distance — Documentary Intimacy ⭐ PRIMARY ENGINE LEVEL
   102|
   103|**Emotional contract:** "This is someone's memory fragment."
   104|
   105|**Physical behavior:**
   106|- Subject 15-35% of frame
   107|- Environment dominant — scene as important as subject
   108|- Camera operator emotionally present but technically imprecise
   109|- "Unposed and unpolished" quality
   110|- Some technical imperfection: slight blur, imperfect focus, poor composition
   111|- "Taken on the way to something, not FOR this"
   112|- Feels like personal archive photo, not content post
   113|
   114|**Scene types:** "Caught in moment" candid, travel photography where subject is aspect of larger scene, party documentation where photographer is IN the party
   115|
   116|**Anti-AI:** AI CANNOT generate forgotten-camera quality — it generates FOR a viewer, always. Forgotten-camera requires camera ABSENT while moment was experienced. **Strongest anti-AI distance.**
   117|
   118|**Moderation:** SAFEST distance category. Camera forgotten = subject not performing. Authenticity inherent. By definition anti-display.
   119|
   120|---
   121|
   122|### DIS-06: Close Overhead — Intimate Soft Tenderness
   123|
   124|**Emotional contract:** "She doesn't know I'm this close."
   125|
   126|**Physical behavior:**
   127|- Overhead angle (camera above face looking down)
   128|- Very close distance (70-90% face)
   129|- Shallow DOF (face sharp, bed/blanket soft)
   130|- Skin texture highly visible
   131|- Morning context likely (love this for first morning)
   132|- Warm light quality (sun through window, lamp)
   133|
   134|**Scene types:** Just-waking morning scene, sleeping/drowsy mid-rest, post-shower towel turban at vanity, morning bed scene
   135|
   136|**Moderation:** Highest intimacy + highest safety. Overhead close creates tenderness, not sexuality. Body usually partially covered (blanket, towel, clothing). Softness primary. Use covered/domestic-clothing context.
   137|
   138|**Anti-AI:** AI makes morning images glamorous. This system requires: sleep-wrinkles, pillow-crease, asymmetrical expression, warmth NOT perfection. Imperfect tenderness > polished beauty.
   139|
   140|---
   141|
   142|### DIS-07: Far Telephoto — Emotional Detachment Compound
   143|
   144|**Emotional contract:** "I am watching from a distance, detached."
   145|
   146|**Physical behavior:**
   147|- Subject 5-15% of frame (very small)
   148|- Background compressed AND subject small (compound telephoto + environmental)
   149|- Viewer at maximum observation distance
   150|- Subject isolated in environment
   151|- Contemplative, isolated, voyaging mood
   152|
   153|**Scene types:** Ferry window long shot across harbor, street from across road compressed, person on beach from distance
   154|
   155|**Anti-AI:** AI uses far telephoto for compression-beauty. V14.6 = environmental isolation — subject small because context is primary, not because compressed attractiveness. Maintain separation quality.
   156|
   157|**Moderation:** Lowest sexual content potential. Subject very small, compressed, distant. Natural anti-display. Good for contemplative environmental.
   158|
   159|---
   160|
   161|### DIS-08: Mirror Selfie — Self-Curation / Self-Documentation
   162|
   163|**Emotional contract:** "She designed this image herself."
   164|
   165|**Physical behavior:**
   166|- Camera/phone visible in frame or reflection
   167|- Selfie angle visible (cramped upward, face-focused)
   168|- Mirror visible in reflection
   169|- Subject AWARE but self-curating
   170|- Often face-focused (not full-body)
   171|- Quality: smartphone camera quality (realistic)
   172|
   173|**Scene types:** Bathroom mirror post-shower, bedroom mirror outfit check, car rearview, storefront window reflection
   174|
   175|**Moderation:** Self-curation = subject controlled image entirely. Less exploitative than observer-documented. Appropriate for self-expression moments.
   176|
   177|**Anti-AI:** AI mirror selfies look "pretty and perfect." Real mirror selfies have specific artifacts: (1) phone visible, (2) slightly awkward angle, (3) mirror in focus behind face, (4) single-source light from reflection, (5) slightly un-posed.
   178|
   179|---
   180|
   181|### DIS-09: Disposable Flash Close — Chaotic Intimacy ⭐ STRONGEST ANTI-AI ELEMENT
   182|
   183|**Emotional contract:** "This was a real night with friends."
   184|
   185|**Physical behavior:**
   186|- Harsh directional flash from near camera (nearest subject lit, rest nearly dark)
   187|- Oversaturated color (too vivid, slightly out-of-control)
   188|- Chaotic grain (not even — unevenly distributed)
   189|- Background drops to near-black (flash falloff)
   190|- Composition slightly off (no rule-of-thirds, accidental)
   191|- Hard shadow on one side of face from flash angle
   192|
   193|**Scene types:** Late-night party, concert inside, bar/club moment, friend celebration at table (indoor, late), indoor social gathering with low/no ambient light
   194|
   195|**Anti-AI:** STRONGEST anti-AI element. Defined by FAILURES: harsh flash, dark background, chaotic grain, oversaturation, wrong composition. AI "cleans up" ALL of these. **Explicitly preserve ALL flaws = anti-AI instruction.**
   196|
   197|**Moderation:** Inherently anti-glamour. Social documentation energy. Harsh flash washes out and flattens, reducing sexual display. Good for social authenticity.
   198|
   199|---
   200|
   201|### DIS-10: Social Group Distance — Belonging Amplification
   202|
   203|**Emotional contract:** "I can see myself in this group."
   204|
   205|**Physical behavior:**
   206|- Subject 30-50% of frame
   207|- At least one other person visible (group context)
   208|- Camera operator likely part of group (friend shot)
   209|- Social activity clear: eating, talking, walking together
   210|- Mid-wide composition: environment where activity happens
   211|
   212|**Scene types:** Friend group at table, walking group in street, rooftop gathering, beach with friend(s)
   213|
   214|**Moderation:** HIGHEST safety for social shots. Group context distributes sexual attention. Camera operator is clearly friend. Social warmth primary.
   215|
   216|**Anti-AI:** AI tends to isolate attractive individual even in group shots. OTHER GROUP MEMBERS must be clear, identifiable, contributing to scene. Group cohesion = anti-AI by preventing individual isolation.
   217|
   218|---
   219|
   220|## V14.6 UPGRADE MODULES
   221|
   222|### DIS-INTIMATE-01: INTIMATE_PROXIMITY_SYSTEM
   223|**Trigger:** Scene requires emotional closeness, tender domestic moment, physical proximity feeling
   224|**Prompt grammar:**
   225|```
   226|[CLOSE INTIMATE DISTANCE]
   227|— [subject 70-90% frame skin texture visible]
   228|— [breath warmth perceivable]
   229|— [shallow DOF: face ultra-sharp background soft]
   230|— [intimacy contract: "I am near this person"]
   231|```
   232|
   233|### DIS-FRIEND-01: FRIEND_SHOT_BELONGING_SYSTEM
   234|**Trigger:** Scene is social activity with group, camera operator is group member
   235|**Prompt grammar:**
   236|```
   237|[FRIEND-SHOT MID DISTANCE]
   238|— [subject 40-60% frame]
   239|— [group members visible and identifiable]
   240|— [social activity clear]
   241|— [belonging contract: "I could be in this photo"]
   242|```
   243|
   244|### DIS-OBSERVE-01: OBSERVATIONAL_DETACHMENT_SYSTEM
   245|**Trigger:** Scene is public space observation without social participation
   246|**Prompt grammar:**
   247|```
   248|[OBSERVATIONAL DISTANCE]
   249|— [subject 20-40% frame]
   250|— [public space context: ethically clear]
   251|— [candid behavior: unaware subject]
   252|— [voyeur tension: unauthorized observation feeling]
   253|```
   254|
   255|### DIS-TELE-01: TELEPHOTO_COMPRESSION_SYSTEM
   256|**Trigger:** Scene requires environmental compression (HK density, building scale, harbor)
   257|**Prompt grammar for HK:**
   258|```
   259|[TELEPHOTO COMPRESSION: HK street density]
   260|— [subject 10-20% frame]
   261|— [environment compressed against subject]
   262|— [compression serves ENVIRONMENTAL DENSITY not beauty]
   263|— [detached contract: "studying from afar"]
   264|```
   265|
   266|### DIS-FORGET-01: FORGOTTEN_CAMERA_MEMORY_SYSTEM ⭐ PRIMARY
   267|**Trigger:** Scene is emotionally significant moment where camera operator was absorbed
   268|**Prompt grammar:**
   269|```
   270|[FORGOTTEN CAMERA DISTANCE] ⭐
   271|— [subject 15-35% frame]
   272|— [environment dominant]
   273|— [technical imperfection: slight blur imperfect focus off-composition]
   274|— [memory fragment quality: "found in drawer" feeling]
   275|— [camera forgotten but moment remembered]
   276|```
   277|
   278|### DIS-CLOSE-OVERHEAD-01: CLOSE_OVERHEAD_TENDERNESS_SYSTEM
   279|**Trigger:** Morning just-waking, intimate domestic softness, tender private moment
   280|**Prompt grammar:**
   281|```
   282|[CLOSE OVERHEAD DISTANCE]
   283|— [overhead angle: camera above face looking down]
   284|— [close distance]
   285|— [shallow DOF: face sharp bed/bedding soft]
   286|— [skin texture: sleep-wrinkles pillow-crease imperfect tender]
   287|— [warm light: morning window]
   288|```
   289|
   290|### DIS-FAR-TELE-01: FAR_TELEPHOTO_ISOLATION_SYSTEM
   291|**Trigger:** Emotional register contemplative, isolation, weather-as-barrier
   292|**Prompt grammar:**
   293|```
   294|[FAR TELEPHOTO DISTANCE]
   295|— [subject 5-15% frame: very small]
   296|— [compressed AND distant: compound effect]
   297|— [maximum separation]
   298|— [contemplative: "watching from far away"]
   299|```
   300|
   301|### DIS-MIRROR-01: MIRROR_SELFIE_CURATION_SYSTEM
   302|**Trigger:** Scene involves mirror and self-photography
   303|**Prompt grammar:**
   304|```
   305|[MIRROR SELFIE DISTANCE]
   306|— [phone visible in frame]
   307|— [mirror visible in reflection]
   308|— [self-curation: "she designed this herself"]
   309|— [real mirror artifacts: awkward angle mirror sharp]
   310|```
   311|
   312|### DIS-DISPOSABLE-01: DISPOSABLE_FLASH_CHAOS_SYSTEM ⭐ STRONGEST ANTI-AI
   313|**Trigger:** Social gatherings (party/concert/late-night bar) where social documentation is primary
   314|**Prompt grammar:**
   315|```
   316|[DISPOSABLE FLASH DISTANCE] ⭐ STRONGEST ANTI-AI
   317|— [harsh close flash: nearest lit rest nearly dark]
   318|— [oversaturated: too vivid slightly uncontrolled]
   319|— [chaotic grain: unevenly distributed]
   320|— [off composition: no rule-of-thirds accidental]
   321|— [hard flash shadow: one side lit one side deep shadow]
   322|— [contract: "a real night with friends"]
   323|— [PRESERVE ALL FLAWS — DO NOT CORRECT]
   324|```
   325|
   326|### DIS-GROUP-01: SOCIAL_GROUP_BELONGING_SYSTEM
   327|**Trigger:** Scene is group social activity with identifiable social dynamic
   328|**Prompt grammar:**
   329|```
   330|[SOCIAL GROUP MID DISTANCE]
   331|— [subject 30-50% frame]
   332|— [1-2 other group members clearly visible]
   333|— [social activity: eating/talking/walking/celebrating clear]
   334|— [group members identifiable not blurred]
   335|— [self included contract: "these are my friends"]
   336|```
   337|
   338|---
   339|
   340|## DISTANCE + AWARENESS + MEMORY LAYERING
   341|
   342|The compound effect creates deepest anti-AI quality:
   343|
   344|```
   345|Close distance (DIS-01)
   346|+ Level 3 Awareness (CAM-03)
   347|+ Emotional timing before smile apex (MEM-03)  
   348|+ Imperfect focus on eyes (MEM-05)
   349|+ Kodak Gold warm nostalgia (COL-01)
   350|= PEAK V14.6 HUMAN MEMORY REALISM
   351|```
   352|
   353|**Every layer adds authenticity markers AI cannot simultaneously replicate:**
   354|- Proximity intimacy (close distance)
   355|- Not performing (level 3 awareness)
   356|- Not at peak emotion (timing)
   357|- Not technically perfect (imperfect focus)
   358|- Not color-accurate (warm nostalgic memory)
   359|
   360|---
   361|
   362|## MODERATION SUMMARY
   363|
   364|| Distance | Safety | Key Consideration |
   365||----------|--------|-------------------|
   366|| DIS-01 Close | Medium | Domestic context for tenderness boundary |
   367|| DIS-02 Friend-shot | HIGH | Group reduces individual sexualization |
   368|| DIS-03 Observational | Medium | Public space + no exploitation signal |
   369|| DIS-04 Telephoto | HIGH | Distance prevents intimacy |
   370|| DIS-05 Forgotten-camera ⭐ | HIGHEST | Camera forgotten = not performing |
   371|| DIS-06 Close Overhead | HIGH | Covered domestic context |
   372|| DIS-07 Far Telephoto | LOWEST | Subject very small distant |
   373|| DIS-08 Mirror Selfie | Medium | Self-curation = intentional |
   374|| DIS-09 Disposable Flash ⭐ | HIGH SAFETY | Anti-glamour by definition |
   375|| DIS-10 Social Group | HIGHEST | Group + belonging energy |
   376|
   377|**Overall V14.6 distance moderation profile:** VERY HIGH SAFETY — distance systems inherently reduce display framing and increase authenticity presence.
   378|

================================================================================
## V14 HUMIDITY HAIR BEHAVIOR SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V14/HUMIDITY_HAIR_BEHAVIOR_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# HUMIDITY_HAIR_BEHAVIOR_SYSTEM.md
     2|### V14.6 Core Module — Hair Physics as Environmental Narrative
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — Primary Environmental Element
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## WHAT THIS SYSTEM IS
     8|
     9|Hair is the most physically visible element of the environment acting on the human body.
    10|
    11|In Hong Kong summer, 70-90% humidity is not "background atmosphere" — **it is the protagonist**. Hair responds to humidity before the conscious mind does. Hair behavior tells the environmental story before any other visual element.
    12|
    13|This system treats hair NOT as aesthetic choice but as **physics-first behavior** — the hair must obey humidity laws before any styling consideration applies.
    14|
    15|---
    16|
    17|## PHILOSOPHY
    18|
    19|**"Humidity writes on hair instantly. The image shows weather BEFORE the person reacts to it."**
    20|
    21|Hair cling. Flyaway expansion. Weight increase. Bangs separating. These are not stylistic choices — they are the physical evidence of the environment moving through the body.
    22|
    23|The image should feel like the subject walked into a room and the air immediately got into their hair. Not hair-styled-for-camera. Hair-responding-to-atmosphere.
    24|
    25|---
    26|
    27|## FUNDAMENTAL PHYSICS
    28|
    29|### Humidity Hair Behaviors
    30|
    31|**HAIR_CLING_PHYSICS**
    32|- Hair absorbs water molecules from air
    33|- Hair shaft swells slightly (2-3% diameter increase)
    34|- Individual strands become heavier and droop
    35|- Surface tension between strands creates cling
    36|- Hair loses volume, collapses toward scalp and neck
    37|- Temples: hair sticks to skin from sweat + humidity combination
    38|- Nape: hair clings in comma patterns from neck curve
    39|- Forehead: baby hairs lift then fall with humidity weight
    40|- Cheeks: short strands adhere from sweat condensation
    41|
    42|**FLYAWAY_EXPANSION_PHYSICS**
    43|- Damaged cuticle scales lift in humidity
    44|- Strands repel each other (less intact cuticle = more static-like repulsion)
    45|- Hair expands outward from head shape
    46|- Maximum expansion at crown and hairline edges
    47|- Flyaways create halo effect around face — **THIS IS NOT FRIZZ, this is physics**
    48|- The halo is a humidity measurement tool
    49|
    50|**WEIGHT_INCREASE_PHYSICS**
    51|- 1 gram of hair can hold 0.3 grams of water
    52|- Long hair visibly stretches and elongates when wet
    53|- Bangs separate and hang rather than spring back
    54|- Ponytail sags lower on head when humidity-high
    55|- Hair doesn't spring back — gravity + water weight combine
    56|- Style memory: styled hair falls out of shape because style product can't fight physics
    57|
    58|**BANG_SEPARATION_PHYSICS**
    59|- Fringe hairs become individual strands not a sheet
    60|- Strands clump then separate as humidity changes minute-to-minute
    61|- Each strand has slightly different water absorption rate
    62|- Natural part in bangs widens or narrows with humidity
    63|- "Opening up" in middle of bangs = humidity rising
    64|- "Closing together" in middle of bangs = humidity dropping (AC effect)
    65|
    66|---
    67|
    68|## HK SUMMER HUMIDITY PROTOCOL
    69|
    70|**Scenario 1: High Humidity (80%+) Hair Response**
    71|```
    72|[AMBIENT: 82% RH, 31°C]
    73|— hair at temples already clinging before subject notices
    74|— nape hair visible damp curl pattern
    75|— flyaways at crown already expanded
    76|— front hairline: fine strands adhering to forehead skin
    77|— hair volume reduced approximately 15-20% from dry-state
    78|— natural texture amplified, not reduced
    79|— hair appears darker (wet strands absorb light differently)
    80|```
    81|
    82|**Scenario 2: Post-Transition Hair Response (AC → Outdoor)**
    83|```
    84|[TRANSITION: Leaving air-conditioned space]
    85|— hair hasn't immediately responded (3-5 min delay)
    86|— hair still in "ac-dried" state for first minutes outside
    87|— as humidity hits: hair begins expanding from temples
    88|— flyaways activate before main hair body
    89|— face: immediate awareness of air thickness on skin
    90|— hair catching sweat as it forms on scalp
    91|— the transition moment is physically visible in hair
    92|```
    93|
    94|**Scenario 3: Indoor High Humidity (No AC)**
    95|```
    96|[AMBIENT: Hong Kong old building without AC, 85% RH]
    97|— hair completely surrendered to gravity
    98|— no volume, all movement downward
    99|— sweat visible on hair strand surface (not scalp sweat only)
   100|— hair clumping with sweat distribution patterns
   101|— strands adhering in groups not individually
   102|— hair at back of neck stuck to skin
   103|— visual: hair looks "heavy" not "styled"
   104|```
   105|
   106|---
   107|
   108|## STATIC ELECTRICITY FROM AIR-CON (Opposite of Humidity)
   109|
   110|Air-conditioning creates the **opposite** of humidity effects on hair:
   111|
   112|**STATIC_ELECTRICITY_PHYSICS**
   113|- AC removes moisture from air
   114|- Dry air strips charge from hair surface
   115|- Hair strands repel each other (same charge)
   116|- Results in: flyaways, lifted strands, separated strands at crown
   117|- "Electric" quality to hair — individual strands visible
   118|- Hair stands away from head slightly
   119|- Short strands around face point outward
   120|
   121|**THE CONFLICT ZONE**
   122|```
   123|When subject moves from AC environment to humid outdoor:
   124|— AC-static hair meets humid air
   125|— charge dissipates as moisture enters cuticle
   126|— hair physically settles (not styles, physics responds)
   127|— flyaways reduce as strands become heavier
   128|— temple strands fall from outward-against-head to downward-against-skin
   129|— THIS IS NOT "HAIR FIXING" — this is charge equilibrium + water absorption
   130|```
   131|
   132|**Static-to-Humidity Transition Timing:**
   133|- First 30 seconds: static still dominant
   134|- 30-90 seconds: moisture equalizing, hair settling
   135|- 90-180 seconds: humidity effects fully visible
   136|- Hair "remembers" the AC state briefly — then surrenders to new environment
   137|
   138|---
   139|
   140|## POST-RAIN HAIR BEHAVIOR
   141|
   142|**Immediate Post-Rain (Still Wet)**
   143|```
   144|— hair fully saturated, each strand visible
   145|— hair stuck to face, neck, shoulders
   146|— water dripping from ends
   147|— hair color significantly darker (wet absorption)
   148|— strands clumped together, not separated
   149|— no volume, total collapse
   150|— hair has "rope" weight feeling
   151|— skin visible through hair more (transparency effect)
   152|```
   153|
   154|**10-20 Minutes Post-Rain**
   155|```
   156|— hair no longer actively dripping but still wet
   157|— surface water absorbed, strands still heavy
   158|— hair beginning to "recover" with ambient humidity
   159|— flyaways still suppressed by water weight
   160|— temple hair still clinging but less saturated
   161|— hair looks "damp" not "dripping"
   162|— color still dark but stabilizing
   163|```
   164|
   165|**30+ Minutes Post-Rain**
   166|```
   167|— hair reaching equilibrium with ambient humidity
   168|— surface dry, internal structure still holding water
   169|— flyaways beginning to activate as surface dries
   170|— hair starting to show natural texture again
   171|— humidity response now visible in "recovery" behavior
   172|— hair doesn't return to pre-rain state — water damage permanent to style
   173|— new shape: combination of water weight + gravity + humidity
   174|```
   175|
   176|---
   177|
   178|## SWEAT-EFFECT ON HAIR
   179|
   180|**Scalp Sweat + Humidity Combination**
   181|```
   182|When body heat rises and scalp sweats:
   183|— sweat follows hair strand down toward temples
   184|— combines with humidity moisture on hair surface
   185|— strands become adhesive with salt + water mixture
   186|— hair clings to forehead and temples simultaneously
   187|— the cling has "sticky" quality not just "wet" quality
   188|— short baby hairs: sweat as separate droplets on strands
   189|— longer strands: sweat travels down strand length
   190|```
   191|
   192|**Sweat Distribution Patterns:**
   193|- Hairline: sweat pools at forehead-hair boundary
   194|- Temples: highest accumulation due to hair proximity to skin heat
   195|- Nape: sweat travels through hair from scalp
   196|- Crown: least affected (heat rises, but hair density prevents accumulation)
   197|
   198|---
   199|
   200|## HAIR-STATIC-CHARGE VISUAL MARKERS
   201|
   202|**Static Charge Level Indicators:**
   203|```
   204|LOW (50% RH or below):
   205|— hair lying flat, minimal flyaway
   206|— strands together, cohesive movement
   207|— no separation at crown or hairline
   208|— hair responds to wind predictably
   209|
   210|MEDIUM (50-65% RH):
   211|— slight lift at crown
   212|— few strands separating at hairline
   213|— minor temple drift
   214|— hair begins to show individual strand quality
   215|
   216|HIGH (65-80% RH):
   217|— visible flyaway count increases
   218|— temple strands lifting from head
   219|— crown volume increase from strand expansion
   220|— nape hair separating into visible strands
   221|
   222|EXTREME (80%+ RH):
   223|— crown fully expanded, halo visible
   224|— temple hair stuck to face
   225|— nape and neck hair clumping
   226|— hair appears 20% larger in volume than dry state
   227|— flyaways visible at all hairline edges
   228|```
   229|
   230|---
   231|
   232|## V14.6 MODULE: HUMIDITY_HAIR_BEHAVIOR_SYSTEM
   233|
   234|### Module HH-01: HUMIDITY_PHYSICS
   235|**Trigger:** Scene where ambient humidity is a factor
   236|**Implementation:**
   237|```
   238|[AMBIENT HUMIDITY level]
   239|— [hair strand behavior: cling/flyaway/weight]
   240|— [specific location on head: temple/nape/crown/hairline]
   241|— [time-since-exposure to humidity]
   242|— [previous environment state if transition]
   243|— [hair color shift from wet absorption]
   244|```
   245|
   246|### Module HH-02: AIR_CON_STATIC_EFFECT
   247|**Trigger:** Subject in air-conditioned space OR transitioning from AC to ambient
   248|**Implementation:**
   249|```
   250|[STATIC CHARGE level from AC]
   251|— [flyaway count and location]
   252|— [strands repelling from head shape]
   253|— [transition state if moving]
   254|— [time-to-equilibrium with new environment]
   255|```
   256|
   257|### Module HH-03: POST_RAIN_HAIR_RESPONSE
   258|**Trigger:** Scene immediately after or during rain
   259|**Implementation:**
   260|```
   261|[RAIN SATURATION level]
   262|— [dripping/damp/recovering state]
   263|— [hair color darkening effect]
   264|— [cling pattern on face/neck]
   265|— [time since rain exposure]
   266|— [recovery stage indicator]
   267|```
   268|
   269|### Module HH-04: SWEAT_HAIR_INTERACTION
   270|**Trigger:** Subject in heat, exertion, or high body temperature
   271|**Implementation:**
   272|```
   273|[BODY HEAT level]
   274|— [sweat accumulation in hair]
   275|— [cling pattern from sweat + humidity]
   276|— [salt crystallization on strands]
   277|— [sweat travel direction on hair shaft]
   278|```
   279|
   280|### Module HH-05: HAIR_STATIC_CHARGE
   281|**Trigger:** Scene in dry AC environment OR static-frizzy moment
   282|**Implementation:**
   283|```
   284|[STATIC CHARGE level]
   285|— [flyaway location and count]
   286|— [strand separation at crown/hairline]
   287|— [individual strand visibility]
   288|— [charge dissipation behavior over time]
   289|```
   290|
   291|---
   292|
   293|## PROMPT GRAMMAR: HUMIDITY_HAIR
   294|
   295|**When humidity is a factor:**
   296|```
   297|humidity-affected hair, [location] hair clinging to [surface],
   298|[count] flyaways at [location], hair weight increased, 
   299|hair expanded [percentage], wet hair color darkened,
   300|bangs separated, hair losing volume, gravity-affected hair,
   301|hair not springing back, humidity droop, temple hair on skin,
   302|nape hair comma pattern, crown expansion halo, 
   303|[time-state] hair: dry/AC-static/humid/post-rain/dripping
   304|```
   305|
   306|**Specific hair behavior prompts:**
   307|```
   308|humid summer hair collapsed against scalp
   309|temple strands stuck to forehead from humidity + sweat
   310|flyaway expansion at crown humidity halo
   311|AC-to-outdoor transition hair settling
   312|post-rain hair water-heavy drooping
   313|bangs separated in humidity individual strands visible
   314|sweat in hair salt crystallization visible
   315|hair volume reduced 15% from humidity weight
   316|hair darkened from light absorption wet strands
   317|nape hair stuck to neck skin humidity sweat combination
   318|```
   319|
   320|**Transition prompts:**
   321|```
   322|just-left-AC hair still in static state [time] minutes
   323|hair beginning to surrender to humidity [time] minutes outside
   324|static charge dissipating as moisture enters cuticle
   325|hair reaching equilibrium with ambient humidity level
   326|```
   327|
   328|---
   329|
   330|## MODERATION PROFILE
   331|
   332|### What This System Prevents:
   333|
   334|| # | Prevent | Reason |
   335||---|---------|--------|
   336|| M01 | Hair styled-perfect in high humidity | Physics violation — humidity collapses hair structure |
   337|| M02 | "Frizz" as aesthetic choice | Frizz is physics, not style — cuticle damage creates repulsion |
   338|| M03 | Humidity as background | Humidity is protagonist — must be visible in hair behavior |
   339|| M04 | AC-static ignored in AC scenes | AC creates opposite of humidity — must be reflected in hair |
   340|| M05 | Post-rain hair returning to pre-rain state | Water damage is permanent — hair never fully recovers |
   341|| M06 | Hair color unchanged when wet | Wet hair absorbs light differently — must be visibly darker |
   342|| M07 | Clean dry hair in humid environment | Clean hair still responds to humidity — damage not required |
   343|| M08 | Bangs maintaining separation | Bangs lose separation in humidity — strands merge from weight |
   344|
   345|### Hair Behavior Moderation Rules:
   346|
   347|1. **Physics First:** Hair behavior is always physically motivated by humidity level
   348|2. **Environment Integration:** Hair is never isolated from environmental causation
   349|3. **Transition Accuracy:** Hair responds with correct timing to environment changes
   350|4. **Realism Over Aesthetic:** Hair looks like it's responding to physics, not styled for camera
   351|5. **No Stylish Humidity:** Hair in high humidity cannot look "good" by styling standards — it looks real
   352|
   353|---
   354|
   355|## CROSS-REFERENCE
   356|
   357|- **FABRIC_CAUSALITY_SYSTEM.md** — Fabric responds to same humidity environment as hair (parallel physics)
   358|- **ENVIRONMENT_EXPANSION_SYSTEM.md** — Weather-dominated environments (D-series) trigger hair physics
   359|- **REALISM_PHHILOSOPHY_V14_6.md** — Physics-first realism foundation for hair behavior
   360|- **FACS_BEHAVIORAL_REALISM_LAYER.md** — Face responding to humidity/sweat same timeline as hair
   361|
   362|---
   363|
   364|## PHYSICS REFERENCE CARD
   365|
   366|| Humidity | Hair State | Visual Markers |
   367||----------|------------|----------------|
   368|| 40-50% | AC-static dominant | Flyaways, strand repulsion, flat volume |
   369|| 50-65% | Transition zone | Mixed static + humidity behavior |
   370|| 65-80% | Humidity dominant | Crown expansion, temple drift, flyaway count rising |
   371|| 80%+ | Full humidity response | Halo, cling, weight droop, dark color, collapsed volume |
   372|| Post-rain | Saturated → recovering | Dripping → damp → dry surface, internal water, recovery tension |
   373|
