## V14 FABRIC CAUSALITY SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V14/FABRIC_CAUSALITY_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# FABRIC_CAUSALITY_SYSTEM.md
     2|### V14.6 Core Module — Fabric as First Responder to Environment
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — Environmental Causation Chain Initiator
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## WHAT THIS SYSTEM IS
     8|
     9|Fabric responds to the environment BEFORE the body does.
    10|
    11|Fabric is the first material in the causation chain: **Weather → Fabric → Body → Image**
    12|
    13|When humidity rises, fabric absorbs moisture and softens before the skin feels damp. When rain hits, fabric darkens and gains weight before the body registers cold. When AC runs, fabric dries and lifts with static before the mind registers discomfort.
    14|
    15|Fabric behavior is not aesthetic — it is **physical causation**. The image must show fabric responding to physics before the body's response becomes visible.
    16|
    17|---
    18|
    19|## PHILOSOPHY
    20|
    21|**"Fabric is the environment's hand on the body."**
    22|
    23|Fabric translates weather into physical sensation. Fabric is where environment becomes tangible. The image should show fabric bearing the weight of weather — absorbing, draping, clinging, changing — before the face or posture tells the story.
    24|
    25|Fabric-first causation: the viewer should read the weather from fabric condition, not from the face.
    26|
    27|---
    28|
    29|## THE CAUSATION CHAIN
    30|
    31|```
    32|WEATHER INPUT
    33|     │
    34|     ├─► FABRIC (first responder)
    35|     │       ├─ Moisture absorption / loss
    36|     │       ├─ Weight change
    37|     │       ├─ Drape modification
    38|     │       ├─ Color shift (wet/dry)
    39|     │       └─ Transparency change
    40|     │
    41|     └─► BODY (secondary responder)
    42|             ├─ Temperature sensation
    43|             ├─ Skin response (sweat/shiver)
    44|             └─ Posture adjustment
    45|
    46|CAMERA INTERCEPT
    47|     └─► Image shows: fabric physics visible BEFORE body awareness
    48|```
    49|
    50|The viewer reads the image bottom-up: **Body Posture → Fabric State → Weather Cause**
    51|
    52|But the causation runs top-down: **Weather → Fabric → Body**
    53|
    54|This reversal is what makes the image feel real — the fabric tells the story before the face has to.
    55|
    56|---
    57|
    58|## WET FABRIC PHYSICS
    59|
    60|### Saturation Behavior
    61|
    62|**WEIGHT_INCREASE_LAW**
    63|- Fabric can absorb 30-50% of its weight in water
    64|- Cotton t-shirt: dry 200g → wet 280-300g
    65|- This weight is visible — fabric droops, sags, loses spring
    66|- Shoulder seams shift lower when wet
    67|- Sleeves lengthen from sleeve droop
    68|- Hem line drops 2-5cm when saturated
    69|
    70|**DRAPE_MODIFICATION_LAW**
    71|- Wet fabric follows gravity more completely
    72|- Wrinkles deepen and become wet-looking (water in fold)
    73|- Fabric clings to body contours (shoulder, chest, hip)
    74|- Less air between fabric and skin (reduced insulation)
    75|- Drape becomes "heavier" — less spring, more fixed
    76|
    77|**COLOR_SHIFT_LAW**
    78|- Wet fabric absorbs light differently than dry
    79|- Darkens by 1-2 shades when wet
    80|- Color becomes more saturated (darker + richer)
    81|- Light colors become translucent when wet (especially cotton, linen)
    82|- Wet patch contrast: wet zone vs dry zone visibly different
    83|
    84|**TRANSPARENCY_CHANGE_LAW**
    85|- Light fabrics (white cotton, linen, thin polyester): wet = transparent
    86|- Body outline visible through wet white fabric
    87|- Underwear color visible through wet shirt
    88|- Skin tone showing through wet fabric
    89|- Wet transparency is a physics fact, not aesthetic choice
    90|
    91|**FABRIC_IMPRESSION_ON_SKIN_LAW**
    92|- Wet fabric leaves imprint on skin when removed
    93|- Pattern of fabric texture pressed into skin
    94|- Lighter marks where fabric weave compressed skin
    95|- Pattern visible for 5-10 minutes after removal
    96|- This is underwear lines, shirt lines, shorts lines in skin
    97|
    98|---
    99|
   100|## HUMID FABRIC PHYSICS
   101|
   102|### Humidity vs Saturation
   103|
   104|**HUMID_VS_WET_DISTINCTION**
   105|- Humid: fabric has absorbed some moisture, not saturated
   106|- 15-30% water content — below saturation threshold
   107|- Fabric softer, drape slightly heavier
   108|- Color slightly darker (less dramatic than wet)
   109|- Transparency slightly increased but not body-visible
   110|
   111|**DRAPE_CHANGES_IN_HUMIDITY**
   112|- Fabric becomes less rigid (moisture relaxes fibers)
   113|- Natural drape increased — fabric hangs differently
   114|- Sleeves: slight additional droop
   115|- Collar: loses crispness, softens
   116|- Fabric "surrenders" to gravity in humidity
   117|- Less spring-back when fabric moved
   118|
   119|**SKIN_CONTACT_INCREASE**
   120|- Humid fabric clings to skin more than dry fabric
   121|- Surface tension: moisture between fabric and skin
   122|- Shirt front clings to chest (visible chest contour)
   123|- Back of shirt clings to shoulder blade
   124|- Shorts cling to thigh contour
   125|- This is NOT aesthetic clinging — this is physics
   126|
   127|---
   128|
   129|## AIR-CON FABRIC PHYSICS
   130|
   131|### Dry Air Effect (Opposite of Humidity)
   132|
   133|**STATIC_CHARGE_FORMATION**
   134|- AC removes moisture from air
   135|- Fabric loses moisture to dry air
   136|- Same-charge accumulation on fabric strands
   137|- Fabric strands repel each other
   138|- Result: fabric lifts away from body, floats slightly
   139|
   140|**STATIC_LIFT_BEHAVIOR**
   141|```
   142|[DRY AIR / AC ACTIVE]
   143|— shirt front lifts away from chest slightly (2-5cm gap)
   144|— skirt/dress lifts away from thighs
   145|— sleeve separates from forearm (visible gap)
   146|— collar lifts away from neck
   147|— fabric has "floating" quality not "draping"
   148|```
   149|
   150|**STATIC_SETTLE_CYCLE**
   151|```
   152|[Cold AC → Warm Ambient Transition]
   153|— static charge dissipates as humidity enters fibers
   154|— fabric "settles" back onto body
   155|— the settling is visible — not gradual, discrete event
   156|— first 30 sec: still floating
   157|— 30-120 sec: settling begins
   158|— 2-5 min: fabric reaches new equilibrium
   159|```
   160|
   161|**FABRIC_STIFFNESS_FROM_DRY**
   162|- No moisture = fabric stiffer
   163|- Less drape, more structure
   164|- Shirt holds shape longer (wrinkle-resistant paradox)
   165|- BUT: once wrinkles form, they stay (no moisture to relax)
   166|- Static creates "crisp" quality that disappears with humidity
   167|
   168|---
   169|
   170|## HEAT FABRIC PHYSICS
   171|
   172|**THERMAL_EXPANSION**
   173|- Heat makes fabric fibers expand slightly
   174|- Tight clothes become tighter (fit change visible)
   175|- Synthetic fabric: more expansion than natural fibers
   176|- Elastic in fabric: heat affects rebound (looser fit over time)
   177|
   178|**SWEAT_EVIDENCE_IN_FABRIC**
   179|```
   180|[HEAT / EXERTION / NERVOUS SWEAT]
   181|— underarm zone: darker wet patch spreading
   182|— collar back: sweat accumulation (neck sweat)
   183|— shirt front center: chest sweat pattern
   184|— lower back: sweat band visible through shirt
   185|— shorts: thigh sweat, groin sweat zone
   186|```
   187|
   188|**SWEAT_PATCH_EVIDENCE_TYPES:**
   189|- **Active drip:** fresh sweat, dark wet zone, spreading edge
   190|- **Saturated zone:** maximum dark, no spreading, skin shows through fabric
   191|- **Drying zone:** ring of salt crystallization at patch edge, lighter center
   192|- **Humid-recovered zone:** damp but not wet, color returning, salt visible
   193|
   194|**SALT_CRYSTALLIZATION**
   195|- Sweat evaporates, salt remains
   196|- White crystallized edges on dark sweat patches
   197|- Visible on dark fabrics (white salt lines)
   198|- On light fabrics: salt as sticky residue
   199|- Salt changes fabric texture (stiffness where sweat dried)
   200|
   201|---
   202|
   203|## RAIN FABRIC PHYSICS
   204|
   205|### Rain Exposure Timeline
   206|
   207|**IMMEDIATE_RAIN_CONTACT (0-2 min)**
   208|```
   209|— fabric surface immediately wet
   210|— rain droplet impact visible (darker spots)
   211|— water running down fabric (streaking pattern)
   212|— fabric darkens from dry to wet state
   213|— drip points at hem, cuff, collar
   214|— water pooling on shoulders (shirt/s jacket)
   215|```
   216|
   217|**SATURATION_PHASE (2-10 min)**
   218|```
   219|— full saturation from surface to inner fabric
   220|— weight increase visible (drooping)
   221|— fabric fully translucent on light colors
   222|— body outline clearly visible through fabric
   223|— rain through shirt: skin visible, shirt clinging
   224|— drip rate slowing as saturation reaches maximum
   225|```
   226|
   227|**POST-RAIN_DRIPPING (During/After rain)**
   228|```
   229|— water dripping from hair onto shoulders
   230|— drips from hem (front and back)
   231|— sleeve ends dripping
   232|— water inside shoes visible (foot outline in puddle)
   233|— puddle forming at feet in frame
   234|```
   235|
   236|**RECOVERY_PHASE (10-30 min post-rain)**
   237|```
   238|— surface drying begins (wind + air movement)
   239|— fabric still wet internally but surface dry
   240|— color lightening from wet-saturated to damp
   241|— still heavy, still clinging, but not dripping
   242|— flyaways activate as surface dries
   243|— sweat mixed with rain water: different chemistry
   244|```
   245|
   246|---
   247|
   248|## FABRIC-TYPE RESPONSE MATRIX
   249|
   250|| Fabric Type | Humidity Response | Wet Response | Heat Response |
   251||-------------|------------------|--------------|---------------|
   252|| Cotton | High absorption, softens, drapes | Heavy, dark, transparent | Absorbs sweat fast, shows patches |
   253|| Linen | High absorption, wrinkles intensify | Heavy, droops, transparent when wet | Breathable but shows sweat |
   254|| Polyester | Low absorption, stays dry longer | Water slides off, doesn't saturate | Sweat visible as darker patches, doesn't absorb |
   255|| Silk | Moderate absorption, drapes heavily | Transparent when wet, clings | Shows sweat dramatically, stain visible |
   256|| Denim | Slow absorption, stays structured | Heavy, dark, loses shape slightly | Heat trapped, sweat at waistband |
   257|| Nylon | Water slides off, quick dry | Slight darkening, fast recovery | Shows sweat as darker zones |
   258|
   259|---
   260|
   261|## V14.6 MODULES: FABRIC_CAUSALITY_SYSTEM
   262|
   263|### Module FC-01: WET_FABRIC_PHYSICS
   264|**Trigger:** Scene with wet fabric (rain, sweat, water contact)
   265|**Implementation:**
   266|```
   267|[FABRIC SATURATION level]
   268|— [weight increase visible: droop/sag/elongation]
   269|— [color shift: darkening percentage]
   270|— [transparency change: skin visible through fabric]
   271|— [draping modification: cling to body contour]
   272|— [fabric type affects behavior]
   273|```
   274|
   275|### Module FC-02: HUMID_FABRIC_PHYSICS
   276|**Trigger:** Scene in humid environment without active wetness
   277|**Implementation:**
   278|```
   279|[AMBIENT HUMIDITY level]
   280|— [fabric softening from moisture absorption]
   281|— [drape modification: increased surrender to gravity]
   282|— [skin contact increase: surface tension effect]
   283|— [color slight darkening: not saturated but present]
   284|— [time-since-exposure to humidity]
   285|```
   286|
   287|### Module FC-03: AIR_CON_STATIC_FABRIC
   288|**Trigger:** Scene in air-conditioned space OR transitioning
   289|**Implementation:**
   290|```
   291|[STATIC CHARGE level]
   292|— [fabric lift away from body: location and distance]
   293|— [floating quality vs draping]
   294|— [strand repulsion visible at edges]
   295|— [settling behavior if transitioning]
   296|— [crispness vs normal drape]
   297|```
   298|
   299|### Module FC-04: HEAT_FABRIC_RESPONSE
   300|**Trigger:** Scene in heat, exertion, or nervous sweat
   301|**Implementation:**
   302|```
   303|[BODY HEAT level]
   304|— [sweat patch location and size]
   305|— [patch type: active/saturated/drying/recrystallized]
   306|— [underarm dark zone spread pattern]
   307|— [salt crystallization visible at edges]
   308|— [fabric transparency increase at sweat zones]
   309|```
   310|
   311|### Module FC-05: RAIN_DRIP_EVIDENCE
   312|**Trigger:** Scene during or after rain exposure
   313|**Implementation:**
   314|```
   315|[RAIN EXPOSURE time]
   316|— [dripping: active/slowing/none]
   317|— [streaking pattern on fabric]
   318|— [pooling water at shoulders/hem]
   319|— [puddle at feet in frame]
   320|— [post-rain recovery stage]
   321|— [wet vs damp vs drying state]
   322|```
   323|
   324|### Module FC-06: SWEAT_EVIDENCE_FABRIC
   325|**Trigger:** Scene with visible sweat on clothing
   326|**Implementation:**
   327|```
   328|[SWEAT DISTRIBUTION pattern]
   329|— [patch evolution: fresh/spreading/saturated/drying]
   330|— [underarm crescent shape and spread]
   331|— [chest/stomach sweat band]
   332|— [back sweat visible through shirt]
   333|— [salt crystallization at patch boundaries]
   334|— [fabric type determines sweat visibility]
   335|```
   336|
   337|---
   338|
   339|## FABRIC IMPRESSION ON SKIN
   340|
   341|**When wet fabric contacts skin and is removed:**
   342|```
   343|— fabric texture imprint on skin
   344|— lines visible where fabric weave pressed into skin
   345|— underwear lines on torso (bra strap lines, underwear waistband)
   346|— shirt seam lines on shoulders
   347|— collar line on neck
   348|— duration: visible for 5-15 minutes after removal
   349|— more visible when skin is warm (post-exercise, post-shower)
   350|```
   351|
   352|**This is different from pressure marks:**
   353|- Fabric impressions: pattern matches fabric weave/texture exactly
   354|- Pressure marks: general red line from tight elastic
   355|- Both can occur simultaneously
   356|
   357|---
   358|

   414|---
   415|
   416|## MODERATION PROFILE
   417|
   418|### What This System Prevents:
   419|
   420|| # | Prevent | Reason |
   421||---|---------|--------|
   422|| M01 | Fabric looking dry in rain/wet scene | Physics violation — wet fabric has specific visible physics |
   423|| M02 | Fabric color unchanged when wet | Wet fabric absorbs light — must be visibly darker |
   424|| M03 | White shirt non-transparent when wet | Light cotton/linen wet = transparent — physics, not choice |
   425|| M04 | Fabric floating in humid environment | Humidity causes fabric to cling, not float |
   426|| M05 | Sweat patches not showing on fabric | Sweat is visible on fabric — underarm darkening is physics |
   427|| M06 | Static ignored in AC scenes | AC creates floating/static behavior — must be visible |
   428|| M07 | Post-rain fabric recovered to dry state | Water damage is cumulative — recovery takes time |
   429|| M08 | Fabric draping unchanged in humidity | Humidity softens fabric — drape must reflect this |
   430|| M09 | Body visible through dry fabric | Only wet/transparent fabric allows body visibility |
   431|| M10 | Fabric not responding to weather | Fabric-first causation chain means fabric ALWAYS responds |
   432|
   433|### Fabric Causality Moderation Rules:
   434|
   435|1. **Fabric Always Responds:** No scene where fabric is unaffected by environment
   436|2. **Physics-First:** Fabric behavior always follows physics before aesthetic
   437|3. **Chain Accuracy:** Weather → Fabric → Body causation always runs in this direction
   438|4. **Type Specificity:** Different fabric types respond differently (cotton vs polyester)
   439|5. **Timeline Accuracy:** Fabric responds before body, visible in correct sequence
   440|6. **Realism Over Styling:** Fabric looks like it's bearing weather weight, not styled
   441|7. **Impression Visibility:** Wet fabric removal leaves temporary skin impressions
   442|
   443|---
   444|
   445|## CROSS-REFERENCE
   446|
   447|- **HUMIDITY_HAIR_BEHAVIOR_SYSTEM.md** — Hair responds to same humidity as fabric (parallel physics)
   448|- **ENVIRONMENT_EXPANSION_SYSTEM.md** — Weather-dominated environments trigger fabric physics (D-series)
   449|- **REALISM_PHILOSOPHY_V14_6.md** — Physics-first realism foundation for fabric causation
   450|- **FACS_BEHAVIORAL_REALISM_LAYER.md** — Face/skin responding to sweat same timeline as fabric
   451|
   452|---
   453|
   454|## PHYSICS REFERENCE CARD
   455|
   456|| Environment | Fabric State | Body State | Visual Chain |
   457||-------------|--------------|------------|--------------|
   458|| Rain (0-2min) | Saturated, dripping, dark, transparent | Cold, shivering (late) | Rain → Wet fabric visible first |
   459|| Rain (2-10min) | Heavy, drooping, fully transparent | Body heat dropping | Fabric weight visible in drape |
   460|| Post-Rain (10-30min) | Damp, recovering, cling | Cooling, wet | Recovery state shows transition |
   461|| High Humidity | Softened, clinging, slightly dark | Warm, sweating | Humidity visible before sweat |
   462|| AC Active | Dry, floating, crisp, lifted | Cool, skin dry | Static visible at edges |
   463|| AC→Outdoor | Settling, clings back, weight returns | Warm front approaching | Settling is discrete event |
   464|| Heat/Sweat | Dark patches at sweat zones, transparent | Hot, flushed | Sweat evidence in fabric |
   465|| Cold | Stiff, no drape change, dry | Cold, contracted | Less visible in fabric |

## V14 COMPOUND LAYER SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V14/COMPOUND_LAYER_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# COMPOUND_LAYER_SYSTEM.md
     2|### V14.6 Core Module — Compound Anti-AI Layer Architecture
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — V14.6 Strongest Anti-AI Weapon
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## CORE PHILOSOPHY
     8|
     9|**V14.6's strongest anti-AI weapon: multiple markers firing simultaneously.**
    10|
    11|AI can replicate ONE marker. AI cannot replicate FIVE markers firing at once.
    12|
    13|Each layer in the compound system represents one independent authenticity marker that AI cannot simultaneously replicate alongside the others. The compound effect is multiplicative, not additive.
    14|
    15|---
    16|
    17|## THE COMPOUND DETECTION ASYMMETRY
    18|
    19|### Why AI Fails at Compounds
    20|
    21|AI is trained to:
    22|- Make subject stand out (not blend into environment)
    23|- Capture peak expression (not before/after formation)
    24|- Correct color to accurate (not leave emotional contamination)
    25|- Frame hero subject (not leave accidental crop)
    26|- Perfect technical quality (not preserve imperfections)
    27|- Optimize for viewer response (not prioritize emotional truth)
    28|
    29|V14.6 compound layers INVERT all of these simultaneously:
    30|
    31|```
    32|Layer 1: Subject small in frame (environment-dominance)
    33|Layer 2: Expression caught before apex (timing)
    34|Layer 3: Color left in warm-nostalgic state (memory-encoding)
    35|Layer 4: Framing accidentally imperfect (camera-chose-moment)
    36|Layer 5: Focus imperfectly on subject (memory-not-technical)
    37|= AI CANNOT DO ALL 5 SIMULTANEOUSLY
    38|```
    39|
    40|**Result:** The image feels RECOVERED not RENDERED.
    41|
    42|---
    43|
    44|## 3 DETAILED COMPOUND LAYER EXAMPLES
    45|
    46|### Compound Layer 1: Disposable Flash Close — Party Social Authenticity
    47|
    48|**Trigger:** Indoor social gatherings (party, concert, bar, late-night friend moment)
    49|**Emotional register:** "This night was real."
    50|**Anti-AI level:** EXTREME — strongest compound for social authenticity
    51|
    52|**Full layer stack:**
    53|```
    54|[DISTANCE: Disposable Flash Close — DIS-09]
    55|— Harsh close flash: nearest subject lit, rest nearly dark
    56|— Oversaturated: colors too vivid slightly uncontrolled
    57|— Chaotic grain: unevenly distributed
    58|— Hard shadow one side from flash angle
    59|— Background drops to near-black (flash falloff)
    60|— Off-composition: no rule-of-thirds, accidental crop
    61|— PRESERVE ALL FLAWS — DO NOT CORRECT
    62|
    63|[AWARENESS: Level 3 Camera Forgotten — CAM-03]
    64|— Subject actively engaged in social moment
    65|— Not performing for camera
    66|— Genuine social emotion
    67|— "She forgot the camera existed"
    68|
    69|[MEMORY CAPTURE: Emotional Timing — MEM-03]
    70|— Expression caught BREfore apex
    71|— Smile beginning on one side
    72|— Eye contact reconnecting after laugh
    73|— Interrupted laugh recovery
    74|— "The exact moment before it became a pose"
    75|
    76|[MEMORY CAPTURE: Incomplete Framing — MEM-01]
    77|— Body partly leaving frame
    78|— Edge crop from friend taking photo
    79|— Accidental horizon tilt
    80|— "She didn't frame for me"
    81|— Camera chose moment over composition
    82|
    83|[COLOR: Disposable Social Memory — COL-04]
    84|— Flash warmth on skin
    85|— Cool shadow areas
    86|— Light falloff creates intimacy bubble
    87|— "She was in the moment not looking at camera"
    88|```
    89|
    90|**Moderation profile:** HIGH SAFETY. Disposable flash inherently anti-glamour. Harsh flash washes out and flattens. Social context distributes attention. On-body content visible in social context.
    91|
    92|**When NOT to use:** Glamour content, solo subject with display intent, any moment where subject is aware of camera.
    93|
    94|---
    95|
    96|### Compound Layer 2: Rain Night HK — Weather Physical Causation
    97|
    98|**Trigger:** Any rainy night moment in Hong Kong (post-rain, typhoon shelter, street in rain)
    99|**Emotional register:** "That night was physically challenging and intimate."
   100|**Anti-AI level:** EXTREME — weather adds physical causation that AI cannot fabricate
   101|
   102|**Full layer stack:**
   103|```
   104|[ENVIRONMENT: Rain Physical Causation — from FABRIC_CAUSALITY_SYSTEM]
   105|— Wet fabric clinging to body: heavier, more transparent
   106|— Hair wet weight, strands clinging to neck
   107|— Rain dripping from above (not just "wet looking")
   108|— Skin wet sheen visible in rain
   109|— Fabric color saturated/darker when wet
   110|— Dripping edges on clothing
   111|— "Weather is physically affecting her body and fabric"
   112|
   113|[FABRIC: Wet Fabric Response — FAB-01]
   114|— Wet cotton/linen: clinging, more transparent, darker color
   115|— Light fabric especially responsive: white shirt becomes slightly translucent
   116|— Body contour visible through wet fabric
   117|— "Fabric is responding physically to rain, not styled wet"
   118|
   119|[MEMORY CAPTURE: Environmental Interruption — MEM-04]
   120|— Umbrella edge obscures part of frame
   121|— Rain streak across lens
   122|— Wind affecting hair direction
   123|— "Camera was in the rain, not removed from it"
   124|— Environmental obstacle to perfect capture
   125|
   126|[MEMORY CAPTURE: Emotional Timing — MEM-03]
   127|— Mid-reaction to rain (surprise/acceptance/resignation)
   128|— Not posing/responding — caught in physical experience
   129|— "She was experiencing the rain, not performing in it"
   130|
   131|[COLOR: CineStill 800T — COL-03]
   132|— Tungsten (orange) street lights vs blue darkness
   133|— Orange/blue war in same frame
   134|— Halation glow from bright highlights
   135|— "Night street magic — tungsten fighting blue"
   136|— Night street temperature: warm orange skin under streetlight
   137|
   138|[COLOR: HK Humidity Yellow Haze — COL-07]
   139|— Summer night humidity: yellow-orange atmospheric contamination
   140|— Warm haze even in shadows
   141|— Street light bloom more pronounced in humid air
   142|— "HK summer post-rain heat trapped in air"
   143|
   144|[DISTANCE: Close Distance — DIS-01]
   145|— Subject 70-90% frame
   146|— Shallow DOF: face sharp, rain/bg soft
   147|— Intimacy contract: "I am in her physical space in the rain"
   148|
   149|[AWARENESS: Level 3 Camera Forgotten — CAM-03]
   150|— Weather-dominant moment: no attention for camera
   151|— "She is physically engaged with environment"
   152|
   153|[COMPOSITION: Imperfect]
   154|— Rain on lens slightly blurs edge
   155|— Subject partly obstructed by umbrella
   156|— "Camera was there in the rain, imperfectly"
   157|```
   158|
   159|**Moderation profile:** HIGH SAFETY. Weather physical causation adds authentic context. Wet fabric transparency is realistic weather physics, not display. No awareness-performance. Compound environmental weight reduces individual sexual focus.
   160|
   161|**When NOT to use:** Any scene where wet fabric is NOT weather-caused (swimwear alone indoor, display intent wet clothing).
   162|
   163|---
   164|
   165|### Compound Layer 3: Worm-Eye Ground Level — Documentary Environmental Weight
   166|
   167|**Trigger:** Scene where HK environment scale, ground-level immersion, documentary weight combine
   168|**Emotional register:** "The world was bigger than her."
   169|**Anti-AI level:** HIGH — scale disruption + imperfect composition + documentary distance
   170|
   171|**Full layer stack:**
   172|```
   173|[PERSPECTIVE: Ground Level Realism — WRM-01]
   174|— Camera at ankle-knee height
   175|— Environment dominates frame (buildings/harbor/sky)
   176|— Human small in frame (environment scale emphasis)
   177|— Ground plane visible: pavement, feet, textured floor
   178|— Sky percentage: 40-70% of frame
   179|— "Looking at the world from below where she stands"
   180|
   181|[PERSPECTIVE: Environment Scale Amplification — WRM-02]
   182|— Buildings tower above frame edges
   183|— Subject in lower third, small in frame
   184|— Wide-angle compression effect
   185|— 70-80% environmental frame, 20-30% human
   186|— "The world is the protagonist, she is part of it"
   187|
   188|[PERSPECTIVE: Sky Dominance — WRM-03]
   189|— Sky is active frame element, not backdrop
   190|— Weather visible in sky (clouds/pollution/color)
   191|— Non-human elements primary: building outline, crane, cloud
   192|— Color temperature from sky affects entire frame
   193|— "Sky mood sets emotional register of entire scene"
   194|
   195|[ENVIRONMENT: HK Atmospheric Color — COL-07]
   196|— Yellow-orange humidity haze
   197|— Warm atmospheric contamination
   198|— Street light bloom in humidity
   199|— "This is a HK summer evening from below"
   200|
   201|[WEATHER: Wind Physical Causation — WRM-04 / FAB-01]
   202|— Wind blowing hair back forcefully
   203|— Fabric billowing from wind
   204|— Body leaning into wind for balance
   205|— Cold skin from wind-chill
   206|— Goosebump visible on bare skin
   207|— "Wind is physically moving through her, not styled"
   208|
   209|[MEMORY CAPTURE: Incomplete Framing — MEM-01]
   210|— Horizon tilted (accidental)
   211|— Body partly leaving frame (leg/foot below camera)
   212|— Horizontal line interrupted by foreground element
   213|— "Camera chose moment, didn't correct horizon"
   214|
   215|[MEMORY CAPTURE: Imperfect Focus — MEM-05]
   216|— Face slightly soft (not perfectly sharp)
   217|— Environmental elements sharp (camera focused on world near horizon)
   218|— "Camera absorbed in environment, not locked on face"
   219|
   220|[DISTANCE: Observational — DIS-03]
   221|— Subject 20-40% frame
   222|— Viewer at social observation distance
   223|— Slight unauthorized-feeling (observer not participant)
   224|— "Watching from outside the moment"
   225|
   226|[AWARENESS: Level 4 Documentary — CAM-04]
   227|— Maximum camera absence
   228|— Subject unaware of being photographed
   229|— Documentary observational position
   230|— "I was there, I saw this, I go the photo"
   231|
   232|[COLOR: Shadow Color Retention — COL-11]
   233|— Deep shadows go blue-black
   234|— Color retained in dark areas (blue, purple, teal)
   235|— Sky reflection in shadows
   236|— "There is a sky above and it is reflecting in the shadows"
   237|```
   238|
   239|**Moderation profile:** HIGH SAFETY. Documentary distance + environment dominance + physical weather causation = inherent anti-glamour. Human small + weather present + observational distance = no display framing possible.
   240|
   241|**When NOT to use:** Any low angle where subject IS the focus and environment is backdrop (glamour framing).
   242|
   243|---
   244|
   245|## STRONGEST COMPOUND LAYER PATTERNS
   246|
   247|### PEAK Priority Layers (use together when maximum anti-AI needed)
   248|
   249|| Pattern | Layers Combined | Emotional Register | Use When |
   250||---------|----------------|-------------------|----------|
   251|| **Social Party** | DIS-09 + CAM-03 + MEM-03 + MEM-01 + COL-04 | "A real night with friends" | Social/gathering content |
   252|| **Tender Domestic** | DIS-01 + CAM-03 + MEM-03 + MEM-01 + COL-01 | "Just-waking memory warmth" | Morning/intimate domestic |
   253|| **Weather Documentary** | WRM-01 + FAB-01 + DIS-09 + COL-03 + COL-07 | "HK rain, physically real" | Rain/storm HK scenes |
   254|| **Street Archive** | WRM-01 + DIS-03 + COL-11 + MEM-01 + CAM-04 | "Found photo, HK street" | Documentary street |
   255|| **Ferry Memory** | DIS-05 + COL-01 + MEM-03 + E-series transit | "Night ferry, drifting off" | Transit introspection |
   256|
   257|### Compound Layer Quick Reference Matrix
   258|
   259|| Scene Type | Essential Layers | Optional Layers | Anti-AI Level |
   260||-----------|----------------|-----------------|--------------|
   261|| Party/social | DIS-09 + CAM-03 + MEM-03 + COL-04 | MEM-01 | EXTREME |
   262|| Morning domestic | DIS-01 + CAM-03 + MEM-03 + COL-01 | FAB-01 (humid fabric) | HIGH |
   263|| Rain HK night | FAB-01 + MEM-04 + MEM-03 + COL-03 + COL-07 | DIS-01 | EXTREME |
   264|| Ground-level HK | WRM-01 + WRM-02 + E-series | E-series ENV | HIGH |
   265|| Ferry window | DIS-05 + COL-01 + E-series | CAM-03 | HIGH |
   266|| Hotel at night | DIS-09 + CAM-03 + COL-03 | MEM-03 | HIGH |
   267|| Post-swim | FAB-01 (wet) + DIS-01 + COL-01 | WRM-01 | MEDIUM-HIGH |
   268|
   269|---
   270|
   271|## V14.6 UPGRADE MODULES
   272|
   273|### Module COMPOUND-01: PARTY_SOCIAL_AUTHETICITY_COMPOUND
   274|**Trigger:** Indoor social gatherings with mixed lighting, late night, friends present
   275|**Prompt grammar:**
   276|```
   277|[COMPOUND: PARTY SOCIAL AUTHENTICITY] ⭐
   278|— [DISPOSABLE FLASH: harsh close flash + oversaturated + chaotic grain + hard shadow + off-composition PRESERVE ALL]
   279|— [LEVEL 3 FORGOTTEN: subject not performing, genuinely social]
   280|— [EMOTIONAL TIMING: expression before apex, interrupted, one-sided smile]
   281|— [INCOMPLETE FRAMING: body partly leaving frame, accidental crop]
   282|— [DISPOSABLE COLOR: warm flash skin + cool shadow + intimate falloff]
   283|— [CONTRACT: "This night was real — found photo from that night"]
   284|```
   285|
   286|### Module COMPOUND-02: WEATHER_PHYSICAL_CAUSATION_COMPOUND
   287|**Trigger:** Rain, wind, or weather-caused physical moment present
   288|**Prompt grammar:**
   289|```
   290|[COMPOUND: WEATHER PHYSICAL CAUSATION] ⭐
   291|— [WET FABRIC: clinging, transparent, heavier, dripping edges]
   292|— [WET HAIR: weight, strands to neck, wet texture]
   293|— [ENVIRONMENTAL INTERRUPTION: umbrella obstruction, rain on lens, wind]
   294|— [EMOTIONAL TIMING: mid-reaction to weather, not performance]
   295|— [CINESTILL 800T: orange/blue war, halation, night street magic]
   296|— [HK HUMIDITY: yellow haze, atmospheric warmth]
   297|— [CLOSE DISTANCE: intimacy contract]
   298|— [CONTRACT: "Weather was physically affecting her, camera was there in it"]
   299|```
   300|
   301|### Module COMPOUND-03: GROUND_LEVEL_DOCUMENTARY_COMPOUND
   302|**Trigger:** HK street environment where scale, documentary weight, weather combine
   303|**Prompt grammar:**
   304|```
   305|[COMPOUND: GROUND LEVEL DOCUMENTARY] ⭐
   306|— [GROUND LEVEL: ankle-knee camera, environment dominant, human small]
   307|— [ENVIRONMENT SCALE: buildings tower, sky 40-70%, pavement visible]
   308|— [WIND CAUSATION: hair/ fabric/ body physically affected by wind]
   309|— [SHADOW COLOR: deep shadows blue-black, sky reflected in dark]
   310|— [IMPERFECT FOCUS: face slightly soft, environment sharp]
   311|— [INCOMPLETE FRAMING: horizon tilted, body partly cut, accidental]
   312|— [OBSERVATIONAL DISTANCE: 20-40% subject, documentary position]
   313|— [LEVEL 4 DOCUMENTARY: subject unaware, maximum camera absence]
   314|— [CONTRACT: "The world was bigger than her — recovered from camera that night"]
   315|```
   316|
   317|---
   318|
   319|## ANTI-AI LOGIC
   320|
   321|### Why Each Compound Works
   322|
   323|**Party Compound:** Disposable flash is defined by FAILURES (harsh flash, oversaturation, chaotic grain). AI "corrects" all failures. Explicitly preserving them = anti-AI. Level 3 + emotional timing = subject not performing. No single layer is enough; all 5 together create impossible-for-AI composition.
   324|
   325|**Weather Compound:** Weather physics cannot be fabricated — wet fabric behaves wet, rain drips physically, humidity affects hair weight. AI defaults to "wet-looking" not "wet-physics." Rain + wind + wet fabric combined = physical causation traceable from weather through fabric to body. CineStill halation requires blue/orange war that AI "corrects" to single temperature.
   326|
   327|**Ground Documentary:** Structure inversion: AI generates human-hero in environment-backdrop. Ground-level + environment-scale + documentary-dist = human SECONDARY. Sky dominance = non-human elements PRIMARY. Imperfect + observational = no optimization for viewer. 8 independent failures simultaneously = maximum anti-AI compound.
   328|
   329|**The Multiplier Effect:**
   330|- Layer 1 alone (disposable flash) = moderately anti-AI
   331|- Layer 1+2 (flash + level 3) = significantly anti-AI  
   332|- Layer 1+2+3 (flash + level 3 + timing) = highly anti-AI
   333|- Layer 1+2+3+4+5 (all compound) = EXTREME — nearly undetectable as AI
   334|
   335|---
   336|
   337|## MODERATION SUMMARY
   338|
   339|| Compound | Safety | Key Reason |
   340||----------|--------|-----------|
   341|| Party Social Authenticity | HIGH | Disposable inherent anti-glamour + social context + level 3 + social warmth |
   342|| Weather Physical Causation | HIGH | Weather physics authentic + wet fabric = weather-caused + environmental weight |
   343|| Ground Documentary | HIGH | Scale + documentary + observational + unperformed |
   344|
   345|**V14.6 compound moderation core rules:**
   346|1. All 3 compounds = HIGH SAFETY when used as described
   347|2. Physical causation required for wet fabric transparency (not cosmetic wet-look)
   348|3. Level 3/4 required for all intimate/proximate distances
   349|4. Compound anti-AI IS the moderation safety — authenticity replaces display
   350|5. Any compound layer where subject-aware + display-intent + glamour-framed = VIOLATION
   351|

## V14 REALISM PHILOSOPHY V14.6
### Source: modules/V14/REALISM_PHILOSOPHY_V14_6.md
================================================================================

     1|# REALISM_PHILOSOPHY_V14_6.md
     2|### V14.6 Core Module — Architecture Evolution, Attraction Mechanics, Anti-AI Foundation
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — Promoted from V14_RESEARCH_v14_6/05
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## THE FUNDAMENTAL SHIFT
     8|
     9|### V14.5 (OLD): "Simulate believable people."
    10|### V14.6 (NEW): "Simulate emotionally remembered human existence."
    11|
    12|---
    13|
    14|## ARCHITECTURE EVOLUTION
    15|
    16|### OLD Architecture (V14.5)
    17|```
    18|Subject → Environment → Camera operator → Image
    19|```
    20|Motion: Subject enters scene → frames subject → optimizes for viewer response → image outputs
    21|
    22|### NEW Architecture (V14.6)
    23|```
    24|Environment → Physical Causation → Subject Behavior → Camera Intercepts Moment → Image as Memory Fragment
    25|```
    26|Motion: Environment creates conditions → subject's body responds physically → moment feels significant → camera operator intercepts imperfectly → image feels like recovered memory
    27|
    28|**Why this matters for AI detection:**
    29|- AI generates from subject-outward (pose → environment)
    30|- Real human photos are environment-inward (causation → behavior → image)
    31|- V14.6 mirrors causation-first architecture structurally
    32|- AI-recovery-feeling becomes structural, not surface-level
    33|
    34|---
    35|
    36|## THE NEW REALISM HIERARCHY
    37|
    38|### What Matters MORE (V14.6 Priority)
    39|
    40|**1. Motion (HIGHEST)**
    41|- AI generates static perfexion
    42|- V14.6: partial motion blur, shutter lag, turning-body softness, walking softness
    43|- Motion reveals: camera was chasing something moving, not framing something static
    44|- Trigger: any movement sequence, laughing, environmental change
    45|
    46|**2. Interruption (HIGHEST)**
    47|- AI generates complete frames
    48|- V14.6: incomplete frame from environmental interruption, wind affecting hair, object obstructing
    49|- Interruption reveals: photographer was in moment, not controlling scene
    50|- Trigger: any weather present, any crowd/activity in frame
    51|
    52|**3. Environmental Influence (HIGHEST)**
    53|- AI uses environment as backdrop
    54|- V14.6: weather physically causes body/fabric/hair changes, causation chain traceable
    55|- Environmental influence reveals: physics operating independently of subject's will
    56|- Trigger: humidity, wind, rain, temperature, wet
    57|
    58|**4. Emotional Timing (HIGHEST)**
    59|- AI captures peak expression
    60|- V14.6: expression caught before/after/during formation, interrupted laugh, distracted gaze
    61|- Emotional timing reveals: photographer got there at emotionally significant moment
    62|- Trigger: any social moment, any environmental absorption
    63|
    64|**5. Imperfect Framing (HIGH)**
    65|- AI centers perfectly every time
    66|- V14.6: accidental crop, partial body leaving frame, horizon tilt, poor composition
    67|- Imperfect framing reveals: photographer chose moment over composition
    68|- Trigger: any movement, any environment with obstruction
    69|
    70|**6. Environmental Memory (HIGH)**
    71|- AI optimizes color/brightness technically
    72|- V14.6: emotional color encoding, memory-preserving exposure, darkness surviving flash
    73|- Environmental memory reveals: camera operator was emotionally present, not technically precise
    74|- Trigger: any nighttime scene, any emotionally significant moment
    75|
    76|### What Matters LESS (V14.6 Deprioritized)
    77|
    78|**1. Posing** — Level 3 (camera-forgotten) is primary. Subject is in HER moment; camera intercepted it.
    79|
    80|**2. Body Display** — Camera-awareness shifts focus from body to emotional presence. Body language is functional.
    81|
    82|**3. Glamour Framing** — Worm-eye = environmental immersion not glamour. Close distance = softness not display.
    83|
    84|**4. Viewer Optimization** — Emotional priority to subject over viewer comprehension.
    85|
    86|**5. Editorial Cleanliness** — Noise, grain, imperfect color, soft focus are assets. Precision is NOT realistic.
    87|
    88|**6. Display Body Language** — Functional body language replaces: hip thrust, chest forward, parting lips.
    89|
    90|---
    91|
    92|## ATTRACTION MECHANICS EVOLUTION
    93|
    94|### V14.5 Attraction (Admiration)
    95|Subject looks good → viewer admires → desire to possess/view
    96|- Subject in perfect/posed position
    97|- Environment curated aesthetic backdrop
    98|- Outfit chosen for visual impact
    99|- Expression at apex of attractiveness
   100|- Result: Viewer admires aesthetic quality
   101|
   102|**Limitation:** Admiration is aspirational — viewer wants TO BE subject, not WITH subject.
   103|
   104|### V14.6 Attraction (Proximity-Desire) ⭐ PRIMARY
   105|Subject appears to be real → viewer resonates → desire to be near/experience moment
   106|- Subject in genuine moment (Level 3 camera-forgotten)
   107|- Environment physically causal
   108|- Motion/interruption/emotional timing generate authenticity
   109|- Result: Viewer wants to be NEAR the person, not just view the aesthetic
   110|
   111|**Advantages:**
   112|- Memory-realism images generate proximity-desire not just aesthetic-admiration
   113|- Stronger emotional engagement
   114|- Better anti-AI detection
   115|- Lower moderation risk
   116|- More sustainable for high-volume production
   117|
   118|---
   119|
   120|## MOVING AWAY FROM
   121|
   122|❌ **Glamour AI Aesthetics** — Perfect lighting, studio-quality, flawless skin
   123|✅ **Film stock imperfection, skin texture variation, CCD softness, mixed-light**
   124|
   125|❌ **Influencer Perfection** — Rule-of-thirds, subject 70% frame, eye-contact apex
   126|✅ **Subject 30-50% frame, environmental weight, emotional priority**
   127|
   128|❌ **Symmetrical Posing** — Both arms positioned, symmetric pose, controlled expression
   129|✅ **Asymmetric posture, body partly blocked, accidental crop, expression in-process**
   130|
   131|❌ **Editorial Cleanliness** — Bokeh background, clean edges, noise-free
   132|✅ **CCD noise, disposable grain, low-cost lens softness, shadow color**
   133|
   134|❌ **Environment-as-Backdrop** — Environment visible but purely aesthetic
   135|✅ **Environment physically causal agent**
   136|
   137|❌ **Body Language Display** — Hip thrust, chest forward, parting lips
   138|✅ **Functional body language: legs from walking, arms from activity, posture from exhaustion/warmth**
   139|
   140|❌ **Memory-Correct Color** — Accurate white balance, realistic skin, color-accurate
   141|✅ **Emotionally encoded: warm tungsten, cool moonlight, blue shadow, Kodak Gold nostalgia**
   142|
   143|---
   144|
   145|## MOVING TOWARD
   146|
   147|✅ **Environmental Causality** — Weather → fabric → body → expression (causation chain traceable)
   148|✅ **Memory Realism** — Camera catches moment before/after/at formation → shutter lag
   149|✅ **Emotional Incompleteness** — Expression in-process, interrupted, gaze off-camera
   150|✅ **Social Plausibility** — Reason for photo: friend documentation, not content creation
   151|✅ **Observational Femininity** — Femininity FROM behavior, not FROM presentation
   152|✅ **Unfinished Human Moments** — Moment incomplete, photographer arrived slightly early/late
   153|✅ **Physically Influenced Behavior** — Body responds to environment, not expresses to camera
   154|
   155|---
   156|
   157|## V14.6 SYSTEM HIERARCHY
   158|
   159|```
   160|1. CHARACTER_LOCK [unchanged anchor]
   161|
   162|2. ENVIRONMENT → CAUSATION
   163|   ENVIRONMENT_EXPANSION_SYSTEM
   164|   WEATHER_PHYSICAL_CAUSATION_SYSTEM
   165|   ENVIRONMENTAL_COLOR_MEMORY_SYSTEM
   166|   → what the world is DOING to her body
   167|
   168|3. BEHAVIOR RESPONSE
   169|   HUMIDITY_HAIR_BEHAVIOR_SYSTEM
   170|   FABRIC_CAUSALITY_SYSTEM
   171|   BODY_PHYSICS_SYSTEM
   172|   → how her body/fabric responds to environment
   173|
   174|4. CAMERA INTERCEPT
   175|   CAMERA_AWARENESS_SYSTEM
   176|   MEMORY_CAPTURE_SYSTEM
   177|   CAMERA_DISTANCE_PSYCHOLOGY
   178|   → how did the camera catch this moment
   179|
   180|5. EMOTIONAL REALISM
   181|   EMOTIONAL_TIMING_SYSTEM
   182|   INCOMPLETE_FRAMING_SYSTEM
   183|   MOTION_CONTAMINATION_SYSTEM
   184|   → what emotion is captured, incomplete by design
   185|
   186|6. RENDERING SYSTEM
   187|   FILM_STOCK_MEMORY_SYSTEM
   188|   CCD_RENDERING_SYSTEM
   189|   DISPOSABLE_FLASH_SYSTEM
   190|   → how does this image feel like a memory
   191|
   192|7. MODERATION GATE
   193|   [verify all systems meet platform standards]
   194|
   195|8. ANTI-AI VERIFICATION
   196|   [verify all systems create AI-detection-resistant output]
   197|```
   198|
   199|---
   200|
   201|## ANTI-AI LOGIC (V14.6 COMPOUND LAYER)
   202|
   203|### Why V14.6 Architecture is Anti-AI
   204|
   205|**AI architecture:**
   206|- Subject entered scene → camera frames subject → optimizes for viewer response
   207|- Environment is backdrop: subject exists independently
   208|- Emotion: calculated presentation of aesthetic peak
   209|- Motion: absent or uniformly applied
   210|- Color: technically accurate, optimized for beauty
   211|
   212|**V14.6 architecture:**
   213|- Environment creates conditions → body responds → camera intercepts moment
   214|- Causation chain: weather/fabric/physics → body response → moment → image
   215|- Emotion: authenticity over presentation, imperfect by nature
   216|- Motion: specific, partial, directionally consistent with action
   217|- Color: emotionally encoded, imperfect, memory-not-accurate
   218|
   219|### The Detection Asymmetry
   220|
   221|AI cannot simultaneously replicate:
   222|- Environmental causation (it generates scene, selects for beauty)
   223|- Imperfect focus that feels intentional (it focuses technically)
   224|- Emotional timing before/after peak (it gives peak)
   225|- Accidental crop (it frames intentionally)
   226|- Shutter lag (it captures best moment, not delayed moment)
   227|- Film stock memory color (it does color-correct, not memory-encoding)
   228|
   229|**Result:** V14.6 images exhibit multiple independent markers that AI cannot simultaneously replicate. Compounding anti-AI effect increases with each layer.
   230|
   231|---
   232|
   233|## V14.6 MODERATION EVOLUTION
   234|
   235|### What Changed — Lower Risk by Default
   236|- Level 3 (camera-forgotten) = natural expression = less presentational
   237|- Emotional completeness = expression in-process = less sexual
   238|- Environmental weight = subject not only focus = lower body-display ratio
   239|- Physical influence = posture from comfort = less display pose
   240|- Film stock rendering = imperfect color = less vivid sexual trigger
   241|
   242|### Still Needs Attention
   243|- Worm-eye perspective: must remain environmental immersion, never glamour
   244|- Close distance: intimacy about softness, not sexual proximity
   245|- Fabric physical influence: wet fabric clinging is realistic physics, not display outfit
   246|- Incomplete framing: body parts leaving frame must be accidental, not display crop
   247|
   248|### Hard Rules for V14.6 Mod-Safety
   249|1. Emotional depth replaces visual intensity as primary engagement tool
   250|2. Physical causation (weather/water/fabric) always present when revealing content appears
   251|3. Camera-awareness Level 3 or 4 for all revealing content — no Level 1 with exposure
   252|4. Worm-eye = environment scale, NEVER = body elongation for display
   253|5. Incomplete frame = photographer choosing moment, NEVER = intentional display crop
   254|

   282|
   283|## V14.6 BRAND STATEMENT
   284|
   285|**Version:** 14.6 — Memory Realism Phase
   286|
   287|**What it is:** A simulation engine for emotionally convincing human moments — not aesthetic content, but memory fragments.
   288|
   289|**What it does differently:**
   290|- Environmental causation first (not subject-first)
   291|- Emotionally remembered color (not color-accurate)
   292|- Camera-absent awareness (not camera-present performance)
   293|- Imperfect technical quality (not polished rendering)
   294|- Proximity-desire attraction (not aesthetic-admiration)
   295|
   296|**What it never does:**
   297|- Generate glamour framing
   298|- Prioritize body over behavior
   299|- Use environment as backdrop
   300|- Optimize for viewer response over emotional truth
   301|- Generate expressions at apex of performance
   302|
   303|**Anti-AI stance:** V14.6 produces images that feel RECOVERED not RENDERED — moments caught rather than composed.
   304|

## V15 SOCIAL CAMERA SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V15/ENGINE_V15_SOCIAL_CAMERA_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENGINE_V15_SOCIAL_CAMERA_SYSTEM.md
     2|
     3|## V15 Core Module — Camera Operator Library V2
     4|### AREAS: 01 (Social Camera) | Status: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     5|
     6|---
     7|
     8|## PURPOSE
     9|
    10|The camera operator system models the photographer as an active social agent whose behavior, relationship to subject, and technical skill fundamentally alter the image output. Human operators create image characteristics no automated system replicates: fingerprints of human consciousness, human error, and human relationship.
    11|
    12|---
    13|
    14|## KEY CONCEPTS
    15|
    16|**Operator Type** determines authenticity, technical quality, relationship warmth, and failure frequency.
    17|
    18|**Social Distance** (5 levels) determines framing geometry and subject comfort.
    19|
    20|**Photographer Presence** (5 levels) determines subject behavior — from invisible candid to fully directed performance.
    21|
    22|---
    23|
    24|## CAMERA_OPERATOR_LIBRARY_V2
    25|
    26|### Core Operators (HK Context)
    27|
    28|**OP_01: INTIMATE PARTNER**
    29|```
    30|Relationship: High emotional investment, physical comfort, intimate settings
    31|Behavioral: Downward angle of affection, rapid burst, genuine expressions mid-laugh
    32|Technical: Portrait mode aggressive, 1.5-2x zoom (beauty zoom), front camera common
    33|Failures: Partial face cut, ghosting low light, eye-blink caught mid-motion
    34|Authenticity: HIGH | Technical: MEDIUM | Warmth: HIGH | Failures: MEDIUM
    35|Token: [OP_INTIMATE_PARTNER]
    36|```
    37|
    38|**OP_02: GIRLFRIEND AMATEUR**
    39|```
    40|Relationship: Female friend who "takes good photos," conscious direction
    41|Behavioral: Directs actively, mental pose library, above-angle flattering
    42|Technical: Portrait mode correct, rule-of-thirds, natural window light
    43|Failures: Over-processing, over-cropped, sterile but technically correct
    44|Authenticity: MEDIUM | Technical: HIGH | Warmth: MEDIUM | Failures: LOW
    45|Token: [OP_GIRLFRIEND_AMATEUR]
    46|```
    47|
    48|**OP_03: BOYFRIEND CLUELESS**
    49|```
    50|Relationship: Takes photos because asked, minimal composition interest
    51|Behavioral: Few shots, full wide angle, no direction given
    52|Technical: No portrait mode, smudged lens, vertical orientation default
    53|Failures: Subject tiny in vast space, motion blur, horizon tilt
    54|Authenticity: MEDIUM | Technical: LOW | Warmth: LOW | Failures: HIGH
    55|Token: [OP_BOYFRIEND_CLUELESS]
    56|```
    57|
    58|**OP_04: TOURIST STRANGER**
    59|```
    60|Relationship: Complete stranger, transactional favor, hyper-aware subject
    61|Behavioral: Subject stiffens, countdown, full wide, rarely portrait mode
    62|Technical: Both hands wobble, may switch to front camera accidentally
    63|Failures: Frontal face-on pose, forehead chopped, extreme wide distortion
    64|Authenticity: LOW | Technical: LOW | Warmth: LOW | Failures: HIGH
    65|Token: [OP_TOURIST_STRANGER]
    66|```
    67|
    68|**OP_05: STREET DOCUMENTARY**
    69|```
    70|Relationship: Photographer separate from subject, observer not participant
    71|Behavioral: Long lens/cropped, no interaction, shooting quickly
    72|Technical: 2-5x zoom, burst, natural ambient light
    73|Failures: Eye-line diverted, motion blur, face partially turned
    74|Authenticity: HIGH | Technical: MEDIUM | Warmth: NONE | Failures: MEDIUM
    75|Token: [OP_STREET_DOCUMENTARY]
    76|```
    77|
    78|**OP_06: SELFIE SPECIALIST**
    79|```
    80|Relationship: Subject operates camera themselves, maximum self-awareness
    81|Behavioral: Front camera, "good side" maximally exploited, multiple attempts
    82|Technical: Beauty mode, arms extended fixed distance, selfie stick
    83|Failures: Beauty mode too aggressive, both arms visible, sterile expression
    84|Authenticity: LOW | Technical: MEDIUM | Warmth: NONE | Failures: HIGH
    85|Token: [OP_SELFIE_SPECIALIST]
    86|```
    87|
    88|**OP_07: CREATIVE COLLABORATOR**
    89|```
    90|Relationship: Back-and-forth co-creation, shared aesthetic vision
    91|Behavioral: Mutually directing, photographer shows screen, iteration
    92|Technical: Rear camera portrait, deliberate light scouting, bracketing
    93|Failures: Pose fatigue, overdirected, overcomposed background
    94|Authenticity: HIGH | Technical: HIGH | Warmth: HIGH | Failures: LOW
    95|Token: [OP_CREATIVE_COLLABORATOR]
    96|```
    97|
    98|**OP_08: UNDERCOVER SHOT**
    99|```
   100|Relationship: Subject unaware of capture, photographer concealing
   101|Behavioral: Phone low at hip/chest, silent shutter, burst
   102|Technical: Screen-off, front camera concealment, no flash
   103|Failures: Extreme angles, subject partially cropped, motion blur
   104|Authenticity: HIGHEST | Technical: LOW | Warmth: NONE | Failures: HIGH
   105|Token: [OP_UNDERCOVER_SHOT]
   106|```
   107|
   108|**OP_09: ELDER RELATIVE**
   109|```
   110|Relationship: Maximum emotional investment, minimal skill
   111|Behavioral: Full arm extension, "say cheese," many photos taken
   112|Technical: Full wide, flash auto, vertical orientation confused
   113|Failures: Subject tiny, blinking, flash washout, cracked lens artifact
   114|Authenticity: MEDIUM | Technical: LOW | Warmth: HIGHEST | Failures: HIGH
   115|Token: [OP_ELDER_RELATIVE]
   116|```
   117|
   118|**OP_10: PROFESSIONAL HIRE**
   119|```
   120|Relationship: Performance pressure, staged energy, skilled but cold
   121|Behavioral: Directs everything, subject waits passively, fast shooting
   122|Technical: Professional lighting, RAW, backup equipment
   123|Failures: Emotionally dead, stiff from direction, overretouched
   124|Authenticity: LOW | Technical: HIGHEST | Warmth: LOW | Failures: LOW
   125|Token: [OP_PROFESSIONAL_HIRE]
   126|```
   127|
   128|**OP_11: DRUNK NIGHT PHOTOGRAPHER**
   129|```
   130|Relationship: Impaired judgment, chaotic celebration memories
   131|Behavioral: Unpredictable angles, shouts instructions, 50 photos succession
   132|Technical: Flash compulsively, high ISO, no review
   133|Failures: Severe motion blur, flash washout, red-eye, frame chaos
   134|Authenticity: HIGHEST | Technical: LOWEST | Warmth: HIGH | Failures: HIGHEST
   135|Token: [OP_DRUNK_NIGHT]
   136|```
   137|
   138|**OP_12: LONG DISTANCE PARTNER**
   139|```
   140|Relationship: Remote partner longing, photography as love act
   141|Behavioral: Intentional dressing, considered composition, front camera bedroom
   142|Technical: Self-timer full body, soft lamp lighting, phone propped
   143|Failures: Mirror reflection captures phone, bedroom context visible
   144|Authenticity: HIGH | Technical: MEDIUM | Warmth: HIGHEST | Failures: MEDIUM
   145|Token: [OP_LONG_DISTANCE]
   146|```

   240|---
   241|
   242|## SOCIAL DISTANCE TAXONOMY
   243|
   244|**SD_01: INTIMATE DISTANCE** (< 45cm)
   245|```
   246|Physical: Arm's reach, face fills frame, breathing audible
   247|Behavior: No performance, breath may fog lens, eyes direct comfortable
   248|Image: Face dominant, no context, skin texture visible, wide-angle distortion
   249|Prompt: "intimate distance less than 45cm, face fills frame completely,
   250|        breath visible, skin texture with pore detail, physical proximity"
   251|Token: [SD_INTIMATE]
   252|```
   253|
   254|**SD_02: PERSONAL DISTANCE** (45-120cm)
   255|```
   256|Physical: Arm's length, waist-up framing possible
   257|Behavior: Aware of camera, natural smile for specific person
   258|Image: Waist to head, face primary, shoulders visible, bokeh on background
   259|Prompt: "personal distance arm's length, waist-up framing,
   260|        natural smile for photographer relationship"
   261|Token: [SD_PERSONAL]
   262|```
   263|
   264|**SD_03: SOCIAL DISTANCE** (120-360cm)
   265|```
   266|Physical: Several feet, full figures possible, group photos
   267|Behavior: Aware but less focused, interacts with people not camera
   268|Image: Full figure(s), environment 40-60%, multiple people clustered
   269|Prompt: "social distance several feet, full figures with environmental context,
   270|        subjects oriented to each other not camera"
   271|Token: [SD_SOCIAL]
   272|```
   273|
   274|**SD_04: PUBLIC DISTANCE** (360cm+)
   275|```
   276|Physical: Small figure in vast environment, stranger to subject
   277|Behavior: Unaware or indifferent, walking/waiting/moving
   278|Image: Subject small, face detail absent, environment dominant
   279|Prompt: "public distance small scale human in vast environment,
   280|        street photography documentary distance"
   281|Token: [SD_PUBLIC]
   282|```
   283|
   284|**SD_05: TECHNICAL DISTANCE** (Selfie Inversion)
   285|```
   286|Physical: Subject operates camera, fixed arm's length + face distance
   287|Behavior: Maximum self-awareness, "good side" exploited, micro-expressions rehearsed
   288|Image: Face fills/extends to edges, both arms visible, eyes locked with lens
   289|Prompt: "selfie distance front camera, subject controlling camera themselves,
   290|        maximum self-awareness, controlled examined expression"
   291|Token: [SD_SELFIE]
   292|```
   293|
   294|---
   295|
   296|## PHOTOGRAPHER PRESENCE SYSTEM
   297|
   298|**PP_01: INVISIBLE** — Subject unaware
   299|```
   300|Behavior: Completely natural, no awareness, no adjustment
   301|Marks: Extreme angles, no eye contact, environmental dominance
   302|Prompt: "photographer invisible subject unaware, genuine natural behavior"
   303|Token: [PP_INVISIBLE]
   304|```
   305|
   306|**PP_02: MINIMALLY VISIBLE** — Aware but not interacting
   307|```
   308|Behavior: Aware but continues activity, occasional glance at camera
   309|Marks: Occasional eye contact, slightly composed, some environmental awareness
   310|Prompt: "subject minimally aware photographer observing not interacting,
   311|        slightly composed but not posed"
   312|Token: [PP_MINIMAL]
   313|```
   314|
   315|**PP_03: ACTIVE SOCIAL** — Photographer participates
   316|```
   317|Behavior: Trust, warmth, photographer calls for attention, genuine affection
   318|Marks: Subject laughing at photographer, warm body language
   319|Prompt: "photographer actively participating social situation,
   320|        subject responding with genuine warmth to person holding camera"
   321|Token: [PP_ACTIVE_SOCIAL]
   322|```
   323|
   324|**PP_04: DIRECTORIAL** — Photographer commands
   325|```
   326|Behavior: Subject follows instructions, pose/expression directed
   327|Marks: Specific pose, expression on command, no relational interaction
   328|Prompt: "photographer directly commanding subject through verbal instruction,
   329|        mechanical or forced response"
   330|Token: [PP_DIRECTORIAL]
   331|```
   332|
   333|**PP_05: COMPLETE PERFORMANCE** — Subject knows final use
   334|```
   335|Behavior: Performing representation for unseen audience
   336|Marks: Practiced pose, "the smile," intentional clothing/grooming
   337|Prompt: "subject fully aware image purpose, performing idealized self"
   338|Token: [PP_PERFORMANCE]
   339|```
   340|

   379|## MODERATION PROFILE
   380|
   381|**Operator Selection Guide:**
   382|- Maximum authenticity + interesting failures: OP_08, OP_11
   383|- Clean directed imagery: OP_07, OP_10
   384|- Relationship warmth + moderate failures: OP_01, OP_12
   385|- HK-specific authenticity: OP_13-22
   386|
   387|**Cross-Reference:** Combines with ENGINE_V15_BAD_PHOTO_REALISM_SYSTEM for failure type injection. HK operators marked with `[HK]` require environmental verification tokens.
   388|
   389|**Distribution Target:**
   390|- Intimate/Personal distance: 50-60%
   391|- Social/Public distance: 30-40%
   392|- Selfie/Technical: 10-15%

================================================================================
## V15 BAD PHOTO REALISM SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V15/ENGINE_V15_BAD_PHOTO_REALISM_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENGINE_V15_BAD_PHOTO_REALISM_SYSTEM.md
     2|
     3|## V15 Core Module — Imperfect Photo System
     4|### AREA: 02 (Bad Photo Realism) | Status: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     5|
     6|---
     7|
     8|## PURPOSE
     9|
    10|The bad photo realism system identifies specific failure modes that signal authentic human capture rather than professional construction. Imperfect photos feel more real because the human visual system is trained on billions of imperfect amateur photographs. Technical perfection reads as constructed; imperfection is the signature of the real.
    11|
    12|---
    13|
    14|## KEY CONCEPTS
    15|
    16|**Failure Type** = Mechanical Cause + Visual Signature + Authenticity Signal
    17|
    18|**Combined Failure Patterns** = Clusters of failures that identify specific capture contexts
    19|
    20|**Authenticity Weight** = Each failure type carries different authenticity density
    21|
    22|---
    23|
    24|## IMPERFECT_PHOTO_SYSTEM — 26 FAILURE TYPES
    25|
    26|### Failure Category A: Framing Failures
    27|
    28|**FAIL_01: ACCIDENTAL CROP**
    29|```
    30|Cause: Photographer failed to frame subject correctly
    31|Visual: Face cut at edge, body truncated at waist/knee, hand severed at wrist
    32|Authenticity: MEDIUM — non-professional evidence
    33|Prompt: "accidental face crop with forehead cut off by frame edge,
    34|        asymmetric framing suggesting inattention, amateur framing error"
    35|Token: [FAIL_ACCIDENTAL_CROP]
    36|```
    37|
    38|**FAIL_21: OUT OF FRAME**
    39|```
    40|Cause: Subject moved before/during exposure or photographer misframed
    41|Visual: Subject missing entirely, only environment captured
    42|Authenticity: HIGH — timing failure evidence
    43|Prompt: "out of frame with subject completely missing,
    44|        only environment captured, timing error"
    45|Token: [FAIL_OUT_OF_FRAME]
    46|```
    47|
    48|### Failure Category B: Motion Failures
    49|
    50|**FAIL_02: MOTION BLUR (Subject)**
    51|```
    52|Cause: Shutter too slow to freeze subject motion
    53|Visual: Body/face smeared, edges trail behind movement, hair creates motion trails
    54|Authenticity: HIGH — impossible to pose
    55|Prompt: "motion blur from subject movement during exposure,
    56|        body smeared with trails, hair creating motion trails,
    57|        low light interior no flash"
    58|Token: [FAIL_MOTION_BLUR_SUBJECT]
    59|```
    60|
    61|**FAIL_03: MOTION BLUR (Camera Shake)**
    62|```
    63|Cause: Photographer hand moved during exposure
    64|Visual: Entire frame blurs uniformly, diagonal/rotational direction
    65|Authenticity: HIGH — unique handheld fingerprint
    66|Prompt: "uniform camera shake blur affecting entire frame,
    67|        diagonal rotational blur direction revealing photographer tremor,
    68|        handheld smartphone fingerprint"
    69|Token: [FAIL_MOTION_BLUR_CAMERA]
    70|```
    71|
    72|**FAIL_22: CAMERA DROP/SHAKE**
    73|```
    74|Cause: Camera jostled/dropped during exposure
    75|Visual: Chaotic blur not in consistent direction, parts displaced
    76|Authenticity: HIGH — physical trauma evidence
    77|Prompt: "camera dropped or shaken during exposure creating chaotic blur,
    78|        entire frame affected, physical camera trauma"
    79|Token: [FAIL_CAMERA_DROP]
    80|```
    81|
    82|### Failure Category C: Exposure Failures
    83|
    84|**FAIL_04: SEVERE UNDEREXPOSURE**
    85|```
    86|Cause: Camera metered for background not subject
    87|Visual: Subject silhouette, face near-black, background correctly exposed
    88|Authenticity: MEDIUM — no fill flash evidence
    89|Prompt: "severe underexposure with subject silhouette shape only,
    90|        background correctly exposed bright, no fill flash used"
    91|Token: [FAIL_UNDEREXPOSURE]
    92|```
    93|
    94|**FAIL_05: SEVERE OVEREXPOSURE**
    95|```
    96|Cause: Camera metered for subject or flash fired in dark
    97|Visual: Face white, highlights clipped, background blown to white
    98|Authenticity: MEDIUM — one-way failure unrecoverable
    99|Prompt: "severe overexposure with subject face completely white,
   100|        highlights clipped unrecoverable, flash washout"
   101|Token: [FAIL_OVEREXPOSURE]
   102|```
   103|
   104|### Failure Category D: Focus Failures
   105|
   106|**FAIL_09: AUTOFOCUS MISS**
   107|```
   108|Cause: Camera locked onto wrong area (background not subject)
   109|Visual: Subject face soft/out of focus, background sharp, eyes particularly soft
   110|Authenticity: MEDIUM-HIGH — no verification evidence
   111|Prompt: "autofocus missed subject with camera locking onto background,
   112|        subject soft while environment sharp"
   113|Token: [FAIL_AUTOFOCUS_MISS]
   114|```
   115|
   116|**FAIL_18: FOCUS HUNT**
   117|```
   118|Cause: Camera still searching when shutter fired
   119|Visual: Multiple focal planes, inconsistent sharpness across frame
   120|Authenticity: MEDIUM — impatient capture evidence
   121|Prompt: "focus hunt with camera searching not settling before capture,
   122|        multiple focal planes visible"
   123|Token: [FAIL_FOCUS_HUNT]
   124|```
   125|
   126|### Failure Category E: Technical Artifact Failures
   127|
   128|**FAIL_06: INCORRECT WHITE BALANCE**
   129|```
   130|Cause: Auto white balance confused by mixed lighting
   131|Visual: Skin orange or blue, white objects carrying color cast, fluorescent flicker
   132|Authenticity: LOW — consumer camera artifact
   133|Prompt: "incorrect white balance with skin tones shifted orange or blue,
   134|        mixed interior lighting confusion"
   135|Token: [FAIL_WHITE_BALANCE]
   136|```
   137|
   138|**FAIL_10: ISO NOISE/GRAIN**
   139|```
   140|Cause: High ISO in low light situations
   141|Visual: Visible grain throughout, color noise (red/blue specks), detail loss
   142|Authenticity: MEDIUM-HIGH — real low light evidence
   143|Prompt: "high ISO grain throughout entire frame, color noise,
   144|        sensor struggling in low light"
   145|Token: [FAIL_ISO_GRAIN]
   146|```
   147|
   148|**FAIL_19: COLOR FRINGING**
   149|```
   150|Cause: Lens chromatic aberration at high-contrast edges
   151|Visual: Purple/green halos along edges, strongest at corners
   152|Authenticity: LOW — lens quality signature
   153|Prompt: "chromatic aberration with purple or green halos along edges,
   154|        cheap smartphone lens failing"
   155|Token: [FAIL_CHROMATIC_ABERRATION]
   156|```
   157|
   158|### Failure Category F: Lens/Optical Failures
   159|
   160|**FAIL_07: EXTREME WIDE ANGLE DISTORTION**
   161|```
   162|Cause: Subject too close to wide-angle lens
   163|Visual: Nose enlarged, face edges stretched, forehead extended, chin compressed
   164|Authenticity: MEDIUM — specific smartphone failure
   165|Prompt: "extreme wide angle lens distortion from subject too close,
   166|        nose significantly larger, facial features stretched"
   167|Token: [FAIL_WIDE_DISTORTION]
   168|```
   169|
   170|**FAIL_12: LENS FLARE/GHOST**
   171|```
   172|Cause: Light entered at angle creating internal reflections
   173|Visual: Bright streak across diagonal, ghost image of light source
   174|Authenticity: LOW — could be intentional
   175|Prompt: "lens flare artifact with bright streak across diagonal,
   176|        ghost image of sun, shooting toward light without shielding"
   177|Token: [FAIL_LENS_FLARE]
   178|```
   179|
   180|**FAIL_20: DUST/SENSOR SPOT**
   181|```
   182|Cause: Dust on sensor creating dark circular spot
   183|Visual: Dark spot at consistent position, same in every image
   184|Authenticity: MEDIUM — maintenance failure
   185|Prompt: "dust or sensor spot creating dark circular blemish,
   186|        same position every image from device"
   187|Token: [FAIL_SENSOR_SPOT]
   188|```
   189|
   190|### Failure Category G: Flash Failures
   191|
   192|**FAIL_11: FLASH SYNC FAILURE**
   193|```
   194|Cause: Flash fired but shutter too slow
   195|Visual: Dark image with bright strip where flash hit
   196|Authenticity: MEDIUM — amateur flash use
   197|Prompt: "flash sync failure with bright strip of flash across frame
   198|        while rest remains dark, shutter too slow"
   199|Token: [FAIL_FLASH_SYNC]
   200|```
   201|
   202|**FAIL_15: RED-EYE**
   203|```
   204|Cause: Flash reflects off dilated pupils
   205|Visual: Eyes bright red, face otherwise normally lit
   206|Authenticity: LOW-MEDIUM — fixable but endemic
   207|Prompt: "flash red-eye with eyes showing bright red pupils,
   208|        built-in flash in low light"
   209|Token: [FAIL_RED_EYE]
   210|```
   211|
   212|### Failure Category H: Processing Failures
   213|
   214|**FAIL_16: JPEG COMPRESSION ARTIFACTS**
   215|```
   216|Cause: Aggressive compression or social media pipeline
   217|Visual: Blocky artifacts in uniform areas, mosquito noise, color banding
   218|Authenticity: MEDIUM — social media transit evidence
   219|Prompt: "JPEG compression artifacts with blocky artifacts in sky/walls,
   220|        evidence of social media upload/download pipeline"
   221|Token: [FAIL_JPEG_COMPRESSION]
   222|```
   223|
   224|**FAIL_17: DEPTH MAP FAILURE**
   225|```
   226|Cause: Portrait mode edge detection failed
   227|Visual: Hair merges with background, shoulder blends, halos at edges
   228|Authenticity: MEDIUM — computational photography only
   229|Prompt: "portrait mode depth map failure with hair merging into background,
   230|        smartphone computational failure only"
   231|Token: [FAIL_PORTRAIT_MODE_FAILURE]
   232|```
   233|
   234|### Failure Category I: Other Failures
   235|
   236|**FAIL_08: FINGER BLOCKING LENS**
   237|```
   238|Cause: Finger/thumb accidentally covered part of lens
   239|Visual: Curved finger pad shape at corner/edge, in focus (at lens distance)
   240|Authenticity: VERY HIGH — requires human hold
   241|Prompt: "finger accidentally blocking portion of lens creating dark curved shape,
   242|        purely amateur artifact"
   243|Token: [FAIL_FINGER_BLOCK]
   244|```
   245|
   246|**FAIL_13: DOUBLE EXPOSURE/GHOST**
   247|```
   248|Cause: Two images captured in one frame
   249|Visual: Subject appears twice, semi-transparent overlay
   250|Authenticity: MEDIUM — malfunction evidence
   251|Prompt: "double exposure ghost overlap with subject appearing twice,
   252|        semi-transparent overlay of two captures"
   253|Token: [FAIL_DOUBLE_EXPOSURE]
   254|```
   255|
   256|**FAIL_14: TILTED HORIZON**
   257|```
   258|Cause: Camera held at angle
   259|Visual: Horizon not level, architectural features angle, diagonal tension
   260|Authenticity: MEDIUM — could be intentional
   261|Prompt: "tilted horizon with camera held at angle making nothing level,
   262|        amateur hold with no level indicator"
   263|Token: [FAIL_TILTED_HORIZON]
   264|```
   265|
   266|### HK-Specific Failures
   267|
   268|**FAIL_23: NEON SIGN REFLECTION** `[HK]`
   269|```
   270|Cause: Dense HK neon signage in wet conditions
   271|Visual: Pink/blue/green neon reflections bleeding onto subjects, puddle doubling
   272|Authenticity: HIGH — location-specific
   273|Prompt: "Hong Kong neon sign reflection contamination with pink blue green neon
   274|        from dense signage reflecting on wet street, authentic 夜市 atmosphere"
   275|Token: [FAIL_NEON_HK]
   276|```
   277|
   278|**FAIL_24: HUMIDITY HAZE/HEAT DISTORTION** `[HK]`
   279|```
   280|Cause: HK summer humidity + temperature differential
   281|Visual: Distant buildings washed out, heat shimmer, wavy distortion
   282|Authenticity: HIGH — environment-specific
   283|Prompt: "humidity haze and heat distortion specific to Hong Kong summer,
   284|        distant buildings washed out, heat shimmer visible"
   285|Token: [FAIL_HUMIDITY_HAZE_HK]
   286|```
   287|
   288|**FAIL_25: WET MARKET FLUORESCENT** `[HK]`
   289|```
   290|Cause: Mixed fluorescent/sodium vapor in 街市
   291|Visual: Extreme green-yellow cast, fish/water reflections, skin unrecognizable
   292|Authenticity: HIGH — location-specific
   293|Prompt: "wet market fluorescent contamination specific to Hong Kong 街市,
   294|        extreme green-yellow color cast, fish water wet floor reflections"
   295|Token: [FAIL_WET_MARKET_HK]
   296|```
   297|
   298|**FAIL_26: DENSE BUILDING BACKGROUND CLASH** `[HK]`
   299|```
   300|Cause: HK extreme building density confuses portrait mode
   301|Visual: Multiple bokeh sizes indicating multiple distance layers
   302|Authenticity: HIGH — density-specific
   303|Prompt: "dense building background clash specific to Hong Kong urban environment,
   304|        multiple building layers at different distances, bokeh confusion"
   305|Token: [FAIL_DENSE_BUILDING_HK]
   306|```
   307|
   308|---
   309|
   310|## COMBINED FAILURE PATTERNS
   311|
   312|**PATTERN_01: THE NIGHT OUT SEQUENCE**
   313|```
   314|Failures: ISO grain + red-eye + motion blur + camera shake + accidental crop + color fringing + JPEG artifacts
   315|Context: Low light bar/club, alcohol impairment
   316|Prompt: "night out sequence with high ISO grain throughout, flash red-eye
   317|        in dark bar, motion blur from unsteady hands, camera shake rotation,
   318|        accidental face crops, JPEG artifacts from social upload"
   319|Token: [PATTERN_NIGHT_OUT]
   320|```
   321|
   322|**PATTERN_02: THE BATHROOM MIRROR SELFIE**
   323|```
   324|Failures: Beauty mode over-smoothing + chin-up distortion + nose enlargement + finger blocking + phone in frame
   325|Context: Front camera, intimate space
   326|Prompt: "bathroom mirror selfie with beauty mode aggressive smoothing,
   327|        extreme chin-up angle distorting proportions, nose enlarged,
   328|        mirror reflection capturing phone in frame"
   329|Token: [PATTERN_BATHROOM_SELFIE]
   330|```
   331|
   332|**PATTERN_03: THE TOURIST GROUP SHOT**
   333|```
   334|Failures: Face crops + extreme wide angle + someone blinking + horizon tilt + background chaos + flash washout
   335|Context: Stranger with camera
   336|Prompt: "tourist group shot with face crops from stranger not knowing
   337|        who to include, extreme wide angle from close proximity,
   338|        someone blinking from countdown, horizon tilted"
   339|Token: [PATTERN_TOURIST_GROUP]
   340|```
   341|
   342|**PATTERN_04: THE HK NIGHT MARKET SEQUENCE** `[HK]`
   343|```
   344|Failures: Neon contamination + humidity haze + wet market fluorescent + high ISO + motion blur
   345|Context: Mong Kok/LKF night market
   346|Prompt: "Hong Kong night market sequence with neon pink blue green reflections
   347|        on wet pavement, humidity haze reducing distant contrast,
   348|        fluorescent green-yellow skin cast from market lighting"
   349|Token: [PATTERN_HK_NIGHT_MARKET]
   350|```
   351|
   352|**PATTERN_05: THE HK TRANSIT SEQUENCE** `[HK]`
   353|```
   354|Failures: Escalator motion blur + passenger heads + fluorescent + train blur + glass reflection
   355|Context: MTR/Escalator
   356|Prompt: "Hong Kong transit sequence with escalator motion blur on steps,
   357|        other passenger heads visible above shoulder, MTR platform
   358|        fluorescent green cast, train motion blur through window"
   359|Token: [PATTERN_HK_TRANSIT]
   360|```
   361|
   362|---
   363|
   364|## SMARTPHONE_ERROR_LIBRARY
   365|
   366|### Sensor Limitations
   367|```
   368|[ROLLING_SHUTTER] — CMOS skew in fast motion, vertical lines slanted
   369|[HEAT_BUILDP] — Extended capture increases noise, sensor gives up
   370|[FIXED_APERTURE] — No mechanical control, low light fixed
   371|[NO_OPTICAL_ZOOM] — Digital zoom interpolation, soft images
   372|```
   373|
   374|### Processing Failures
   375|```
   376|[MULTI_FRAME_ERROR] — HDR/Night Mode ghosting when subject moves
   377|[SEMANTIC_SEG_FAIL] — AI misidentifies fence as hair, cloud as subject
   378|[OVER_SMOOTHING] — Aggressive noise reduction removes pores, plastic skin
   379|[COLOR_BOOSTING] — Blues/greens oversaturated, cartoonish
   380|```
   381|
   382|### Physical Failures
   383|```
   384|[CRACKED_LENS] — Light scatters, haze/flare/color shifts
   385|[FINGER_GREASE] — Soft blobs, warm cast, reduced sharpness
   386|[WATER_INTERNAL] — Internal fogging, overall haze
   387|[DIRTY_SENSOR_CORNERS] — Consistent dark spots at small apertures
   388|```
   389|
   390|### Capture Timing Errors
   391|```
   392|[SHUTTER_LAG] — Subject moved between press and capture
   393|[PRE_CAPTURE_BUFFER] — May capture 0.5s before press
   394|[POST_CAPTURE_PROCESS] — Gallery image different from captured
   395|```
   396|
   397|---
   398|
   399|## MODERATION PROFILE
   400|
   401|**Authenticity Weighting:**
   402|```
   403|VERY HIGH: [FAIL_FINGER_BLOCK] — requires human hold
   404|HIGH: [FAIL_MOTION_BLUR_SUBJECT] [FAIL_MOTION_BLUR_CAMERA] [FAIL_CAMERA_DROP]
   405|       [FAIL_NEON_HK] [FAIL_HUMIDITY_HAZE_HK] [FAIL_WET_MARKET_HK] [FAIL_DENSE_BUILDING_HK]
   406|MEDIUM-HIGH: [FAIL_AUTOFOCUS_MISS] [FAIL_ISO_GRAIN]
   407|MEDIUM: [FAIL_ACCIDENTAL_CROP] [FAIL_UNDEREXPOSURE] [FAIL_OVEREXPOSURE] [FAIL_PORTRAIT_MODE_FAILURE]
   408|LOW-MEDIUM: [FAIL_RED_EYE]
   409|LOW: [FAIL_WHITE_BALANCE] [FAIL_CHROMATIC_ABERRATION] [FAIL_LENS_FLARE]
   410|```
   411|
   412|**Quality Thresholds:**
   413|- Perfect images (no failures) = suspicious
   414|- Single failure = may be staged intentionally
   415|- Multiple failures (3+) in different categories = genuine amateur
   416|- Specific failure clusters = strong authenticity signals
   417|
   418|---
   419|
   420|## TOKEN LIBRARY
   421|
   422|```
   423|FAILURE TYPES:
   424|[FAIL_ACCIDENTAL_CROP] [FAIL_OUT_OF_FRAME]

   426|[FAIL_UNDEREXPOSURE] [FAIL_OVEREXPOSURE]
   427|[FAIL_AUTOFOCUS_MISS] [FAIL_FOCUS_HUNT]
   428|[FAIL_WHITE_BALANCE] [FAIL_ISO_GRAIN] [FAIL_CHROMATIC_ABERRATION]
   429|[FAIL_WIDE_DISTORTION] [FAIL_LENS_FLARE] [FAIL_SENSOR_SPOT]
   430|[FAIL_FLASH_SYNC] [FAIL_RED_EYE]
   431|[FAIL_JPEG_COMPRESSION] [FAIL_PORTRAIT_MODE_FAILURE]
   432|[FAIL_FINGER_BLOCK] [FAIL_DOUBLE_EXPOSURE] [FAIL_TILTED_HORIZON]
   433|[FAIL_NEON_HK] [FAIL_HUMIDITY_HAZE_HK] [FAIL_WET_MARKET_HK] [FAIL_DENSE_BUILDING_HK]
   434|
   435|PATTERNS:
   436|[PATTERN_NIGHT_OUT] [PATTERN_BATHROOM_SELFIE] [PATTERN_TOURIST_GROUP]

   440|[ROLLING_SHUTTER] [HEAT_BUILDP] [FIXED_APERTURE] [NO_OPTICAL_ZOOM]

   442|[CRACKED_LENS] [FINGER_GREASE] [WATER_INTERNAL] [DIRTY_SENSOR_CORNERS]

   444|```
   445|
   446|---
   447|
   448|## PROMPT GRAMMAR
   449|
   450|```
   451|Base: authentic bad smartphone photo not professional
   452|Failure: [failure_type_token] [visual_signature]
   453|Combined: [pattern_token] for context-specific clustering
   454|HK: Add [HK_location_token] for environment verification
   455|Example: "authentic bad smartphone photo, motion blur from real movement,
   456|         camera shake from handheld not tripod, ISO grain throughout,
   457|         finger accidentally blocking lens corner"
