================================================================================
## V15 CONTINUITY PERSISTENCE SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V15/ENGINE_V15_CONTINUITY_PERSISTENCE_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENGINE_V15_CONTINUITY_PERSISTENCE_SYSTEM.md
     2|
     3|## V15 Core Module — Continuity Object Library + Outfit Repeat
     4|### AREA: 03 (Continuity Persistence) | Status: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     5|
     6|---
     7|
     8|## PURPOSE
     9|
    10|Recurring visual objects create the feeling of continuous life. The same bikini across summers. The pendant never removed. The tote bag with fraying straps. These objects function as life timestamps — evidence that this is a real person existing in real time, accumulating wear, returning to places.
    11|
    12|---
    13|
    14|## KEY CONCEPTS
    15|
    16|**Personal Item Chronology**: 3-7 recurring objects per character across sessions
    17|
    18|**Temporal Signatures**: Wear patterns that allow viewer to place object on timeline
    19|
    20|**Diegetic Continuity**: Same object appearing in same physical world across sessions
    21|
    22|---
    23|
    24|## CONTINUITY_OBJECT_LIBRARY
    25|
    26|### Category A: Apparel Repeat Items
    27|
    28|**A1: STATEMENT BIKINI**
    29|```
    30|Description: Brand-specific bikini appearing across 2-4 summers
    31|Continuity Markers:
    32|  - Fade: vibrant → slightly faded → noticeably faded
    33|  - Elastic: band stretched, straps slightly slack
    34|  - Hardware: clasp dulled, underwire possibly warped
    35|  - Tanning lines: strap marks intensifying across years
    36|Wear Tier:
    37|  T0: crisp vibrant no fade
    38|  T1: minimal fade still supportive
    39|  T2: elastic relaxed color mildly diminished
    40|  T3: faded elastic clearly stretched wire possibly poking
    41|Prompt: "same [brand_color] bikini from [year_1/year_2/year_3] beach photos,
    42|        fade level [light/medium/heavy], elastic wear on [straps/band/underwire],
    43|        tanning lines from previous summers visible"
    44|Token: [CONT_BIKINI_YEAR_1-4]
    45|```
    46|
    47|**A2: SIGNATURE NECKLACE/PENDANT**
    48|```
    49|Description: Chain/pendant worn consistently, accumulates skin oils/scratches
    50|Continuity Markers:
    51|  - Metal oxidation: bright → dulled → green tarnish at connections
    52|  - Chain links: subtle kinks from repeated wear
    53|  - Clasp: slightly worn, easier to open than original
    54|  - Skin contact: chain stained from lotion/sweat
    55|Prompt: "[metal_type] [pendant_style] necklace worn daily for [years],
    56|        patina accumulation, chain flexibility reduced,
    57|        clasp slightly worn from repeated opening"
    58|Token: [CONT_NECKLACE_WORN]
    59|```
    60|
    61|**A3: EMOTIONAL HOODIE**
    62|```
    63|Description: Favorite hoodie worn repeatedly, appears in informal sessions
    64|Continuity Markers:
    65|  - Pilling: fabric pills at cuffs/pockets/hem
    66|  - Color degradation: particularly at elbows
    67|  - Shape memory: molded slightly to body shape
    68|  - Lint accumulation: around pocket and hem
    69|  - Zipper: slider slightly stiff or teeth misaligned
    70|Prompt: "[color] supremel-branded hoodie worn for 18+ months,
    71|        fabric pilling at [cuffs/pockets/hem], color fade at stress points,
    72|        shape molded to body, lint accumulation in pocket"
    73|Token: [CONT_HOODIE_WORN]
    74|```
    75|
    76|**A4: ROTATIONAL TOTE BAG**
    77|```
    78|Description: Canvas/leather tote for shopping/daily/beach trips
    79|Continuity Markers:
    80|  - Handle wear: one handle more worn if single-hand bias
    81|  - Body shape: loses structure, bottom stress, corners rub
    82|  - Interior: liner with pen marks, lip gloss exploded, old receipts
    83|  - Hardware: metal studs on bottom dulled/scratched
    84|Prompt: "[material] canvas tote bag with [single_hand_bias/symmetric] handle wear,
    85|        body slightly sagged, corner rub [mild/noticeable],
    86|        interior contents [detail_level], bottom studs dulled"
    87|Token: [CONT_TOTE_WORN]
    88|```
    89|
    90|**A5: SPECIFIC UNDERWEAR SET**
    91|```
    92|Description: Bra/panties visible at edges through sheer/low-back clothing
    93|Continuity Markers:
    94|  - Elastic degradation: band less supportive, straps widened
    95|  - Color: slight migration/staining from daily wear
    96|  - Fabric texture: lived-in rather than new crispness
    97|  - Hook-and-eye: closure points worn
    98|Prompt: "same bra/panties set visible at edges, slight elastic degradation,
    99|        band less supportive, straps slightly widened,
   100|        fabric texture lived-in not new"
   101|Token: [CONT_UNDERWEAR_SET]
   102|```
   103|
   104|### Category B: Personal Possessions
   105|
   106|**B1: PHONE CASE WITH DAMAGE**
   107|```
   108|Description: Phone case carried everywhere, impact damage accumulates
   109|Continuity Markers:
   110|  - Case corners: impact damage from drops
   111|  - Screen protector: bubbles, edge scratches, yellowing
   112|  - USB port: slight tilt from repeated plugging
   113|  - Button areas: heavily worn smooth at volume/power
   114|Prompt: "[brand_model] phone case with [corners_damaged/screen_bubbles],
   115|        button areas smooth from wear, USB port misalignment,
   116|        case clearly matched to [1-2+] year old phone purchase"
   117|Token: [CONT_PHONE_CASE]
   118|```
   119|
   120|**B2: HOME SCATTER OBJECTS**
   121|```
   122|Description: Objects on bedroom shelf/desk/nightstand appearing in backgrounds
   123|Types: half-empty perfume, protein powder, coral vase, worn paperback,
   124|       medication blister pack, charging cable brand
   125|Continuity: Appear inconsistently across sessions creating diegetic density
   126|Prompt: "bedroom shelf scatter: [specific_object] visible in background,
   127|        same object appears across multiple sessions inconsistent between shots"
   128|Token: [CONT_SCATTER_OBJECT]
   129|```
   130|
   131|**B3: JEWELRY STACK**
   132|```
   133|Description: Rings/bracelets/anklets consistently stacked in same combinations
   134|Continuity Markers:
   135|  - Metal pairing: matching patina/oxidation levels
   136|  - Sizing: rings slightly loose (worn for years)
   137|  - Stack order: character's consistent pattern
   138|Prompt: "[metal_combo] jewelry stack [number] pieces,
   139|        matching patina across pieces, rings slightly loose,
   140|        stack order [consistent/variable], [anklet_present/absent]"
   141|Token: [CONT_JEWELRY_STACK]
   142|```
   143|
   144|**B4: REPEATED EYEGLASSES**
   145|```
   146|Description: Specific pair worn in daily-life shots, not just posed
   147|Continuity Markers:
   148|  - Nose pad: marks on bridge from daily wear
   149|  - Temple tips: slightly bent from removal/placement
   150|  - Lens: micro-scratches from cleaning
   151|  - Case: possibly more worn than glasses
   152|Prompt: "same eyeglasses worn consistently in daily shots,
   153|        nose pad marks on bridge, temple tips slightly bent,
   154|        lens micro-scratches visible, case worn"
   155|Token: [CONT_EYEGLASSES]
   156|```
   157|
   158|### Category C: Environmental Continuity
   159|
   160|**C1: SPECIFIC BEDDING SET**
   161|```
   162|Description: Same sheets/pillowcases/blanket in bedroom over months/years
   163|Continuity Markers:
   164|  - Wrinkle patterns: consistent placement creating baseline
   165|  - Light staining: subtle pillowcase discoloration at mouth
   166|  - Fabric softener: slightly built-up texture
   167|  - Tear progression: small tear possibly visible in later sessions
   168|Prompt: "same [color/material] bedding set appearing in bedroom portraits over months,
   169|        consistent wrinkle placement, subtle skincare product staining on pillowcase,
   170|        fabric softener buildup texture, [small_tear_progressing]"
   171|Token: [CONT_BEDDING_SET]
   172|```
   173|
   174|**C2: ROOM SLIPPERS (拖鞋)**
   175|```
   176|Description: Indoor slippers worn at home, visible in floor-level shots
   177|Continuity Markers:
   178|  - Insole compression: permanent foot-shape depression
   179|  - Outside sole: wear pattern from specific floor types
   180|  - Material: slight separation at seam if daily wear
   181|Prompt: "same indoor [material] slippers with foot-shape sole impression,
   182|        wear pattern from walking on [specific_floor], [slight_separation_at_seam]"
   183|Token: [CONT_ROOM_SLIPPERS]
   184|```
   185|
   186|**C3: SPECIFIC TOWEL/HAIR TOWEL**
   187|```
   188|Description: Same towel in bathroom selfies, post-shower shots
   189|Continuity Markers:
   190|  - Slight discoloration: rust-tint at hem from water exposure
   191|  - Fabric softening: subsequent washes creating worn softness
   192|  - Hanging wear: towel rod discoloration if consistent spot
   193|Prompt: "same [color] towel appearing in bathroom selfies over months,
   194|        rust-tint at hem, fabric softened from multiple washes,
   195|        [towel_rod_discoloration_present]"
   196|Token: [CONT_TOWEL]
   197|```
   198|
   199|### Category D: Situational Repeat Items
   200|
   201|**D1: TRAVEL BAG**
   202|```
   203|Description: Specific bag for beach trips/weekend getaways
   204|Continuity Markers:
   205|  - Duffel crease: specific crease lines from folding
   206|  - Interior: possibly old sunscreen, sand residue, not cleaned between trips
   207|  - Strap wear: specific hand-carry pattern
   208|Prompt: "same [style] travel bag appearing across [number] beach trips,
   209|        duffel crease from storage, interior sand residue in corners,
   210|        strap wear pattern, [water_bottle_moisture_damage]"
   211|Token: [CONT_TRAVEL_BAG]
   212|```
   213|
   214|**D2: SPECIFIC BEACH TOWEL**
   215|```
   216|Description: Distinctive towel in beach/shore shots
   217|Continuity Markers:
   218|  - Sand staining: bottom of towel consistently shows sand
   219|  - Bleaching: chlorine/salt fade on colorful towel
   220|  - Fold memory: wants to fold certain ways
   221|  - Fringe fray: edges progressively fraying
   222|Prompt: "same [color] beach towel with sand staining at bottom,
   223|        [chlorine/salt] bleaching creating inconsistent fade,
   224|        fold memory visible, fringe [fraying_progression]"
   225|Token: [CONT_BEACH_TOWEL]
   226|```
   227|
   228|**D3: WATER BOTTLE ROUTINE**
   229|```
   230|Description: Reusable bottle in fitness/street/home contexts
   231|Continuity Markers:
   232|  - Beverage residue: internal staining if unwashed
   233|  - Cap wear: O-ring degrading, cap not threading smoothly
   234|  - Dents/dings: if metal, accumulated impacts
   235|  - Label state: scratched/peeling from extensive use
   236|Prompt: "same [material] water bottle with [residue_staining/dents/label_peeling],
   237|        cap O-ring [degrading/smooth], threads [catching/smooth]"
   238|Token: [CONT_WATER_BOTTLE]
   239|```
   240|
   241|### Category E: Footwear Persistence
   242|
   243|**E1: DAILY WEAR SNEAKERS**
   244|```
   245|Description: Sneakers for regular daily use, not special occasion
   246|Continuity Markers:
   247|  - Outsole wear: specific walk patterns in heel/toe
   248|  - Upper creasing: horizontal creases at flex point
   249|  - Tongue stain: lace grooves visible in padding
   250|  - Collar deformation: ankle collar deformed from insertion
   251|  - Insole: darkened from sweat absorption
   252|Prompt: "same [brand/color] sneakers worn daily for [months],
   253|        outsole [heel_toe_wear_pattern], upper creasing at flex points,
   254|        tongue stain from lace pressure, collar deformed from ankle insertion,
   255|        insole darkened from sweat"
   256|Token: [CONT_SNEAKERS_DAILY]
   257|```
   258|
   259|**E2: BATHROOM SLIPPERS (Shower)**
   260|```
   261|Description: Rubber slippers worn in shower
   262|Continuity Markers:
   263|  - Bottom tread: possible mold in grooves if not dried
   264|  - Sole flexibility: becoming more flexible from water cycles
   265|  - Color fading: rubber degrading
   266|Prompt: "same [color] rubber shower slippers with [mold_in_tread/sol_flexible],
   267|        color [faded/consistent], [not_fully_dried_moisture]"
   268|Token: [CONT_SHOWER_SLIPPERS]
   269|```
   270|
   271|---
   272|
   273|## OBJECT-TIME MAPPING
   274|
   275|### Tier System
   276|
   277|```
   278|TIER_0: NEW/FRESHLY ACQUIRED
   279|  - Crisp, no wear, tags possibly visible
   280|  - "first wear tag visible"
   281|
   282|TIER_1: 3-6 MONTHS REGULAR USE
   283|  - New-product feel gone, early wear visible
   284|  - "3-6 months regular use, early wear markers"
   285|
   286|TIER_2: 1 YEAR REGULAR USE
   287|  - Full break-in, meaningful wear, character mold developing
   288|  - "1 year of daily wear, meaningful wear visible"
   289|
   290|TIER_3: 2+ YEARS REGULAR USE
   291|  - Visible degradation, possibly seeking replacement
   292|  - "2+ years heavy use, elastic degraded, fading visible"
   293|
   294|TIER_4: VINTAGE/SENTIMENTAL
   295|  - Old but maintained past normal replacement point
   296|  - "vintage worn, maintained past replacement necessity"
   297|```
   298|
   299|### Moderation Profile
   300|
   301|- Each character: 3-7 persistent items across categories
   302|- No more than 2 items TIER_0 in use at once
   303|- TIER_3+ items need narrative explanation (sentimental, financial constraint, loyalty)
   304|- Correlated wear: objects worn together should age together
   305|
   306|---
   307|
   308|## OUTFIT-REPEAT SYSTEM
   309|
   310|### Rotation Frequency Model
   311|
   312|| Outfit Type | Repeat Cadence | Max Years | Wear Progression |
   313||-------------|----------------|-----------|------------------|
   314|| Statement piece (bikini) | 2-4x per year | 3-4 | Slow |
   315|| Daily wear (hoodie, tee) | 15-30x per year | Continuous | Fast (6mo) |
   316|| Special occasion | 1x per year max | 5+ | None |
   317|| Active/sports | 3-5x per month | 1-2 | Fast (sweat/salt) |
   318|
   319|**Key**: "Times worn" to "times photographed" ratio should skew heavily toward times worn.
   320|
   321|### Outfit-State Tracking
   322|
   323|```
   324|SAME OUTFIT (immediate): Worn within 48hrs, minimal laundering difference
   325|SAME OUTFIT (contextual): Worn 2-4 weeks later, washed once, storage wrinkles
   326|SAME ITEM DIFFERENT COMPLETION: Same top + different bottom/footwear
   327|SAME ITEM WEAR PROGRESSION: Same bikini Year 2 vs Year 3 = visible age
   328|```
   329|
   330|### Prompt Grammar
   331|
   332|```
   333|SAME_ITEM_REPEAT:
   334|[item_description] worn [frequency] wash_cycle [number]
   335|wrinkle_storage_pattern [level] item_age [tier]
   336|
   337|NEW_FROM_WARDROBE:
   338|[item_description] first_wear tag_[visible/not_visible]
   339|store_starch_[present/absent] size_label_[brand_size]
   340|
   341|COMPLETE_OUTFIT_REPEAT:
   342|[full_outfit_description] all_items_from_same_session_[date]
   343|```
   344|
   345|---
   346|
   347|## TRAVEL CONTINUITY MODULE
   348|
   349|### Travel Object Types
   350|
   351|**Type 1: Packed-Luggage Items** (Identity Anchors)
   352|- Same tote bag, water bottle, phone case in foreign context
   353|- "carried_to_[destination]_from_[origin]"
   354|
   355|**Type 2: Destination-Appropriate Items** (Location Markers)
   356|- New purchases appearing only in travel context
   357|- "acquired_at_[specific_location]_first_wear_[destination]"
   358|
   359|**Type 3: Travel-Specific Items** (Departure/Arrival Signals)
   360|- Passport, travel adapter, foreign currency
   361|- Appear in departure shots, absent during domestic sessions
   362|
   363|### Cross-Location Rules
   364|
   365|1. No object in more than 2 dramatically different environment types without explanation
   366|   - Exception: phone case, jewelry in ALL environments
   367|2. Travel wear progression is compressed (1 week = 3-5 contexts)
   368|3. Destination items accumulate wear independently
   369|
   370|### Prompt Grammar
   371|
   372|```
   373|TRAVEL_OBJECT_PRESENT:
   374|[item_description] carried_to_[destination]_from_[origin]
   375|destination_context_[tourist/local/off-duty]
   376|
   377|DESTINATION_PURCHASE:
   378|[new_item] acquired_at_[specific_location]_first_wear_[destination]
   379|return_wear_[origin_after_trip]
   380|
   381|DEPARTURE_EVIDENCE:
   382|passport_[character_name] travel_[destination] carry-on_items_[list]
   383|```
   384|
   385|---
   386|
   387|## TOKEN LIBRARY
   388|
   389|```
   390|APPAREL:
   391|[CONT_BIKINI_YEAR_1-4] [CONT_NECKLACE_WORN] [CONT_HOODIE_WORN]
   392|[CONT_TOTE_WORN] [CONT_UNDERWEAR_SET]
   393|
   394|PERSONAL:
   395|[CONT_PHONE_CASE] [CONT_SCATTER_OBJECT] [CONT_JEWELRY_STACK] [CONT_EYEGLASSES]
   396|
   397|ENVIRONMENTAL:
   398|[CONT_BEDDING_SET] [CONT_ROOM_SLIPPERS] [CONT_TOWEL]
   399|
   400|SITUATIONAL:
   401|[CONT_TRAVEL_BAG] [CONT_BEACH_TOWEL] [CONT_WATER_BOTTLE]
   402|
   403|FOOTWEAR:
   404|[CONT_SNEAKERS_DAILY] [CONT_SHOWER_SLIPPERS]
   405|
   406|TIERS:
   407|[TIER_0_NEW] [TIER_1_6MONTHS] [TIER_2_1YEAR] [TIER_3_2YEAR+] [TIER_4_VINTAGE]
   408|
   409|MODIFIERS:
   410|[same_item_repeat] [new_from_wardrobe] [complete_outfit_repeat]
   411|[wear_correlated] [destination_purchase] [departure_evidence]
   412|```

================================================================================
## V15 EXPRESSION TIMING SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V15/ENGINE_V15_EXPRESSION_TIMING_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENGINE_V15_EXPRESSION_TIMING_SYSTEM.md
     2|
     3|## V15 Core Module — Expression Timing Library V2
     4|### AREA: 04 (Emotional Instability) | Status: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     5|
     6|---
     7|
     8|## PURPOSE
     9|
    10|Human emotional expression is never perfectly timed. The smile isn't finished before the camera catches it. The laugh catches mid-breath. The expression lags, anticipates, interrupts, and trails off. Emotional Instability is the temporal imperfection of internal state expression — the opposite of "ready for camera" performance.
    11|
    12|---
    13|
    14|## KEY CONCEPTS
    15|
    16|**Timing Spectrum**: Every expression exists on anticipation → activation → peak → dissolution → residual
    17|
    18|**Completeness Scale**: LEVEL 0-6 from neutral to peak to returning
    19|
    20|**Unfinished Types**: Cut-off, held, fading, misaligned, stated-then-interrupted
    21|
    22|**Distinction from Camera Awareness**: AREA 01 = whether subject knows they're photographed. AREA 04 = whether expression is fully formed.
    23|
    24|---
    25|
    26|## EXPRESSION_TIMING_LIBRARY_V2
    27|
    28|### Category A: Joy-Laughter Spectrum
    29|
    30|**A1: LAUGH ONSET (Pre-Sound)**
    31|```
    32|Description: Moment before laughter becomes audible — face changes before sound
    33|Visual: Eye contraction FIRST (Orbicularis oculi), nasolabial furrows deepen
    34|        Shoulders begin upward 100-200ms before vocalization
    35|Duration: 150-400ms from first eye contraction to full mouth open
    36|Realism: Photographing just before audible laugh = face already laughing
    37|Prompt: "laugh onset with eye contraction before mouth opens,
    38|        shoulder anticipation upward, pre-sound facial engagement,
    39|        150-400ms before vocalization"
    40|Token: [EXPR_LAUGH_ONSET]
    41|```
    42|
    43|**A2: LAUGH PEAK HOLD (Overextended)**
    44|```
    45|Description: Laughter continues past moment joke ended — overshot natural endpoint
    46|Visual: Laughter 500-1000ms longer than script, head tilt back maintained
    47|        Breath intake visible mid-resolution
    48|Duration: 400-1200ms beyond expected endpoint
    49|Realism: Captured at natural comedown = caught in actual joy
    50|Prompt: "laugh overextended holding peak past joke ending,
    51|        head tilted back, breath intake visible at end,
    52|        500-1000ms longer than expected"
    53|Token: [EXPR_LAUGH_PEAK_HOLD]
    54|```
    55|
    56|**A3: LAUGH DISSOLUTION (Trail-Off)**
    57|```
    58|Description: Laugh ends incompletely — mini-burst reformations after apparent end
    59|Visual: Mouth open → teeth show → tongue visible → [moment] → slight reopening
    60|        Residual eye crinkling 500ms+ after mouth closes
    61|Duration: 800-2000ms total dissolution
    62|Realism: Reformation signals genuine emotional overflow
    63|Prompt: "laugh dissolution with mouth returning toward neutral then mini-reopening,
    64|        eye crinkling residual 500ms+ after mouth closes,
    65|        800-2000ms total"
    66|Token: [EXPR_LAUGH_DISSOLUTION]
    67|```
    68|
    69|**A4: SMILE INCOMPLETE (Doesn't Finish)**
    70|```
    71|Description: Smile begins but doesn't complete — attention redirects before peak
    72|Visual: Mouth opens briefly → returns halfway, asymmetric onset (one side first)
    73|        Orbicularis oculi: NO eye engagement = social smile not genuine
    74|Prompt: "smile onset mouth slightly open then freezes before full engagement,
    75|        asymmetric onset left/right first, eye contraction absent,
    76|        expression incomplete disrupted mid-state"
    77|Token: [EXPR_SMILE_INCOMPLETE]
    78|```
    79|
    80|**A5: SLEEPY JOY (Low-Arousal Positive)**
    81|```
    82|Description: Tired/sleepy person finds something genuinely funny
    83|Visual: Eyelids 40-60% closed during laugh, delayed response 500-800ms
    84|        Facial flush from effort, head nod forward from tiredness
    85|Realism: Contrast between humor strength and physical limitation = complexity
    86|Prompt: "sleepy joy with eyes half-open 40-60% closure attempting full engagement,
    87|        laugh delayed 500-800ms from stimulus, head nodding forward from fatigue,
    88|        slight facial flush from staying present"
    89|Token: [EXPR_SLEEPY_JOY]
    90|```
    91|
    92|### Category B: Startle-Surprise States
    93|
    94|**B1: PRE-PEAK ANTICIPATORY TENSION**
    95|```
    96|Description: Registering surprise but not yet at peak expression
    97|Visual: Eyebrows rising but not fully, eyes still engaged not widened
    98|        Hands possibly in motion toward face, body leaning toward
    99|Timing: 50-150ms after surprising stimulus
   100|Prompt: "pre-peak anticipation with eyebrows rising not yet fully elevated,
   101|        eyes still engaged not widened, body leaning toward,
   102|        50-150ms after stimulus before peak"
   103|Token: [EXPR_SURPRISE_PRE_PEAK]
   104|```
   105|
   106|**B2: PEAK REACTION OVERHOLD**
   107|```
   108|Description: Full surprise held slightly beyond natural duration
   109|Visual: Full eyebrow elevation sustained, hand(s) to face
   110|        Slight backward lean, mouth "O" fully open
   111|Timing: 300-600ms past natural de-escalation point
   112|Prompt: "surprise overexaggeration with full eyebrow elevation sustained,
   113|        hands to face, mouth O fully open, held 300-600ms past peak natural duration"
   114|Token: [EXPR_SURPRISE_OVERHOLD]
   115|```
   116|
   117|### Category C: Fatigue-Sleep States
   118|
   119|**C1: SLEEPY DROWSINESS (Not Yet Asleep)**
   120|```
   121|Description: Approaching sleep but not there — awareness fluctuating
   122|Visual: Eyelids 30-50% closure, blinks lasting 400-700ms (normal 100-200ms)
   123|        Head forward droop developing, body sinking into support
   124|Prompt: "sleepy drowsiness with eyelids drooping 30-50% closed,
   125|        single blinks lasting 400-700ms, head forward drooping,
   126|        body sinking into support"
   127|Token: [EXPR_DROWSINESS]
   128|```
   129|
   130|**C2: MICRO-SLEEP FRAGMENT (Involuntary)**
   131|```
   132|Description: Brief loss of awareness 2-10 seconds
   133|Visual: Sudden head drop to chest, eyelid flutter, body jerk
   134|        Recovery: startled reawakening 2-5 seconds later
   135|Prompt: "micro-sleep fragment with sudden head drop chin to chest,
   136|        eyelid flutter, body jerk, 2-10 seconds duration"
   137|Token: [EXPR_MICRO_SLEEP]
   138|```
   139|
   140|**C3: FATIGUE PAIN (Accumulated)**
   141|```
   142|Description: Accumulated fatigue showing on face
   143|Visual: Malar flush on cheekbones, under-eye puffiness/dark circles
   144|        Shoulders elevated forward, mouth slightly open for breathing
   145|Prompt: "fatigue face with malar flush concentrated on cheekbones,
   146|        under-eye puffiness and darkened circles, shoulders elevated forward,
   147|        mouth slightly open facilitating breathing"
   148|Token: [EXPR_FATIGUE_FACE]
   149|```
   150|
   151|### Category D: Distraction-Interruption States
   152|
   153|**D1: MID-SENTENCE INTERRUPTION**
   154|```
   155|Description: Person talking, photographed while mid-thought
   156|Visual: Mouth still in position for recently finished word
   157|        Eyes looking at something else mouth wasn't addressed to
   158|        Eyebrows in position appropriate to thought being held
   159|Prompt: "mid-sentence interruption with mouth still forming finished word,
   160|        eyes not synchronized with mouth, looking elsewhere,
   161|        eyebrows still in expression position from prior thought"
   162|Token: [EXPR_MID_SENTENCE]
   163|```
   164|
   165|**D2: ATTENTION MIGRATION (Partially There)**
   166|```
   167|Description: Attention divided — part engaged with camera, part with something else
   168|Visual: Eyes looking at camera but focus "through" it at something else
   169|        Mouth slight smile but eyes not reciprocating
   170|        One eyebrow raised one neutral (divided attention)
   171|Prompt: "attention divided with eyes looking at camera but focused through,
   172|        mouth smile not supported by eyes, one eyebrow raised one neutral,
   173|        body shoulders angled back toward distraction source"
   174|Token: [EXPR_ATTENTION_DIVIDED]
   175|```
   176|
   177|### Category E: Cognitive Load Expressions
   178|
   179|**E1: THINKING FACE (Mid-Process)**
   180|```
   181|Description: Working through thought — not yet reached conclusion
   182|Visual: Gaze upward and lateral (searching for words/memory)
   183|        Eyebrows slightly inward contracted (Corrugator)
   184|        Lips pressed or slight protrusion, head slight lateral tilt
   185|Duration: 2-30 seconds depending on complexity
   186|Prompt: "thinking face with gaze upward and lateral searching,
   187|        eyebrows contracted inward, lips pressed or protruding,
   188|        head tilted laterally, 2-30 seconds duration"
   189|Token: [EXPR_THINKING]
   190|```
   191|
   192|**E2: THOUGHT INTERRUPTION (Just Got Idea)**
   193|```
   194|Description: Mid-thought, idea strikes suddenly
   195|Visual: Sudden eyebrow raise (frontalis), eye roll-up straight not lateral
   196|        Mouth small "o" or lips parted "oh", gesture frozen mid-air
   197|Prompt: "thought interruption with sudden eyebrow raise and eye roll-up,
   198|        mouth forming small o, hands frozen mid-gesture,
   199|        brief recognition flash before full engagement"
   200|Token: [EXPR_THOUGHT_IDEA]
   201|```
   202|
   203|### Category F: Social Inhibition Expressions
   204|
   205|**F1: SUPPRESSED LAUGHTER**
   206|```
   207|Description: Something funny but social context requires suppression
   208|Visual: Orbicularis oculi WITHOUT full mouth engagement (crow's feet, slight upturn)
   209|        Head turn/duck away, hand to mouth covering, shoulder elevation
   210|Prompt: "suppressed laughter with eye engagement present crow's feet visible,
   211|        mouth just slightly upturned, hand to mouth covering,
   212|        head turning away, shoulder elevated"
   213|Token: [EXPR_LAUGH_SUPPRESSED]
   214|```
   215|
   216|**F2: EXPRESSION ASYMMETRY (Controlled/Uncontrolled)**
   217|```
   218|Description: One side expressing state while other maintains control
   219|Visual: One corner more elevated than other, one eyebrow raised other neutral
   220|        One eye engaged while other neutral
   221|Prompt: "expression asymmetry with one corner mouth elevated asymmetric,
   222|        one eyebrow raised one neutral, one eye engaged one neutral,
   223|        controlled versus genuine self visible"
   224|Token: [EXPR_ASYMMETRIC]
   225|```
   226|
   227|### Category G: Residual Expression States
   228|
   229|**G1: POST-EMOTION RESIDUAL**
   230|```
   231|Description: Expression complete but muscles not fully returned to neutral
   232|Visual: Nasolabial folds still slightly deepened, residual crow's feet
   233|        Mouth corner slight upward turn, eyebrows not fully returned
   234|Duration: 1-3 seconds after expression resolves
   235|Prompt: "post-emotion residual with nasolabial folds still deepened,
   236|        residual crow's feet visible, mouth corner still slightly upturned,
   237|        1-3 seconds post-expression"
   238|Token: [EXPR_RESIDUAL]
   239|```
   240|
   241|**G2: EMOTION-CONTAMINATED NEUTRAL**
   242|```
   243|Description: Face trying to return to neutral but emotion bleeds through
   244|Visual: Slight mouth corner elevation, brow almost neutral but slight inner raise
   245|        Eye brightness remaining from recent positive emotion
   246|Prompt: "emotion-contaminated neutral with slight mouth corner elevation,
   247|        brow almost neutral with subtle inner raise suggesting recent humor,
   248|        residual eye brightness from positive emotion"
   249|Token: [EXPR_CONTAMINATED_NEUTRAL]
   250|```
   251|
   252|---
   253|
   254|## COMPLETENESS SPECTRUM
   255|
   256|```
   257|LEVEL 0: NO EXPRESSION (neutral baseline)
   258|LEVEL 1: ANTICIPATORY (beginning but not externally visible)
   259|LEVEL 2: ONSET (micro-expression under 200ms)
   260|LEVEL 3: EMERGING (expression beginning to claim face)
   261|LEVEL 4: PEAK (fully formed expression)
   262|LEVEL 5: POST-PEAK (dissolving, residual activation)
   263|LEVEL 6: RETURNING (almost neutral but contamination visible)
   264|
   265|Distribution Target:
   266|- 50% non-peak (LEVEL 1-2, LEVEL 5-6)
   267|- 30% peak expressions (natural timing)
   268|- 15% interrupted or incomplete
   269|- 5% overexaggerated (specific character types)
   270|```
   271|
   272|---
   273|
   274|## UNFINISHED_EXPRESSION_SYSTEM
   275|
   276|**TYPE_1: CUT-OFF SMILE**
   277|```
   278|What Missing: Onset present but mouth doesn't fully engage
   279|Visual: Mouth opens slightly then freezes rather than drawing back
   280|Reader: "Something interrupted before smile could complete"
   281|Prompt: "smile_onset_mouth_slightly_open_before_full_engagement
   282|        orbicularis_incomplete_activation expression_cut"
   283|Token: [UNFINISHED_CUTOFF_SMILE]
   284|```
   285|
   286|**TYPE_2: HELD LAUGH**
   287|```
   288|What Missing: Laugh begins but held back internally
   289|Visual: Eye engagement present, mouth just slightly upturned, breath held
   290|Reader: "Something very funny but subject chose not to fully laugh"
   291|Prompt: "genuine_laugh_suppressed_hand_to_mouth_breath_held
   292|        orbicularis_fully_active_mouth_slight_smile"
   293|Token: [UNFINISHED_HELD_LAUGH]
   294|```
   295|
   296|**TYPE_3: FADING EXPRESSION**
   297|```
   298|What Missing: Already dissolving when captured (peak missed)
   299|Visual: Nasolabial partially deepened, residual eye crinkling, mouth returning
   300|Reader: "This expression was real and already passing"
   301|Prompt: "expression_fading_smile_residual_nasolabial_crowfeet
   302|        activation_300ms_post_peak_level_moderate"
   303|Token: [UNFINISHED_FADING]
   304|```
   305|
   306|**TYPE_4: MISALIGNED EXPRESSION**
   307|```
   308|What Missing: Simultaneous contradictory emotional positions
   309|Visual: Eyes showing attention to environment, mouth showing engagement with camera/person
   310|Reader: "Attention and expression divided — caught between two states"
   311|Prompt: "divided_attention_face_eye_looking_at_mouth_smile_asymmetric
   312|        left_eye_right_mouth_mismatch simultaneous_contradiction"
   313|Token: [UNFINISHED_MISALIGNED]
   314|```
   315|
   316|**TYPE_5: STATED-THEN-INTERRUPTED**
   317|```
   318|What Missing: Residual markers from earlier event + current different state
   319|Visual: Residual Duchenne markers (eye crinkling) + current neutral/negative
   320|Reader: "This face was just laughing — caught in transition back"
   321|Prompt: "post_expression_residual_smile_current_state_neutral
   322|        transition_ongoing muscle_return_rate_slow"
   323|Token: [UNFINISHED_STATED_INTERRUPTED]
   324|```
   325|
   326|---
   327|
   328|## INSTABILITY TYPE DISTRIBUTION
   329|
   330|```
   331|Sleepy-joy combos: 15-20%
   332|Laugh interruption: 20-25%
   333|Distracted mid-expression: 20-25%
   334|Cognitive interruption: 10-15%
   335|Residual expression: 15-20%
   336|```
   337|
   338|---
   339|
   340|## TOKEN LIBRARY

================================================================================
## V15 SMARTPHONE GEOMETRY SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V15/ENGINE_V15_SMARTPHONE_GEOMETRY_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENGINE_V15_SMARTPHONE_GEOMETRY_SYSTEM.md
     2|
     3|## V15 Core Module — Smartphone Distortion + Geometry
     4|### AREA: 05 (Smartphone Distortion) | Status: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     5|
     6|---
     7|
     8|## PURPOSE
     9|
    10|Smartphone cameras create characteristic geometric distortions at close range (30-60cm). These arise from wide-angle lens physics, small sensors, and the "arms-length selfie" pose. Understanding these distortions allows precise emulation of authentic smartphone photography aesthetics.
    11|
    12|---
    13|
    14|## KEY CONCEPTS
    15|
    16|**Distortion Zones**: A (Extreme <30cm), B (Close 30-60cm), C (Medium 60-100cm), D (Normal >100cm)
    17|
    18|**Proximity Gradient**: Inverted from natural vision — closer parts appear LARGER
    19|
    20|**HK-Specific Scenarios**: Steam bathrooms, MTR crowded contact, convenience store fluorescent, arm-extended upward angle
    21|
    22|---
    23|
    24|## SMARTPHONE_GEOMETRY_SYSTEM
    25|
    26|### Lens Physics Baselines
    27|
    28|```
    29|| Lens Type    | Focal Length | FOV      | Distortion |
    30||--------------|--------------|----------|------------|
    31|| Ultra-wide   | 13-16mm      | 118-123° | Severe     |
    32|| Wide         | 24-27mm      | 84-90°   | Moderate   |
    33|| Standard     | 28-35mm      | 75-84°   | Mild       |
    34|| Telephoto    | 50mm+        | 46°      | Negligible |
    35|
    36|Modern smartphones: Ultra-wide (0.5x) or Wide (1x) as defaults
    37|```
    38|
    39|### Distortion Zones
    40|
    41|**ZONE A: EXTREME PROXIMITY** (< 30cm)
    42|```
    43|Forehead enlargement: 15-25% vertical stretch
    44|Nose-tip protrusion: 8-12% forward bias
    45|Chin compression: 5-10% vertical squash
    46|Ear recession: 10-15% apparent size reduction
    47|Token: [ZONE_A_EXTREME]
    48|```
    49|
    50|**ZONE B: CLOSE RANGE** (30-60cm)
    51|```
    52|Knee enlargement: 20-35% (arms-length pose)
    53|Shoulder widening: 12-18% horizontal stretch
    54|Hand/finger elongation: 10-20%
    55|Forehead stretching: 8-12%
    56|Token: [ZONE_B_CLOSE]
    57|```
    58|
    59|**ZONE C: MEDIUM RANGE** (60-100cm)
    60|```
    61|Mild barrel distortion only
    62|Proportions approach orthoscopic
    63|Background elements begin perspective compression
    64|Token: [ZONE_C_MEDIUM]
    65|```
    66|
    67|**ZONE D: NORMAL RANGE** (> 100cm)
    68|```
    69|Near-zero geometric distortion
    70|Standard portrait proportions restored
    71|Token: [ZONE_D_NORMAL]
    72|```
    73|
    74|### Barrel Distortion Curve
    75|
    76|```
    77|BARREL_K_FACTOR = 0.15 (wide angle default)
    78|K_ULTRA_WIDE = 0.28 (0.5x lens)
    79|K_WIDE = 0.12 (1x lens)
    80|
    81|Center pulls IN, edges push OUT
    82|Human face at 40cm: nose 12% too large, ears 18% too small
    83|```
    84|
    85|---
    86|
    87|## PROXIMITY_DISTORTION_LIBRARY
    88|
    89|**ENLARGED_KNEES**
    90|```
    91|Cause: Arm-length shooting + low angle + wide lens
    92|Magnitude: 20-35% apparent size increase
    93|Visual: Knees nearest camera pushed toward viewer
    94|Trigger: legs-extended pose, sitting on edge, squat
    95|Token: [KNEES_PROXIMAL] [WIDE_LENS] [LOW_ANGLE]
    96|```
    97|
    98|**WIDENED_SHOULDERS**
    99|```
   100|Cause: Perpendicular orientation to plane of focus
   101|Magnitude: 12-18% horizontal expansion
   102|Visual: Upper body trapezius widens toward edges
   103|Trigger: Full-body selfie, mirror shot
   104|Token: [SHOULDERS_BARREL] [EDGE_DISTORTION] [FULL_BODY_SELFIE]
   105|```
   106|
   107|**STRETCHED_FOREHEAD**
   108|```
   109|Cause: Face tilted forward at extreme proximity
   110|Magnitude: 8-15% vertical elongation
   111|Visual: Hairline recedes, upper face dominates
   112|Trigger: Makeup selfie, chin-up angle
   113|Token: [FOREHEAD_STRETCH] [TILTED_FORWARD] [EXTREME_PROXIMITY]
   114|```
   115|
   116|**ARM_LENGTH_DISTORTION**
   117|```
   118|Cause: Arm extended, camera closer to lower body
   119|Magnitude: 15-25% foreshortening bias
   120|Visual: Torso/hips compressed, limbs elongated
   121|Trigger: Full-length arm selfie, grooming videos
   122|Token: [ARM_EXTENDED] [LOWER_BODY_PROXIMAL] [FATAL_PROPORTION]
   123|```
   124|
   125|**FINGER_ELONGATION**
   126|```
   127|Cause: Fingers extended toward lens in grooming context
   128|Magnitude: 10-20% length increase
   129|Trigger: Applying makeup, skincare, hair styling
   130|Token: [FINGER_PROXIMAL] [WIDE_CONTEXT] [EXTENDED_HAND]
   131|```
   132|
   133|**LENS_CURVATURE_EDGE_EFFECT**
   134|```
   135|Cause: Barrel distortion pulls vertical lines inward
   136|Magnitude: 5-12% edge compression
   137|Visual: Sides of frame curve inward, center stretches
   138|Trigger: Mirror selfies, full-length mirror shots
   139|Token: [LENS_CURVATURE] [MIRROR_FRAME] [EDGE_COMPRESSION]
   140|```
   141|

   144|## HK_SPECIFIC_DISTORTION_SCENARIOS
   145|
   146|**HK_ARM_EXTENDED_UPWARD_ANGLE** `[HK]`
   147|```
   148|Cause: Arm extended overhead, phone tilted upward 25-40°
   149|Magnitude: 15-25% chin elongation + neck foreshortening
   150|Visual: Double chin minimized, throat exposed, Adam's apple prominent
   151|Context: HK clubbing photos, dim sum brunch selfies
   152|Token: [ARM_OVERHEAD] [UPWARD_ANGLE] [NECK_FORESHORTEN] [THROAT_EXPOSED]
   153|Note: HK variant emphasizes neck elongation for V-face perception
   154|```
   155|
   156|**HK_BATHROOM_MIRROR_WIDE_ANGLE_PROXIMITY** `[HK]`
   157|```
   158|Cause: 15-25cm distance to steam-fogged mirror in small HK bathrooms
   159|Magnitude: Severe barrel distortion on upper body
   160|Visual: Shoulders 20-30% too wide, face slightly elongated
   161|Context: Post-shower steam, humid environment, tiled walls
   162|Token: [STEAM_MIRROR] [PROXIMAL_MIRROR] [SHOULDERS_BARREL] [FOG_EDGE]
   163|Note: Mirror fog creates natural vignette, edges softer
   164|```
   165|
   166|**HK_MTR_CROWDED_CONTACT_PROXIMITY** `[HK]`
   167|```
   168|Cause: Arm raised in crowd, 20-35cm from other passengers
   169|Magnitude: Unintentional body contact blur + motion
   170|Visual: Elbows and shoulders of others in frame edges
   171|Context: MTR rush hour, standing room only, intimate proximity
   172|Token: [MTR_CROWD] [PROXIMAL_STRANGER] [ARM_RAISED] [MOTION_BLUR]
   173|Note: Authenticity marker — other bodies partially in frame
   174|```
   175|
   176|**HK_CONVENIENCE_STORE_FLUORESCENT_ANGLE_SHOT** `[HK]`
   177|```
   178|Cause: Fluorescent tube lighting + shooting at 30-45° angle
   179|Magnitude: Color temperature distortion + lens flare
   180|Visual: Greenish tint from fluorescent, skin appears slightly sallow
   181|Context: 7-11, OK便利店, fluorescent tubes at 6500K equivalent
   182|Token: [FLUORESCENT_LIGHT] [ANGLE_SHOT] [GREEN_TINT] [SALLOW_SKIN]
   183|Note: Fluorescent creates flat lighting, minimal shadows
   184|```
   185|
   186|**HK_NIGHTTIME_STREET_SELFIE_DISTORTION** `[HK]`
   187|```
   188|Cause: Low-light forces wider aperture + longer focal length
   189|Magnitude: Soft focus edges, slight barrel on lit signage
   190|Visual: Neon reflections on wet skin, bokeh on background
   191|Context: Temple Street, Mong Kok night market, humid air
   192|Token: [LOW_LIGHT] [NEON_REFLECT] [WET_SKIN_SHINE] [BOKEH_BACKGROUND]
   193|Note: Humidity adds skin sheen amplification
   194|```
   195|
   196|**HK_WHITENER_CREAM_GLOW_DISTORTION** `[HK]`
   197|```
   198|Cause: PAO cream / whitening products create strong light diffusion
   199|Magnitude: 10-15% facial luminosity increase, soft focus effect
   200|Visual: Skin appears "glowy" with diffused edges
   201|Context: Common skincare in HK humidity, SPF50+ with whitening
   202|Token: [WHITENING_GLOW] [DIFFUSED_SKIN] [SPF_LUMINOSITY] [SOFT_EDGE]
   203|Note: Product residue creates light scattering on skin surface
   204|```
   205|
   206|---
   207|
   208|## ARM_LENGTH_PERSPECTIVE_RULES
   209|
   210|**RULE_01: INVERTED PROXIMITY GRADIENT**
   211|```
   212|Closer body parts appear LARGER (opposite of natural vision)
   213|At 40cm: subject's knees can be 35% "larger" than head
   214|```
   215|
   216|**RULE_02: 30-DEGREE EXPANSION RULE**
   217|```
   218|Subjects at 30° to camera axis appear 8-12% wider
   219|Perpendicular body segments widest
   220|```
   221|
   222|**RULE_03: COMPRESSION-FILL COMPENSATION**
   223|```
   224|Distortion in one axis causes apparent compression in perpendicular axis
   225|Wide shoulders = slightly flattened chest depth
   226|```
   227|
   228|**RULE_04: SEQUENTIAL PROXIMITY MATCH**
   229|```
   230|Camera-to-knees distance MUST BE LESS than camera-to-head distance
   231|If head is at 60cm → knees at 30-40cm → systematic lower body enlargement
   232|```
   233|
   234|**RULE_05: SKIN PROXIMITY EMPHASIS**
   235|```
   236|Close-range skin texture amplified (pores visible)
   237|Wetness/sheen exaggerated in same proportion
   238|Sweat, water, skincare products all amplified
   239|```
   240|
   241|**RULE_06: HK ARM-OVERHEAD RULE**
   242|```
   243|Arm overhead creates vertical proximity gradient INVERSE to standard
   244|Camera closer to face than torso → face enlargement, torso compression
   245|Chin elongation + neck foreshortening dominant effect
   246|```
   247|
   248|**RULE_07: STEAM CHAMBER AMPLIFICATION**
   249|```
   250|Humid enclosed space (bathroom) softens edge definition
   251|Distortion becomes less geometric, more diffuse
   252|Skin appears more uniform, less textured
   253|```
   254|
   255|---

================================================================================
## V15 POST-SWIM SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V15/ENGINE_V15_POST_SWIM_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENGINE_V15_POST_SWIM_SYSTEM.md
     2|
     3|## V15 Core Module — Wet Hair Mechanics + Post-Swim Behavioral
     4|### AREA: 06 (Wet Hair Post-Swim) | Status: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     5|
     6|---
     7|
     8|## PURPOSE
     9|
    10|Post-swim appearance carries distinctive realism markers: wet tangled strands, chlorine-affected dryness, reduced alertness, relaxed musculature, and genuine tiredness. This "just-swam" state combines authenticity and desirability through physics-first wet hair behavior, fatigue sexiness, and post-swim behavioral mechanics.
    11|
    12|---
    13|
    14|## KEY CONCEPTS
    15|
    16|**Wet Hair Physics**: Hydration weight, tangle topology, chlorine/salt interaction
    17|
    18|**Fatigue Sexiness**: Sleepy eyes, tired smile, exhausted posture, relaxed gait
    19|
    20|**Post-Swim Behavioral**: Uncoordinated grace, water toss, cold shiver, towel handling
    21|
    22|---
    23|
    24|## WET_HAIR_MECHANICS
    25|
    26|**HYDRATION_WEIGHT**
    27|```
    28|Wet hair weighs 20-40% more than dry
    29|Strand diameter increases 15-25%
    30|Gravity creates lengthward elongation
    31|Visual: Longer appearance, reduced volume at crown
    32|Token: [WET_HEAVY] [STRAND_EXPANDED] [GRAVITY_PULL]
    33|```
    34|
    35|**TANGLE_TOPOLOGY**
    36|```
    37|Post-swim tangles: irregular, clumped sections
    38|Less "styled" than deliberate teased wet-look
    39|Random knot formations at nape, behind ears
    40|Token: [UNTANGLED_CLUMP] [IRREGULAR_KNOT] [POST_SWIM_TANGLE]
    41|```
    42|
    43|**CHLORINE_INTERACTION**
    44|```
    45|Chlorine binds to hair cuticle, removes natural oils
    46|Creates: dullness, slight greenish tint (blondes), rough texture
    47|Hair becomes: porous, absorbent, matte finish
    48|Token: [CHLORINE_MATTE] [POROUS_TEXTURE] [CUTICLE_STRIPPED]
    49|```
    50|
    51|**SEA_SALT_INTERACTION** (alternative)
    52|```
    53|Salt crystallizes on strand surface
    54|Creates: crunchy texture, enhanced wave definition
    55|Slightly lighter color (bleaching effect)
    56|Token: [SALT_CRYSTAL] [CRUNCHY_TEXTURE] [WAVE_ENHANCED]
    57|```
    58|
    59|**WATER_DRIP_SIGNATURE**
    60|```
    61|Isolated droplets on nape, shoulders, collarbone
    62|Beading pattern: irregular, gravity-determined
    63|Drip rate: immediate post-swim (heavy to light over 5-15 min)
    64|Token: [WATER_DRIP] [DRIP_TRICKLE] [COLLARBONE_DROPS]
    65|```
    66|
    67|---
    68|
    69|## FATIGUE_SEXINESS_MODULE
    70|
    71|**SLEEPY_EYES**
    72|```
    73|Pupils slightly dilated (post-exertion relaxation)
    74|Eyelids heavy, 5-15% more closed than alert state
    75|Sclera shows slight redness (capillary flush)
    76|Token: [SLEEPY_HEAVY_LID] [DILATED_PUPIL] [CAPILLARY_FLUSH]
    77|```
    78|
    79|**TIRED_SMILE**
    80|```
    81|Genuine smile with reduced muscle tension
    82|Slightly asymmetric (natural fatigue asymmetry)
    83|Corners of mouth 2-5° lower than full-energy smile
    84|Accompanied by cheek rise, softened eye crinkle
    85|Token: [RELAXED_SMILE] [ASYMMETRIC_LOWER] [SOFT_CHEEK]
    86|```
    87|
    88|**EXHAUSTED_POSTURE**
    89|```
    90|Shoulder elevation reduced (dropped shoulders)
    91|Upper spine posterior curve (slight slouch)
    92|Neck tilt: chin slightly elevated, throat exposed
    93|Hip shift: weight distribution more relaxed, uneven
    94|Token: [DROPPED_SHOULDERS] [SLIGHT_SLOUCH] [NAPE_EXPOSED]
    95|```
    96|
    97|**RELAXED_GAIT_AND_MOVEMENT**
    98|```
    99|Arms slightly abducted from body
   100|Steps slower, less bouncy
   101|Movement efficiency over style
   102|Token: [RELAXED_GAIT] [SLOW_STEPS] [ARM_ABDUCTED]
   103|```
   104|
   105|**FLUSHED_SKIN**
   106|```
   107|Capillary dilation from exertion + cool-down
   108|Cheeks: warmer tone (0.5-2 skin tone shades rosy)
   109|Neck/chest: visible flush gradient
   110|Skin texture: slightly dewy (residual moisture)
   111|Token: [CAPILLARY_FLUSH] [WARM_CHEEKS] [DEWY_TEXTURE]
   112|```
   113|
   114|---
   115|
   116|## FATIGUE_SEXINESS_BEHAVIORAL_MECHANICS (EXTENDED)
   117|
   118|**HEAVY_LID_DROOP**
   119|```
   120|Direct fixation requires more effort post-swim
   121|Gaze becomes slightly unfocused / distant
   122|Eye contact breaks more frequently (natural, not shy)
   123|Blink rate increases 10-20% (fatigue marker)
   124|Token: [UNFOCUSED_GAZE] [BLINK_RATE_UP] [CONTACT_BREAK]
   125|```
   126|
   127|**THROAT_EXPOSURE_TILT**
   128|```
   129|Chin lifts slightly to compensate for heavy eyelids
   130|Exposes submental area and throat
   131|Creates vulnerability signal (relaxation + fatigue)
   132|Token: [CHIN_LIFT] [THROAT_OPEN] [VULNERABILITY_SIGNAL]
   133|```
   134|
   135|**WEIGHT_SHIFT_RELAXATION**
   136|```
   137|Standing: hip sways, one leg relaxed, slight lean
   138|Sitting: spine curves, head tilts back against support
   139|Creates S-curve silhouette vs alert straight line
   140|Token: [HIP_SWAY] [SPINE_CURVE] [DELIBERATE_MOVEMENT]
   141|```
   142|
   143|**ARM_HEAVINESS**
   144|```
   145|Arms hang with reduced muscle tone
   146|Hands rest on surfaces (not actively posed)
   147|Fingers slightly curled (relaxed flexion)
   148|Elbows rest on tables, knees, or own shoulders
   149|Token: [ARM_HEAVY] [HAND_REST] [RELAXED_FLEXION] [ELBOW_REST]
   150|```
   151|
   152|**SHOULDER_RELEASE**
   153|```
   154|Trapezius muscles visibly released
   155|Shoulders drop 1-3cm from alert position
   156|Creates elongated neck appearance
   157|Shoulder line slopes toward viewer
   158|Token: [SHOULDER_RELEASE] [TRAPEZIUS_DOWN] [NECK_LENGTHEN]
   159|```
   160|
   161|**BREATH_RHYTHM_VISUAL**
   162|```
   163|Post-swim breath rate still elevated
   164|Chest rises/falls more visible than resting
   165|Creates subtle movement even in static poses
   166|Accompanied by slightly parted lips
   167|Token: [BREATH_VISIBLE] [CHEST_RISE] [SLIGHTLY_PARTED]
   168|```
   169|
   170|**LAZY_EYE_RUB**
   171|```
   172|Back of hand rubs eye area (not dainty, functional)
   173|Rub is slow, eyes close during rub
   174|Accompanied by slight squint release
   175|Token: [EYE_RUB] [SLOW_RUB] [SQUINT_RELEASE]
   176|```
   177|
   178|**MOUTH_GAPE**
   179|```
   180|Jaw relaxes, mouth slightly open
   181|Not dramatic, just slack
   182|Tongue may press against teeth
   183|Creates vacant, unfocused, "just swam" expression
   184|Token: [JAW_SLACK] [MOUTH_GAPE] [VACANT_EXPRESSION]
   185|```
   186|
   187|**PROVOCATIVE_LAZINESS**
   188|```
   189|Post-swim fatigue removes performance anxiety
   190|Actions become less coordinated, more honest
   191|Sexual availability signals increase (unconscious)
   192|Eye contact is slower, more deliberate when it occurs
   193|Token: [NO_PERFORMANCE] [HONEST_SIGNAL] [LAZY_SEXUAL]
   194|```
   195|
   196|---
   197|
   198|## POST_SWIM_BEHAVIORAL_MECHANICS (EXTENDED)
   199|
   200|**UNCOORDINATED_GRACE**
   201|```
   202|Post-swim movement is genuine-fresh (not staged)
   203|Hair adjustment attempts: multiple small touches
   204|Expression: neutral with micro-flinch at cold air
   205|Token: [FRESH_WET] [MULTI_TOUCH_HAIR] [COLD_FLICH]
   206|```
   207|
   208|**WATER_TOSS_MECHANICS**
   209|```
   210|Head toss to clear eyes: incomplete, water still in hair
   211|Animation: slower than dry hair flip, follows gravity briefly
   212|Ends with slight head shake, residual drips
   213|Token: [INCOMPLETE_TOSS] [GRAVITY_FOLLOW] [RESIDUAL_DRIP]
   214|```
   215|
   216|**CHLORINE_SNIFF_RESPONSE**
   217|```
   218|Slight nose wrinkling at chlorine smell
   219|Occurs naturally, not performed
   220|Small nose scrunch, quick release
   221|Token: [CHLORINE_WRINKLE] [NATURAL_NOSE_SCRUNCH]
   222|```
   223|
   224|**SKIN_PRESS_RESPONSE**
   225|```
   226|Residual wetness on skin invites immediate wipe
   227|Hand goes to cheek, temple, or neck
   228|Quick, efficient, not pose-like
   229|Token: [WET_WIPE_REFLEX] [EFFICIENT_HAND] [CHEEK_WIPE]
   230|```
   231|
   232|**TOWEL_HANDLING**
   233|```
   234|Pat-dry motion (not rub) for hair
   235|Towel turban attempt: often loose, slides
   236|Hand holds towel in place (no clip/bands)
   237|Token: [PAT_DRY] [SLIDING_TURBAN] [HAND_HOLD]
   238|```
   239|
   240|**CHLORINE_SUNSCREEN_STICKY_RESIDUE**
   241|```
   242|Combination creates tacky texture
   243|Skin feels "gummy" when dry
   244|Especially visible on shoulders, upper arms, back of neck
   245|Touch response: fingers stick briefly when pressing
   246|Token: [STICKY_RESIDUE] [CHLORINE_SPF] [TACKY_TEXTURE]
   247|Note: Texture audible when fabric slides against skin
   248|```
   249|
   250|**POST_SWIM_GOOSEBUMPS**
   251|```
   252|Cool water triggers piloerection response
   253|Visible on shoulders, upper arms, sides of torso
   254|Accompanies slight shivering (not always visible)
   255|Creates skin texture detail (pores + goosebumps together)
   256|Timing: immediate post-swim, reduces after 5-10 min
   257|Token: [GOOSEBUMPS] [PILOERECTION] [COOL_RESPONSE]
   258|```
   259|
   260|**HAIR_STUCK_TO_POSTERIOR_CERVICAL**
   261|```
   262|Wet hair adheres to back of neck completely
   263|No air gap between hair and skin
   264|Creates visible hair strand patterns pressed into skin
   265|Water transfer visible: skin appears darker where wet
   266|Token: [HAIR_STUCK_BACK] [CERVICAL_WET] [STRAND_PRESS]
   267|```
   268|
   269|**TOWEL_MARK_ON_SHOULDER**
   270|```
   271|Sitting on damp towel creates impressions
   272|Visible rectangular pattern lines on shoulder blade
   273|Pattern: woven towel texture transfer
   274|Fades as skin dries or towel moved
   275|Token: [TOWEL_IMPRINT] [SHOULDER_MARK] [DAMP_SITTING]
   276|```
   277|
   278|**EXHAUSTED_BEACH_CHAIR_SITTING**
   279|```
   280|Body weight fully deposited in plastic chair
   281|Arms hang off sides, head tilts back
   282|Legs spread wider than alert sitting
   283|Chair creaks with each micro-movement
   284|Token: [DEPOSITED_SITTING] [CHAIR_CREEK] [ARM_HANG] [HEAD_BACK]
   285|```
   286|
   287|**POST_SWIM_MIRROR_SELFIE_ENERGY**
   288|```
   289|Standing at mirror, slight lean toward reflection
   290|Hand holds towel at chest (not dropped)
   291|Eyes checking hair status, not performing
   292|Slight exhale-fog on mirror surface
   293|Token: [MIRROR_ASSESS] [LEAN_REFLECT] [TOWEL_HOLD] [FOG_BREATH]
   294|```
   295|
   296|**MELTED_SUNSCREEN_RESIDUE**
   297|```
   298|SPF melts from body heat + sun exposure
   299|Creates white cast streaks on shoulders, collarbone
   300|Texture slightly chalky when touched
   301|Combined with sweat creates milky drips
   302|Token: [SPF_MELT] [WHITE_CAST] [CHALKY_RESIDUE] [MILKY_DRIP]
   303|```
   304|
   305|**WATER_DRIPPING_FROM_HAIR_ENDS**
   306|```
   307|Gravity pulls remaining water to lowest points
   308|Drip rate intermittent, 1 drop per 3-10 seconds
   309|Location hair tips especially at back and sides
   310|Creates dark wet spots on towel or floor beneath
   311|Token: [DRIP_FALL] [HAIR_TIP_DROP] [INTERMITTENT_DRIP]
   312|```
   313|
   314|**POST_SWIM_COLD_SHIVER**
   315|```
   316|Body temperature regulation response
   317|Visible small tremor in shoulders, arms
   318|Occurs immediately post-swim after leaving water
   319|Duration 30-60 seconds of visible shivering
   320|May be suppressed by sunlight exposure
   321|Token: [COLD_SHIVER] [BODY_TREMOR] [THERMAL_REGULATE]
   322|```
   323|
   324|**CHLORINE_HAND_SMELL**
   325|```
   326|Distinctive chemical odor on hands
   327|Triggers smell-specific micro-expression
   328|Nose scrunch + slight upper lip lift
   329|Token: [CHLORINE_ODOR] [HAND_SMELL] [CHEMICAL_SCRUNCH]
   330|```
   331|
   332|**BEACH_SAND_IN_BIKINI_LINE**
   333|```
   334|Sand adheres to wet skin in intimate areas
   335|Creates gritty texture in bikini edges
   336|Especially bikini bottom lines, underband
   337|Token: [SAND_STICK] [WET_GRIT] [BIKINI_ADHERE]
   338|```
   339|
   340|**POST_SWIM_LIPS_CHEKS_SALT**
   341|```
   342|Salt water residue creates taste response
   343|Tongue licks lips, slight lip smack
   344|Creates glistening momentary
   345|Token: [SALT_LICK] [LIP_SMACK] [TASTE_RESPONSE]
   346|```
   347|
   348|**INCOMPLETE_TOWEL_WRAP**
   349|```
   350|Towel gap reveals midriff or hip
   351|Wrapping is rushed, not adjusted
   352|One side higher than other
   353|Token: [TOWEL_GAP] [RUSHED_WRAP] [ASYMMETRIC_TOWEL]
   354|```
   355|
   356|---
   357|
   358|## WET_HAIR_FRAMING_SYSTEM
   359|
   360|**NAPE_MOISTURE_DETAIL**
   361|```
   362|Water pools in hairline at nape
   363|Drip pattern: single channel down center OR spray pattern scattered
   364|Token: [NAPE_DRIP] [CERVICAL_POOL] [WATER_COLLECT]
   365|```
   366|
   367|**SHOULDER_WATER_PATTERN**
   368|```
   369|Shoulder plane retains pooled water
   370|Gravity creates trailing droplets toward deltoid
   371|Shirt neckline shows wet front border
   372|Token: [SHOULDER_POOL] [DELTOID_DRIP] [WET_NECKLINE]
   373|```
   374|
   375|**POSTERIOR_CERVICAL_HAIR_ADHESION**
   376|```
   377|Wet hair sticks to back of neck
   378|Creates direct view of nape, hairline, cervical vertebrae bumps
   379|Hair separates in strands not uniform coverage
   380|Small water beads visible between hair strands on skin
   381|Token: [CERVICAL_ADHERE] [NAPE_BARE] [STRAND_SEPARATION]

   383|```
   384|
   385|**UPPER_BACK_HAIR_DRAPE**
   386|```
   387|Wet hair falls across upper back
   388|Strand groups cling to trapezius muscles
   389|Water drips along spine path
   390|Creates cool sensation visible in goosebump response

## V15 PHOTODUMP RHYTHM SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V15/ENGINE_V15_PHOTODUMP_RHYTHM_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|---
     2|name: ENGINE_V15_PHOTODUMP_RHYTHM_SYSTEM
     3|description: Photodump Rhythm System for authentic social media documentation
     4|areas: AREA 07
     5|version: V15
     6|status: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     7|---
     8|
     9|# ENGINE_V15_PHOTODUMP_RHYTHM_SYSTEM
    10|
    11|## Core Philosophy
    12|
    13|**Photodump** = posting multiple low-stakes photos in sequence, treating the camera as a documentation device rather than a performance tool. The subject doesn't know they're being photographed. The photographer isn't directing. The result feels like "found footage" of a real moment.
    14|
    15|Key distinction from posed content: **no aesthetic optimization**. The point is not to look good — it's to document that you were there.
    16|
    17|---
    18|
    19|## PHOTODUMP_RHYTHM_LIBRARY
    20|
    21|### Rhythm Types
    22|
    23|| Type | Description | Visual Markers | Prompt Token |
    24||------|-------------|----------------|--------------|
    25|| RAPID_FIRE | 3-5 shots within seconds | Identical lighting, similar pose, slight blur | [RAPID_FIRE] |
    26|| BURST_MODE | 8-15 shots over 1-2 minutes | Mixed expressions, outfit changes, movement | [BURST_MODE] |
    27|| SPREAD_DOC | 1 shot per hour over day | Different locations, consistent subject | [SPREAD_DOC] |
    28|| ACCIDENTAL | 1-2 shots total, unplanned | Awkward angle, blur, background dominate | [ACCIDENTAL_SHOT] |
    29|| EVIDENCE | Documenting specific object/moment | Subject secondary or absent | [EVIDENCE_SHOT] |
    30|
    31|### Modulation Profiles
    32|
    33|```
    34|PROFILE_A: LOW_EFFORT_AUTHENTIC
    35|- Shooting frequency: Random, spontaneous
    36|- Framing: Auto-composition (device defaults)
    37|- Subject awareness: Unaware or forgetful
    38|- Failure tolerance: HIGH (failures are authentic)
    39|- Token: [LOW_EFFORT_AUTHENTIC]
    40|
    41|PROFILE_B: DOCUMENTARY_CAPTURE
    42|- Shooting frequency: Consistent, pattern-based
    43|- Framing: Environmental context prioritized
    44|- Subject awareness: Forgotten camera
    45|- Failure tolerance: MEDIUM (some intentional blur)
    46|- Token: [DOCUMENTARY_CAPTURE]
    47|
    48|PROFILE_C: FRIEND_COLLECTION
    49|- Shooting frequency: Medium, conversational
    50|- Framing: 2+ subjects, group dynamics
    51|- Subject awareness: Semi-aware (cooperating friend)
    52|- Failure tolerance: HIGH (imperfect chemistry)
    53|- Token: [FRIEND_COLLECTION]
    54|
    55|PROFILE_D: TRAVEL_LOG
    56|- Shooting frequency: High volume, location-driven
    57|- Framing: Landmark + subject (landmark primary)
    58|- Subject awareness: Photo-taking is part of experience
    59|- Failure tolerance: LOW (travel photos are curated)
    60|- Token: [TRAVEL_LOG]
    61|```
    62|
    63|---
    64|
    65|## Prompt Grammar
    66|
    67|```
    68|[rhythm_type]_photodump_
    69|[modulation_profile]_
    70|[documenting_moment]:_[what_is_documented]_
    71|[subject_state]:_[awareness_level]_
    72|[device_type]:_[capture_mode]
    73|```
    74|
    75|**Examples:**
    76|```
    77|[BURST_MODE]_photodump_[LOW_EFFORT_AUTHENTIC]
    78|documenting_moment:beach_afternoon_sunset
    79|subject_state:swimming_in_fully_aware_could_be_photographed
    80|device_type:iphone_14_pro_auto_mode
    81|
    82|[EVIDENCE_SHOT]_photodump_[DOCUMENTARY_CAPTURE]
    83|documenting_moment:late_night_market_street_food
    84|subject_state:ordering_from_stall_half_turned_away
    85|device_type:android_auto_night_mode
    86|```
    87|
    88|---
    89|
    90|## HK-Specific Content
    91|
    92|- **MTR Journey Photodump**: Transit documentation, platform arrivals, crowd moments
    93|- **Tea Restaurant Photodump**: Ordering process, food arrival, incomplete dishes
    94|- **Night Market Photodump**: Street food discovery, walking documentation
    95|- **Ferry Crossing Photodump**: Harbour moments, outdoor deck sequences
    96|
    97|**HK Tokens:** [MTR_DOC] [TEA_RESTAURANT_DOC] [NIGHT_MARKET_DOC] [FERRY_DOC]
    98|
    99|---
   100|
   101|## Moderation Profile
   102|
   103|**PRESERVES:**
   104|- Casual settings (no professional staging)
   105|- Natural subject expressions (unaware)
   106|- Environmental authenticity (documentary context)
   107|
   108|**REMOVES:**
   109|- Aesthetic optimization signals
   110|- Professional lighting setups
   111|- Directed poses or expressions
   112|
   113|**WARNINGS:**
   114|- Avoid evidence shots that capture strangers without awareness
   115|- Travel log profile should not approach professional photography aesthetics
   116|
   117|---
   118|
   119|## Cross-References
   120|
   121|- Complements BAD_PHOTO_REALISM (accidental failures are photodump-native)
   122|- Complements ENVIRONMENTAL_AIR (environmental context is photodump priority)
   123|- HK-specific profiles integrate with SOCIAL_CAMERA operators (OP_13-OP_22)
   124|
   125|---
   126|
   127|*Module: ENGINE_V15_PHOTODUMP_RHYTHM_SYSTEM.md*
   128|*Source: AREA 07 — V15 Research*
   129|*Status: READY FOR INTEGRATION*
   130|

================================================================================
## V15 ENVIRONMENTAL AIR SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V15/ENGINE_V15_ENVIRONMENTAL_AIR_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|---
     2|name: ENGINE_V15_ENVIRONMENTAL_AIR_SYSTEM
     3|description: Environmental Air System for atmospheric contamination and layered air quality
     4|areas: AREA 08
     5|version: V15
     6|status: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     7|---
     8|
     9|# ENGINE_V15_ENVIRONMENTAL_AIR_SYSTEM
    10|
    11|## Core Philosophy
    12|
    13|Environmental "air" = the invisible atmospheric contamination that humans sense but rarely articulate. Humidity, pollution, temperature, condensation, steam, smoke — these invisible forces alter how humans look, feel, and photograph. V14 captured environment as backdrop. V15 captures environment as physical medium.
    14|
    15|---
    16|
    17|## ATMOSPHERIC_CONTAMINATION_SYSTEM
    18|
    19|### 7 Contamination Types
    20|
    21|| Type | Cause | Visual Signature | Token |
    22||------|-------|------------------|-------|
    23|| HUMIDITY_VISUAL | 80%+ RH, visible moisture in air | Skin sheen, hair frizz, fabric cling | [HUMIDITY_AIR] |
    24|| CONDENSATION_LAYER | Temperature differential, fog/mist | Soft focus background, halo effect | [CONDENSATION_AIR] |
    25|| FLUORESCENT_POLLUTION | Indoor artificial light mix | Green/yellow skin cast, flat shadows | [FLUORESCENT_AIR] |
    26|| PARTICULATE_MATTER | Pollution/haze, visibility reduction | Muted colors, soft contrast, gray haze | [PM_AIR] |
    27|| STEAM_SATURATION | Cooking, hot springs, sauna | White-out zones, silhouette edges | [STEAM_AIR] |
    28|| COLD_DRY_ATMOSPHERE | Winter conditions, AC | Skin tightness visible, chapped lips | [COLD_DRY_AIR] |
    29|| CHLORINE_SUSPENSION | Indoor pool, chemical smell visible | Chemical sheen on skin, eye redness | [CHLORINE_AIR] |
    30|
    31|---
    32|
    33|## INTENSITY SCALE (1-10)
    34|
    35|```
    36|1-3: AMBIENT — subtle atmospheric presence, barely noticeable
    37|4-6: NOTICEABLE — visible effects, subject aware of environment
    38|7-8: DOMINANT — environment is primary visual element
    39|9-10: EXTREME — environment overwhelms subject, atmospheric hazard
    40|```
    41|
    42|---
    43|
    44|## Prompt Grammar
    45|
    46|```
    47|[air_type]_atmosphere_
    48|[intensity]:[1-10]_
    49|[effect_on_subject]:_[specific_manifestation]_
    50|[visibility]:_[clear_to_obscured]
    51|```
    52|
    53|**Examples:**
    54|```
    55|[HUMIDITY_AIR]_atmosphere_8
    56|effect_on_subject:skin_glistening_hair_adsorbing_moisture
    57|visibility:clear_but_heavy
    58|
    59|[FLUORESCENT_AIR]_atmosphere_6
    60|effect_on_subject:skin_green_cast_underarm_pit_darkening
    61|visibility:interior_lit_environment
    62|
    63|[STEAM_AIR]_atmosphere_9
    64|effect_on_subject:face_silhouetted_partial_obscure
    65|visibility:obscured_50_percent
    66|```
    67|
    68|---
    69|
    70|## HK-Specific Content
    71|
    72|- **Summer Humidity**: 85-95% RH, sticky heat, visible sweat
    73|- **MTR Air Conditioning**: Cold recycled air, condensation on skin entering station
    74|- **Indoor Pool Chlorine**: Chemical suspension, red eyes, skin residue
    75|- **Night Market Grease**: Cooking steam, oil particles, warm humid mix
    76|- **Tunnel Wind**: Moving air visible in hair, fabric movement
    77|
    78|**HK Tokens:** [HONG_KONG_HUMID] [MTR_AC_CONTRAST] [POOL_CHLORINE_AIR] [NIGHT_MARKET_GREASE]
    79|
    80|---
    81|
    82|## Multi-Layer Approach
    83|
    84|For maximum authenticity, stack atmospheric layers:
    85|
    86|```
    87|BASE: [HUMIDITY_AIR] 7 (Hong Kong ambient)
    88|LAYER_1: [FLUORESCENT_AIR] 5 (indoor convenience store)
    89|LAYER_2: [CONDENSATION_AIR] 3 (entering cold AC from heat)
    90|RESULT: Subject visibly transitioning between environments, temperature differential visible on skin
    91|```
    92|
    93|---
    94|
    95|## Moderation Profile
    96|
    97|**PRESERVES:**
    98|- Natural environmental effects (sweat, skin sheen from heat)
    99|- Atmospheric authenticity (indoor pool chlorine smell visible)
   100|- Temperature-based visual markers (goosebumps, flushed skin)
   101|
   102|**REMOVES:**
   103|- Excessive air effects that obscure subject entirely
   104|- Overly dramatic atmospheric conditions (unless intentionally styled)
   105|
   106|**WARNINGS:**
   107|- Environmental air should enhance subject, not compete with subject for attention
   108|
   109|---
   110|
   111|*Module: ENGINE_V15_ENVIRONMENTAL_AIR_SYSTEM.md*
   112|*Source: AREA 08 — V15 Research*
   113|*Status: READY FOR INTEGRATION*
   114|

================================================================================
## V15 MICRO SOCIAL SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V15/ENGINE_V15_MICRO_SOCIAL_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|---
     2|name: ENGINE_V15_MICRO_SOCIAL_SYSTEM
     3|description: Micro Social Interaction System for authentic interpersonal moments
     4|areas: AREA 09
     5|version: V15
     6|status: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     7|---
     8|
     9|# ENGINE_V15_MICRO_SOCIAL_SYSTEM
    10|
    11|## Core Philosophy
    12|
    13|Micro social = the tiny, involuntary, real-time adjustments humans make toward each other. A hand on a shoulder, a glance, adjusting someone's hair, sharing a bite — moments so small they rarely make it into photography. These micro-interactions are the "glue" that makes subjects look like they're in relationship, not just adjacent.
    14|
    15|---
    16|
    17|## MICRO_SOCIAL_INTERACTION_LIBRARY
    18|
    19|### 5 Interaction Categories
    20|
    21|| Category | Type | Description | Token |
    22||----------|------|-------------|-------|
    23|| A | PRACTICAL_ADJUSTMENT | Functional touch: towel, hair, clothing | [PRACTICAL_ADJUST] |
    24|| B | PLAYFUL_TOUCH | Light, brief, consensual: splash, poke, tickle | [PLAYFUL_TOUCH] |
    25|| C | INTIMATE_GESTURE | Affectionate: hug, lean, hold | [INTIMATE_GESTURE] |
    26|| D | SOCIAL_GESTURE | Handshake, wave, high-five, fist bump | [SOCIAL_GESTURE] |
    27|| E | ENVIRONMENTAL_SHARE | Passing objects, pointing, directing attention | [ENV_SHARE] |
    28|
    29|---
    30|
    31|## INTERRUPTION_ACTION_SYSTEM
    32|
    33|### 5 Patterns
    34|
    35|| Pattern | What Happens | Visual Signature | Token |
    36||---------|--------------|------------------|-------|
    37|| B1 | TUCKING_BEHIND_EAR | Fixer tucks strand, brief ear contact | [EAR_TUCK] |
    38|| B2 | HAIR_FLIP_ASSIST | Hand through hair, gravity assist | [HAIR_FLIP_ASSIST] |
    39|| B3 | SHOULDER_TAP | Attention redirect, light touch | [SHOULDER_TAP] |
    40|| B4 | HAND_HOLD_ADJUST | Re-grasping, repositioning hands | [HAND_ADJUST] |
    41|| B5 | SPATIAL_REDIRECT | Hand pointing, body angle shift | [SPATIAL_REDIRECT] |
    42|
    43|### Candid Reaction Grammar (6 Rules)
    44|
    45|1. **Reaction precedes recognition** — Subject reacts to person before reacting to camera
    46|2. **Gaze vector indicates relationship** — Who subject looks at = who's important in frame
    47|3. **Touch = relationship marker** — Who touches whom, duration, intent
    48|4. **Body orientation follows social hierarchy** — Subject turns toward higher-status person
    49|5. **Expression matching** — Subject's expression mirrors interaction type
    50|6. **Environmental accommodation** — Subjects use environment as social prop
    51|
    52|---
    53|
    54|## Prompt Grammar
    55|
    56|```
    57|[micro_interaction]:[category]_
    58|[interruption_pattern]:[if_applicable]_
    59|[candid_reaction]:[rule_1-6_applied]_
    60|[gaze_vector]:_[target]_
    61|[touch_duration]:_[brief_prolonged]_
    62|[relationship_marker]:_[type]
    63|```
    64|
    65|**Examples:**
    66|```
    67|[PRACTICAL_ADJUST]_micro_social
    68|interruption_pattern:[EAR_TUCK]_hair_strand_behind_ear
    69|candid_reaction:subject_looks_at_friend_not_camera_first
    70|gaze_vector:friend_center_camera_right
    71|touch_duration:brief_under_1_second
    72|relationship_marker:sister_comfortable_intimate
    73|
    74|[PLAYFUL_TOUCH]_micro_social
    75|interruption_pattern:[SHOULDER_TAP]_attention_redirect_laugh_follows
    76|candid_reaction:expression_mirrors_social_gesture
    77|gaze_vector:friend_center_camera_left
    78|touch_duration:brief_flash_tap
    79|relationship_marker:close_friend_spontaneous
    80|```
    81|
    82|---
    83|
    84|## 76 Core Tokens
    85|
    86|**Practical:** [TOWEL_ADJUST] [HAIR_TUCK] [COLLAR_FIX] [SHOULDER_BRUSH] [ARM_CLEAR]
    87|**Playful:** [LIGHT_TAP] [GENTLE_POKE] [TICKLE_RESPONSE] [SPLASH_MOMENT] [HAIR_RUFFLE]
    88|**Intimate:** [LEAN_AGAINST] [ARM_AROUND] [HAND_HOLD] [FOREHEAD_TOUCH] [BACK_RUB]
    89|**Social:** [WAVE] [HIGH_FIVE] [FIST_BUMP] [HANDSHAKE] [POINT_SHARE]
    90|**Environmental:** [PASS_BOTTLE] [DIRECT_ATTENTION] [REACH_OVER] [SHARE_ITEM] [SPATIAL_GESTURE]
    91|
    92|**Reaction Tokens:** [GENUINE_LAUGH] [SURPRISE_BLINK] [CONFUSED_FURROW] [HAPPY_SCRUNCH] [CONTENT_SOFT] [INTERESTED_FORWARD]
    93|
    94|---
    95|
    96|## HK-Specific Content
    97|
    98|- **Tea Restaurant Sharing**: Chopstick food sharing, tea pouring, menu pointing
    99|- **MTR Crowding**: Accidental touch, spatial negotiation, ignore culture
   100|- **Karaoke Close**: Micro-social amplified by confined space
   101|- **BBQ Social**: Food sharing, fire proximity, casual intimacy
   102|
   103|**HK Tokens:** [TEA_RESTAURANT_SHARE] [MTR_CROWD_TOUCH] [KARAOKE_CLOSE] [BBQ_SHARE]
   104|
   105|---
   106|
   107|## Moderation Warnings
   108|
   109|⚠ **COERCIVE = BAD**: Subject visibly flinching, holding breath, frozen, eyes averted
   110|⚠ **ACCEPTABLE = GOOD**: Subject initiates or readily accepts, brief functional, mutual consent visible
   111|⚠ Practical adjustments: brief, functional, not sensual
   112|⚠ Never capture subjects in genuinely distressed states
   113|
   114|---
   115|
   116|## Distribution Targets
   117|
   118|- Category A (Practical): 30% — most common in HK social contexts
   119|- Category B (Playful): 20% — friends, casual relationships
   120|- Category C (Intimate): 25% — couples, close friends
   121|- Category D (Social): 15% — greeting, farewell moments
   122|- Category E (Environmental): 10% — active social scenes
   123|
   124|---
   125|
   126|## Cross-References
   127|
   128|- Complements SOCIAL_CAMERA (relationship dynamic drives interaction choice)
   129|- Complements FACE_FIRST (micro social triggers face expressions)
   130|- Complements CONTINUITY_PERSISTENCE (repeated interactions = relationship signal)
   131|
   132|---

   134|*Module: ENGINE_V15_MICRO_SOCIAL_SYSTEM.md*
