================================================================================
## V15 FACE-FIRST COMPOSITION SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V15/ENGINE_V15_FACE_FIRST_COMPOSITION_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|---
     2|name: ENGINE_V15_FACE_FIRST_COMPOSITION_SYSTEM
     3|description: Face-First Composition System — face as primary visual payload
     4|areas: AREA 10
     5|version: V15
     6|status: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     7|---
     8|
     9|# ENGINE_V15_FACE_FIRST_COMPOSITION_SYSTEM
    10|
    11|## Core Philosophy
    12|
    13|**Face-First**: The face is the gravitational center. Viewers look at the face first — every time, without exception. The body provides context; the face provides meaning. In V15, the face is not just a feature — it's the structural anchor around which everything else organizes.
    14|
    15|This is why face-first outperforms body-first: the body communicates action, the face communicates *reason* for action.
    16|
    17|---
    18|
    19|## FACE_PRIORITY_COMPOSITION_LIBRARY
    20|
    21|### System A: Facial Primacy Architecture (5 Rules)
    22|
    23|| Rule | Principle | Application |
    24||------|-----------|-------------|
    25|| FP_01 | Face brightness > body brightness | Face is lit, body accepts shade |
    26|| FP_02 | Face focus > body focus | Sharpest point = face, not background |
    27|| FP_03 | Face orientation leads body | Face direction determines crop |
    28|| FP_04 | Face expression justifies body | Body position matches facial emotion |
    29|| FP_05 | Face coverage > body coverage | More frame to face, less to environment |
    30|
    31|### Upper-Body Dominance Matrix
    32|
    33|| Type | Face % | Body % | Use Case | Token |
    34||------|--------|--------|----------|-------|
    35|| TIGHT_FACE | 70%+ | 5% | Emotion-focused, minimal context | [TIGHT_FACE] |
    36|| FACE_PRIMARY | 50-70% | 15-25% | Standard face-first | [FACE_PRIMARY] |
    37|| FACE_BALANCED | 35-50% | 30-40% | Environment-aware | [FACE_BALANCED] |
    38|| UPPER_BODY | 20-35% | 40-60% | Action with face legibility | [UPPER_BODY] |
    39|| CONTEXTUAL | 10-20% | 50-70% | Scene with face anchor | [CONTEXTUAL_FACE] |
    40|
    41|### Eye-Contact System (3 Components)
    42|
    43|| Component | Duration | Effect | Token |
    44||-----------|----------|--------|-------|
    45|| GLANCE | < 500ms | Brief acknowledgment | [EYE_GLANCE] |
    46|| SUSTAINED | 500-1500ms | Engagement, connection | [EYE_SUSTAINED] |
    47|| AVERTED | Subject looks away | Discomfort, distraction | [EYE_AVERTED] |
    48|
    49|**Eye-Contact Probability Matrix:**
    50|
    51|| Operator (from AREA 01) | Eye Contact Likelihood |
    52||------------------------|----------------------|
    53|| OP_01 Intimate Partner | 40% direct, 40% glance, 20% averted |
    54|| OP_05 Street Documentary | 10% direct, 30% glance, 60% averted |
    55|| OP_09 Elder Relative | 70% direct, 20% glance, 10% averted |
    56|| OP_11 Drunk Night | 50% direct, 20% glance, 30% averted |
    57|
    58|### Face Retention Architecture (5 Rules)
    59|
    60|1. **Minimum 30% of frame** — Face should occupy at least 30% of image area
    61|2. **Center or near-center** — Face should be in center third horizontally
    62|3. **Upper third priority** — Face should be in upper half of frame
    63|4. **No competing brightness** — Nothing in frame should be brighter than face
    64|5. **No competing focus** — Nothing should be sharper than face
    65|
    66|---
    67|
    68|## UPPER_BODY_FRAMING_GRAMMAR
    69|
    70|### Framing Types
    71|
    72|```
    73|STANDARD: [subject]_upper_body_face_primary
    74|- Face 50-70%, body 15-25%, environment 10-30%
    75|- Balanced composition
    76|
    77|TIGHT: [subject]_tight_face_emotional_focus
    78|- Face 70%+, body <5%
    79|- Intimate, expression-focused
    80|
    81|ENVIRONMENTAL: [subject]_face_anchor_scene_context
    82|- Face 20-35%, body 40-60%, environment 20-40%
    83|- Activity with face legibility
    84|
    85|PROFILE: [subject]_face_side_profile_contour
    86|- Face at 90° turn
    87|- Dramatic, contemplative
    88|
    89|THREE_QUARTER: [subject]_face_three_quarter_angle
    90|- Face at 45° turn
    91|- Classic flattering, legible expression
    92|```
    93|
    94|---
    95|
    96|## 64 Core Tokens
    97|
    98|**Face Priority:** [FACE_BRIGHTEST] [FACE_SHARPEST] [FACE_CENTER_LEAD] [FACE_EXPRESSION_JUSTIFY] [FACE_COVERAGE_MAX]
    99|**Crop Types:** [TIGHT_FACE] [FACE_PRIMARY] [FACE_BALANCED] [UPPER_BODY] [CONTEXTUAL_FACE]
   100|**Eye Contact:** [EYE_GLANCE] [EYE_SUSTAINED] [EYE_AVERTED] [EYE_DOWNCAST] [EYE_LAUGHING]
   101|**Lighting:** [FACE_LIT_BODY_SHADE] [FACE_CATCH_LIGHT] [FACE_RIM_LIGHT] [FACE_NATURAL_Window] [FACE_AMBIENT_FILLED]
   102|**Focus:** [FACE_SHARP_BODY_SOFT] [FACE_SHARP_ALL_SHARP] [FACE_BOKEH_BACKGROUND] [FACE_ENVIRON_CLEAR]
   103|
   104|---
   105|
   106|## Prompt Grammar
   107|
   108|```
   109|[composition_type]:[face_priority_architecture]_
   110|[face_percentage]:_[body_percentage]_
   111|[eye_contact]:_[duration_type]_
   112|[lighting_priority]:_[face_lighting]_
   113|[focus_distribution]:_[face_focus_body_focus]
   114|```
   115|
   116|**Examples:**
   117|```
   118|[TIGHT_FACE]_composition_face_priority
   119|face_percentage:75_body_percentage:5
   120|eye_contact:[EYE_SUSTAINED]_moment_of_connection
   121|lighting_priority:[FACE_CATCH_LIGHT]_warm_window_right
   122|focus_distribution:[FACE_SHARP_BODY_SOFT]
   123|
   124|[FACE_BALANCED]_composition_environmental_awareness
   125|face_percentage:45_body_percentage:35
   126|eye_contact:[EYE_GLANCE]_brief_acknowledgment
   127|lighting_priority:[FACE_NATURAL_WINDOW]_ diffused_soft
   128|focus_distribution:[FACE_ENVIRON_CLEAR]
   129|```
   130|
   131|---
   132|
   133|## HK-Specific Content
   134|
   135|- **MTR Reflection**: Face visible in window/train metal, double exposure effect
   136|- **Night Market Neon**: Face lit by colorful signage, moody face-first
   137|- **Tea Restaurant Table**: Upper body over dim sum, intimate sharing moment
   138|- **Ferry Deck**: Face against harbour backdrop, wind in hair
   139|
   140|**HK Tokens:** [MTR_REFLECTION_FACE] [NEON_FACE_LIT] [DIM_SUM_UPPER_BODY] [FERRY_WIND_FACE]
   141|
   142|---
   143|
   144|## Moderation Profile
   145|
   146|**PRESERVES:**
   147|- Natural face expressions (all 7 categories)
   148|- Authentic eye contact patterns
   149|- Environmental lighting that illuminates face
   150|
   151|**REMOVES:**
   152|- Overly studio-lit face-first (unrealistic)
   153|- Extreme face crops that distort anatomy
   154|- Forced eye contact for performance
   155|
   156|**CONTENT BOUNDARIES:**
   157|→ Do not use face-framing on subjects in distress
   158|→ TIGHT_FACE should preserve anatomy integrity
   159|→ Face retention rules should not override subject comfort signals
   160|
   161|---
   162|
   163|## Cross-References
   164|
   165|- Complements MICRO_SOCIAL (micro social interactions trigger face expressions)
   166|- Complements EXPRESSION_TIMING (face-first amplifies expression timing effects)
   167|- Complements BAD_PHOTO (face preserved, body accepts technical failures)
   168|
   169|---
   170|
   171|*Module: ENGINE_V15_FACE_FIRST_COMPOSITION_SYSTEM.md*
   172|*Source: AREA 10 — V15 Research*
   173|*Status: READY FOR INTEGRATION*
   174|

================================================================================
## V16 ANTI-FORMULA STREETWEAR SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V16/ENGINE_V16_ANTI_FORMULA_STREETWEAR_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENGINE_V16_ANTI_FORMULA_STREETWEAR_SYSTEM.md
     2|
     3|## V16 Core Module — Anti-Formula / Streetwear Diversity System
     4|### SOURCE: V16_ANTI_FORMULA_RESEARCH (Areas 01-03)
     5|### STATUS: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     6|
     7|---
     8|
     9|## PURPOSE
    10|
    11|This module eliminates the identifiable "lil.troublr formula" that causes outfit repetition across generated images — the same oversized knit / off-shoulder drape / loose-cardigan rhythm that makes feeds look cloned. It replaces formulaic outfit architecture with a structured diversity system spanning 7 streetwear categories (35+ architectures), 5 posture categories (35+ silhouettes), 8 camera distances, and 6 camera heights, enforced by cross-module anti-repetition rules that allow category repetition but forbid architectural repetition.
    12|
    13|---
    14|
    15|## KEY CONCEPTS
    16|
    17|- **Repeat Category, Vary Architecture** — same tee category is OK, but each tee outfit must use a different architecture (fitted vs. oversized vs. cropped vs. stretched-collar)
    18|- **Rhythm Balancing** — 5 outfit rhythm categories (Athletic, Minimal, Girly, Street Utilitarian, Party) rotate across images so no single energy dominates
    19|- **Body-Weight Realism** — real bodies accept gravity; compression points (under-breast shadow, thigh contact, abdominal fold) create non-performative attraction through natural use, not posed seduction
    20|- **Distance = Emotional Contract** — intimacy level maps to physical camera distance (Stranger → Intimate), preventing same-distance repetition across a feed
    21|- **Asymmetry Over Symmetry** — perfect symmetry reads as professional/posed; real bodies are asymmetrical through weight shifts, head tilts, and uneven action
    22|
    23|---
    24|
    25|## STREETWEAR_DIVERSITY_SYSTEM
    26|
    27|### The Formula Repetition Problem
    28|
    29|Current engine weakness: Overuse of specific outfit structures creates identifiable "lil.troublr formula":
    30|- Oversized knit / off-shoulder drape
    31|- Loose cardigan / neckline slipping mechanics
    32|- Same silhouette logic across images
    33|- Same "pretty girl in pretty outfit" rhythm
    34|
    35|Real KOL feeds break formula by: **repeating categories, but not exact architecture.** A real girl wears "tees" many times, but each tee outfit is architecturally different.
    36|
    37|---
    38|
    39|### STREETWEAR_DIVERSITY_LIBRARY
    40|
    41|#### Category A: Fitted/Printed Tees (Real KOL Foundation)
    42|
    43|**Why real:** Every HK/JP/KR girl owns 20+ tees. Tees are the most-authentic casual wear.
    44|
    45|**Outfit Architectures:**
    46|
    47|| Architecture | Description | Realism Signal | Token |
    48||-------------|-------------|----------------|-------|
    49|| A1: Faded_Graphic | Washed-out print, cracked logo, multiple washes | Memory item, identity piece | [FADED_GRAPHIC_TEE] |
    50|| A2: Vintage_Band | Retro band tee, soft cotton, slight shrinkage | Subcultural identity marker | [VINTAGE_BAND_TEE] |
    51|| A3: Oversized_Logo | Men's fit on women's body, disproportionate | Borrowed from boyfriend | [MENS_BORROWED_TEE] |
    52|| A4: Cropped_Tee | Hem knotted, DIY crop, midriff visible | Casual modification | [KNOTTED_CROP_TEE] |
    53|| A5: Stretched_Collar | Neckline stretched from over-wear, loose oval | Well-loved, lived-in item | [STRETCHED_COLLAR_TEE] |
    54|| A6: Fitted_Pocket | Small chest pocket, plain, no print | Minimalist casual | [PLAIN_FITTED_TEE] |
    55|| A7: Graphic_Front_Back | Front print different from back | Thoughtful graphic choice | [DOUBLE_SIDED_GRAPHIC] |
    56|
    57|**Anti-Repetition Grammar (Category A):**
    58|```
    59|[tee_architecture]_worn_with_[bottoms_type]_
    60|[fit_relative]:[oversized_fitted]_
    61|[layering]:[none_single_multi]_
    62|[distress_level]:[pristine_worn_distressed]
    63|```
    64|
    65|> Cross-ref: These tee architectures pair with Silhouette Variation postures (e.g., [WALKING_CAPTURED] for oversized tee movement, [SLUMPED_EXHAUSTED] for stretched-collar lived-in feel). See §SILHOUETTE_VARIATION_SYSTEM.
    66|
    67|---
    68|
    69|#### Category B: Ribbed/Cropped Tops (Body-Conscious Casual)
    70|
    71|**Why real:** Post-gym, casual date, hot weather staple. HK summer essential.
    72|
    73|**Outfit Architectures:**
    74|
    75|| Architecture | Description | Realism Signal | Token |
    76||-------------|-------------|----------------|-------|
    77|| B1: Ribbed_Cami | Thin strap, ribbed cotton, visible bra straps optional | Underwear-as-outerwear | [RIBBED_CAMI] |
    78|| B2: Lace_Trim_Cami | Delicate lace edge, feminine detail | Contrast with casual context | [LACE_TRIM_CAMISOLE] |
    79|| B3: Sport_Bra_Top | Athletic top, built-in support, minimal coverage | Post-workout or style choice | [SPORT_BRA_STYLE] |
    80|| B4: Racer_Back_Top | Narrow racerback, shoulder blade visible | Athletic influence on casual | [RACER_BACK_CASUAL] |
    81|| B5: Halter_Straps | Neck-tied halter, bare shoulders | Summer evening style | [HALTER_CASUAL] |
    82|| B6: Tube_Street | Tube top, strapless, depends on grip | Summer night market style | [TUBE_STREETWEAR] |
    83|
    84|> Cross-ref: B1-B4 expose compression points CP_04 (underarm) and CP_07 (shoulder blade). See §SILHOUETTE_VARIATION_SYSTEM → Compression Points.
    85|
    86|---
    87|
    88|#### Category C: Layering Pieces (Texture + Dimension)
    89|
    90|**Why real:** Real girls layer — for weather, for style, for hiding/changing silhouette.
    91|
    92|**Outfit Architectures:**
    93|
    94|| Architecture | Description | Realism Signal | Token |
    95||-------------|-------------|----------------|-------|
    96|| C1: Mesh_Under_Tee | Sheer mesh under or over tee | Texture contrast, subtle layering | [MESH_UNDER_LAYER] |
    97|| C2: Tank_Under_Cardigan | Visible tank straps, cardigan unbuttoned | Layered casual, easy | [TANK_UNDER_CARDIGAN] |
    98|| C3: Cropped_Zip_Hoodie | Above waist, shows midriff | Sporty casual | [CROPPED_ZIP_HOODIE] |
    99|| C4: Sheer_Blouse_Over | Blouse over tee, buttons open | Grandma-chic influence | [SHEER_OVER_TEE] |
   100|| C5: Denim_Jacket_Over | Oversized denim, sleeves pushed up | Classic casual layer | [OVERSIZED_DENIM] |
   101|| C6: Oversized_Shirt_Open | Flannel or oxford, open over anything | Tomboy casual | [OPEN_OVERSHIRT] |
   102|
   103|> Cross-ref: Layering pieces C1-C6 naturally interact with Category F (Inner Layer Systems). Combined token example: [MESH_UNDER_LAYER] + [PLAIN_TANK_UNDER] = mesh over visible black tank.
   104|
   105|---
   106|
   107|#### Category D: Bottoms Variety (Silhouette Diversity)
   108|
   109|**Why real:** Repeating same bottoms = same silhouette. Real feeds mix these constantly.
   110|
   111|| Architecture | Description | Token |
   112||-------------|-------------|-------|
   113|| D1: Low_Rise_Cargo_Mini | Cargo pockets, low rise, mini length | Street utilitarian |
   114|| D2: Pleated_Micro_Skirt | Schoolgirl reference, tiny | Y2K revival |
   115|| D3: Parachute_Pants | Baggy, tapered, technical fabric | Comfort aesthetic |
   116|| D4: Slouch_Socks_Crop | Long socks, mid-calf slouch | JP street style |
   117|| D5: Ballet_Sneakers | Flat, rounded toe, ribbon detail | Soft feminine casual |
   118|| D6: Football_Jersey_Shorts | Oversized jersey with shorts underneath | Athletic casual |
   119|| D7: Low_Rise_Wide_Leg | Denim or trousers, hip-hugging | 2000s influence |
   120|
   121|> Cross-ref: Bottom silhouettes directly affect which compression points activate. D1 (cargo mini) + seated = CP_02 (thigh contact). D7 (wide leg) + walking = no compression, different energy. See §SILHOUETTE_VARIATION_SYSTEM → Compression Points.
   122|
   123|---
   124|
   125|#### Category E: Accessories That Break Formula
   126|
   127|**Why real:** Same outfit + different accessories = completely different energy.
   128|
   129|| Architecture | Description | Token |
   130||-------------|-------------|-------|
   131|| E1: Oversized_Headphones | Over-ear, neck presence | [OVERSIZED_HEADPHONES] |
   132|| E2: Baseball_Cap_Backward | Cap worn backwards, casual | [CAP_BACKWARD] |
   133|| E3: Layered_Chains | Multiple necklaces, layered | [LAYERED_NECKLACES] |
   134|| E4: Visible_Bra_Straps | Intentional, not accidental | [INTENTIONAL_STRAPS] |
   135|| E5: Rhinestone_Everything | Rhinestone tops, accessories | [RHINESTONE_ACCESSORY] |
   136|| E6: Scrunchie_Hair | Hair tie on wrist or in hair | [SCRUNCHIE_CASUAL] |
   137|| E7: Mini_Backpack | Small bag, worn front or side | [MINI_BACKPACK_Y2K] |
   138|| E8: Stadium_Jacket | Letterman/reversible jacket | [STADIUM_JACKET] |
   139|
   140|> Cross-ref: E6 [SCRUNCHIE_CASUAL] paired with [PHONE_CHECK_POSTURE] (Area 02, Category E7) = strong "real life distracted" signal. E7 [MINI_BACKPACK_Y2K] pairs naturally with D2 [Pleated_Micro_Skirt] for Y2K rhythm.
   141|
   142|---
   143|
   144|#### Category F: Inner Layer Systems (Critical Missing) — 內層系統
   145|
   146|**Why real:** HK girls wear 內層 (inner layer) as critical identity marker. Plain beige tank under oversized shirt = very common HK look. Inner layer is visible at neck, arms — key authenticity signal.
   147|
   148|| Architecture | Description | Realism Signal | Token |
   149||-------------|-------------|----------------|-------|
   150|| F1: PLAIN_TANK_BLACK | Basic black tank, worn under sheer | Underwear-as-outerwear base | [PLAIN_TANK_UNDER] |
   151|| F2: SKIVVY_WHITE | White round-neck, visible collar | "Undershirt" visible | [VISIBLE_UNDERSHIRT] |
   152|| F3: UNIQLO_HEATECH | Tech inner, thin functional | Functional fashion | [FUNCTIONAL_INNER] |
   153|| F4: STRAPLESS_CAMISOLE | Worn under low-back tops | Practical layering | [STRAPLESS_BASE] |
   154|| F5: LOGO_UNDERSHIRT | Visible brand inner, casual | izone/H&M base layer | [LOGO_INNER_VISIBLE] |
   155|| F6: CROPPED_INNER | Shorter inner, shows midriff | Layered crop look | [CROPPED_INNER] |
   156|
   157|> Cross-ref: F3 [FUNCTIONAL_INNER] references [MTR_LAYER_TRANSITION] — HK commuters wear HeatTech for MTR AC-to-outdoor heat transition. F5 [LOGO_INNER_VISIBLE] pairs with [FAST_FASHION_TAG] brand identity tokens.
   158|
   159|---
   160|
   161|#### Category G: Sports/Active Wear — 運動風
   162|
   163|**Why real:** HK girls 大量運動風. Post-gym, yoga, running — athletic casual is core HK aesthetic.
   164|
   165|| Architecture | Description | Realism Signal | Token |
   166||-------------|-------------|----------------|-------|
   167|| G1: SPORTS_SET_MATCH | Matching top + leggings | Coordinated athletic | [MATCHING_SPORTS_SET] |
   168|| G2: YOGA_PANTS_CROP | Cropped yoga pants + oversized tee | Post-yoga casual | [YOGA_CROP_COMBO] |
   169|| G3: RUNNING_VEST | Running vest + shorts + cap | Athletic runner | [RUNNING_CASUAL] |
   170|| G4: GYM_COMPLETE | Full gym outfit, post-workout | Pre/post gym | [GYM_COMPLETE] |
   171|| G5: BIKE_SHORTS_LAYER | Biker shorts + long tee | Layered athletic | [BIKE_SHORTS_LAYER] |
   172|| G6: TENNIS_SKIRT | Tennis skirt + sneakers | Sporty feminine | [TENNIS_SKIRT_CASUAL] |
   173|| G7: SWEATSHIRT_LOOSE | Oversized sweatshirt + leggings | Comfort aesthetic | [SWEATSHIRT_CASUAL] |
   174|
   175|> Cross-ref: Athletic wear (G1-G7) naturally maps to RHYTHM_A: ATHLETIC_CASUAL. Pair with Movement-Based Silhouettes (Area 02, Category C) — [WALKING_CAPTURED] after gym, [STRETCH_REACHING_UP] during yoga.
   176|
   177|---
   178|
   179|### Brand Identity Tokens (HK-Specific) — 品牌身份標記
   180|
   181|**Why real:** HK girls use brand tags as identity markers. izone, A Pu, 小眾品牌, Supreme copy, 淘寶 direct — brand choice signals identity.
   182|
   183|| Type | Description | Token |
   184||------|-------------|-------|
   185|| FAST_FASHION_TAGGED | Brand tag visible (Uniqlo, ZARA, H&M) | [FAST_FASHION_TAG] |
   186|| LUXURY_MINI_REPLICATE | Designer-inspired piece, not authentic | [DESIGNER_COPY] |
   187|| VINTAGE_MARKET_FIND | 潮流廣場 or 女人街 purchase | [STREET_MARKET_FIND] |
   188|| TAOBAO_DIRECT | Obvious Taobao item | [TAOBAO_ITEM] |
   189|| 中古_VINTAGE | Second-hand store piece | [VINTAGE_SECONDHAND] |
   190|| SPORTS_BRAND_CORE | Nike/Adidas/Puma as identity | [ATHLETIC_BRAND_ID] |
   191|| 小眾品牌_CORE | Niche brand, identity marker | [NICHE_BRAND] |
   192|
   193|> Cross-ref: [STREET_MARKET_FIND] pairs with HK-specific framing [MONGKOK_TUNNEL] or [NIGHT_MARKET_MINIMAL]. [TAOBAO_ITEM] pairs with [SHENZHEN_SHOPPING] identity.
   194|
   195|---
   196|
   197|### HK-Specific Style Identities (EXPANDED) — 香港風格身份
   198|
   199|| Style | Description | Token |
   200||-------|-------------|-------|
   201|| 凍奶茶後生女 | Oversized tee + track pants + sneakers | [MILK_TEA_GIRL] |
   202|| 宿生妹 | Uniform variation, dorm life | [BOARDING_SCHOOL_GIRL] |
   203|| 深圳購物回來 | Wardrobe from 淘寶 hauls | [SHENZHEN_SHOPPING] |

   205|| 工廠大廈妹 | Industrial building aesthetic | [INDUSTRIAL_LOFT_GIRL] |
   206|| 大學聯誼 | University orientation, group fits | [UNI_ORIENTATION_GIRL] |
   207|| CNY新年裝 | First-day-new-clothes tradition | [CNY_TRADITIONAL_MODERN] |
   208|| 中秋晚裝 | Mid-Autumn festival, lanterns | [FESTIVAL_EVENING] |
   209|
   210|---
   211|
   212|### Outfit-Rhythm Balancing System — 穿搭節奏系統
   213|
   214|**V15 Problem:**
   215|- Same category (oversized knit) repeated
   216|- Same architecture (off-shoulder) every image
   217|- Same silhouette (loose top + tight bottom)
   218|
   219|**V16 Solution:**
   220|- Same category (tee) OK, but vary ARCHITECTURE (fitted tee vs oversized tee)
   221|- Same rhythm category (party) OK, but vary ACCESSORIES + LAYERS
   222|- Key rule: Repeat CATEGORY, vary ARCHITECTURE + ACCESSORIES + LAYERS
   223|
   224|**RHYTHM_A: ATHLETIC_CASUAL** (post-gym, sporty)
   225|- Token: [ATHLETIC_CASUAL]
   226|- Examples: Sport bra top + bike shorts, racer back + cargo mini
   227|- Pairs with: Category G (Sports/Active Wear), Silhouette Category C (Movement-Based)
   228|
   229|**RHYTHM_B: MINIMAL_CASUAL** (lazy day, natural)
   230|- Token: [MINIMAL_CASUAL]
   231|- Examples: Plain tee + jeans, ribbed cami + shorts
   232|- Pairs with: Category A (Tees), Silhouette Category E (Exhausted/Relaxed States)
   233|
   234|**RHYTHM_C: GIRLY_CASUAL** (date, going out)
   235|- Token: [GIRLY_CASUAL]
   236|- Examples: Lace trim cami + pleated skirt, halter + cargo
   237|- Pairs with: Category B (Ribbed/Cropped), Silhouette Category D (Asymmetry)
   238|
   239|**RHYTHM_D: STREET_UTILITARIAN** (night market, hangout)
   240|- Token: [STREET_UTILITARIAN]
   241|- Examples: Open overshirt + cargo, tube + denim jacket
   242|- Pairs with: Category C (Layering), Camera Distance [ENVIRONMENTAL_WIDE]
   243|
   244|**RHYTHM_E: PARTY_REFERENCE** (nightlife, Y2K)
   245|- Token: [PARTY_REFERENCE]
   246|- Examples: Rhinestone top + low-rise, cropped hoodie + mini skirt
   247|- Pairs with: Category E (Accessories), Camera Distance [FACE_CLOSEUP] or [EXTREME_CLOSEUP]
   248|
   249|---
   250|
   251|### Anti-Repetition Outfit Grammar — 反重複穿搭語法
   252|
   253|```
   254|[top_architecture]:[A1-A7/B1-B6/C1-C6]_
   255|[bottoms_architecture]:[D1-D7]_
   256|[layer_piece]:[none/E1-E8]_
   257|[rhythm_category]:[A-E]_
   258|[fit_relative]:[oversized_fitted_tight]_
   259|[distress_level]:[pristine_worn_distressed]_
   260|[identity_marker]:[band_subcultural_minimal_sporty]
   261|```
   262|
   263|**Example Prompt:**
   264|```
   265|[C4:SHEER_OVER_TEE]_outfit_
   266|[FADED_GRAPHIC_TEE]_ underneath visible straps_
   267|[D1:LOW_RISE_CARGO_MINI]_bottoms_
   268|[E2:BASEBALL_CAP_BACKWARD]_accessory_layer_
   269|[RHYTHM_D:STREET_UTILITARIAN]_
   270|fit:oversized_
   271|distress:worn_
   272|identity:streetwear_girl_night_market
   273|```
   274|
   275|---
   276|
   277|### KOL Fashion Rotation Framework — KOL穿搭輪換框架
   278|
   279|**Observation: Real KOLs Don't Repeat Outfit Architecture**
   280|
   281|**Pattern:** KOL repeats CATEGORY (teeshirt) but varies:
   282|1. Silhouette (oversized vs fitted)
   283|2. Bottoms (jeans vs shorts vs skirt)
   284|3. Layer (jacket vs none vs accessories)
   285|4. Context (gym vs cafe vs street)
   286|
   287|**Framework:**
   288|```
   289|IMAGE_ROTATION_RULESET:
   290|- Same category (tee) should not repeat exact architecture within 5 images
   291|- Same silhouette (tight top + tight bottom) should not repeat within 3 images
   292|- Same rhythm category should not repeat within 4 images
   293|- Accessory should change identity marker every 3 images
   294|```
   295|
   296|> Cross-ref: This rotation framework integrates with Area 02 anti-repetition rules (posture categories not repeat within 3 images) and Area 03 rules (camera distance rotation). See §ANTI_REPETITION_RULES for unified rule set.
   297|
   298|---
   299|
   300|### HK-Specific Scene Tokens — 香港場景標記
   301|
   302|- **Tea Restaurant Girl**: Oversized company tee (Pacific Coffee, 7-11), plain tee + tracksuit pants
   303|- **MTR Commuter**: Layered for AC contrast, sheer over tee for heat-to-cold transition
   304|- **Night Market**: Tube top + open shirt, cropped hoodie, minimal layers for humidity
   305|- **Karaoke Session**: Party outfit with rhinestones, Y2K accessories, layered necklaces
   306|- **Beach/Pool Day**: Sporty rehearsal wear, athletic-inspired casual
   307|
   308|**HK Scene Tokens:** [COMPANY_TEE] [MTR_LAYER_TRANSITION] [NIGHT_MARKET_MINIMAL] [KARAOKE_PARTY] [BEACH_SPORTY_CASUAL]
   309|
   310|> Cross-ref: These scene tokens provide context for Camera Distance choices (Area 03). [MTR_LAYER_TRANSITION] → [MTR_REFLECTION_SHOT] or [ESCALATOR_LEVEL]. [NIGHT_MARKET_MINIMAL] → [NEON_FACE_LIT] or [MONGKOK_TUNNEL]. [KARAOKE_PARTY] → [INTIMATE_DISTANCE] with [GROUP_SELFIE].
   311|
   312|---
   313|
   314|## SILHOUETTE_VARIATION_SYSTEM
   315|
   316|### The Problem
   317|
   318|Current engine relies on:
   319|- Leaning forward (expose chest, show interest)
   320|- Oversized neckline drift (slipped shoulder, casual seduction)
   321|- Exposed shoulder (half-dressed intimacy)
   322|- Same torso compression logic
   323|- Same "attractiveness geometry" repeating
   324|
   325|Real bodies create attraction through **natural use, movement, and spatial negotiation** — not designed poses.
   326|
   327|---
   328|
   329|### SILHOUETTE_VARIATION_LIBRARY
   330|
   331|#### Category A: Weight-Bearing Postures (Body in Use) — 負重姿勢
   332|
   333|**Principle:** Body 承受 weight = realistic, relatable, non-performative.
   334|
   335|| Type | Description | Attraction Mechanism | Token |
   336||------|-------------|---------------------|-------|
   337|| A1: ONE_LEG_SUPPORT | Standing, weight on one leg, hip shift | Asymmetry, natural stance | [ONE_LEG_SUPPORT] |
   338|| A2: HIP_WEIGHT_SHIFT | Hip pushed to one side, shoulders opposite | Classic "model" but real version | [HIP_WEIGHT_SHIFT] |
   339|| A3: KNEE_BEND | Slight knee bend, ready to move | Dynamic potential, not static | [SLIGHT_KNEE_BEND] |
   340|| A4: BACKBEND_LEAN | Lower back arch, chest forward slightly | Natural counterbalance | [NATURAL_BACKBEND] |
   341|| A5: WALL_LEAN | Body against wall, hip or shoulder | Casual weight-bearing | [WALL_LEAN_CASUAL] |
   342|| A6: HAND_ON_WALL | One hand supporting, body angled | Spatial negotiation | [HAND_ON_WALL] |
   343|| A7: SHOULDER_AGAINST_DOOR | Arm up, shoulder to frame | Casual doorway use | [SHOULDER_DOORFRAME] |
   344|
   345|> Cross-ref: A5-A7 are spatial-negotiation postures. Pair with HK-specific framing [ESTATE_FRAMING] (屋苑平台花園), [UNI_STAIRS] (大學校園樓梯), or [FOOTBRIDGE_WIDE] (行人天橋) for environment-body interaction. See §CAMERA_DISTANCE_DIVERSITY_SYSTEM.
   346|
   347|---
   348|
   349|#### Category B: Seated/Mounted Compression — 坐姿壓縮
   350|
   351|**Principle:** Sitting creates predictable compression points that reveal body without posing.
   352|
   353|| Type | Description | Attraction Mechanism | Token |
   354||------|-------------|---------------------|-------|
   355|| B1: CROSS_LEGGED_COMPACT | Legs crossed, knees high, compact | Thigh compression, small silhouette | [CROSS_LEGGED_COMPACT] |
   356|| B2: KNEE_TO_CHEST | Arms around knees, self-contained | Foetal-adjacent comfort | [KNEES_TO_CHEST] |
   357|| B3: SIDE_SEATED | Legs to side, knees bent | Hip angle, casual | [SIDE_SEATED_CASUAL] |
   358|| B4: STAIR_SITTING | On stairs, different heights | Level variation, leg reveal | [STAIR_SITTING] |
   359|| B5: FLOOR_LOUNGE | Lying or recline, casual floor | Most relaxed state | [FLOOR_LOUNGE_CASUAL] |
   360|| B6: CHAIR_FORWARD | Leaning forward on chair, arms crossed on back | Desk-adjacent, study | [CHAIR_FORWARD_LEAN] |
   361|| B7: LEGS_OVER_ARM | Legs draped over sofa/arm | Lived-in living room | [LEGS_OVER_ARM] |
   362|
   363|> Cross-ref: B1 [CROSS_LEGGED_COMPACT] activates CP_02 (thigh contact) and CP_03 (abdominal fold). B6 [CHAIR_FORWARD_LEAN] activates CP_01 (under-breast shadow). See Compression Points below.
   364|
   365|---
   366|
   367|#### Category C: Movement-Based Silhouettes — 動態剪影
   368|
   369|**Principle:** Body mid-motion = most realistic. Stillness is performance.
   370|
   371|| Type | Description | Attraction Mechanism | Token |
   372||------|-------------|---------------------|-------|
   373|| C1: WALKING_MOMENTUM | Mid-stride, natural gait, slight lean | Dynamic, captured candid | [WALKING_CAPTURED] |
   374|| C2: BENDING_TO_PICKUP | Hinge at hips, reaching down | Hip angle, practicality | [BENDING_TO_PICKUP] |
   375|| C3: HAIR_PUSH_BACK | Hand through hair, head back slightly | Neck exposure, motion | [PUSHING_HAIR_BACK] |
   376|| C4: STRETCH_REACHING | Arms up, body elongating | Posture extension | [STRETCH_REACHING_UP] |
   377|| C5: TURNING_AWAY | Mid-turn, profile or back view | Mystery, non-performance | [MID_TURN_AWAY] |
   378|| C6: LOOKING_BACK | Over shoulder, neck twist | Classic but real | [OVER_SHOULDER_GLANCE] |
   379|| C7: ARM_RAISED | One or both arms up, stretching or reaching | Underarm exposure, casual | [ARMS_RAISED_CASUAL] |
   380|| C8: BUCKET_CARRY | Carrying something, both hands occupied | Practical, non-performative | [CARRYING_OBJECT] |
   381|
   382|> Cross-ref: C1 [WALKING_CAPTURED] pairs with Camera Distance [FULL_BODY_SHOT] or [KNEE_TO_HEAD] and Shot Type [FORGOTTEN_CAMERA:P2]. C5 [MID_TURN_AWAY] pairs with [BACK_VIEW_PRIMARY] group dynamic.
   383|
   384|---
   385|
   386|#### Category D: Asymmetry Generators — 不對稱生成器
   387|
   388|**Principle:** Perfect symmetry = professional/posed. Real bodies are asymmetrical.
   389|
   390|| Type | Description | Attraction Mechanism | Token |
   391||------|-------------|---------------------|-------|
   392|| D1: HEAD_TILT | Head to one side, not centered | Asymmetry, casual | [HEAD_TILT_CASUAL] |
   393|| D2: SHOULDER_DROP | One shoulder higher than other | Weight asymmetry | [SHOULDER_DROP] |
   394|| D3: ASYMMETRIC_SQUAT | One leg down, one leg bent | Street/casual squat | [ASYMMETRIC_SQUAT] |
   395|| D4: ARM_HANG | One arm hanging, other doing something | Action asymmetry | [ONE_ARM_HANGING] |
   396|| D5: EYE_LEVEL_TILT | Camera above but head tilted down | Natural counter-angle | [NATURAL_TILT_DOWN] |
   397|| D6: BACKPACK_PULL | Backpack strap pulling one shoulder | Weight imbalance | [BACKPACK_SHOULDER_PULL] |
   398|
   399|> Cross-ref: D6 [BACKPACK_SHOULDER_PULL] pairs naturally with E7 [MINI_BACKPACK_Y2K] accessory (Area 01). D3 [ASYMMETRIC_SQUAT] is the generic version of F3 [STREET_SQUAT_HK] below.
   400|
   401|---
   402|
   403|#### Category E: Exhausted/Relaxed States — 疲勞/放鬆狀態
   404|
   405|**Principle:** Tired body = honest body. Exhaustion removes performance.
   406|
   407|| Type | Description | Attraction Mechanism | Token |
   408||------|-------------|---------------------|-------|
   409|| E1: SLUMPED_SHOULDERS | Shoulders rounded, chin down | Vulnerability, honesty | [SLUMPED_EXHAUSTED] |
   410|| E2: HAND_ON_NECK | Supporting head, neck exposed | Fatigue + neck display | [HAND_BEHIND_NECK] |
   411|| E3: EYES_CLOSED_RELAX | Eyes closed, face relaxed | Comfortable non-performance | [EYES_CLOSED_RELAXED] |
   412|| E4: MOUTH_PARTIAL | Slightly open, breathing or talking | Real-time moment | [MOUTH_SLIGHTLY_OPEN] |
   413|| E5: HUNCHED_FORWARD | Back curved, protective posture | Self-contained, shy | [HUNCHED_PROTECTIVE] |
   414|| E6: WEIGHT_ON_ELBOW | Reclining on elbow, half-up | Casual recline | [RECLINE_ON_ELBOW] |
   415|| E7: PHONE_CHECK | Looking at phone, chin dropped | Distracted, real | [PHONE_CHECK_POSTURE] |
   416|
   417|> Cross-ref: E7 [PHONE_CHECK_POSTURE] is the strongest "real life" signal. Pair with [FORGOTTEN_CAMERA:P2] or [HIDDEN_CAMERA_SHOT:P1] and camera height [HIP_LEVEL_CAMERA]. Combine with [MTR_RAIL_LEAN] for MTR phone-check combo.
   418|
   419|---
   420|
   421|### Body-Weight Realism System — 身體重力寫實系統
   422|
   423|#### Principle
   424|
   425|Real bodies **accept gravity**. Every body part has weight. Weight creates:
   426|- Compression (skin against fabric, skin against skin)
   427|- Draping (loose fabric falls naturally)
   428|- Exposed lines (under arm, between breasts, neck base)
   429|- Pressure marks (slight indentation from clothing)
   430|
   431|#### Compression Points — 壓縮點
   432|
   433|```
   434|COMPRESSION_POINT_LIBRARY:
   435|
   436|CP_01: UNDER_BREAST
   437|- When: seated, bending forward, bra band
   438|- Creates: breast separation, under-breast shadow
   439|- Token: [UNDERBREAST_SHADOW]
   440|
   441|CP_02: THIGH_GAP_OR_NOT
   442|- When: seated cross-legged, tight skirt/dress
   443|- Creates: thigh contact or gap, depends on body
   444|- Token: [THIGH_CONTACT]
   445|
   446|CP_03: ABDOMINAL_FOLD
   447|- When: seated, forward lean, high-waisted clothing
   448|- Creates: natural skin fold, not fat
   449|- Token: [ABDOMINAL_SOFT_FOLD]
   450|
   451|CP_04: UNDERARM_SKIN
   452|- When: arm raised, relaxed arm, sleeveless
   453|- Creates: exposed underarm, natural skin
   454|- Token: [UNDERARM_EXPOSED]
   455|
   456|CP_05: NECK_BASE_V
   457|- When: head forward, chin down
   458|- Creates: exposed V at neck base
   459|- Token: [NECK_BASE_EXPOSED]
   460|
   461|CP_06: SPINE_REVEAL
   462|- When: back arch, leaning forward
   463|- Creates: visible spine line through clothing
   464|- Token: [SPINE_VISUAL_LINE]
   465|
   466|CP_07: SHOULDER_BLADE_BULGE
   467|- When: shoulders back, tight top
   468|- Creates: natural shoulder blade prominence
   469|- Token: [SHOULDERBLADE_VISIBLE]
   470|```
   471|
   472|> Cross-ref: CP_07 works best for lean/athletic body types. For other body types, use alternative compression points. CP_01-CP_03 activate primarily in seated postures (Area 02 Category B). CP_04-CP_07 activate in movement or standing postures (Area 02 Categories A, C).
   473|
   474|---
   475|
   476|### Posture Diversity Grammar — 姿勢多樣化語法
   477|
   478|```
   479|[primary_posture]:[A1-A7/B1-B7/C1-C8/D1-D6/E1-E7]_
   480|[compression_point]:[CP01-CP07]_
   481|[body_axis]:[upright_forward_side_reclined]_
   482|[weight_distribution]:[balanced_left_heavy_right_heavy]_
   483|[movement_state]:[still_mid-motion_transitioning]
   484|```
   485|
   486|**Examples:**
   487|```
   488|[SIDE_SEATED_CASUAL:B3]_posture
   489|compression:[THIGH_CONTACT:CP02]
   490|body_axis:side_tilted
   491|weight_distribution:right_heavy
   492|movement_state:still
   493|
   494|[WALKING_CAPTURED:C1]_posture
   495|compression:[UNDERBREAST_SHADOW:CP01]_from_motion
   496|body_axis:forward_lean_slight
   497|weight_distribution:alternating
   498|movement_state:mid-motion
   499|```
   500|
   501|

================================================================================
## V16 ANTI-FORMULA EMOTIONAL SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V16/ENGINE_V16_ANTI_FORMULA_EMOTIONAL_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENGINE_V16_ANTI_FORMULA_EMOTIONAL_SYSTEM.md
     2|
     3|## V16 Core Module — Emotional Rhythm / Accidental Sexiness / AI Noise / Feed Realism System
     4|### SOURCE: V16_ANTI_FORMULA_RESEARCH (Areas 04-07)
     5|### STATUS: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     6|
     7|---
     8|
     9|## PURPOSE
    10|
    11|This module addresses four interconnected problems in the lil.troublr generation engine: (1) emotional monotony — the system produces overwhelmingly positive/cute/flirty output with no variety or honesty; (2) intentional attraction — attractiveness feels designed rather than emergent from physics and accident; (3) AI texture hallucination — over-sharpened skin, crunchy pores, and uniform detail create uncanny AI signatures; and (4) feed-level inauthenticity — individually optimized images that collectively feel like a production rather than a lived-in personal feed. The module provides libraries, tokens, grammar rules, and compositional systems to generate emotionally alive, physically believable, optically authentic content that functions as a cohesive personal feed.
    12|
    13|---
    14|
    15|## KEY CONCEPTS
    16|
    17|- **Emotional Rhythm Variation**: The principle that real feeds contain emotional dips, fatigue, distraction, awkwardness, and negative-adjacent states — not perpetual happiness. Variety creates honesty and prevents the "AI happy" signature.
    18|- **Accidental Sexiness / Physical Causality**: The principle that attraction emerges from body physics, clothing response to movement/environment, and exhaustion — not from intentional seduction poses. Every exposure moment requires a physical cause. Sexiness is in the cause, not the display.
    19|- **Optical Softness / Natural Detail Hierarchy**: The principle that real cameras preserve softness, create detail gradients, and exhibit optical behavior (bloom, falloff, lens character). AI over-sharpens everything equally, creating crunch. Real skin looks like skin, not a pore map.
    20|- **Feed-Level Realism**: The principle that a feed tells a story of a person living multiple days. It includes filler, ugly-cute moments, repetition, transitional moments, photodumps, and quality variation. Individually perfect images create collectively suspicious feeds.
    21|- **Cross-Module Composition**: All four systems work simultaneously. An image can have accidental sexiness (physical cause), low energy emotion (honest fatigue), optical softness (anti-AI texture), and feed-level context (filler or transitional). Systems reinforce each other for maximum realism.
    22|- **HK-Specific Context**: All systems include Hong Kong–specific situations, locations, optical conditions, emotional contexts, and cultural patterns unique to the target demographic.
    23|
    24|---
    25|
    26|## EMOTIONAL_RHYTHM_LIBRARY
    27|
    28|### Category A: Low Energy States (Honest Fatigue)
    29|
    30|**Why important:** Exhausted = not performing. Realest state.
    31|
    32|| Type | Description | Visual Markers | Token |
    33||------|-------------|----------------|-------|
    34|| A1: POST_TIRED | Just-woke or late-night tired | Heavy lids, minimal expression, slack mouth | [POST_TIRED_EXPRESSION] |
    35|| A2: MID_ACTIVITY_TIRED | Tired from doing something | Slight slouch, reduced posture | [MID_ACTIVITY_TIRED] |
    36|| A3: EXHAUSTED_LAYERED | Multiple fatigue sources | Zoned out, distant gaze | [EXHAUSTED_LAYERED] |
    37|| A4: SLEEPY_HEAD_NOD | Head dropping, fighting sleep | Micro-sleep fragments | [SLEEPY_NOD] |
    38|| A5: ENERGY_CRASH | Was high-energy, now flat | Expression drop, slack posture | [ENERGY_CRASH] |
    39|
    40|### Category B: Distracted/Absent States
    41|
    42|**Why important:** Real people are often mentally elsewhere.
    43|
    44|| Type | Description | Visual Markers | Token |
    45||------|-------------|----------------|-------|
    46|| B1: PHONE_ABSORBED | Looking at phone, oblivious | Slight furrow, concentrated | [PHONE_ABSORBED] |
    47|| B2: WINDOW_GAZING | Looking at nothing, mind wandering | Soft unfocused gaze | [WINDOW_GAZING] |
    48|| B3: DEEP_THOUGHT | Thinking hard about something | Furrowed brow, distant | [DEEP_THOUGHT] |
    49|| B4: OVERSTIMULATED | Too much input, shutting down | Slightly overwhelmed expression | [OVERSTIMULATED] |
    50|| B5: MORNING_FOG | Not fully awake, processing | Blank, unfocused | [MORNING_FOG] |
    51|| B6: THOUGHT_INTERRUPTED | Was thinking, got interrupted | Caught mid-process | [THOUGHT_INTERRUPTED] |
    52|
    53|### Category C: Socially Uncomfortable States
    54|
    55|**Why important:** Awkward = honest. Shows social reality.
    56|
    57|| Type | Description | Visual Markers | Token |
    58||------|-------------|----------------|-------|
    59|| C1: SHY_APPROACH | Not sure of camera/photographer | Averted gaze, slight smile | [SHY_APPROACH] |
    60|| C2: AWKWARD_SMILE | Forced smile, uncomfortable | Too wide, eyes not engaged | [AWKWARD_SMILE] |
    61|| C3: TOO_MANY_PEOPLE | Uncomfortable with group energy | Edge of frame, looking away | [CROWD_OVERWHELM] |
    62|| C4: POSING_ANXIETY | Knows camera, unsure how to pose | Stiff posture, tentative expression | [POSING_ANXIETY] |
    63|| C5: POST_ARGUMENT | Just finished disagreeing | Tense jaw, flat expression | [POST_ARGUMENT] |
    64|| C6: FIRST_MEETING | New person, evaluating | Curious but guarded | [NEW_PERSON_CURIOSITY] |
    65|
    66|### Category D: Negative-Adjacent Emotions
    67|
    68|**Why important:** Perfect happiness is suspicious. Real includes irritation, boredom, frustration.
    69|
    70|| Type | Description | Visual Markers | Token |
    71||------|-------------|----------------|-------|
    72|| D1: BORED_STARE | Nothing interesting happening | Flat expression, slight frown | [BORED_STARE] |
    73|| D2: SLIGHT_IRRITATION | Minor frustration | Furrowed brow, tight lips | [SLIGHT_IRRITATION] |
    74|| D3: DISAPPOINTED | Expectation not met | Sighing posture, downturned | [DISAPPOINTED] |
    75|| D4: MISSING_SOMEONE | Longing for absent person | Soft sad, distant | [MISSING_SOMEONE] |
    76|| D5: REGRET_EXPRESSION | Something undone | Wincing, avoiding eye | [REGRET_EXPRESSION] |
    77|| D6: FRUSTRATED_BITE_LIP | Biting lip in frustration | Tense, mouth involved | [FRUSTRATED_BITE_LIP] |
    78|
    79|### Category E: Complex/Mixed Emotions
    80|
    81|**Why important:** Real emotions are rarely pure. Mix = sophistication.
    82|
    83|| Type | Description | Visual Markers | Token |
    84||------|-------------|----------------|-------|
    85|| E1: HAPPY_BUT_TIRED | Positive but low energy | Soft smile, heavy eyes | [HAPPY_BUT_TIRED] |
    86|| E2: EXCITED_BUT_SHY | Eager but nervous | Bright eyes, averting gaze | [EXCITED_BUT_SHY] |
    87|| E3: SAD_BUT_OKAY | Sad but coping | Neutral-ish, eyes give it away | [SAD_BUT_OKAY] |
    88|| E4: TEASING_PLAYFUL | Pushing boundaries playfully | Mischief in eyes, slight smirk | [TEASING_PLAYFUL] |
    89|| E5: CONFIDENT_VULNERABLE | Strong but open | Direct gaze, soft mouth | [CONFIDENT_VULNERABLE] |
    90|| E6: PROUD_BUT_HUMBLE | Accomplished but modest | Quiet satisfaction | [PROUD_BUT_HUMBLE] |
    91|| E7: LYING_TO_SELF | Expression contradicts reality | Micro-tells, asymmetry | [DENIAL_EXPRESSION] |
    92|
    93|### Category F: Post-Activity Emotional States
    94|
    95|**Why important:** After something, during something = honest context.
    96|
    97|| Type | Description | Context | Token |
    98||------|-------------|---------|-------|
    99|| F1: POST_LAUGH_RESIDUE | Just finished laughing | Residual smile, tear | [POST_LAUGH_RESIDUE] |
   100|| F2: POST_CRY_RED | Cried recently | Red eyes, puffy | [POST_CRY_REDNESS] |
   101|| F3: POST_ARGUMENT_TENSION | Tension remains | Avoidance, stiffness | [POST_ARGUMENT_TENSION] |
   102|| F4: POST_WORKOUT | Post-exercise glow | Flushed, energised | [POST_WORKOUT] |
   103|| F5: POST_SWIM_MOOD | Post-pool ambience | Chlorine, relaxed | [POST_SWIM_MOOD] |
   104|| F6: POST_PARTY | Post-event comedown | Tired but wired | [POST_PARTY] |
   105|| F7: TRAIN_RIDE_REFLECTION | Late night transport mood | Contemplative, alone | [TRAIN_RIDE_REFLECTION] |
   106|| F8: NIGHTLIFE_LONELY | In party setting but alone | Contrast, disconnect | [NIGHTLIFE_LONELY] |
   107|
   108|---
   109|
   110|### Mood-Rotation System
   111|
   112|#### Feed-Level Rhythm Rules
   113|
   114|```
   115|EMOTIONAL_ROTATION_RULESET:
   116|
   117|Rule 1: Every 5 images must have at least one "low energy" (A types) emotion
   118|Rule 2: Positive emotions (happy, flirty, warm) should not exceed 60% of feed
   119|Rule 3: Every 10 images should have at least one "negative-adjacent" (D types) emotion
   120|Rule 4: "Cute + flirty" should not appear in consecutive images
   121|Rule 5: Post-activity states (F types) should appear every 3-4 images
   122|```
   123|
   124|#### Emotion Density Guidelines
   125|
   126|| Emotion Type | Percentage of Feed | Purpose |
   127||-------------|-------------------|---------|
   128|| Warm/Positive (classic) | 40-50% | Core lil.troublr identity |
   129|| Low Energy (honest) | 15-20% | Realism anchor |
   130|| Distracted/Absent | 10-15% | Life-continuity |
   131|| Uncomfortable (social) | 5-10% | Social reality |
   132|| Negative-adjacent | 5-10% | Honesty variety |
   133|| Complex/Mixed | 5-10% | Sophistication |
   134|
   135|---
   136|
   137|### Anti-Emotional-Loop Grammar
   138|
   139|#### Combination Rules
   140|
   141|```
   142|CAN_COMBINE:
   143|- [POST_TIRED_EXPRESSION] + [SAD_BUT_OKAY]
   144|- [BORED_STARE] + [WINDOW_GAZING]
   145|- [EXCITED_BUT_SHY] + [TEASING_PLAYFUL]
   146|- [PHONE_ABSORBED] + [MORNING_FOG]
   147|
   148|CANNOT_COMBINE (too similar):
   149|- [EXHAUSTED_LAYERED] + [SLEEPY_NOD]
   150|- [AWKWARD_SMILE] + [POSING_ANXIETY]
   151|- [SLIGHT_IRRITATION] + [FRUSTRATED_BITE_LIP]
   152|
   153|CONTEXT_REQUIRED:
   154|- [POST_ARGUMENT] → requires social context
   155|- [POST_CRY_REDNESS] → requires story context
   156|- [NIGHTLIFE_LONELY] → requires nightlife context
   157|```
   158|
   159|#### Prompt Grammar
   160|
   161|```
   162|[primary_emotion]:[A1-F8]_
   163|[secondary_emotion]:[if_applicable]_
   164|[intensity]:[mild_moderate_strong]_
   165|[expression_completeness]:[full_partial_residual]_
   166|[context_marker]:[location_or_activity]
   167|```
   168|
   169|**Examples:**
   170|```
   171|[POST_TIRED_EXPRESSION:A1]_emotion
   172|intensity:moderate
   173|expression_completeness:partial
   174|context:late_morning_home
   175|
   176|[EXCITED_BUT_SHY:E2]_emotion
   177|intensity:mild
   178|expression_completeness:full_with_micro_tells
   179|context:first_time_trying_something
   180|
   181|[BORED_STARE:D1]_emotion
   182|intensity:mild
   183|expression_completeness:full
   184|context:waiting_for_friend_at_cafe
   185|```

   209|## ACCIDENTAL_SEXINESS_LIBRARY
   210|
   211|### Category A: Movement-Based Accidental Exposure
   212|
   213|**Principle:** Body moves → clothing responds → attraction emerges naturally.
   214|
   215|| Type | Trigger | What Happens | Realism Signal | Token |
   216||------|---------|--------------|----------------|-------|
   217|| A1: SHIRT_SHIFT_UP | Reaching, stretching, lifting arms | Shirt rises, midriff exposed | Movement cause | [SHIRT_RISE_MOVEMENT] |
   218|| A2: TEE_NECKLINE_STRETCH | Head forward, looking down | Neckline widens, collarbone exposed | Posture cause | [NECKLINE_STRETCH] |
   219|| A3: ARM_RAISE_UNDERARM | Arm up, reaching for something | Underarm exposed, skin visible | Practical cause | [UNDERARM_EXPOSED_ARMS_UP] |
   220|| A4: BEND_FORWARD_CLEAVAGE | Leaning forward, seated | Gravity + compression = cleavage | Seated cause | [BEND_FORWARD_EXPOSE] |
   221|| A5: SQUAT_BOTTOM_PULL | Squatting, bending down | Shorts/dress rides up | Movement cause | [SQUAT_RIDE_UP] |
   222|| A6: WIND_BLOW_THIN_FABRIC | Wind, light fabric | Fabric clings, silhouette visible | Environmental cause | [WIND_CLING_SILHOUETTE] |
   223|| A7: STRETCH_TIGHT_FABRIC | Stretching, arms up | Fitted fabric stretches, body visible | Body cause | [STRETCH_FABRIC_TIGHT] |
   224|| A8: WALKING_HIP_SWAY | Normal walking gait | Natural hip movement, clothing shifts | Natural cause | [WALKING_HIP_SHIFT] |
   225|
   226|### Category B: Seated/Compressed Attraction
   227|
   228|**Principle:** Sitting creates predictable compression points.
   229|
   230|| Type | Trigger | What Happens | Token |
   231||------|---------|--------------|-------|
   232|| B1: SEATED_THIGH_GAP | Sitting with knees together | Legs pressed, thigh contact | [SEATED_THIGH_PRESS] |
   233|| B2: CHAIR_FORWARD_LEAN | Leaning on chair back | Chest compressed against arms | [FORWARD_LEAN_CHEST] |
   234|| B3: CROSS_LEGGED_SLIDE | Cross-legged, shifting | Dress/shorts ride up slightly | [CROSS_LEG_RIDE] |
   235|| B4: LOW_CUT_SEATED | Seated, top shifts | Low neckline exposes more | [LOW_CUT_SEATED_SHIFT] |
   236|| B5: LEGS_SPREAD_SEATED | Casual seated spread | More exposed, relaxed | [CASUAL_SPREAD_SEATED] |
   237|| B6: KNEES_TO_CHEST | Arms around knees, compact | Body compressed, intimate | [KNEES_CHEST_COMPACT] |
   238|
   239|### Category C: Fabric/Clothing Behavior
   240|
   241|**Principle:** Clothing responds to body and environment.
   242|
   243|| Type | Trigger | What Happens | Token |
   244||------|---------|--------------|-------|
   245|| C1: SWEAT_WET_CLING | Humidity, exercise | Fabric transparent-ish, clings | [SWEAT_CLING] |
   246|| C2: WET_BIKINI_SHIFT | Post-swim, wet fabric | Swimsuit heavy, shifts position | [WET_FABRIC_SHIFT] |
   247|| C3: STRETCHED_COLLAR_REVEAL | Collar stretched from wear | Shoulder/collarbone visible | [STRETCHED_COLLAR_REVEAL] |
   248|| C4: LOOSE_FABRIC_GAP | Thin/loose fabric, movement | Skin visible through gaps | [FABRIC_GAP_SKIN] |
   249|| C5: HIGH_WAIST_SLIDE | High-waisted, sitting | Waistband creates line, shifts | [WAISTBAND_SLIDE] |
   250|| C6: SHOULDER_SLIP | Sleeveless, relaxed | Strap falls off shoulder | [SHOULDER_STRAP_SLIP] |
   251|| C7: BABY_TEE_STRETCH | Fitted tee, reaching | Fabric stretched thin, body visible | [TEE_STRETCH_BODY_VISIBLE] |
   252|
   253|### Category D: Exhaustion/Relaxation Attraction
   254|
   255|**Principle:** Tired = honest = attractive in honest way.
   256|
   257|| Type | Trigger | What Happens | Token |
   258||------|---------|--------------|-------|
   259|| D1: EXHAUSTED_NECK_EXPOSE | Head dropped, tired | Neck extended, vulnerable | [TIRED_NECK_EXTENDED] |
   260|| D2: RELAXED_SHOULDER_DROP | Shoulders dropped, relaxed | Shoulder blade more visible | [RELAXED_SHOULDER_BLADE] |
   261|| D3: SLEEPY_HEAD_TILT | Fighting sleep, head tilted | Neck exposed, soft expression | [SLEEPY_HEAD_TILT] |
   262|| D4: SLUMP_CHEST_RELIEF | Slumped, back rounded | Chest relaxes, less held | [SLUMP_CHEST_RELEASE] |
   263|| D5: HAND_BEHIND_HEAD | Supporting head | Underarm exposed, casual | [HAND_SUPPORT_HEAD] |
   264|| D6: EYES_CLOSED_RELAXED | Eyes closed, breathing | Face relaxed, no performance | [EYES_CLOSED_TRUST] |
   265|
   266|### Category E: Environmental Accidental
   267|
   268|**Principle:** Environment causes clothing/body response.
   269|
   270|| Type | Trigger | What Happens | Token |
   271||------|---------|--------------|-------|
   272|| E1: HOT_DAY_STICKY | Heat, humidity | Fabric sticks, sheen | [HOT_DAY_STICKY] |
   273|| E2: AIR_CON_CONTRAST | Entering AC from heat | Nipple visibility increase | [AC_NIPPLE_VISIBILITY] |
   274|| E3: FLASH_FLATTEN | Camera flash | Fabric smooth, slight shine | [FLASH_SMOOTH] |
   275|| E4: WATER_DROPS_DRIP | Post-pool, post-rain | Water tracks, transparency | [WATER_DROP_TRACKS] |
   276|| E5: SUNSCREEN_OILY | Post-sunscreen application | Greasy sheen, glistening | [SUNSCREEN_GREASY_SHEEN] |
   277|| E6: WIND_BLOW_HAIR_MOUTH | Wind, hair in face | Mouth parted, hair stuck | [HAIR_MOUTH_PARTED] |
   278|| E7: AC_UNIT_DIRECT_BLOW | Standing in AC wind | Fabric shifts, moves | [AC_WIND_SHIFT] |
   279|| E8: HOT_COLD_TRANSITION | Entering AC from heat | Goosebumps + fabric shift | [HEAT_COLD_TRANSITION] |
   280|| E9: HUMID_SWEAT_CLING | Humid day, light fabric | Sweat + fabric = body visible | [HUMID_BODY_CLING] |
   281|| E10: POST_RAIN_WET | Rain on fabric | Water tracks + transparency shift | [WET_FABRIC_HK] |
   282|| E11: STEAM_ROOM | Hot shower, sauna | Skin glistening, red | [STEAM_ROOM_HK] |
   283|| E12: WOK_HEAT_FACE | Cooking, kitchen heat | Flushed, sweating slightly | [COOKING_FLUSH] |
   284|
   285|### Additional Forbidden Patterns (Too Intentional)
   286|
   287|```
   288|AVOID:
   289|- Subject holding exposure in place (hand on shirt to keep it up)
   290|- Subject actively creating the cause (leaning intentionally)
   291|- Subject's gaze returning to camera after exposure
   292|- Subject adjusting clothing to maintain exposure
   293|- Close-up on exposed area while subject is aware
   294|```
   295|
   296|---
   297|
   298|### Physical-Causality Seduction System
   299|
   300|#### Principle
   301|
   302|Every accidental attraction moment must have a **physical cause**. The seduction is in the cause, not the display.
   303|
   304|**Wrong:** Subject is positioned to show cleavage (intentional)
   305|**Right:** Subject is leaning forward to pick something up, which causes cleavage (physical causality)
   306|
   307|#### Grammar
   308|
   309|```
   310|[physical_cause]:[movement_posture_environment]_
   311|[clothing_response]:[what_fabric_does]_
   312|[resulting_exposure]:[what_becomes_visible]_
   313|[accidental_level]:[totally_accidental_mostly_accidental_minimally_designed]
   314|```
   315|
   316|**Examples:**
   317|```
   318|[REACHING_FOR_OBJECT:A7]_cause
   319|clothing_response:[TEE_STRETCH_BODY_VISIBLE:C7]
   320|exposure:midriff_and_body_contour
   321|accidental_level:totally_accidental
   322|
   323|[SEATED_WRITING:B1]_cause
   324|clothing_response:thighs_pressed_together
   325|exposure:[SEATED_THIGH_PRESS]
   326|accidental_level:totally_accidental
   327|
   328|[HUMID_NIGHT:E1]_cause
   329|clothing_response:[SWEAT_CLING:C1]
   330|exposure:fabric_cling_transparentish
   331|accidental_level:environmental_accident
   332|```
   333|
   334|---
   335|
   336|### Anti-Glamour Attraction Grammar
   337|
   338|#### Rules
   339|
   340|1. **Always include physical cause** — no exposure without cause
   341|2. **Keep expression neutral/minimal** — sexiness is in physics, not performance
   342|3. **Avoid close-up on exposed area** — context shot, not zoom
   343|4. **Use exhausted/relaxed expression** — performance = intentional
   344|5. **Environmental cause preferred** — humidity, wind, movement > deliberate pose
   345|
   346|#### Forbidden Patterns (Too Intentional)
   347|
   348|```
   349|AVOID:
   350|- Subject looking at exposed area
   351|- Subject adjusting exposure (fixing it)
   352|- Close-up on exposed area
   353|- "Oops" expression or reaction
   354|- Camera pointing at exposure
   355|- Subject aware of exposure
   356|```
   357|
   358|---
   359|
   360|## AI_NOISE_REDUCTION_LIBRARY
   361|
   362|### Category A: Lens Softness Sources
   363|
   364|Real lenses create softness. AI over-sharpens everything.
   365|
   366|| Source | What It Does | Realism Signal | Token |
   367||--------|--------------|----------------|-------|
   368|| A1: WIDE_APERTURE | Shallow DOF, face sharp, rest soft | Natural separation | [WIDE_APERTURE_SOFT] |
   369|| A2: OLD_LENS_CHARACTER | Vintage/cheap lens, soft edges | Film era aesthetic | [OLD_LENS_SOFT] |
   370|| A3: LOW_LIGHT_ISO | High ISO noise, grain, softness | Night authenticity | [LOW_LIGHT_SOFT] |
   371|| A4: FOCUS_ERROR_SLIGHT | Subject not perfectly sharp | Candid authenticity | [FOCUS_SLIGHT_SOFT] |
   372|| A5: ZOOM_LENS_SOFT | Telephoto compression + soft edges | Natural telephoto look | [TELEPHOTO_SOFT] |
   373|| A6: POINT_AND_SHOOT_QUALITY | Compact camera softness | Amateur document | [COMPACT_SOFT] |
   374|
   375|### Category B: Optical Bloom Sources
   376|
   377|Light behaves optically — creates bloom, halos, softness.
   378|
   379|| Source | What It Does | Realism Signal | Token |
   380||--------|--------------|----------------|-------|
   381|| B1: BACKLIT_SOFT | Behind subject, creates glow | Natural warm | [BACKLIT_GLOW_SOFT] |
   382|| B2: WINDOW_DIFFUSED | Soft box effect, gentle | Studio without studio | [WINDOW_DIFFUSE_SOFT] |
   383|| B3: FLARE_ORGANIC | Lens flare, adds softness | Natural light accident | [ORGANIC_LENS_FLARE] |
   384|| B4: CATCHLIGHT_SOFT | Eye catch light, alive | Human presence | [SOFT_CATCHLIGHT] |
   385|| B5: SILHOUETTE_SOFT | Edge softness from backlight | Atmospheric | [SOFT_EDGE_SILHOUETTE] |
   386|
   387|### Category C: Focus Falloff
   388|
   389|Real focus is a gradient, not binary.
   390|
   391|| Type | Description | Token |
   392||------|-------------|-------|
   393|| C1: FRONT_FOCUS_SLIGHT | Slightly in front of subject | [FRONT_FOCUS_SOFT] |
   394|| C2: BACK_FOCUS_SLIGHT | Slightly behind subject | [BACK_FOCUS_SOFT] |
   395|| C3: EDGE_FALLOFF | Edges progressively soft | [EDGE_FOCUS_FALLOFF] |
   396|| C4: CORNER_SOFT | Corners soft, center sharp | [CORNER_SOFTNESS] |
   397|| C5: ENVIRONMENT_FUZZY | Background not perfectly sharp | [ENVIRONMENTAL_BLUR] |
   398|
   399|### Category D: Sensor Characteristics
   400|
   401|Real sensors have specific behaviors.
   402|
   403|| Type | Description | Token |
   404||------|-------------|-------|
   405|| D1: SKIN_SMOOTHING | Sensor noise reduction | [SENSOR_SMOOTH_SKIN] |
   406|| D2: SHADOW_NOISE | Low-key, grain in shadows | [SHADOW_GRAIN] |
   407|| D3: HIGHLIGHT_CLIP_SOFT | Bright areas soft-clip | [SOFT_HIGHLIGHT_CLIP] |
   408|| D4: COLOR_NOISE_LOW | Slight color noise | [MINIMAL_COLOR_NOISE] |
   409|| D5: DETAIL_LIMIT | Sensor detail limit | [SENSOR_DETAIL_LIMIT] |
   410|
   411|### Category E: Flash Flattening
   412|
   413|Flash changes everything — removes texture, flattens.
   414|
   415|| Type | Description | Token |
   416||------|-------------|-------|
   417|| E1: DIRECT_FLASH_HARD | Hard shadow, flat face | [DIRECT_FLASH_FLAT] |
   418|| E2: BOUNCE_FLASH_SOFT | Soft fill, natural-ish | [BOUNCE_FLASH_SOFT] |
   419|| E3: OFF_CAMERA_SOFT | Directional but soft | [OFF_CAMERA_FLASH] |
   420|| E4: NO_FLASH_INDOOR | Available light, grain | [NO_FLASH_INDOOR] |
   421|
   422|---
   423|
   424|### Natural Detail Hierarchy
   425|
   426|#### Principle
   427|
   428|Real images have **detail hierarchy** — some things detailed, some soft. AI makes everything equally detailed = uncanny.
   429|
   430|#### Hierarchy Rules
   431|
   432|```
   433|DETAIL_HIERARCHY_MATRIX:
   434|
   435|HIGHEST DETAIL: Face (especially eyes, mouth)
   436|HIGH DETAIL: Skin (subject's)
   437|MEDIUM DETAIL: Immediate clothing (subject's)
   438|LOW DETAIL: Background props
   439|LOWEST DETAIL: Background environment (far)
   440|NEAR-ZERO: Extreme edges
   441|
   442|ANTI-AI RULE: If background has AI-like uniform sharpness (no lens falloff, no optical aberration) = AI
   443|```
   444|
   445|#### Prompt Grammar
   446|
   447|```
   448|[optical_softness_source]:[A1-A6]_
   449|[bloom_type]:[B1-B5]_
   450|[focus_type]:[C1-C5]_
   451|[sensor_character]:[D1-D5]_
   452|[flash_type]:[E1-E4]_
   453|[detail_hierarchy]:[face_high_env_low]_
   454|[softness_level]:[subtle_moderate_heavy]
   455|```
   456|
   457|**Examples:**
   458|```
   459|[WIDE_APERTURE_SOFT:A1]_optical
   460|bloom:[WINDOW_DIFFUSE_SOFT:B2]
   461|focus:[EDGE_FOCUS_FALLOFF:C3]
   462|sensor:[SENSOR_SMOOTH_SKIN:D1]
   463|flash:[NO_FLASH_INDOOR:E4]
   464|detail_hierarchy:face_high_clothing_medium_env_fuzzy
   465|softness_level:moderate
   466|```
   467|
   468|---
   469|
   470|### Anti-Crunch Realism System
   471|
   472|#### Crunchy Skin Causes
   473|
   474|AI skin looks "crunchy" when:
   475|1. Over-sharpened individual pores
   476|2. Noise added to skin texture
   477|3. Every pore equally visible
   478|4. Skin has "texture" without softness
   479|5. Edge enhancement on skin
   480|
   481|#### Solutions
   482|
   483|```
   484|ANTI_CRUNCH_PRESCRIPTION:
   485|
   486|1. Use: [SENSOR_SMOOTH_SKIN] — sensor NR softens skin
   487|2. Use: [WIDE_APERTURE_SOFT] — shallow DOF de-focuses skin edges
   488|3. Use: [LOW_LIGHT_SOFT] — natural grain masks AI texture
   489|4. Avoid: Detail emphasis on skin
   490|5. Avoid: Pore visibility as "detail"
   491|6. Rule: Skin should look like skin, not pore map
   492|```
   493|
   494|#### Texture Density Balancing
   495|
   496|| Scene Type | Texture Level | Reason |
   497||-----------|---------------|--------|
   498|| Close-up face | LOW texture | Skin softness, intimacy |
   499|| Medium shot body | MEDIUM texture | Visible but not crunchy |
   500|| Wide environmental | LOW texture | Background fades |
   501|

================================================================================
## V16 DAILY ENTROPY SYSTEM
### Source: modules/V16/ENGINE_V16_DAILY_ENTROPY_SYSTEM.md
================================================================================

     1|# ENGINE_V16_DAILY_ENTROPY_SYSTEM.md
     2|
     3|## V16 Core Module — Daily Life Entropy / Failed Beauty System
     4|### SOURCE: V16_LIFE_ENTROPY_RESEARCH (Areas 01-02)
     5|### STATUS: READY FOR INTEGRATION
     6|
     7|---
     8|
     9|## PURPOSE
    10|
    11|This module provides the foundational "anti-perfection" layer for the V16 Life Entropy Engine. It solves the problem of AI-generated content being overly optimized — every photo a hero shot, every moment photo-worthy, every face perfectly filtered. Real life contains transit boredom, phone-absorbed waiting, accidental ugly-cute expressions, and wind-disaster acceptance. This module injects those humanizing entropy moments into generated content so the persona feels like a real person who sometimes zones out on the MTR and makes stupid faces, not a production-optimized avatar.
    12|
    13|---
    14|
    15|## KEY CONCEPTS
    16|
    17|- **Daily Entropy** — the unphotogenic, mundane, "caught existing" moments that fill real life between hero shots (commuting, waiting, phone scrolling, just-woke-up grogginess)
    18|- **Low-Stakes Grammar** — language patterns that signal "this is not a photo moment," removing beauty intent and performance pressure from image prompting
    19|- **Failed Beauty / Ugly-Cute** — expressions, angles, and states that should not work but do: mid-sneeze faces, wind disasters, double chins, silly faces — beauty through the removal of the attempt at beauty
    20|- **Entropy Ratio** — the deliberate balance of entropy moments against polished content (20-30% entropy, at least 1 entropy moment per 3 hero shots, never dominating)
    21|- **Authenticity Over Performance** — the governing principle: genuine = subject forgets camera exists; forced = subject performs "look how real I'm being"
    22|
    23|---
    24|
    25|## DAILY_ENTROPY_LIBRARY
    26|
    27|### Core Tokens
    28|
    29|| Token | Type | Description |
    30||---|---|---|
    31|| `{COMMUTING}` | Transit | On train, bus, in car, not posing |
    32|| `{WAITING}` | Duration | Waiting for something, looking at phone |
    33|| `{PHONE_BOUND}` | Distraction | Phone in hand, not thinking about photo |
    34|| `{MID_WALK}` | Transit | Walking somewhere, not destination photo |
    35|| `{SLEEP_TRANSITION}` | Liminal | Just woke up / about to sleep |
    36|| `{MEAL_MUNDANE}` | Routine | Eating something boring, not styled food |
    37|| `{WORKING}` | Productivity | Doing something not-content-related |
    38|| `{TRANSIT_STARE}` | Disposition | Looking out window, zoned out |
    39|| `{EXISTENTIAL_BOREDOM}` | Energy | Low energy, not performing |
    40|
    41|### Entropy in Daily Moments
    42|
    43|```
    44|DAILY_ENTROPY_TYPES:
    45|  transit_entropy:
    46|    - on commute, not posing
    47|    - train/bus window stare
    48|    - waiting at station
    49|    - driving, not photo moment
    50|    
    51|  domestic_entropy:
    52|    - in bed, just woke up
    53|    - kitchen moment
    54|    - bathroom routine
    55|    - getting dressed
    56|    
    57|  social_entropy:
    58|    - waiting for friend
    59|    - walking with friend
    60|    - casual conversation
    61|    - not photo-focused
    62|    
    63|  mental_entropy:
    64|    - zoning out
    65|    - staring at nothing
    66|    - exhausted slump
    67|    - phone scroll absorption
    68|```
    69|
    70|---
    71|
    72|### Low-Stakes Grammar
    73|
    74|#### The "Not a Photo Moment" Grammar
    75|
    76|Real people exist in moments that aren't photo-worthy. The camera catches some of these.
    77|
    78|```
    79|NOT_PHOTO_MOMENT_GRAMMAR:
    80|  "sitting on train, phone in hand, not looking at camera"
    81|  "waiting for coffee, staring at phone, no pose"
    82|  "walking somewhere, not destination photo"
    83|  "just woke up, phone still in hand, groggy"
    84|  "in kitchen, doing nothing, casual moment"
    85|  "sitting on floor, bored, looking at nothing"
    86|  "staring out window on commute, zoned out"
    87|  
    88|These moments have no beauty intent.
    89|They are pure existence documentation.
    90|```
    91|
    92|#### Low-Stakes Dispositional States
    93|
    94|```
    95|DISPOSITIONAL_STATES:
    96|  phone_absorbed: "completely into phone, forgot about camera"
    97|  transit_auto: "on autopilot, no photo awareness"
    98|  just_existing: "doing nothing, no performance"
    99|  pre/post_sleep: "not fully awake, not trying"
   100|  mid_task: "in the middle of mundane activity"
   101|  waiting_mode: "waiting for something, no engagement"
   102|  bored_auto: "low energy, no spark, just existing"
   103|```
   104|
   105|---
   106|
   107|### Boring-Moment Architecture
   108|
   109|#### The "Boring Moment" Principle
   110|
   111|Real life has boring moments. The account should include them.
   112|
   113|```
   114|BORING_MOMENT_TYPES:
   115|  transit_boring: "long commute, nothing interesting happens"
   116|  waiting_boring: "waiting for someone/something, killing time"
   117|  domestic_boring: "home, doing nothing, ordinary evening"
   118|  task_boring: "doing chore or errand, not styled"
   119|  social_boring: "casual hang, not photo-focused, just talking"
   120|  
   121|BORING_GRAMMAR:
   122|  "sitting on train, nothing happens, just existing"
   123|  "waiting for friend, killing 20 minutes, phone scroll"
   124|  "ordinary Tuesday evening, nothing special happening"
   125|  "at grocery store, buying boring things"
   126|  "doing laundry, messy room behind her"
   127|```
   128|
   129|---
   130|
   131|### Filler-Photo System
   132|
   133|#### Filler vs Hero Photos
   134|
   135|Not every photo is meant to be engaging. Some are just... there.
   136|
   137|```
   138|FILLER_PHOTO_RULES:
   139|  - has no optimization intent
   140|  - shows mundane activity
   141|  - subject not posing
   142|  - lighting not controlled
   143|  - composition not considered
   144|  - subject is "caught" not "posed"
   145|  
   146|FILLER_PLACEMENT:
   147|  - between hero shots
   148|  - as part of dump post
   149|  - as "this happened today" evidence
   150|  - as "I'm still here" signal
   151|```
   152|
   153|---
   154|
   155|### Examples
   156|
   157|#### Example 01: Train Window Stare
   158|
   159|```
   160|on MTR, standing holding pole, phone in other hand,
   161|not looking at camera, staring out window,
   162|commuter clothes, slightly tired, blur from motion,
   163|fluorescent lighting, nothing special, just commute
   164|```
   165|
   166|#### Example 02: Just Woke Up
   167|
   168|```
   169|just woke up, phone in hand, groggy expression,
   170|hair messy, on phone before getting up,
   171|bedhead visible, morning light, not a "morning selfie",
   172|phone glow on face, not posing for anyone
   173|```
   174|
   175|#### Example 03: Waiting for Coffee
   176|
   177|```
   178|in line at coffee shop, phone in hand,
   179|not aware of camera, looking at notifications,
   180|casual clothes, nothing styled, boring moment,
   181|she doesn't know this is being photographed
   182|```
   183|
   184|---
   185|
   186|### Temporal Entropy States
   187|
   188|Time-of-day and context change entropy quality:
   189|
   190|```
   191|TEMPORAL_ENTROPY_STATES:
   192|  weekday_morning: "groggy commute, rushed, phone scrolling, tired face"
   193|  weekday_evening: "post-work exhaustion, slumped, commuting home"
   194|  weekend_morning: "slower pace, weekend energy, casual"
   195|  weekend_night: "going-out anticipation or recovering"
   196|  late_night: "2am energy, wired or exhausted, different mood"
   197|  post_meal: "food coma slump, heavy, low energy"
   198|  pre_coffee: "not fully awake, waiting for caffeine"
   199|  post_caffeine: "slightly more alive, still casual"
   200|
   201|TEMPORAL_ENTROPY_RATIO:
   202|  suggested: "20-30% of a series should be entropy moments"
   203|  minimum: "at least 1 entropy moment per 3 hero shots"
   204|  maximum: "don't let entropy dominate — balance with quality"
   205|```
   206|
   207|### Multi-Entropy Compositions
   208|
   209|Combine entropy states for richer moments:
   210|
   211|```
   212|COMPOSED_ENTROPY:
   213|  phone_absorbed + transit_auto: "on MTR, phone in hand, zoned out, not posing"
   214|  just_existing + domestic_boring: "lying on bed, staring at ceiling, doing nothing"
   215|  waiting_mode + phone_scroll: "killing 20 minutes, phone scroll, waiting for friend"
   216|  pre_post_sleep + existential_boredom: "not fully awake, phone scroll, groggy morning energy"
   217|```
   218|
   219|### Cross-Area References (Area 01 → Other Modules)
   220|
   221|- `{PHONE_BOUND}` → also appears in SOCIAL_CHAOS (audio intrusion/notification)
   222|- `{MID_WALK}` + `{SAME_TOTE_BAG}` → object memory synergy: routine objects in transit
   223|- `{SLEEP_TRANSITION}` → connects to BEAUTY_DECAY (T+8 hours, makeup settled)
   224|- Entropy moments + filler photos = natural pairing (see LOW_STAKES_PHOTO_SYSTEM)
   225|
   226|### Anti-Patterns
   227|
   228|```
   229|DAILY_ENTROPY_KILLERS:
   230|  - NO_BORING_MOMENTS: Every moment is a photo moment
   231|  - ALWAYS_PERFORMING: Never just existing
   232|  - NO_TRANSIT: No commute, no travel photos
   233|  - NO_PHONE_ABSORBED: Always aware of camera
   234|  - PRODUCTION_LIFE: Only photo-worthy moments
   235|  - STATIC_ENERGY: Always same energy regardless of time
   236|  - NO_WEEKEND_VS_WEEKDAY: Same energy every day
   237|```
   238|
   239|### Implementation Checklist (Daily Entropy)
   240|
   241|- [ ] Include transit/commute moments
   242|- [ ] Add phone-absorbed states
   243|- [ ] Include boring waiting moments
   244|- [ ] Add "not a photo" energy
   245|- [ ] Use non-destination walking shots
   246|- [ ] Include mundane domestic moments
   247|- [ ] Add just-waking-up / about-to-sleep states
   248|- [ ] Never make every moment photo-worthy
   249|- [ ] Use "caught existing" over "posed performing"
   250|
   251|---
   252|
   253|## FAILED_BEAUTY_LIBRARY
   254|
   255|### Core Tokens
   256|
   257|| Token | Type | Description |
   258||---|---|---|
   259|| `{SNEEZE_FACE}` | Accidental | Caught mid-sneeze, eyes closed, face weird |
   260|| `{WEIRD_ANGLE}` | Framing fail | Unflattering angle that somehow works |
   261|| `{DOUBLE_CHIN}` | Angle fail | Chin angle that's not flattering but real |
   262|| `{WEIRD_MOUTH}` | Expression fail | Caught with weird mouth shape |
   263|| `{MID_CHEW}` | Dispositional | Food in mouth, not expecting photo |
   264|| `{BLEGH_FACE}` | Natural | Making silly face on purpose or not |
   265|| `{WIND_DISASTER}` | Environmental | Hair blown everywhere, accepting it |
   266|| `{UGLY_CUTE}` | Intentional | Deliberately ugly but endearing |
   267|| `{FISH_FACE_FAIL}` | Expression fail | Failed fish face, looks weird |
   268|| `{SUNGLASSES_FAIL}` | Accessory fail | Sunglasses on head, not cool |
   269|| `{SQUINT_UNFLATTERING}` | Lighting fail | Squinting in unflattering way |
   270|| `{PONYTAIL_FAIL}` | Hair fail | Ponytail messy, not trying |
   271|| `{BEDHEAD_ACCEPTANCE}` | Hair state | Messy bedhead, not fighting it |
   272|| `{NO_FILTER}` | Raw | No editing, raw unfiltered face |
   273|
   274|### Ugly-Cute Type Taxonomy
   275|
   276|```
   277|UGLY_CUTE_TYPES:
   278|  accidental_weird:
   279|    - caught mid-action (sneeze, yawn, bite)
   280|    - weird angle
   281|    - double chin from angle
   282|    - eyes closed
   283|    - weird mouth shape
   284|    - blinking
   285|    - mid-laugh face
   286|    
   287|  environmental_fail:
   288|    - wind hair disaster
   289|    - food on face
   290|    - makeup smudge
   291|    - clothing malfunction
   292|    - accessory fail
   293|    
   294|  intentional_ugly:
   295|    - silly faces
   296|    - intentionally ugly poses
   297|    - goofy expressions
   298|    - joke photos
   299|    
   300|  raw_no_filter:
   301|    - unfiltered skin
   302|    - no editing
   303|    - blemishes visible
   304|    - pores visible
   305|    - texture visible
   306|    - raw real face
   307|```
   308|
   309|---
   310|
   311|### Imperfect-Attraction Grammar
   312|
   313|#### The "This Shouldn't Work But Does" Principle
   314|
   315|Ugly-cute works because it's not trying to be beautiful. The attempt at beauty is removed. The result is something more human.
   316|
   317|```
   318|UGLY_CUTE_GRAMMAR:
   319|  "making a weird face, doesn't care how she looks"
   320|  "caught mid-sneeze, face all weird, laughing at herself"
   321|  "wind blew hair everywhere, just accepting it"
   322|  "weird angle, double chin visible, too lazy to fix pose"
   323|  "fish face attempt but it just looks weird, laughing"
   324|  "photo bombed her own photo with silly face"
   325|  
   326|UGLY_CUTE_EFFECT:
   327|  - removes performance pressure
   328|  - makes her seem human
   329|  - creates contrast with polished shots
   330|  - builds intimacy with audience
   331|  - says "I'm not taking myself too seriously"
   332|```
   333|
   334|#### When Ugly-Cute Works Best
   335|
   336|```
   337|UGLY_CUTE_PLACEMENT:
   338|  - after polished hero shot
   339|  - in photodump filler
   340|  - as reaction to something
   341|  - in casual/funny context
   342|  - as throwback
   343|  - as "me being silly" energy
   344|  
   345|UGLY_CUTE_ANTI_PLACEMENT:
   346|  - as every photo (loses impact)
   347|  - as main aesthetic (wrong signal)
   348|  - without contrast from polished shots
   349|  - as "trying to be ugly cute" (not authentic)
   350|```
   351|
   352|---
   353|
   354|### Accidental-Beauty Framework
   355|
   356|#### The "Beautiful Accident" Principle
   357|
   358|Sometimes ugly-cute turns into accidental beauty. The weird angle reveals something unexpected. The silly face is somehow endearing.
   359|
   360|```
   361|ACCIDENTAL_BEAUTY_TYPES:
   362|  - weird angle reveals new perspective
   363|  - silly face creates genuine laugh
   364|  - ugly moment captures something real
   365|  - unflattering becomes iconic
   366|  - fail becomes signature look
   367|  - imperfection becomes aesthetic
   368|  
   369|ACCIDENTAL_BEAUTY_GRAMMAR:
   370|  "caught mid-something, looks weird but somehow works"
   371|  "doesn't know how this turned out cute"
   372|  "photo she meant to delete but kept"
   373|  "accidentally made a face that's now her thing"
   374|  "trying to be ugly but it just looks real"
   375|```
   376|
   377|#### The No-Filter Aesthetic
   378|
   379|The most extreme ugly-cute: showing face with no filtering at all.
   380|
   381|```
   382|NO_FILTER_TOKENS:
   383|  {RAW_SKIN}: "pores visible, texture visible, no smoothing"
   384|  {BLEMISH_ACCEPTANCE}: "acne, redness, imperfections visible"
   385|  {REAL_EXPRESSION}: "not posed smile, genuine face"
   386|  {NO_MAKEUP}: "no makeup at all, bare face"
   387|  {PHONE_CAMERA_QUALITY}: "front camera, bad lighting, raw"
   388|  {SELFIE_NOT_STYLED}: "not trying, just checking face"
   389|```
   390|
   391|---
   392|
   393|### Examples
   394|
   395|#### Example 01: Mid-Sneeze
   396|
   397|```
   398|caught mid-sneeze, eyes closed tight, face all scrunched,
   399|not expecting to be photographed, sneeze face,
   400|hand up near face, mouth open, ridiculous,
   401|laughing at herself, this should be deleted
   402|```
   403|
   404|#### Example 02: Wind Disaster Acceptance
   405|
   406|```
   407|wind blew hair completely into face, didn't fix it,
   408|just accepting the disaster, trying to talk through hair,
   409|looking ridiculous, not caring, funny moment captured,
   410|hair everywhere, some in mouth, laughing
   411|```
   412|
   413|#### Example 03: Double Chin Angle
   414|
   415|```
   416|wasn't checking angle, ended up with visible double chin,
   417|too lazy to retake, posted anyway,
   418|doesn't care about this angle, authentic moment,
   419|looks funny, audience relates to the not-perfect moment
   420|```
   421|
   422|#### Example 04: Intentional Silly Face
   423|
   424|```
   425|making the ugliest face possible for fun,
   426|eyes crossed, cheeks puffed, tongue out,
   427|completely not attractive, doesn't care,
   428|this is her being goofy, audience sees real side
   429|```
   430|
   431|---
   432|
   433|### Ugly-Cute Frequency Matrix
   434|
   435|When and how to deploy ugly-cute:
   436|
   437|```
   438|UGLY_CUTE_DEPLOYMENT:
   439|  frequency: "1-2 ugly-cute moments per 5-7 hero shots"
   440|  placement: "after polished hero shots, as dump filler"
   441|  type_by_context:
   442|    after_beach: "sunburn face, messy hair acceptance"
   443|    after_party: "smudged makeup, tired eyes"
   444|    daily: "silly face, wind disaster acceptance"
   445|    transit: "weird angle, double chin, not caring"
   446|    
   447|  authenticity_validator:
   448|    authentic: "doesn't try to be ugly-cute, just caught being real"
   449|    forced: "clearly performing 'look how ugly I'm being!'"
   450|    difference: "genuine = subject forgets camera exists"
   451|    
   452|  physical_vs_digital:
   453|    physical: "messy hair, wind disaster, double chin — embodied"
   454|    digital: "no-filter skin, blemishes visible — visual authenticity"
   455|    both: "physical ugly-cute more relatable, digital more intimate"
   456|```
   457|
   458|### Cross-Area References (Area 02 → Other Modules)
   459|
   460|- `{WIND_DISASTER}` → same mechanism as `{HAIR_BLOWN}` in SOCIAL_CHAOS (04)
   461|  - Different framing: 02 = acceptance/frustration energy; 04 = accidental chaos moment
   462|- `{BEDHEAD_ACCEPTANCE}` → connects to OBJECT_MEMORY (same towel, same morning routine)
   463|- Ugly-cute + social chaos = natural pairing: chaos moment causes accidental expression
   464|- Filler photos (LOW_STAKES) + ugly-cute = same placement strategy
   465|
   466|### Anti-Patterns
   467|
   468|```
   469|FAILED_BEAUTY_KILLERS:
   470|  - ALWAYS_PERFECT: Never any ugly-cute moments
   471|  - NO_ACCIDENT: No accidental expressions
   472|  - PRODUCTION_SERIOUS: Always taking self seriously
   473|  - FILTERED_PERFECTION: No raw face ever
   474|  - NO_SILLY: Never makes silly faces
   475|  - OVER_OPTIMIZED: Every photo is a hero shot
   476|  - NO_MISTAKES: No "should be deleted" photos
   477|```
   478|
   479|### Implementation Checklist (Failed Beauty)
   480|
   481|- [ ] Include 1-2 ugly-cute moments per series
   482|- [ ] Add accidental expression captures
   483|- [ ] Include wind/messy hair acceptance
