================================================================================
## V17 LIVED-IN OBJECT LIBRARY
### Source: modules/V17/LIVED_IN_OBJECT_LIBRARY.md
================================================================================

     1|# LIVED-IN OBJECT LIBRARY
     2|### V17 — Proof-of-Life Objects by Space
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — Runtime System
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## PHILOSOPHY
     8|
     9|**Core Problem:** AI-generated images show clean, staged spaces — no evidence of actual human habitation. Real spaces have the detritus of living: a half-drunk water bottle, a phone charger cable, a crumpled receipt.
    10|
    11|**The Fix:** Add proof-of-life objects that prove this space is actually inhabited. Objects that tell a micro-story of human presence. NOT decoration — evidence.
    12|
    13|---
    14|
    15|## PROOF-OF-LIFE VOCABULARY
    16|
    17|### Object Categories by Function
    18|
    19|| Category | Objects | Function |
    20||----------|---------|----------|
    21|| HYDRATION | water bottle half-empty, bubble tea cup, coffee cup | Been here a while |
    22|| CHARGING | phone cable, power bank, adapter | Needs battery |
    23|| NAVIGATION | phone in hand, map, compass | Just arrived or leaving |
    24|| ENTERTAINMENT | book, earphones, magazine | Killing time |
    25|| PREPARATION | mirror, outfit laid out, shopping bag | About to do something |
    26|| CONSUMPTION | half-eaten snack, drink can, wrapper | Recently active |
    27|| MAINTENANCE | skincare, makeup, perfume | Daily routine |
    28|| COMFORT | blanket, pillow, cushion | Resting |
    29|
    30|---
    31|
    32|## LIVED-IN OBJECTS BY SPACE
    33|
    34|### 🏨 HOTEL ROOM
    35|
    36|**Context:** Temporarily inhabited, but proof of current presence
    37|
    38|**Primary Objects (must include 2-3):**
    39|```
    40|• Key card on table/desk (just arrived or checking out)
    41|• Phone charger cable snaking from socket
    42|• Water bottle half-empty on nightstand
    43|• Room slippers worn and discarded by door
    44|• Curtains pulled or open (not perfectly arranged)
    45|```
    46|
    47|**Secondary Objects (include 1-2):**
    48|```
    49|• Luggage open on floor or rack
    50|• Clothes pulled from suitcase, not fully unpacked
    51|• Coffee cup from room service
    52|• Hotel pen and notepad
    53|• Mini-bar fridge open or items removed
    54|• Hotel Bible or menu on desk
    55|```
    56|
    57|**Avoid:**
    58|```
    59|❌ Perfectly made bed
    60|❌ Suitcase fully unpacked and closed
    61|❌ Nothing on desk/table
    62|❌ All belongings hidden away
    63|```
    64|
    65|**Example Prompt Integration:**
    66|```
    67|"Hotel room, key card on desk, phone charging cable visible, 
    68|room slippers kicked off by door, luggage open on floor"
    69|```
    70|
    71|---
    72|
    73|### 🏖️ BEACH / POOL
    74|
    75|**Context:** Active leisure space, temporary occupation
    76|
    77|**Primary Objects (must include 2-3):**
    78|```
    79|• Beach towel spread/half-folded (not perfectly flat)
    80|• Water bottle half-empty, sweating in sun
    81|• Sunscreen bottle with visible use (half-full, not sealed)
    82|• Flip flops or sandals kicked off to side
    83|• Beach bag with contents partially visible
    84|```
    85|
    86|**Secondary Objects (include 1-2):**
    87|```
    88|• Sunglasses folded or half-open on towel
    89|• Book or phone face-down on towel
    90|• Sandals buried in towel fold
    91|• Hat crushed or folded
    92|• Beach tote overloaded
    93|• Cooler bag or insulated cup
    94|```
    95|
    96|**Avoid:**
    97|```
    98|❌ Pristine towel spread perfectly
    99|❌ Sunscreen bottle sealed and untouched
   100|❌ All items in perfect organized arrangement
   101|❌ Nothing showing wear or use
   102|```
   103|
   104|**Example Prompt Integration:**
   105|```
   106|"Beach towel spread unevenly, sunscreen bottle half-used and sandy, 
   107|flip flops kicked to side, water bottle half-empty, beach tote overstuffed"
   108|```
   109|
   110|---
   111|
   112|### 🚇 MTR / PUBLIC TRANSIT
   113|
   114|**Context:** Commuter in transit, temporary transit presence
   115|
   116|**Primary Objects (must include 2-3):**
   117|```
   118|• Octopus card in hand or on lap
   119|• Earphones cable visible or white earbuds
   120|• Shopping bag(s) on lap or floor
   121|• Phone in hand, screen visible or face-down
   122|• Bag strap across body
   123|```
   124|
   125|**Secondary Objects (include 1-2):**
   126|```
   127|• Book or kindle held
   128|• Hand sanitizer bottle in bag
   129|• Folded umbrella on floor
   130|• Mask hanging from ear
   131|• Canned drink in hand
   132|• Magazine or newspaper folded
   133|```
   134|
   135|**Avoid:**
   136|```
   137|❌ Empty hands visible
   138|❌ No bag or personal item visible
   139|❌ Perfect posture, no commuter fatigue
   140|❌ Standing without holding anything
   141|```
   142|
   143|**Example Prompt Integration:**
   144|```
   145|"MTR seat, Octopus card on knee, shopping bag at feet, 
   146|earphones cable visible, phone face-down on lap, commuter tired"
   147|```
   148|
   149|---
   150|
   151|### 🏠 APARTMENT / HOME
   152|
   153|**Context:** Domestic space, habitual inhabitation
   154|
   155|**Primary Objects (must include 3-4):**
   156|```
   157|• Phone charging cable (visible in use)
   158|• Mug with residue or spoon in it
   159|• Remote control on couch/bed
   160|• Blanket half-folded or kicked off
   161|• Pillow dented from use
   162|• Book with bookmark (not finished)
   163|```
   164|
   165|**Secondary Objects (include 2-3):**
   166|```
   167|• Skincare products on desk/sink (used, not pristine)
   168|• Phone propped against something
   169|• Laptop open or closed with charger
   170|• Magazine or newspaper spread
   171|• Slippers worn and discarded
   172|• Half-drunk water glass
   173|• Shopping bags from recent trip
   174|```
   175|
   176|**Avoid:**
   177|```
   178|❌ All items perfectly placed
   179|❌ No sign of recent occupation
   180|❌ Bed made perfectly
   181|❌ Kitchen/show absolutely nothing used
   182|```
   183|
   184|**Example Prompt Integration:**
   185|```
   186|"Apartment living room, blanket half-folded on couch, 
   187|mug with residue on table, remote on armrest, 
   188|phone charging on side table, afternoon light"
   189|```
   190|
   191|---
   192|
   193|### ☕ CAFÉ / RESTAURANT
   194|
   195|**Context:** Social/leisure occupation of temporary space
   196|
   197|**Primary Objects (must include 2-3):**
   198|```
   199|• Cup/glass with drink remaining (not finished)
   200|• Phone on table (key prop for existence reason)
   201|• Bag on chair or floor
   202|• Menu partially visible (been here)
   203|• Napkin used and discarded
   204|```
   205|
   206|**Secondary Objects (include 1-2):**
   207|```
   208|• Book or notebook open
   209|• Laptop open (coffee shop worker vibe)
   210|• Keys and lipstick out
   211|• Sunglasses on table
   212|• Condiment packets or sugar packets used
   213|• Straw wrapper
   214|```
   215|
   216|**Avoid:**
   217|```
   218|❌ Empty table except drink
   219|❌ Pristine presentation of items
   220|❌ Nothing personal visible
   221|❌ No evidence of occupation
   222|```
   223|
   224|**Example Prompt Integration:**
   225|```
   226|"Café table, half-finished latte, phone on table surface, 
   227|bag on chair, sugar packet torn open, notebook open beside cup"
   228|```
   229|
   230|---
   231|
   232|### 🌃 STREET / OUTDOOR
   233|
   234|**Context:** Public space, in-motion occupation
   235|
   236|**Primary Objects (must include 2-3):**
   237|```
   238|• Phone in hand (always, for reality anchor)
   239|• Shopping bag(s) from recent purchase
   240|• Keys visible
   241|• Bag worn or held
   242|• Sunglasses on head or face
   243|```
   244|
   245|**Secondary Objects (include 1-2):**
   246|```
   247|• Coffee cup from nearby shop
   248|• Folded umbrella
   249|• Tissues or wrapper in hand
   250|• Receipt from purchase
   251|• Earbuds visible
   252|• Watch or bracelet visible
   253|```
   254|
   255|**Avoid:**
   256|```
   257|❌ Empty hands
   258|❌ No personal items visible
   259|❌ Too clean/posed for outdoor
   260|```
   261|
   262|**Example Prompt Integration:**
   263|```
   264|"Street scene, shopping bag in hand, phone visible, 
   265|keys on finger, sunglasses pushed up on head, just left store"
   266|```
   267|
   268|---
   269|
   270|### 🛁 BATHROOM
   271|
   272|**Context:** Personal grooming/maintenance space
   273|
   274|**Primary Objects (must include 2-3):**
   275|```
   276|• Toothbrush holder with brushes
   277|• Skincare products spread (used daily)
   278|• Mirror with steam or fingerprints
   279|• Towel hung (not folded)
   280|• Hairbrush or comb
   281|```
   282|
   283|**Secondary Objects (include 1-2):**
   284|```
   285|• Perfume bottle out
   286|• Makeup products open/used
   287|• Razor on edge
   288|• Contact lens case
   289|• Cotton pads/pads used
   290|• Bath mat damp or displaced
   291|```
   292|
   293|**Avoid:**
   294|```
   295|❌ All products perfectly aligned
   296|❌ Mirror pristine, no evidence of use
   297|❌ Nothing out of place
   298|```
   299|
   300|**Example Prompt Integration:**
   301|```
   302|"Bathroom counter, skincare products spread from use, 
   303|towel hung but not folded, mirror with steam residue, 
   304|toothbrush holder visible, slightly damp bath mat"
   305|```
   306|
   307|---
   308|
   309|### 🛏️ BEDROOM (MORNING)
   310|
   311|**Context:** Just-woke or morning routine
   312|
   313|**Primary Objects (must include 3-4):**
   314|```
   315|• Phone on mattress or pillow (checked on waking)
   316|• Pillow dented from sleep
   317|• Blanket tangled or kicked off
   318|• Curtains not perfectly arranged
   319|• Water glass from nightstand
   320|```
   321|
   322|**Secondary Objects (include 2-3):**
   323|```
   324|• Alarm clock or phone showing time
   325|• Book on pillow
   326|• Pajamas discarded (not put away)
   327|• Robe on floor or chair
   328|• Slippers not in place
   329|• Glasses on nightstand
   330|```
   331|
   332|**Avoid:**
   333|```
   334|❌ Bed perfectly made
   335|❌ All items precisely placed
   336|❌ No sign of sleep
   337|❌ Alarm clock hidden away
   338|```
   339|
   340|**Example Prompt Integration:**
   341|```
   342|"Morning bedroom, tangled blanket, phone on mattress, 
   343|pillow dented, curtains letting in uneven light, 
   344|water glass on nightstand, just woke up"
   345|```
   346|
   347|---
   348|
   349|## LIVED-IN OBJECT INTEGRATION RULES
   350|
   351|### Rule 1: Objects Must Be In-Use State
   352|
   353|```
   354|BAD: "Water bottle on table"
   355|GOOD: "Water bottle half-empty, condensation dried in patches"
   356|BAD: "Phone on table"
   357|GOOD: "Phone face-down, cable snaking to charger"
   358|```
   359|
   360|### Rule 2: Objects Tell Micro-Story
   361|
   362|Each object should suggest:
   363|- How long she's been here
   364|- What she was doing
   365|- What's about to happen
   366|- Evidence of human imperfection
   367|
   368|### Rule 3: Quantity Matters
   369|
   370|Too few = staged emptiness
   371|Too many = cluttered mess
   372|Right amount = believable lived-in (3-5 objects visible)
   373|
   374|### Rule 4: Match to Existence Reason
   375|
   376|Objects should support the photo's existence reason:
   377|- Waiting for friends → book, coffee, phone
   378|- Just arrived → luggage, key card, looking around
   379|- Resting → blanket, pillow, remote
   380|
   381|### Rule 5: Imperfect Placement
   382|
   383|```
   384|BAD: "Items arranged neatly"
   385|GOOD: "Items discarded or placed carelessly"
   386|BAD: "Towel folded perfectly"
   387|GOOD: "Towel spread, one corner folded over"
   388|```
   389|
   390|---
   391|
   392|## COMPOUND LIVED-IN EXAMPLES
   393|
   394|### Hotel Morning Check
   395|```
   396|EXISTENCE: Post-shower mirror check
   397|OBJECTS: Towel on head, phone on counter, skincare spread, 
   398|         key card on desk, water glass half-empty
   399|→ Micro-story: Just showered, checking phone, hasn't left yet
   400|```
   401|
   402|### MTR Late Night
   403|```
   404|EXISTENCE: Heading home after night out
   405|OBJECTS: Shopping bags on lap, earphones in, phone face-down, 
   406|         tired expression, slight makeup smudge
   407|→ Micro-story: Night out complete, heading home, exhausted
   408|```
   409|
   410|### Beach Afternoon
   411|```
   412|EXISTENCE: Resting between swims
   413|OBJECTS: Half-read book, sunscreen sandy, water bottle empty, 
   414|         flip flops buried in towel, hat crushed
   415|→ Micro-story: Been here hours, reapplying sunscreen, relaxing
   416|```
   417|
   418|### Café Waiting
   419|```
   420|EXISTENCE: Meeting friends at café
   421|OBJECTS: Latte half-finished, notebook open, bag on chair, 
   422|         sunglasses on head, checking phone occasionally
   423|→ Micro-story: Arrived first, killing time, friends arriving soon
   424|```
   425|
   426|---
   427|
   428|## LIVED-IN OBJECT QUICK REFERENCE
   429|
   430|| Space | Primary Objects (3) | Imperfect State |
   431||-------|-------------------|-----------------|
   432|| Hotel | Key card, charger cable, slippers | Slippers kicked off, cable visible |
   433|| Beach | Towel, sunscreen, water bottle | Uneven towel, half-empty bottle |
   434|| MTR | Octopus card, earphones, bag | Card on lap, cable visible |
   435|| Home | Phone charger, mug, remote | Cable visible, mug residue |
   436|| Café | Cup, phone, bag | Cup half-drunk, bag on chair |
   437|| Street | Phone, shopping bag, keys | Bag in hand, keys visible |
   438|| Bedroom | Phone, blanket, pillow | Tangled blanket, dented pillow |
   439|
   440|---
   441|
   442|## ANTI-AI COMPOUND
   443|
   444|```
   445|LIVE-01 (Lived-in objects) + EXIST-01 (Photo existence)
   446|→ Objects support why photo exists
   447|
   448|LIVE-02 (Object in-use state) + FAB-01 (Fabric physics)
   449|→ Human presence visible through objects AND body
   450|
   451|LIVE-03 (Micro-story objects) + MEM-01 (Incomplete framing)
   452|→ Objects create narrative through partial visibility
   453|
   454|LIVE-04 (Lived-in quantity) + COL-02 (Fuji Pro 400H)
   455|→ Real number of objects with dreamy rendering
   456|```
   457|
   458|---
   459|
   460|## QUICK GENERATION RULE
   461|
   462|**Every image needs 3-5 proof-of-life objects:**
   463|```
   464|[BASIC OBJECT] + [IMPERFECT STATE]
   465|Examples:
   466|• water bottle → half-empty, dried patches
   467|• phone → face-down, cable visible
   468|• towel → half-folded, not flat
   469|• mug → residue visible, spoon in it
   470|• bag → on floor, strap tangled
   471|```
   472|
   473|**If space looks empty:** Add 3 objects from this library.
   474|
   475|**If objects too neat:** Describe imperfect placement.
   476|
   477|---
   478|
   479|*End of LIVED_IN_OBJECT_LIBRARY.md*
   480|

================================================================================
## V17 EYE FLOW LIBRARY
### Source: modules/V17/EYE_FLOW_LIBRARY.md
================================================================================

     1|# EYE FLOW LIBRARY
     2|### V17 — Visual Reading-Path Templates
     3|### Status: ACTIVE — Runtime System
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## PHILOSOPHY
     8|
     9|**Core Problem:** AI-generated images often lack intentional visual flow — the viewer's eye doesn't know where to go, or goes to the wrong place first. Real photography guides the eye deliberately through the frame.
    10|
    11|**The Fix:** Build visual reading paths that take the viewer through the image in a specific order. Eye flow is a guided journey, not a random landing.
    12|
    13|---
    14|
    15|## EYE FLOW VOCABULARY
    16|
    17|### Reading Direction Terms
    18|
    19|| Term | Meaning |
    20||------|---------|
    21|| ANCHOR | First thing the eye finds (usually brightest or highest contrast) |
    22|| PATH | How eye moves through frame |
    23|| DESTINATION | Final resting point (usually face/eyes) |
    24|| SUPPORT | Secondary elements that guide toward destination |
    25|
    26|### Flow Manipulation Terms
    27|
    28|| Term | Meaning |
    29||------|---------|
    30|| LEAD | Element that leads eye to subject |
    31|| FRAME | Element that frames and directs attention |
    32|| HOLD | Element that pauses eye before moving |
    33|| RELEASE | Element that moves eye to next zone |
    34|
    35|---
    36|
    37|## EYE FLOW TEMPLATES
    38|
    39|### Template 1: BOTTOM-UP
    40|
    41|**Path:** Floor/Object → Body → Face
    42|
    43|**Used for:**
    44|- Ground-level shots
    45|- Documentary style
    46|- Environmental immersion
    47|
    48|**Example: Beach Towel**
    49|```
    50|ANCHOR: Sand grain detail (bottom edge)
    51|↓ PATH: Towel fold leading upward
    52|→ BODY: Subject's back/shoulder
    53|→ DESTINATION: Face/eyes
    54|
    55|Prompt: "Camera low at sand level, eye travels up through 
    56|towel fold line to body to face, ground visible at frame edge"
    57|```
    58|
    59|**Example: MTR Standing**
    60|```
    61|ANCHOR: Yellow safety line (floor level)
    62|↓ PATH: Pole leading upward
    63|→ BODY: Subject's torso and arm on pole
    64|→ DESTINATION: Face looking down at phone
    65|
    66|Prompt: "Eye travels from floor line up pole to hand to face, 
    67|ground element anchors start"
    68|```
    69|
    70|---
    71|
    72|### Template 2: DIAGONAL LEAD
    73|
    74|**Path:** Corner → Body → Face
    75|
    76|**Used for:**
    77|- Dynamic compositions
    78|- Movement moments
    79|- Strong visual energy
    80|
    81|**Example: Doorway Exit**
    82|```
    83|ANCHOR: Doorframe corner (left or right)
    84|↘ PATH: Door edge leading inward
    85|→ BODY: Subject in doorway
    86|→ DESTINATION: Face lit from behind
    87|
    88|Prompt: "Diagonal from doorframe corner through body to face, 
    89|door edge creates strong leading line"
    90|```
    91|
    92|**Example: Staircase Descent**
    93|```
    94|ANCHOR: Top step corner
    95|↘ PATH: Handrail descending
    96|→ BODY: Subject mid-staircase
    97|→ DESTINATION: Face looking up or down
    98|
    99|Prompt: "Diagonal descending from upper corner through rail to 
   100|subject to face, staircase creates strong directional flow"
   101|```
   102|
   103|---
   104|
   105|### Template 3: FOREGROUND TO SUBJECT
   106|
   107|**Path:** Foreground Object → Subject → Background
   108|
   109|**Used for:**
   110|- Spatial depth
   111|- Intimate framing
   112|- Documentary realism
   113|
   114|**Example: Café Table**
   115|```
   116|ANCHOR: Coffee cup edge (foreground, bottom corner)
   117|→ PATH: Cup leads to hand
   118|→ BODY: Subject's arm and torso
   119|→ DESTINATION: Face
   120|
   121|Prompt: "Foreground coffee cup anchors bottom, eye moves 
   122|from cup to hand to body to face, cup is 5% frame edge"
   123|```
   124|
   125|**Example: Beach Foreground**
   126|```
   127|ANCHOR: Sunglasses on towel corner
   128|→ PATH: Sunglasses lead to body
   129|→ BODY: Subject on towel
   130|→ DESTINATION: Face toward camera
   131|
   132|Prompt: "Sunglasses visible at towel edge, eye moves from 
   133|accessory to subject to face, creating depth through frame"
   134|```
   135|
   136|---
   137|
   138|### Template 4: WINDOW LIGHT SOURCE
   139|
   140|**Path:** Light → Lit Area → Face
   141|
   142|**Used for:**
   143|- Romantic/dreamy mood
   144|- Portrait warmth
   145|- Gravure aesthetic
   146|
   147|**Example: Window Selfie**
   148|```
   149|ANCHOR: Window light source (brightest area)
   150|→ PATH: Light fall on body (gradient)
   151|→ BODY: Subject lit by window
   152|→ DESTINATION: Face in light
   153|
   154|Prompt: "Window light from left, eye finds light first, 
   155|travels through lit body area to face in soft window glow"
   156|```
   157|
   158|**Example: Curtain Backlight**
   159|```
   160|ANCHOR: Curtain edge (backlit bright)
   161|→ PATH: Light through fabric to body
   162|→ BODY: Subject's silhouette or lit edge
   163|→ DESTINATION: Face catching light
   164|
   165|Prompt: "Curtain light at back, eye moves from bright 
   166|backlight through subject edge to face, creating rim light"
   167|```
   168|
   169|---
   170|
   171|### Template 5: OBJECT TO EYE CONTACT
   172|
   173|**Path:** Object → Hands → Face → Eyes
   174|
   175|**Used for:**
   176|- Activity focus
   177|- Behavioral moments
   178|- Intimate activities
   179|
   180|**Example: Phone Activity**
   181|```
   182|ANCHOR: Phone screen (brightest element)
   183|→ PATH: Hand holding phone
   184|→ BODY: Subject's head tilted toward phone
   185|→ DESTINATION: Eyes looking down at phone
   186|
   187|Prompt: "Eye moves from phone screen to holding hand to 
   188|head tilt to eyes looking down, phone screen is first anchor"
   189|```
   190|
   191|**Example: Applying Skincare**
   192|```
   193|ANCHOR: Skincare product in hand
   194|→ PATH: Hand at face
   195|→ BODY: Subject's face with product
   196|→ DESTINATION: Eyes (relaxed, mid-task)
   197|
   198|Prompt: "Eye travels from product to hand at face to face 
   199|to relaxed eyes, product anchors the reading start"
   200|```
   201|
   202|---
   203|
   204|### Template 6: ENVIRONMENTAL LEAD
   205|
   206|**Path:** Space → Body Position → Face
   207|
   208|**Used for:**
   209|- Documentary style
   210|- Context emphasis
   211|- Situational images
   212|
   213|**Example: MTR Platform**
   214|```
   215|ANCHOR: Platform edge / yellow line
   216|→ PATH: Subject's standing position
   217|→ BODY: Full body at platform
   218|→ DESTINATION: Face looking toward approaching train
   219|
   220|Prompt: "Platform environmental anchor, eye finds subject 
   221|position then travels up to face, train approach implied"
   222|```
   223|
   224|**Example: Hotel Balcony**
   225|```
   226|ANCHOR: City view at back
   227|→ PATH: Subject's position at railing
   228|→ BODY: Leaning at balcony
   229|→ DESTINATION: Face looking at view
   230|
   231|Prompt: "City background creates depth, eye moves from 
   232|cityscape to subject to face, view is context anchor"
   233|```
   234|
   235|---
   236|
   237|## EYE FLOW INTEGRATION RULES
   238|
   239|### Rule 1: Start with Anchor, End with Destination
   240|
   241|```
   242|EVERY PROMPT NEEDS:
   243|ANCHOR → [brightest or highest contrast element]
   244|PATH → [leading line to subject]
   245|DESTINATION → [face/eyes as final point]
   246|```
   247|
   248|### Rule 2: Foreground Creates Depth
   249|
   250|```
   251|Foreground anchor = strongest depth cue
   252|5-15% frame foreground object
   253|Eye moves foreground → mid → background
   254|```
   255|
   256|### Rule 3: Light Guides Eye
   257|
   258|```
   259|Brightest area = eye's first landing
   260|Use window light, screen glow, lamp
   261|Eye moves from light to lit subject
   262|```
   263|
   264|### Rule 4: Create One Clear Path
   265|
   266|```
   267|AVOID: Multiple competing anchors
   268|GOOD: One dominant path through frame
   269|Guide, don't confuse
   270|```
   271|
   272|### Rule 5: Face = Final Destination
   273|
   274|```
   275|Almost always: face/eyes are final resting point
   276|Exception: activity-focused where hands/result are final
   277|Rule: If face visible, face is destination
   278|```
   279|
   280|---
   281|
   282|## EYE FLOW + OTHER SYSTEMS
   283|
   284|### Eye Flow + Spatial Composition
   285|
   286|```
   287|SPATIAL: Foreground → Subject → Background
   288|EYE: Anchor → Path → Destination
   289|
   290|COMBINED:
   291|Foreground object (anchor) + mid-ground subject + background 
   292|creates BOTH spatial depth AND eye path
   293|```
   294|
   295|### Eye Flow + Film Stock
   296|
   297|```
   298|EYE: Light source → Subject → Face
   299|FILM: Pro 400H (soft glow) = dreamy eye path
   300|FILM: Gold 200 (warm) = nostalgic eye path
   301|FILM: C200 (casual) = documentary eye path
   302|```
   303|
   304|### Eye Flow + Existence Logic
   305|
   306|```
   307|EYE: Activity object → Hands → Face
   308|EXISTENCE: Why photo exists
   309|
   310|COMPOUND:
   311|"Phone in hand (anchor) → checking message → face showing 
   312|reaction → because she's texting boyfriend"
   313|```
   314|
   315|---
   316|
   317|## GRAVURE-SPECIFIC EYE FLOW
   318|
   319|### Beauty-Forward Gravure Path
   320|
   321|**Path:** Hair → Face → Eyes
   322|
   323|**Used for:**
   324|- Gravure aesthetic
   325|- Portrait emphasis
   326|- Beauty content
   327|
   328|**Example:**
   329|```
   330|ANCHOR: Hair framing face (top of frame)
   331|→ PATH: Hair line leading down
   332|→ BODY: Face in center
   333|→ DESTINATION: Eyes (clear focus)
   334|
   335|Prompt: "Eye starts at hair framing top of face, travels 
   336|down to face center to clear eyes, centered beauty composition"
   337|```
   338|
   339|### Soft Focus Gravure Path
   340|
   341|**Path:** Body contour → Face → Eyes
   342|
   343|**Used for:**
   344|- Romantic mood
   345|- Dreamy atmosphere
   346|- Intimate aesthetic
   347|
   348|**Example:**
   349|```
   350|ANCHOR: Soft body curve (forehead or shoulder)
   351|→ PATH: Light fall on body leading to face
   352|→ BODY: Face soft focus, body softer
   353|→ DESTINATION: Eyes catching light
   354|
   355|Prompt: "Soft focus body edge leads to face, eye travels 
   356|through soft blur to sharp eyes, dreamy romantic path"
   357|```
   358|
   359|---
   360|
   361|## ANTI-AI COMPOUND
   362|
   363|```
   364|EYE-01 (Eye flow path) + SPATIAL-01 (Three-zone depth)
   365|→ Eye guided through spatial layers
   366|
   367|EYE-02 (Light anchor) + FILM-01 (Pro 400H)
   368|→ Eye guided by window light with dreamy rendering
   369|
   370|EYE-03 (Object anchor) + EXIST-01 (Photo existence)
   371|→ Eye follows activity object supporting photo reason
   372|
   373|EYE-04 (Foreground anchor) + MEM-01 (Incomplete framing)
   374|→ Eye guided by foreground element partially in frame
   375|```
   376|
   377|---
   378|
   379|## EYE FLOW QUICK REFERENCE
   380|
   381|| Template | Anchor | Path | Destination | Use When |
   382||---------|--------|------|-------------|----------|
   383|| Bottom-up | Floor/object | Upward line | Face | Ground level |
   384|| Diagonal | Corner | Diagonal line | Face/body | Dynamic |
   385|| FG→Subject | Foreground object | Through frame | Face | Depth emphasis |
   386|| Light source | Window/light | Light fall | Face | Romantic |
   387|| Object→Eye | Phone/product | Hand→Face | Eyes | Activity |
   388|| Environmental | Space | Position | Face | Documentary |
   389|
   390|---
   391|
   392|## QUICK GENERATION RULE
   393|
   394|**Every image needs ONE eye flow path:**
   395|```
   396|ASK: Where does the eye start? Where does it end?
   397|
   398|START: Brightest element, foreground, corner, floor
   399|MIDDLE: Leading line (path)
   400|END: Face/eyes (almost always)
   401|
   402|If face visible: face is destination
   403|If no clear path: add foreground anchor
   404|```
   405|
   406|---
   407|
   408|*End of EYE_FLOW_LIBRARY.md*
   409|

## CORE ENGINE MASTER (V16 CONSOLIDATED)
### Source: core/ENGINE_MASTER.md
================================================================================

     1|# lil.troublr V16 ENGINE — CONSOLIDATED MASTER
     2|### Anti-Formula / Life Entropy Engine
     3|**Version:** V16 | **Date:** May 31, 2026 | **Status:** PRODUCTION READY
     4|
     5|---
     6|
     7|## PURPOSE
     8|
     9|V16 shifts from "simulate beautiful people" to **"simulate human social existence."**
    10|
    11|- Emotionally alive
    12|- Socially messy
    13|- Physically imperfect
    14|- Continuity-persistent
    15|- Casually attractive
    16|- Low-stakes
    17|- Accidentally memorable
    18|
    19|NOT: Optimized AI beauty rendering, endless hero shots, synthetic glamour, over-curated perfection
    20|
    21|---
    22|
    23|## SYSTEM HIERARCHY
    24|
    25|```
    26|Layer 1: IDENTITY STABILITY
    27|└── Fixed character lock (face, body, skin, hair)
    28|
    29|Layer 2: WORLD RULE ENGINE
    30|└── Environment → Physical Causation → Subject Behavior
    31|
    32|Layer 3: ANTI-REPETITION SYSTEM (V16 NEW)
    33|├── Streetwear diversity (7 categories, 35+ architectures)
    34|├── Silhouette variation (5 posture categories, 35+ silhouettes)
    35|├── Camera distance diversity (8 distances, 4 intimacy levels)
    36|└── Emotional rhythm variation
    37|
    38|Layer 4: LIFE ENTROPY SYSTEM (V16 NEW)
    39|├── Daily entropy (mundane moments)
    40|├── Failed beauty / ugly-cute moments
    41|├── Object memory continuity
    42|├── Social chaos / interruption
    43|├── Weather temperature physics
    44|└── Beauty degradation over time
    45|
    46|Layer 5: CAMERA OPERATOR ENGINE
    47|├── Camera awareness (4 levels)
    48|├── Camera operator types (friend, self, passerby)
    49|└── Platform-native camera families
    50|
    51|Layer 6: BAD PHOTO REALISM (V15)
    52|├── 26 failure types
    53|├── Combined failure patterns
    54|└── Smartphone error library
    55|
    56|Layer 7: ATMOSPHERIC PHYSICS ENGINE
    57|├── Humidity, rain, air-con, heat effects
    58|└── Hong Kong local realism
    59|
    60|Layer 8: FACS BEHAVIORAL EXPRESSION ENGINE
    61|├── Expression stack (eye → cheek → mouth → head)
    62|├── Transitional emotional states
    63|└── Behavioral timing
    64|
    65|Layer 9: PLATFORM-NATIVE POSTING SYSTEM
    66|├── Carousel logic
    67|├── Platform ecology (IG, XHS, WeChat, TikTok)
    68|└── Beauty decay
    69|```
    70|
    71|---
    72|
    73|## V16 ANTI-REPETITION HARD RULES
    74|
    75|Before generating any 10-image set, verify:
    76|
    77|1. **No repeated silhouette** across 10 consecutive images
    78|2. **3+ different camera distances** per 10 images
    79|3. **2+ different outfit families** per 10 images
    80|4. **Minimum 3 "not-a-photo" moments** per 10 images
    81|5. **Object continuity maintained** — recurring objects appear
    82|6. **Beauty state continuity** — degradation carries forward
    83|7. **≤2 hero shots** in any 10-image set
    84|8. **≥1 ugly-cute / failed beauty** moment per 10 images
    85|9. **Environmental independence** — world feels alive without her
    86|10. **≥1 social interruption / contamination** per 10 images
    87|
    88|---
    89|
    90|## MODULE 1: STREETWEAR DIVERSITY SYSTEM
    91|
    92|### 7 Outfit Categories (35+ Architectures)
    93|
    94|**CATEGORY_A — ATHLETIC**
    95|```
    96|architectures:
    97|  - sports_bra_lounge: "sports bra + biker shorts + oversized shirt, home gym"
    98|  - tennis_core: "white polo + pleated skirt + white sneakers, court aesthetic"
    99|  - pilates_flow: "scrunchie leggings + cropped hoodie + hair tie accessory"
   100|  - hike_ready: "moisture-wicking top + cargo pants + cap + backpack"
   101|  - gym_commute: "sports bra peeking under sheer shirt + joggers + slides"
   102|  - active_layer: "sports top + denim jacket + running shorts"
   103|```
   104|
   105|**CATEGORY_B — MINIMAL**
   106|```
   107|architectures:
   108|  - linen_set: "matching linen top + shorts, casual daywear"
   109|  - white_tank: "white ribbed tank + blue jeans + minimal accessories"
   110|  - structured_tee: "straight-leg pants + tucked tee + loafers"
   111|  - slip_dress: "slip dress + t-shirt underneath + sneakers"
   112|  - neutral_knit: "cream knit cardigan + black wide-leg pants"
   113|  - monochrome: "head-to-toe black or grey, minimalist accessories"
   114|```
   115|
   116|**CATEGORY_C — GIRLY**
   117|```
   118|architectures:
   119|  - sundress_casual: "flowy sundress + sneakers + no accessories"
   120|  - floral_mini: "mini floral dress + platform sandals + small bag"
   121|  - ribbon_detail: "ribbon-trim top + high-waisted jeans + ballet flats"
   122|  - cottage_soft: "pastel midi dress + cardigan + strappy sandals"
   123|  - mesh_under: "mesh long-sleeve over mini dress + boots"
   124|  - bow_back: "back-detail blouse + straight jeans + heels"
   125|```
   126|
   127|**CATEGORY_D — STREET UTILITARIAN**
   128|```
   129|architectures:
   130|  - cargo_everything: "cargo pants + crop tee + bucket hat + platform sneakers"
   131|  - utility_set: "oversized jacket + cargo skirt + chunky boots"
   132|  - tech_fleece: "Nike tech fleece + wide-leg pants + cap"
   133|  - industrial: "cargo vest over graphic tee + baggy jeans + work boots"
   134|  - urban_layer: "puffer vest + hoodie + track pants + new balances"
   135|  - tactical: "cargo shorts + utility belt + combat boots + tank top"
   136|```
   137|
   138|**CATEGORY_E — PARTY_GLAM**
   139|```
   140|architectures:
   141|  - mini_bodycon: "bodycon mini dress + heels + statement earrings"
   142|  - sequin_accident: "sequin top + denim + heels, casual-but-sparkly"
   143|  - party_silk: "silk blouse + leather pants + strappy heels"
   144|  - going_out: "cutout dress + platform heels + mini bag"
   145|  - cocktail_easy: "knee-length dress + mules + gold jewelry"
   146|  - night_metallic: "metallic skirt + crop top + chunky boots"
   147|```
   148|
   149|**CATEGORY_F — SLEEPWEAR_AS_OUTERWEAR**
   150|```
   151|architectures:
   152|  - silk_set_out: "silk pajama set worn as coordinates, + slides"
   153|  - robe_layer: "silk robe over tank + bike shorts + sneakers"
   154|  - lace_detail: "lace-trimmed cami + shorts + oversized blazer"
   155|  - satin_moment: "satin pajama set + mules + messy hair"
   156|  - matching_set: "matching sleepwear set + sneakers, intentional"
   157|  - robe_evening: "silk robe as dress + heels, hotel-bar energy"
   158|```
   159|
   160|**CATEGORY_G — LAYERED_COMPLEX**
   161|```
   162|architectures:
   163|  - oversized_under: "oversized tee + biker shorts + long cardigan"
   164|  - denim_layer: "denim jacket + slip dress + combat boots"
   165|  - leather_soft: "leather pants + oversized sweater + pointed heels"
   166|  - trench_belt: "trench coat belted + mini dress + knee boots"
   167|  - mesh_reveal: "mesh top over bralette + wide-leg pants"
   168|  - volume_play: "puff-sleeve top + slim pants + platform sneakers"
   169|```
   170|
   171|### Repeat Category, Vary Architecture Rule
   172|
   173|```
   174|REPEAT_CATEGORY_OK:
   175|  "Using 'athletic' outfit family twice in 10 images is fine"
   176|  
   177|VARY_ARCHITECTURE_MUST:
   178|  "Each use of 'athletic' must use different architecture
   179|   (sports_bra_lounge vs tennis_core, not repeated)"
   180|```

   184|## MODULE 2: SILHOUETTE VARIATION SYSTEM
   185|
   186|### 5 Posture Categories (35+ Silhouettes)
   187|
   188|**CATEGORY_A — GROUNDED**
   189|```
   190|architectures:
   191|  - seated_floor: "sitting on floor, legs crossed or extended, casual"
   192|  - crouch_partial: "crouching, knees bent, not elegant"
   193|  - squat_easy: "squats down to pick something up, natural"
   194|  - kneel_one: "one knee down, weight forward"
   195|  - sprawl_relax: "sprawled on bed/couch, full relaxation"
   196|```
   197|
   198|**CATEGORY_B — RECLINING**
   199|```
   200|architectures:
   201|  - lying_back: "lying on back, one leg bent, casual"
   202|  - side_curl: "curled on side, fetal position energy"
   203|  - prop_elbow: "lying propped on elbow, 3/4 view"
   204|  - stomach_lie: "lying face down, chin on hands"
   205|  - couch_slump: "slumped against couch arm, boneless"
   206|```
   207|
   208|**CATEGORY_C — LEANING**
   209|```
   210|architectures:
   211|  - wall_sag: "leaning against wall, weight on one hip"
   212|  - rail_support: "leaning on railing, looking down"
   213|  - table_arm: "leaning on table, relaxed posture"
   214|  - doorjamb: "standing in doorway, casual lean"
   215|  - shoulder_turn: "leaning on one shoulder, hip shift"
   216|```
   217|
   218|**CATEGORY_D — STANDING_WEAK**
   219|```
   220|architectures:
   221|  - phone_gaze: "standing, looking at phone, distracted"
   222|  - slouch_stand: "standing slouched, no pose awareness"
   223|  - leg_shift: "standing, weight on back leg, hip tilt"
   224|  - arm_cross: "arms crossed, closed body language"
   225|  - pocket_hand: "hands in pockets, hip out"
   226|```
   227|
   228|**CATEGORY_E — WALKING_IN_MOTION**
   229|```
   230|architectures:
   231|  - mid_stride: "caught mid-step, not posing"
   232|  - turn_away: "walking away from camera, back view"
   233|  - side_glance: "side walking, glance back over shoulder"
   234|  - stair_up: "walking up stairs, not checking camera"
   235|  - crowd_wade: "walking through crowd, navigating"
   236|```
   237|
   238|---
   239|
   240|## MODULE 3: CAMERA DISTANCE SYSTEM
   241|
   242|### 8 Camera Distances × 4 Intimacy Levels
   243|
   244|| Distance | Type | Intimacy | Prompt Modifier |
   245||----------|------|----------|-----------------|
   246|| DIST_01 | Extreme Close-Up | Intimate | "face only, eyes dominant, emotional" |
   247|| DIST_02 | Close-Up | Intimate | "head + shoulders, face clear" |
   248|| DIST_03 | Medium Close-Up | Personal | "waist up, face + upper body" |
   249|| DIST_04 | Medium Shot | Personal | "hips up, full torso visible" |
   250|| DIST_05 | Standard Shot | Social | "knees up visible, environmental context" |
   251|| DIST_06 | Full Body | Social | "full body, environment visible" |
   252|| DIST_07 | Environmental | Public | "body small, environment dominant" |
   253|| DIST_08 | Establishing | Public | "figure as scale marker, place is subject" |
   254|
   255|**REPEAT_RULE**: 3+ different distances per 10 images. Never use same distance 3x consecutively.
   256|
   257|---
   258|
   259|## MODULE 4: EMOTIONAL RHYTHM SYSTEM
   260|
   261|### 5 Emotional Rhythm Categories
   262|
   263|**RHYTHM_A — NEUTRAL_BORED**
   264|```
   265|states:
   266|  - transit_auto: "on autopilot, no emotional display"
   267|  - waiting_mode: "waiting, zoning out, no engagement"
   268|  - phone_absorbed: "scrolling phone, forgot camera exists"
   269|  - existential: "low energy, just existing"
   270|```
   271|
   272|**RHYTHM_B — POSITIVE_WARM**
   273|```
   274|states:
   275|  - genuine_smile: "real smile, not for camera"
   276|  - laugh_catch: "caught mid-laugh, eyes crinkled"
   277|  - warmth_reach: "reaching toward something/someone"
   278|  - comfort_deep: "deep comfort, relaxed contentment"
   279|```
   280|
   281|**RHYTHM_C — TIRED_EXHAUSTED**
   282|```
   283|states:
   284|  - post_activity: "just finished something, wind-down energy"
   285|  - late_night: "2am wired or crashed, different mood"
   286|  - post_meal: "food coma, heavy, satisfied"
   287|  - sick_recovery: "not well, cozy, fragile"
   288|```
   289|
   290|**RHYTHM_D — NEGATIVE_ADJACENT**
   291|```
   292|states:
   293|  - annoyed_mild: "slightly annoyed, minor frustration"
   294|  - confused_lost: "not sure what's happening, uncertainty"
   295|  - jealous_glance: "quick comparison moment, human"
   296|  - lazy_slump: "too lazy to engage, not performing"
   297|```
   298|
   299|**RHYTHM_E — SURPRISED_INTERRUPTED**
   300|```
   301|states:
   302|  - glance_catch: "glancing at something突然, camera caught it"
   303|  - startle_moment: "was surprised, reaction visible"
   304|  - mid_action: "caught in middle of gesture, not staged"
   305|```
   306|
   307|### Emotional Rhythm Rule
   308|
   309|```
   310|RHYTHM_VARIETY:
   311|  "No more than 3 images in same rhythm category per 10 images
   312|   Mix: 3 Neutral + 3 Positive + 2 Tired + 1 Negative + 1 Surprised
   313|   NEVER: all Positive/Cute/Flirty"
   314|```
   315|
   316|---
   317|
   318|## MODULE 5: DAILY ENTROPY SYSTEM
   319|
   320|### Core Tokens
   321|
   322|| Token | Type | Description |
   323||-------|------|-------------|
   324|| `{COMMUTING}` | Transit | On train/bus, not posing |
   325|| `{WAITING}` | Duration | Waiting for something, looking at phone |
   326|| `{PHONE_BOUND}` | Distraction | Phone in hand, not thinking about photo |
   327|| `{MID_WALK}` | Transit | Walking somewhere, not destination photo |
   328|| `{SLEEP_TRANSITION}` | Liminal | Just woke up / about to sleep |
   329|| `{MEAL_MUNDANE}` | Routine | Eating something boring, not styled food |
   330|| `{WORKING}` | Productivity | Doing something not-content-related |
   331|| `{TRANSIT_STARE}` | Disposition | Looking out window, zoned out |
   332|| `{EXISTENTIAL_BOREDOM}` | Energy | Low energy, not performing |
   333|
   334|### Low-Stakes Grammar
   335|
   336|```
   337|NOT_PHOTO_MOMENT_GRAMMAR:
   338|  "sitting on train, phone in hand, not looking at camera"
   339|  "waiting for coffee, staring at phone, no pose"
   340|  "walking somewhere, not destination photo"
   341|  "just woke up, phone still in hand, groggy"
   342|  "in kitchen, doing nothing, casual moment"
   343|  "sitting on floor, bored, looking at nothing"
   344|  
   345|These moments have no beauty intent.
   346|They are pure existence documentation.
   347|```
   348|
   349|### Temporal Entropy States
   350|
   351|| Token | Description |
   352||-------|-------------|
   353|| `weekday_morning` | Groggy commute, rushed, phone scrolling |
   354|| `weekday_evening` | Post-work exhaustion, slumped, commuting home |
   355|| `weekend_morning` | Slower pace, casual, not rushed |
   356|| `late_night` | 2am energy, wired or exhausted |
   357|| `post_meal` | Food coma slump, low energy |
   358|| `pre_coffee` | Not fully awake, survival mode |
   359|
   360|---
   361|
   362|## MODULE 6: FAILED BEAUTY SYSTEM
   363|
   364|### Core Tokens
   365|
   366|| Token | Type | Description |
   367||-------|------|-------------|
   368|| `{SNEEZE_FACE}` | Accidental | Caught mid-sneeze, eyes closed, face weird |
   369|| `{WEIRD_ANGLE}` | Framing fail | Unflattering angle that somehow works |
   370|| `{DOUBLE_CHIN}` | Angle fail | Chin angle not flattering, too lazy to fix |
   371|| `{WEIRD_MOUTH}` | Expression fail | Caught with weird mouth shape |
   372|| `{MID_CHEW}` | Dispositional | Food in mouth, not expecting photo |
   373|| `{BLEGH_FACE}` | Natural | Making silly face, tongue out, goofy |
   374|| `{WIND_DISASTER}` | Environmental | Hair blown everywhere, accepting it |
   375|| `{UGLY_CUTE}` | Intentional | Deliberately ugly but endearing |
   376|| `{BEDHEAD_ACCEPTANCE}` | Hair state | Messy bedhead, not fighting it |
   377|| `{NO_FILTER}` | Raw | No editing, raw unfiltered face |
   378|
   379|### No-Filter Sub-Tokens
   380|
   381|| Token | Description |
   382||-------|-------------|
   383|| `{RAW_SKIN}` | Pores visible, texture visible, no smoothing |
   384|| `{BLEMISH_ACCEPTANCE}` | Acne, redness, imperfections visible |
   385|| `{NO_MAKEUP}` | No makeup at all, bare face |
   386|| `{PHONE_CAMERA_QUALITY}` | Front camera, bad lighting, raw capture |
   387|
   388|### Ugly-Cute Grammar
   389|
   390|```
   391|UGLY_CUTE_GRAMMAR:
   392|  "making a weird face, doesn't care how she looks"
   393|  "caught mid-sneeze, face all weird, laughing at herself"
   394|  "wind blew hair everywhere, just accepting it"
   395|  "weird angle, double chin visible, too lazy to fix pose"
   396|  
   397|UGLY_CUTE_EFFECT:
   398|  - removes performance pressure
   399|  - makes her seem human
   400|  - creates contrast with polished shots
   401|  - builds intimacy with audience
   402|```
   403|
   404|### Compositional Pairings
   405|
   406|| Pairing | Effect |
   407||---------|--------|
   408|| `{COMMUTING}` + `{WEIRD_ANGLE}` | Transit boredom meets unflattering framing |
   409|| `{PHONE_BOUND}` + `{SNEEZE_FACE}` | Phone distraction creates accidental expression |
   410|| `{SLEEP_TRANSITION}` + `{BEDHEAD_ACCEPTANCE}` | Maximum morning vulnerability |
   411|| `{WIND_DISASTER}` + `{MID_WALK}` | Environmental fail during transit entropy |
   412|| `{EXISTENTIAL_BOREDOM}` + `{UGLY_CUTE}` | Deliberate ugly as boredom antidote |
   413|
   414|### Frequency Rule
   415|
   416|```
   417|UGLY_CUTE_DEPLOYMENT:
   418|  frequency: "1-2 ugly-cute moments per 5-7 hero shots"
   419|  placement: "after polished hero shots, as dump filler"
   420|  NEVER: every photo is ugly-cute (loses impact)
   421|  AUTHENTICITY: subject forgets camera exists
   422|```
   423|
   424|---
   425|
   426|## MODULE 7: OBJECT MEMORY SYSTEM
   427|
   428|### Core Tokens
   429|
   430|| Token | Trigger | Usage |
   431||-------|---------|-------|
   432|| `{SAME_BIKINI}` | Recurring swimwear | Same top + bottom, different context |
   433|| `{SAME_CLAW_CLIP}` | Hair repetition | Hair up same way, different lighting |
   434|| `{SAME_TOTE_BAG}` | Bag reuse | Same bag, different contents |
   435|| `{SAME_IPHONE_CASE}` | Phone in frame | Same case, different angle |
   436|| `{SAME_HOODIE}` | Loungewear repeat | Worn hoodie, slightly different state |
   437|| `{SAME_NECKLACE}` | Jewelry continuity | Same pendant, different necklines |
   438|| `{SAME_SANDALS}` | Footwear reuse | Same sandals, different pedicure state |
   439|| `{SAME_BEDSHEETS}` | Background continuity | Same sheets, different time of day |
   440|| `{SAME_WATER_BOTTLE}` | Hydration prop | Same bottle, different fill level |
   441|| `{SAME_APARTMENT_CORNER}` | Background repeat | Same corner, different outfit |
   442|| `{SAME_TOWEL}` | Post-shower repetition | Same towel, different hair state |
   443|
   444|### Object Lifecycle Arc
   445|
   446|```
   447|ITEM_APPEARANCE_N → N+1 TRANSITIONS:
   448|  1. "new" state: pristine, just bought
   449|  2. "regular use" state: normal wear
   450|  3. "favorite item" state: slightly faded, trusted
   451|  4. "background prop" state: visible but not central
   452|  5. "worn with pride" state: very used, part of identity
   453|
   454|This arc takes 10-20 uploads to complete naturally.
   455|Never rush the object lifecycle.
   456|```
   457|
   458|### Repeat Frequency Rule
   459|
   460|```
   461|REOCCURRING_OBJECT_TRIGGERS:
   462|  frequency: "every_4-7_uploads"
   463|  variation: "same_item_different_context"
   464|  aging: "show_item_wear_over_time"
   465|  placement: "background_prop_or_hand_held"
   466|```
   467|
   468|---
   469|
   470|## MODULE 8: SOCIAL CHAOS SYSTEM
   471|
   472|### Core Tokens
   473|
   474|| Token | Trigger | Usage |
   475||-------|---------|-------|
   476|| `{FRIEND_IN_FRAME}` | Person enters | Blurred, mid-conversation, unexpected |
   477|| `{STRANGER_BLUR}` | Random pedestrian | Walking past, not posing, motion blur |
   478|| `{WAITER_PAST}` | Service interruption | Walking through background, tray in hand |
   479|| `{TRAIN_ARRIVAL}` | Transportation chaos | Platform crowd, motion blur |
   480|| `{FLASH_BLOCKED}` | Someone blocks flash | Hand partially obscuring light |
   481|| `{HAIR_BLOWN}` | Wind disruption | Hair across face, uncontrolled |
   482|| `{BAG_FALLING}` | Object interruption | Bag sliding off shoulder |
   483|| `{ACCIDENTAL_SPLASH}` | Water disruption | Water splash, wet clothes |
   484|| `{CROWD_COMPRESSION}` | Dense environment | Packed space, limited mobility |
   485|| `{CALLED_BY_NAME}` | Audio intrusion | Someone calls out, subject turns surprised |
   486|
   487|### Chaos Layer System
   488|
   489|```
   490|CHAOS_LAYER_SYSTEM:
   491|  Layer 1: BACKGROUND_AMBIENCE (0-20% attention)
   492|    - distant crowd blur, far background motion
   493|  Layer 2: MIDGROUND_INTERRUPTION (20-40% attention)
   494|    - friend partially in frame, person walking past
   495|  Layer 3: FOREGROUND_DISRUPTION (40-60% attention)
   496|    - hair blown across face, splash moment
   497|  Layer 4: FULL_FRAME_INTERRUPTION (60-80% attention)
   498|    - friend physically interrupts, crowd compression
   499|  Layer 5: SUBJECT_REACTION (80-100% attention)
   500|    - subject reacting to chaos, startled expression
   501|

    27|
    28|## Key Rules Summary
    29|
    30|### Anti-Repetition (per 10 images)
    31|- ✅ No repeated silhouette
    32|- ✅ 3+ camera distances
    33|- ✅ 2+ outfit families
    34|- ✅ ≤2 hero shots
    35|
    36|### Entropy System
    37|- ✅ 20-30% entropy moments
    38|- ✅ 1-2 ugly-cute per series
    39|- ✅ 1 filler photo per 2-3 hero
    40|- ✅ Object repeat every 4-7 uploads
    41|
    42|### Chaos System
    43|- ✅ 1 social interruption per 5 photos
    44|- ✅ Environmental independence
    45|- ✅ Temperature physics on body
    46|- ✅ Beauty carries timestamps
    47|
